// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/epg/EpgStore.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.epg

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.EpgProgram
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.io.File

class EpgStore(context: Context) {
    private val file = File(context.applicationContext.filesDir, "epg_cache.jsonl")

    fun save(programs: List<EpgProgram>) = synchronized(LOCK) {
        if (!file.parentFile.exists()) file.parentFile.mkdirs()
        val byKey = (readAll() + programs).associateBy { cacheKey(it) }.values
            .filter { it.endTimeMs > System.currentTimeMillis() - 60 * 60 * 1000L }
            .sortedBy { it.startTimeMs }
        file.bufferedWriter().use { writer ->
            byKey.forEach { program ->
                writer.append(toJson(program).toString())
                writer.newLine()
            }
        }
    }

    fun getPrograms(channelStableKey: String? = null): List<EpgProgram> = synchronized(LOCK) {
        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        readAll()
            .filter { channelStableKey == null || it.channelStableKey == channelStableKey }
            .filter { it.endTimeMs > now - 30 * 60 * 1000L }
            .sortedBy { it.startTimeMs }
    }

    fun getNowNext(channelStableKey: String): List<EpgProgram> = getPrograms(channelStableKey).take(4)

    private fun readAll(): List<EpgProgram> {
        if (!file.exists()) return emptyList()
        return file.useLines { lines -> lines.mapNotNull { line -> runCatching { fromJson(JSONObject(line)) }.getOrNull() }.toList() }
    }

    private fun toJson(program: EpgProgram): JSONObject = JSONObject()
        .put("channelStableKey", program.channelStableKey)
        .put("channelTitle", program.channelTitle)
        .put("programTitle", program.programTitle)
        .put("description", program.description)
        .put("startTimeMs", program.startTimeMs)
        .put("endTimeMs", program.endTimeMs)
        .put("source", program.source)

    private fun fromJson(obj: JSONObject): EpgProgram = EpgProgram(
        channelStableKey = obj.optString("channelStableKey"),
        channelTitle = obj.optString("channelTitle"),
        programTitle = obj.optString("programTitle", "Program"),
        description = obj.optString("description", ""),
        startTimeMs = obj.optLong("startTimeMs", 0L),
        endTimeMs = obj.optLong("endTimeMs", 0L),
        source = obj.optString("source", "Cache")
    )

    private fun cacheKey(program: EpgProgram): String = "${program.channelStableKey}:${program.startTimeMs}:${program.programTitle}"

    companion object { private val LOCK = Any() }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CatalogInsightEngine.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import java.text.Normalizer
import kotlin.math.roundToInt

object CatalogInsightEngine {
    data class QualityInsight(
        val item: IptvItem,
        val score: Int,
        val grade: String,
        val tags: List<String>,
        val issues: List<String>,
        val duplicateKey: String
    )

    data class DuplicateGroup(
        val key: String,
        val title: String,
        val items: List<QualityInsight>,
        val best: QualityInsight
    )

    fun score(item: IptvItem): QualityInsight {
        var score = 35
        val tags = mutableListOf<String>()
        val issues = mutableListOf<String>()
        val text = listOf(item.title, item.categoryName.orEmpty(), item.sourceLabel.orEmpty()).joinToString(" ").lowercase()

        if (item.isPlayable || item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES) {
            score += 16
            tags.add("Playable")
        } else {
            score -= 20
            issues.add("No playable stream")
        }

        if (!item.coverUrl.isNullOrBlank()) score += 8 else issues.add("Missing poster")
        if (!item.backdropUrl.isNullOrBlank()) score += 5
        if (!item.year.isNullOrBlank()) score += 5 else issues.add("Missing year")
        if (!item.rating.isNullOrBlank()) score += ((item.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0).coerceIn(0.0, 10.0) * 1.3).roundToInt()
        if (item.genres.isNotEmpty()) score += 6 else issues.add("Missing genre")
        if (!item.metadataProvider.isNullOrBlank() || !item.tmdbId.isNullOrBlank() || !item.imdbId.isNullOrBlank()) {
            score += 8
            tags.add("Metadata matched")
        } else {
            issues.add("Not metadata matched")
        }

        val isUltra = text.contains("4k") || text.contains("uhd") || text.contains("2160")
        val isHd = text.contains("fhd") || text.contains("1080") || text.contains("hd")
        when {
            isUltra -> { score += 10; tags.add("4K/UHD") }
            isHd -> { score += 4; tags.add("HD") }
            text.contains("cam") || text.contains("telesync") || text.contains(" ts ") -> { score -= 22; issues.add("Likely CAM/TS quality") }
        }

        if (text.contains("adult") || text.contains("xxx") || text.contains("18+")) {
            score -= 30
            issues.add("Adult/clutter risk")
        }
        if (text.contains("duplicate") || text.contains("backup") || text.contains("test")) {
            score -= 16
            issues.add("Provider clutter keyword")
        }
        if (item.title.length > 92) {
            score -= 6
            issues.add("Noisy title")
        }

        val cleanScore = score.coerceIn(0, 100)
        val grade = when {
            cleanScore >= 85 -> "A"
            cleanScore >= 72 -> "B"
            cleanScore >= 58 -> "C"
            cleanScore >= 42 -> "D"
            else -> "F"
        }
        return QualityInsight(
            item = item,
            score = cleanScore,
            grade = grade,
            tags = tags.distinct(),
            issues = issues.distinct(),
            duplicateKey = duplicateKey(item)
        )
    }

    fun qualityReport(items: List<IptvItem>): List<QualityInsight> = items
        .asSequence()
        .filter { it.contentType != ContentType.ACTION }
        .map(::score)
        .sortedWith(compareBy<QualityInsight> { it.score }.thenBy { it.item.title.lowercase() })
        .toList()

    fun duplicateGroups(items: List<IptvItem>): List<DuplicateGroup> {
        return qualityReport(items)
            .filter { it.duplicateKey.isNotBlank() }
            .groupBy { it.duplicateKey }
            .values
            .filter { group -> group.size > 1 }
            .map { group ->
                val sorted = group.sortedWith(compareByDescending<QualityInsight> { it.score }.thenByDescending { it.item.addedAtMs })
                DuplicateGroup(
                    key = sorted.first().duplicateKey,
                    title = displayTitle(sorted.first().item),
                    items = sorted,
                    best = sorted.first()
                )
            }
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<DuplicateGroup> { it.items.size }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase() })
    }

    fun smartPicks(items: List<IptvItem>, mode: String, limit: Int = 40): List<IptvItem> {
        val insights = qualityReport(items).asSequence().filter { it.item.isPlayable || it.item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES }
        val filtered = when (mode) {
            "short" -> insights.filter { (it.item.durationMs in 1L..6_300_000L) || it.item.contentType == ContentType.EPISODE }
            "family" -> insights.filterNot { insight ->
                val text = listOf(insight.item.title, insight.item.categoryName.orEmpty(), insight.item.description).joinToString(" ").lowercase()
                listOf("adult", "xxx", "18+", "horror", "violent", "violence", "mature").any { text.contains(it) }
            }
            "new" -> insights.filter { it.item.addedAtMs > 0L }
            "hidden" -> insights.filter { it.score in 62..86 && (it.item.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0) >= 6.5 }
            "quality" -> insights.filter { it.score >= 72 }
            else -> insights
        }
        return filtered
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<QualityInsight> { it.score }.thenByDescending { it.item.addedAtMs })
            .take(limit)
            .map { it.item.copy(sourceLabel = "${mode.replaceFirstChar(Char::titlecase)} pick \u2022 ${it.grade} quality") }
            .toList()
    }

    fun duplicateKey(item: IptvItem): String {
        val clean = normalizeTitle(item.parentSeriesTitle ?: item.title)
        if (clean.length < 4) return ""
        val year = item.year?.takeIf { it.matches(Regex("\\d{4}")) }.orEmpty()
        return when (item.contentType) {
            ContentType.EPISODE -> listOf(item.providerAccountId.orEmpty(), "episode", clean, item.seasonNumber ?: 0, item.episodeNumber ?: 0).joinToString(":")
            else -> listOf(item.providerAccountId.orEmpty(), item.contentType.name.lowercase(), clean, year).joinToString(":")
        }
    }

    fun normalizeTitle(raw: String): String {
        val normalized = Normalizer.normalize(raw, Normalizer.Form.NFD).replace(Regex("\\p{Mn}+"), "")
        return normalized.lowercase()
            .replace(Regex("\\[[^]]*]"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\([^)]*\\)"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("(?i)\\b(4k|uhd|fhd|hd|sd|hdr|dv|x264|x265|hevc|h264|h265|bluray|blu ray|web[- ]?dl|webrip|brrip|hdrip|1080p|720p|2160p|multi|dubbed|subbed|complete)\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\b(19|20)\\d{2}\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("[^a-z0-9]+"), " ")
            .trim()
    }

    private fun displayTitle(item: IptvItem): String = item.parentSeriesTitle ?: item.title
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CatalogMatcher.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType

object CatalogMatcher {
    fun findLocalCatalogMatch(localCatalog: List<IptvItem>, item: IptvItem): IptvItem? {
        return localCatalog.firstOrNull { it.stableKey == item.stableKey && it.isDisplayPlayable() }
            ?: localCatalog.firstOrNull { item.streamId.isNotBlank() && it.streamId == item.streamId && it.contentType == item.contentType }
            ?: bestMatchByScore(localCatalog.filter { it.isDisplayPlayable() }, item)
    }

    fun matchPlayableLocalCatalog(localCatalog: List<IptvItem>, item: IptvItem): IptvItem? {
        return findLocalCatalogMatch(localCatalog.filter { it.isDisplayPlayable() }, item)
    }

    fun IptvItem.isDisplayPlayable(): Boolean {
        return isPlayable || contentType == ContentType.SERIES
    }

    fun sameCatalogIdentity(left: IptvItem, right: IptvItem): Boolean {
        return left.stableKey == right.stableKey ||
            (!left.tmdbId.isNullOrBlank() && left.tmdbId == right.tmdbId && left.contentType == right.contentType) ||
            (!left.imdbId.isNullOrBlank() && left.imdbId == right.imdbId && left.contentType == right.contentType) ||
            (left.contentType == right.contentType && normalizeTitle(left.title) == normalizeTitle(right.title))
    }

    fun mergePlayableMatch(metadataItem: IptvItem, playableMatch: IptvItem): IptvItem {
        return playableMatch.copy(
            description = metadataItem.description.ifBlank { playableMatch.description },
            rating = metadataItem.rating ?: playableMatch.rating,
            year = metadataItem.year ?: playableMatch.year,
            coverUrl = metadataItem.coverUrl ?: playableMatch.coverUrl,
            backdropUrl = metadataItem.backdropUrl ?: playableMatch.backdropUrl,
            metadataProvider = metadataItem.metadataProvider ?: playableMatch.metadataProvider,
            metadataId = metadataItem.metadataId ?: playableMatch.metadataId,
            serverStableKey = metadataItem.serverStableKey ?: playableMatch.serverStableKey,
            traktSlug = metadataItem.traktSlug ?: playableMatch.traktSlug,
            traktType = metadataItem.traktType ?: playableMatch.traktType,
            imdbId = metadataItem.imdbId ?: playableMatch.imdbId,
            tmdbId = metadataItem.tmdbId ?: playableMatch.tmdbId,
            genres = metadataItem.genres.ifEmpty { playableMatch.genres },
            sourceLabel = metadataItem.sourceLabel?.replace("Not matched", "Available") ?: playableMatch.sourceLabel
        )
    }

    fun normalizeTitle(value: String): String {
        return value.lowercase()
            .replace(Regex("\\[[^]]*]"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\([^)]*\\)"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("(?i)\\b(nf|netflix|amzn|amazon|hbo|max|disney|apple\\s*tv|itunes)\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("(?i)\\b(4k|uhd|fhd|hd|sd|hdr|dv|x264|x265|hevc|h264|h265|bluray|blu ray|web[- ]?dl|webrip|brrip|hdrip|1080p|720p|2160p)\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("(?i)\\b(s\\d{1,2}|season\\s*\\d{1,2}|complete|multi|dual audio|subbed|dubbed)\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\b(19|20)\\d{2}\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("[^a-z0-9]+"), " ")
            .trim()
    }

    private fun bestMatchByScore(localCatalog: List<IptvItem>, item: IptvItem): IptvItem? {
        return localCatalog
            .asSequence()
            .filter { contentTypesCompatible(it, item) }
            .map { candidate -> candidate to matchScore(candidate, item) }
            .filter { (_, score) -> score >= 70 }
            .maxByOrNull { (_, score) -> score }
            ?.first
    }

    private fun matchScore(candidate: IptvItem, item: IptvItem): Int {
        var score = 0
        if (!item.tmdbId.isNullOrBlank() && candidate.tmdbId == item.tmdbId) score += 120
        if (!item.imdbId.isNullOrBlank() && candidate.imdbId == item.imdbId) score += 115
        if (!item.metadataId.isNullOrBlank() && item.metadataProvider?.contains("tmdb", ignoreCase = true) == true && candidate.tmdbId == item.metadataId) score += 110
        if (!candidate.metadataId.isNullOrBlank() && candidate.metadataProvider?.contains("tmdb", ignoreCase = true) == true && candidate.metadataId == item.tmdbId) score += 110

        val candidateTitle = normalizeTitle(candidate.title)
        val itemTitle = normalizeTitle(item.title)
        if (candidateTitle.isNotBlank() && itemTitle.isNotBlank()) {
            if (candidateTitle == itemTitle) score += 85
            else if (titlesLooselyMatch(candidate.title, item.title)) score += 62
            score += (titleTokenOverlap(candidateTitle, itemTitle) * 45).toInt()
        }

        val candidateYear = yearFrom(candidate.year ?: candidate.title)
        val itemYear = yearFrom(item.year ?: item.title)
        if (candidateYear != null && itemYear != null) {
            score += if (candidateYear == itemYear) 20 else -20
        }
        return score
    }

    private fun contentTypesCompatible(left: IptvItem, right: IptvItem): Boolean {
        if (left.contentType == right.contentType) return true
        return left.contentType == ContentType.SERIES && right.contentType == ContentType.EPISODE ||
            left.contentType == ContentType.EPISODE && right.contentType == ContentType.SERIES
    }

    private fun titleTokenOverlap(left: String, right: String): Double {
        val a = left.split(" ").filter { it.length >= 3 }.toSet()
        val b = right.split(" ").filter { it.length >= 3 }.toSet()
        if (a.isEmpty() || b.isEmpty()) return 0.0
        return a.intersect(b).size.toDouble() / maxOf(a.size, b.size).toDouble()
    }

    private fun yearFrom(value: String?): String? {
        return Regex("\\b(19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})\\b").find(value.orEmpty())?.groupValues?.getOrNull(1)
    }

    private fun titlesLooselyMatch(left: String, right: String): Boolean {
        val a = normalizeTitle(left)
        val b = normalizeTitle(right)
        return a.length >= 4 && b.length >= 4 && (a.contains(b) || b.contains(a) || titleTokenOverlap(a, b) >= 0.72)
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CatalogStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.io.File

class CatalogStore(context: Context) {
    private val appContext = context.applicationContext
    private val prefs = appContext.getSharedPreferences("catalog_store", Context.MODE_PRIVATE)
    private val catalogDir = File(appContext.filesDir, "catalog_store")

    fun isCacheExpired(contentType: ContentType, intervalDays: Int): Boolean {
        val lastSync = prefs.getLong(keySync(contentType), 0L)
        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        return (now - lastSync) > (intervalDays.toLong() * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000L)
    }

    fun isRefreshAttemptExpired(contentType: ContentType, intervalDays: Int): Boolean {
        val lastAttempt = prefs.getLong(keyRefreshAttempt(contentType), 0L)
        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        return (now - lastAttempt) > (intervalDays.toLong() * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000L)
    }

    fun getLastSyncedAt(contentType: ContentType): Long = prefs.getLong(keySync(contentType), 0L)

    fun markSynced(contentType: ContentType) {
        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        prefs.edit()
            .putLong(keySync(contentType), now)
            .putLong(keyRefreshAttempt(contentType), now)
            .apply()
    }

    fun markRefreshAttempt(contentType: ContentType) {
        prefs.edit().putLong(keyRefreshAttempt(contentType), System.currentTimeMillis()).apply()
    }

    fun clearCache() {
        memoryCache.clear()
        prefs.edit().clear().apply()
        deleteCatalogFiles()
    }

    fun setServerIgnoredStableKeys(keys: Set<String>) {
        prefs.edit().putStringSet(KEY_SERVER_IGNORED, keys).apply()
    }

    fun ignoreItem(item: IptvItem) {
        val ignored = getLocalIgnoredStableKeys().toMutableSet()
        ignored.add(item.stableKey)
        prefs.edit().putStringSet(KEY_LOCAL_IGNORED, ignored).apply()
    }

    fun unignoreItem(item: IptvItem) {
        val ignored = getLocalIgnoredStableKeys().toMutableSet()
        ignored.remove(item.stableKey)
        prefs.edit().putStringSet(KEY_LOCAL_IGNORED, ignored).apply()
    }

    fun isIgnored(item: IptvItem): Boolean = ignoredStableKeys().contains(item.stableKey)

    fun getServerIgnoredStableKeys(): Set<String> {
        return prefs.getStringSet(KEY_SERVER_IGNORED, emptySet()) ?: emptySet()
    }

    private fun getLocalIgnoredStableKeys(): Set<String> {
        return prefs.getStringSet(KEY_LOCAL_IGNORED, emptySet()) ?: emptySet()
    }

    private fun ignoredStableKeys(): Set<String> = getServerIgnoredStableKeys() + getLocalIgnoredStableKeys()

    fun saveItems(items: List<IptvItem>) {
        upsertItems(items)
    }

    fun upsertItems(items: List<IptvItem>) {
        ensureMigrated()
        items
            .filter { it.title.isNotBlank() && it.contentType != ContentType.ACTION }
            .groupBy { it.contentType }
            .forEach { (contentType, incoming) ->
                val merged = (readItemsForType(contentType) + incoming)
                    .associateBy { it.stableKey }
                    .values
                    .sortedWith(compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.addedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase() })
                writeItemsForType(contentType, merged)
                writeSummary(contentType, merged)
            }
    }

    fun replaceType(contentType: ContentType, items: List<IptvItem>) {
        ensureMigrated()
        val cleanItems = items
            .filter { it.title.isNotBlank() && it.contentType == contentType }
            .associateBy { it.stableKey }
            .values
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.addedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase() })
        writeItemsForType(contentType, cleanItems)
        writeSummary(contentType, cleanItems)
    }

    fun getAllItems(): List<IptvItem> {
        ensureMigrated()
        val ignored = ignoredStableKeys()
        return ContentType.values()
            .filterNot { it == ContentType.ACTION }
            .flatMap { readItemsForType(it) }
            .filterNot { ignored.contains(it.stableKey) }
    }

    fun getItems(contentType: ContentType): List<IptvItem> {
        ensureMigrated()
        val ignored = ignoredStableKeys()
        return readItemsForType(contentType).filterNot { ignored.contains(it.stableKey) }
    }

    fun getItems(contentType: ContentType, categoryName: String?): List<IptvItem> {
        if (categoryName.isNullOrBlank()) return getItems(contentType)
        ensureMigrated()
        val ignored = ignoredStableKeys()
        return readItemsForType(contentType)
            .asSequence()
            .filterNot { ignored.contains(it.stableKey) }
            .filter { it.categoryName?.equals(categoryName, ignoreCase = true) == true }
            .toList()
    }

    fun countItems(contentType: ContentType): Int {
        ensureMigrated()
        return prefs.getInt(keyCount(contentType), -1).takeIf { it >= 0 } ?: readItemsForType(contentType).size
    }

    fun getCategoryCounts(contentType: ContentType): Map<String, Int> {
        ensureMigrated()
        val raw = prefs.getString(keyCategoryCounts(contentType), null)
        if (!raw.isNullOrBlank()) {
            val obj = JSONObject(raw)
            val counts = mutableMapOf<String, Int>()
            obj.keys().forEach { name -> counts[name] = obj.optInt(name, 0) }
            return counts
        }
        val counts = readItemsForType(contentType)
            .groupingBy { it.categoryName ?: "Uncategorized" }
            .eachCount()
        writeSummary(contentType, readItemsForType(contentType))
        return counts
    }

    fun getSpecialCounts(contentType: ContentType): SpecialCounts {
        ensureMigrated()
        val raw = prefs.getString(keySpecialCounts(contentType), null)
        if (!raw.isNullOrBlank()) {
            val obj = JSONObject(raw)
            return SpecialCounts(
                recentlyAdded = obj.optInt("recentlyAdded", 0),
                ultraHd = obj.optInt("ultraHd", 0),
                playable = obj.optInt("playable", 0)
            )
        }
        val items = readItemsForType(contentType)
        writeSummary(contentType, items)
        return buildSpecialCounts(items)
    }

    fun search(query: String): List<IptvItem> {
        val tokens = query.lowercase().split(" ").map { it.trim() }.filter { it.isNotBlank() }
        if (tokens.isEmpty()) return emptyList()
        return getAllItems()
            .filter { item ->
                val searchable = listOf(
                    item.title,
                    item.description,
                    item.categoryName.orEmpty(),
                    item.year.orEmpty(),
                    item.genres.joinToString(" "),
                    item.sourceLabel.orEmpty(),
                    item.parentSeriesTitle.orEmpty()
                ).joinToString(" ").lowercase()
                tokens.all { searchable.contains(it) }
            }
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.lastWatchedAtMs }.thenByDescending { it.addedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase() })
            .take(100)
    }

    fun getRecentlyAdded(contentType: ContentType, limit: Int): List<IptvItem> {
        return getAllItems()
            .filter { it.contentType == contentType }
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.addedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase() })
            .take(limit)
    }

    private fun ensureMigrated() {
        val raw = prefs.getString(KEY_ITEMS, null) ?: return
        val legacyItems = readLegacyItems(raw)
        legacyItems
            .filter { it.title.isNotBlank() && it.contentType != ContentType.ACTION }
            .groupBy { it.contentType }
            .forEach { (contentType, items) -> writeItemsForType(contentType, items) }
        prefs.edit().remove(KEY_ITEMS).apply()
    }

    private fun readLegacyItems(raw: String): List<IptvItem> {
        val array = JSONArray(raw)
        val items = mutableListOf<IptvItem>()
        for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
            val obj = array.optJSONObject(index) ?: continue
            items.add(fromJson(obj))
        }
        return items
    }

    private fun readItemsForType(contentType: ContentType): List<IptvItem> {
        val cached = memoryCache[contentType]
        if (cached != null) return cached

        val file = fileForType(contentType)
        if (!file.exists()) return emptyList()
        val items = file.bufferedReader().useLines { lines ->
            lines.mapNotNull { line ->
                runCatching { fromJson(JSONObject(line)) }.getOrNull()
            }.toList()
        }
        memoryCache[contentType] = items
        return items
    }

    private fun writeItemsForType(contentType: ContentType, items: Collection<IptvItem>) {
        val list = if (items is List) items else items.toList()
        memoryCache[contentType] = list
        if (!catalogDir.exists()) catalogDir.mkdirs()
        val target = fileForType(contentType)
        val temp = File(catalogDir, "${target.name}.tmp")
        temp.bufferedWriter().use { writer ->
            list.forEach { item ->
                writer.append(toJson(item).toString())
                writer.newLine()
            }
        }
        if (target.exists()) target.delete()
        if (!temp.renameTo(target)) {
            temp.copyTo(target, overwrite = true)
            temp.delete()
        }
    }

    private fun writeSummary(contentType: ContentType, items: Collection<IptvItem>) {
        val categoryCounts = JSONObject()
        items.groupingBy { it.categoryName ?: "Uncategorized" }
            .eachCount()
            .toSortedMap()
            .forEach { (name, count) -> categoryCounts.put(name, count) }
        val special = buildSpecialCounts(items)
        prefs.edit()
            .putInt(keyCount(contentType), items.size)
            .putString(keyCategoryCounts(contentType), categoryCounts.toString())
            .putString(
                keySpecialCounts(contentType),
                JSONObject()
                    .put("recentlyAdded", special.recentlyAdded)
                    .put("ultraHd", special.ultraHd)
                    .put("playable", special.playable)
                    .toString()
            )
            .apply()
    }

    private fun buildSpecialCounts(items: Collection<IptvItem>): SpecialCounts {
        return SpecialCounts(
            recentlyAdded = items.count { it.addedAtMs > 0L },
            ultraHd = items.count(::isUltraHd),
            playable = items.count { it.isPlayable }
        )
    }

    private fun isUltraHd(item: IptvItem): Boolean {
        val text = listOf(item.title, item.categoryName.orEmpty(), item.sourceLabel.orEmpty()).joinToString(" ").lowercase()
        return text.contains("4k") || text.contains("uhd") || text.contains("2160")
    }

    private fun deleteCatalogFiles() {
        if (!catalogDir.exists()) return
        catalogDir.listFiles()?.forEach { it.delete() }
    }

    private fun fileForType(contentType: ContentType): File = File(catalogDir, "${contentType.name.lowercase()}.jsonl")

    private fun toJson(item: IptvItem): JSONObject = WatchRepository.itemToJson(item)

    private fun fromJson(obj: JSONObject): IptvItem = WatchRepository.itemFromJson(obj)

    private fun keySync(type: ContentType) = "last_sync_${type.name}"
    private fun keyRefreshAttempt(type: ContentType) = "last_refresh_attempt_${type.name}"
    private fun keyCount(type: ContentType) = "count_${type.name}"
    private fun keyCategoryCounts(type: ContentType) = "category_counts_${type.name}"
    private fun keySpecialCounts(type: ContentType) = "special_counts_${type.name}"

    data class SpecialCounts(
        val recentlyAdded: Int,
        val ultraHd: Int,
        val playable: Int
    )

    companion object {
        private const val KEY_ITEMS = "items"
        private const val KEY_SERVER_IGNORED = "server_ignored_stable_keys"
        private const val KEY_LOCAL_IGNORED = "local_ignored_stable_keys"
        
        private val memoryCache = java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap<ContentType, List<IptvItem>>()

        fun clearMemoryCache() {
            memoryCache.clear()
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CategorySyncStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType

class CategorySyncStore(context: Context) {
    private val prefs = context.applicationContext.getSharedPreferences("category_sync_store", Context.MODE_PRIVATE)

    fun isCategoryEnabled(categoryId: String, contentType: ContentType): Boolean {
        // Default to true until the user has made a selection for this content type.
        if (!isConfigured(contentType)) return true
        return prefs.getBoolean(key(categoryId, contentType), false)
    }

    fun setCategoryEnabled(categoryId: String, contentType: ContentType, enabled: Boolean) {
        prefs.edit()
            .putBoolean(key(categoryId, contentType), enabled)
            .putBoolean(configuredKey(contentType), true)
            .putLong(KEY_VERSION, System.currentTimeMillis())
            .apply()
    }

    fun saveEnabledCategoryIds(contentType: ContentType, enabledIds: Set<String>, knownIds: Set<String>) {
        val editor = prefs.edit()
            .putBoolean(configuredKey(contentType), true)
            .putLong(KEY_VERSION, System.currentTimeMillis())
        knownIds.forEach { id -> editor.putBoolean(key(id, contentType), enabledIds.contains(id)) }
        editor.apply()
    }

    fun clearContentType(contentType: ContentType) {
        val editor = prefs.edit()
            .remove(configuredKey(contentType))
            .putLong(KEY_VERSION, System.currentTimeMillis())
        prefs.all.keys
            .filter { it.startsWith("${contentType.name}:") }
            .forEach { editor.remove(it) }
        editor.apply()
    }

    fun getEnabledCategoryIds(contentType: ContentType): Set<String> {
        return prefs.all.filter { it.key.startsWith(contentType.name) && it.value == true }
            .map { it.key.substringAfter(":") }
            .toSet()
    }

    fun isConfigured(contentType: ContentType): Boolean = prefs.getBoolean(configuredKey(contentType), false)

    fun getVersion(): Long = prefs.getLong(KEY_VERSION, 0L)

    private fun key(id: String, type: ContentType) = "${type.name}:$id"
    private fun configuredKey(type: ContentType) = "configured_${type.name}"

    companion object {
        private const val KEY_VERSION = "version"
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CleanCatalogStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context

class CleanCatalogStore(context: Context) {
    private val prefs = context.applicationContext.getSharedPreferences("clean_catalog", Context.MODE_PRIVATE)

    fun getHiddenKeywords(): Set<String> {
        return prefs.getStringSet(KEY_HIDDEN_KEYWORDS, defaultHiddenKeywords()) ?: defaultHiddenKeywords()
    }

    fun saveHiddenKeywords(keywords: Set<String>) {
        prefs.edit().putStringSet(KEY_HIDDEN_KEYWORDS, keywords.map { it.trim() }.filter { it.isNotBlank() }.toSet()).apply()
    }

    fun resetDefaults() {
        prefs.edit().putStringSet(KEY_HIDDEN_KEYWORDS, defaultHiddenKeywords()).apply()
    }

    fun shouldHide(title: String, categoryName: String? = null): Boolean {
        val haystack = listOfNotNull(title, categoryName).joinToString(" ").lowercase()
        return getHiddenKeywords().any { keyword -> keyword.isNotBlank() && haystack.contains(keyword.lowercase()) }
    }

    fun isKidsSafe(categoryName: String?, title: String): Boolean {
        val haystack = listOfNotNull(title, categoryName).joinToString(" ").lowercase()
        val unsafe = listOf("adult", "xxx", "18+", "horror", "violent", "violence", "mature")
        return unsafe.none { haystack.contains(it) }
    }

    private fun defaultHiddenKeywords(): Set<String> {
        return setOf("adult", "xxx", "18+", "cam", "telesync", "ts cam", "duplicate", "test", "backup")
    }

    companion object {
        private const val KEY_HIDDEN_KEYWORDS = "hiddenKeywords"
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CredentialStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials
import java.util.UUID

class CredentialStore(context: Context) {
    private val appContext = context.applicationContext
    private val prefs = SecurePreferences.open(appContext, SECURE_PREFS_NAME).also {
        SecurePreferences.migrateIfNeeded(appContext, LEGACY_PREFS_NAME, it)
    }

    fun save(credentials: IptvCredentials) {
        prefs.edit()
            .putOrRemove(KEY_SERVER_URL, credentials.serverUrl.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(::normalizeIptvServerUrl))
            .putOrRemove(KEY_USERNAME, credentials.username.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_PASSWORD, credentials.password.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_URL, credentials.syncServerUrl?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(::normalizeControlPlaneUrl))
            .putOrRemove(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_USERNAME, credentials.syncServerUsername?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_PASSWORD, credentials.syncServerPassword?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_TOKEN, credentials.syncServerToken?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_TRAKT_CLIENT_ID, credentials.traktClientId?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_TRAKT_CLIENT_SECRET, credentials.traktClientSecret?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_TRAKT_ACCESS_TOKEN, credentials.traktAccessToken?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putOrRemove(KEY_TRAKT_REFRESH_TOKEN, credentials.traktRefreshToken?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() })
            .putString(KEY_USER_ID, credentials.userId.ifBlank { getOrCreateUserId() })
            .apply()
    }

    fun get(): IptvCredentials? {
        val saved = getAny()
        return saved?.takeIf {
            it.serverUrl.isNotBlank() && it.username.isNotBlank() && it.password.isNotBlank()
        }
    }

    fun getAny(): IptvCredentials? {
        val serverUrl = prefs.getString(KEY_SERVER_URL, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val username = prefs.getString(KEY_USERNAME, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val password = prefs.getString(KEY_PASSWORD, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val syncServerUrl = prefs.getString(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_URL, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(::normalizeControlPlaneUrl)
        val syncServerUsername = prefs.getString(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_USERNAME, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val syncServerPassword = prefs.getString(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_PASSWORD, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val syncServerToken = prefs.getString(KEY_SYNC_SERVER_TOKEN, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktClientId = prefs.getString(KEY_TRAKT_CLIENT_ID, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktClientSecret = prefs.getString(KEY_TRAKT_CLIENT_SECRET, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktAccessToken = prefs.getString(KEY_TRAKT_ACCESS_TOKEN, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktRefreshToken = prefs.getString(KEY_TRAKT_REFRESH_TOKEN, null)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val userId = getOrCreateUserId()
        val hasAny = listOf(
            serverUrl, username, password, syncServerUrl, syncServerUsername, syncServerPassword,
            syncServerToken, traktClientId, traktClientSecret, traktAccessToken, traktRefreshToken
        ).any { !it.isNullOrBlank() }
        if (!hasAny) return null
        return IptvCredentials(
            serverUrl = serverUrl.orEmpty(),
            username = username.orEmpty(),
            password = password.orEmpty(),
            syncServerUrl = syncServerUrl,
            syncServerUsername = syncServerUsername,
            syncServerPassword = syncServerPassword,
            syncServerToken = syncServerToken,
            traktClientId = traktClientId,
            traktClientSecret = traktClientSecret,
            traktAccessToken = traktAccessToken,
            traktRefreshToken = traktRefreshToken,
            userId = userId
        )
    }

    fun hasCredentials(): Boolean = get() != null

    fun clear() {
        val userId = getOrCreateUserId()
        prefs.edit().clear().putString(KEY_USER_ID, userId).apply()
    }

    fun getOrCreateUserId(): String {
        val existing = prefs.getString(KEY_USER_ID, null)
        if (!existing.isNullOrBlank()) return existing
        val created = UUID.randomUUID().toString()
        prefs.edit().putString(KEY_USER_ID, created).apply()
        return created
    }

    fun getSyncIntervalDays(): Int = prefs.getInt(KEY_SYNC_INTERVAL, 3).coerceIn(1, 30)

    fun setSyncIntervalDays(days: Int) {
        prefs.edit().putInt(KEY_SYNC_INTERVAL, days.coerceIn(1, 30)).apply()
    }

    private fun normalizeIptvServerUrl(raw: String): String {
        val trimmed = raw.trim().trimEnd('/')
        if (trimmed.isBlank()) return ""
        return if (trimmed.startsWith("http://") || trimmed.startsWith("https://")) trimmed else "http://$trimmed"
    }

    private fun normalizeControlPlaneUrl(raw: String): String {
        val trimmed = raw.trim().trimEnd('/')
        if (trimmed.isBlank()) return ""
        return if (trimmed.startsWith("http://") || trimmed.startsWith("https://")) trimmed else "https://$trimmed"
    }

    private fun android.content.SharedPreferences.Editor.putOrRemove(
        key: String,
        value: String?
    ): android.content.SharedPreferences.Editor {
        return if (value.isNullOrBlank()) remove(key) else putString(key, value)
    }

    companion object {
        const val DEFAULT_SYNC_SERVER_URL = ""
        private const val LEGACY_PREFS_NAME = "iptv_credentials"
        private const val SECURE_PREFS_NAME = "iptv_credentials_secure"
        private const val KEY_SERVER_URL = "serverUrl"
        private const val KEY_USERNAME = "username"
        private const val KEY_PASSWORD = "password"
        private const val KEY_SYNC_SERVER_URL = "syncServerUrl"
        private const val KEY_SYNC_SERVER_USERNAME = "syncServerUsername"
        private const val KEY_SYNC_SERVER_PASSWORD = "syncServerPassword"
        private const val KEY_SYNC_SERVER_TOKEN = "syncServerToken"
        private const val KEY_TRAKT_CLIENT_ID = "traktClientId"
        private const val KEY_TRAKT_CLIENT_SECRET = "traktClientSecret"
        private const val KEY_TRAKT_ACCESS_TOKEN = "traktAccessToken"
        private const val KEY_TRAKT_REFRESH_TOKEN = "traktRefreshToken"
        private const val KEY_USER_ID = "userId"
        private const val KEY_SYNC_INTERVAL = "syncIntervalDays"
    }
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context

class ProfileHomeSettings(context: Context) {
    private val prefs = context.applicationContext.getSharedPreferences("profile_home_settings", Context.MODE_PRIVATE)

    fun isRowEnabled(profileId: String, row: HomeRow): Boolean = prefs.getBoolean(key(profileId, row), true)

    fun setRowEnabled(profileId: String, row: HomeRow, enabled: Boolean) {
        prefs.edit().putBoolean(key(profileId, row), enabled).apply()
    }

    fun toggleRow(profileId: String, row: HomeRow): Boolean {
        val enabled = !isRowEnabled(profileId, row)
        setRowEnabled(profileId, row, enabled)
        return enabled
    }

    private fun key(profileId: String, row: HomeRow): String = "${profileId}_${row.name}"

    enum class HomeRow(val label: String) {
        MOVIES("Recently Added Movies"),
        SERIES("Recently Added Series"),
        LIVE("Live TV"),
        TRENDING("Trending"),
        WATCHLIST("Watchlist"),
        AI("AI Picks")
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/ProfileStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.UserProfile
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.util.UUID

class ProfileStore(context: Context) {
    private val prefs = context.applicationContext.getSharedPreferences("profiles", Context.MODE_PRIVATE)

    fun getProfiles(): List<UserProfile> {
        val raw = prefs.getString(KEY_PROFILES, null)
        if (raw.isNullOrBlank()) {
            val default = listOf(UserProfile(id = DEFAULT_PROFILE_ID, name = "Luan"))
            saveProfiles(default)
            setCurrentProfile(default.first())
            return default
        }
        val array = JSONArray(raw)
        val profiles = mutableListOf<UserProfile>()
        for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
            val obj = array.optJSONObject(index) ?: continue
            profiles.add(
                UserProfile(
                    id = obj.optString("id", UUID.randomUUID().toString()),
                    name = obj.optString("name", "Profile"),
                    isKidsProfile = obj.optBoolean("isKidsProfile", false)
                )
            )
        }
        return profiles.ifEmpty { listOf(UserProfile(id = DEFAULT_PROFILE_ID, name = "Luan")) }
    }

    fun getCurrentProfile(): UserProfile {
        val profiles = getProfiles()
        val currentId = prefs.getString(KEY_CURRENT_PROFILE_ID, null)
        return profiles.firstOrNull { it.id == currentId } ?: profiles.first()
    }

    fun setCurrentProfile(profile: UserProfile) {
        prefs.edit().putString(KEY_CURRENT_PROFILE_ID, profile.id).apply()
    }

    fun addProfile(name: String, isKidsProfile: Boolean = false): UserProfile {
        val profile = UserProfile(UUID.randomUUID().toString(), name.ifBlank { "Profile" }, isKidsProfile)
        saveProfiles(getProfiles() + profile)
        return profile
    }

    private fun saveProfiles(profiles: List<UserProfile>) {
        val array = JSONArray(profiles.map { profile ->
            JSONObject()
                .put("id", profile.id)
                .put("name", profile.name)
                .put("isKidsProfile", profile.isKidsProfile)
        })
        prefs.edit().putString(KEY_PROFILES, array.toString()).apply()
    }

    companion object {
        private const val DEFAULT_PROFILE_ID = "default"
        private const val KEY_PROFILES = "profiles"
        private const val KEY_CURRENT_PROFILE_ID = "currentProfileId"
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/SecurePreferences.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context
import android.content.SharedPreferences
import android.util.Log
import androidx.security.crypto.EncryptedSharedPreferences
import androidx.security.crypto.MasterKey

object SecurePreferences {
    private const val TAG = "SecurePreferences"

    fun open(context: Context, name: String): SharedPreferences {
        val appContext = context.applicationContext
        fun create(): SharedPreferences {
            val masterKey = MasterKey.Builder(appContext)
                .setKeyScheme(MasterKey.KeyScheme.AES256_GCM)
                .build()
            return EncryptedSharedPreferences.create(
                appContext,
                name,
                masterKey,
                EncryptedSharedPreferences.PrefKeyEncryptionScheme.AES256_SIV,
                EncryptedSharedPreferences.PrefValueEncryptionScheme.AES256_GCM
            )
        }

        return runCatching(::create).recoverCatching { firstError ->
            Log.e(TAG, "Encrypted preferences could not be opened for $name; recreating the encrypted store", firstError)
            appContext.deleteSharedPreferences(name)
            create()
        }.getOrElse { error ->
            throw IllegalStateException("Secure storage is unavailable for $name", error)
        }
    }

    fun migrateIfNeeded(context: Context, legacyName: String, secure: SharedPreferences) {
        val legacy = context.applicationContext.getSharedPreferences(legacyName, Context.MODE_PRIVATE)
        if (legacy.all.isEmpty() || secure.getBoolean("__migrated", false)) return
        val editor = secure.edit()
        legacy.all.forEach { (key, value) ->
            when (value) {
                is String -> editor.putString(key, value)
                is Int -> editor.putInt(key, value)
                is Long -> editor.putLong(key, value)
                is Float -> editor.putFloat(key, value)
                is Boolean -> editor.putBoolean(key, value)
                is Set<*> -> editor.putStringSet(key, value.filterIsInstance<String>().toSet())
            }
        }
        editor.putBoolean("__migrated", true).commit()
        legacy.edit().clear().apply()
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/SocialRepository.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialMessage
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialRoom
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialWebSocketClient
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.MutableSharedFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.MutableStateFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.asSharedFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.asStateFlow
import java.util.UUID

class SocialRepository(
    val apiClient: SocialApiClient,
    private val settings: SocialSettings
) {
    private val _messages = MutableSharedFlow<SocialMessage>()
    val messages = _messages.asSharedFlow()

    private val _isConnected = MutableStateFlow(false)
    val isConnected = _isConnected.asStateFlow()

    private var wsClient: SocialWebSocketClient? = null

    suspend fun connect() {
        if (!settings.isConfigured()) return
        val token = apiClient.getSessionToken() ?: return
        wsClient = SocialWebSocketClient(settings, {
            _messages.tryEmit(it)
        }, {
            _isConnected.value = it
        })
        wsClient?.connect(token)
    }

    fun disconnect() {
        wsClient?.disconnect()
        wsClient = null
        _isConnected.value = false
    }

    suspend fun getWatchPartyRoom(item: IptvItem): SocialRoom? {
        val existing = apiClient.getRooms(item.stableKey, "watchParty")
        if (existing.isNotEmpty()) return existing.first()
        
        return apiClient.createRoom("watchParty", item.stableKey, "Watching ${item.title}")
    }

    suspend fun getCurrentViewers(item: IptvItem) = apiClient.getCurrentViewers(item)

    suspend fun announceWatching(item: IptvItem, roomId: String? = null, positionMs: Long = 0L, durationMs: Long = 0L) =
        apiClient.updateWatchPresence(item, roomId, positionMs, durationMs)

    suspend fun getUsers() = apiClient.getUsers()

    suspend fun getFriends() = apiClient.getFriends()

    suspend fun requestFriend(userId: String) = apiClient.requestFriend(userId)

    suspend fun createViewingParty(item: IptvItem, title: String, scheduledForIso: String? = null, inviteUserIds: List<String> = emptyList()) =
        apiClient.createViewingParty(item, title, scheduledForIso, inviteUserIds)

    suspend fun getMessages(roomId: String) = apiClient.getMessages(roomId)

    fun joinRoom(roomId: String) {
        wsClient?.joinRoom(roomId)
    }

    fun leaveRoom(roomId: String) {
        wsClient?.leaveRoom(roomId)
    }

    fun sendMessage(roomId: String, text: String) {
        val clientMessageId = UUID.randomUUID().toString()
        wsClient?.sendMessage(roomId, text, clientMessageId)
    }

    suspend fun sendMessageReliable(roomId: String, text: String): SocialMessage? {
        val clientMessageId = UUID.randomUUID().toString()
        val sent = wsClient?.sendMessage(roomId, text, clientMessageId) == true
        return if (sent) null else apiClient.sendMessage(roomId, text, clientMessageId)
    }

    suspend fun sendWatchPartyControl(roomId: String, action: String, positionMs: Long = 0L, durationMs: Long = 0L) =
        apiClient.sendWatchPartyControl(roomId, action, positionMs, durationMs)

    suspend fun shareMedia(roomId: String, item: IptvItem, text: String? = null) = 
        apiClient.shareMedia(roomId, item, text)

    suspend fun getInboxRooms() = apiClient.getRooms(roomType = "discussion")
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/SocialSettings.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context

class SocialSettings(context: Context) {
    private val prefs = SecurePreferences.open(context.applicationContext, "social_settings_secure").also {
        SecurePreferences.migrateIfNeeded(context.applicationContext, "social_settings", it)
    }

    fun getServerUrl(): String? = prefs.getString(KEY_SERVER_URL, null)
    fun setServerUrl(url: String?) {
        val trimmed = url?.trim()?.trimEnd('/').orEmpty()
        val normalized = when {
            trimmed.isBlank() -> null
            trimmed.startsWith("http://") || trimmed.startsWith("https://") -> trimmed
            else -> "https://$trimmed"
        }
        prefs.edit().putString(KEY_SERVER_URL, normalized).apply()
    }

    fun getDisplayName(): String? = prefs.getString(KEY_DISPLAY_NAME, null)
    fun setDisplayName(name: String?) = prefs.edit().putString(KEY_DISPLAY_NAME, name).apply()

    fun getToken(): String? = prefs.getString(KEY_TOKEN, null)
    fun setToken(token: String?) = prefs.edit().putString(KEY_TOKEN, token).apply()

    fun isConfigured(): Boolean = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.NetworkPolicy.isAllowedControlPlaneUrl(getServerUrl())

    companion object {
        private const val KEY_SERVER_URL = "server_url"
        private const val KEY_DISPLAY_NAME = "display_name"
        private const val KEY_TOKEN = "token"
    }
}

================================================================================
// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/WatchRepository.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher.isDisplayPlayable
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.util.UUID

class WatchRepository(context: Context) {
    private val appContext = context.applicationContext
    private val prefs = appContext.getSharedPreferences("watch_repository", Context.MODE_PRIVATE)
    private val profileStore = ProfileStore(appContext)
    
    private val memoryCache = mutableMapOf<String, List<IptvItem>>()
    private var lastCacheProfileId: String? = null

    private fun profileId(): String = profileStore.getCurrentProfile().id
    private fun key(base: String): String = "${profileId()}_$base"

    private fun clearCacheIfProfileChanged() {
        val current = profileId()
        if (lastCacheProfileId != current) {
            memoryCache.clear()
            lastCacheProfileId = current
        }
    }

    fun getWatchlist(): List<IptvItem> {
        clearCacheIfProfileChanged()
        val k = key(KEY_WATCHLIST)
        return memoryCache[k] ?: readItems(k).also { memoryCache[k] = it }
    }

    fun matchWatchlistItems(localCatalog: List<IptvItem>): List<IptvItem> {
        if (localCatalog.isEmpty()) return getWatchlist()
        var changed = false
        val matched = getWatchlist().map { item ->
            if (item.isDisplayPlayable()) {
                item
            } else {
                val playable = CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(localCatalog, item)
                if (playable == null) {
                    item
                } else {
                    changed = true
                    CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(item, playable).copy(
                        positionMs = item.positionMs,
                        durationMs = item.durationMs,
                        lastWatchedAtMs = item.lastWatchedAtMs,
                        completed = item.completed,
                        watchedCount = item.watchedCount
                    )
                }
            }
        }
        val deduped = matched.fold(mutableListOf<IptvItem>()) { acc, item ->
            acc.removeAll { CatalogMatcher.sameCatalogIdentity(it, item) }
            acc.add(item)
            acc
        }
        if (changed || deduped.size != matched.size) saveItems(key(KEY_WATCHLIST), deduped)
        return deduped
    }

    fun addToWatchlist(item: IptvItem, localCatalog: List<IptvItem> = emptyList()): IptvItem {
        val matchedItem = if (item.isDisplayPlayable()) {
            item
        } else {
            CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(localCatalog, item)?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(item, it) } ?: item
        }
        val items = getWatchlist().filterNot {
            CatalogMatcher.sameCatalogIdentity(it, item) || CatalogMatcher.sameCatalogIdentity(it, matchedItem)
        }.toMutableList()
        val savedItem = matchedItem.copy(positionMs = 0L, lastWatchedAtMs = 0L)
        items.add(savedItem)
        saveItems(key(KEY_WATCHLIST), items)
        return savedItem
    }

    fun removeFromWatchlist(item: IptvItem) {
        saveItems(key(KEY_WATCHLIST), getWatchlist().filterNot { CatalogMatcher.sameCatalogIdentity(it, item) })
    }

    fun isInWatchlist(item: IptvItem): Boolean = getWatchlist().any { CatalogMatcher.sameCatalogIdentity(it, item) }

    fun getContinueWatching(): List<IptvItem> {
        clearCacheIfProfileChanged()
        val inProgressK = key(KEY_PROGRESS)
        val liveK = key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY)
        val inProgress = (memoryCache[inProgressK] ?: readItems(inProgressK).also { memoryCache[inProgressK] = it })
            .filter { it.positionMs > 0L && !it.completed }
        val live = memoryCache[liveK] ?: readItems(liveK).also { memoryCache[liveK] = it }
        return (inProgress + live)
            .sortedByDescending { it.lastWatchedAtMs }
            .take(40)
    }

    fun getRecentlyWatchedLive(): List<IptvItem> {
        clearCacheIfProfileChanged()
        val k = key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY)
        return (memoryCache[k] ?: readItems(k).also { memoryCache[k] = it })
            .sortedByDescending { it.lastWatchedAtMs }
            .take(30)
    }

    fun getFinishEpisodes(): List<IptvItem> {
        clearCacheIfProfileChanged()
        val k = key(KEY_PROGRESS)
        return (memoryCache[k] ?: readItems(k).also { memoryCache[k] = it })
            .filter { it.contentType == ContentType.EPISODE && it.positionMs > 0L && !it.completed }
            .sortedByDescending { it.lastWatchedAtMs }
            .take(30)
    }

    fun getHistory(): List<IptvItem> {
        clearCacheIfProfileChanged()
        val k = key(KEY_HISTORY)
        return (memoryCache[k] ?: readItems(k).also { memoryCache[k] = it })
            .sortedByDescending { it.lastWatchedAtMs }.take(200)
    }

    fun getWatchNext(): List<IptvItem> {
        clearCacheIfProfileChanged()
        val k = key(KEY_WATCH_NEXT)
        return memoryCache[k] ?: readItems(k).also { memoryCache[k] = it }
    }

    fun addToWatchNext(item: IptvItem) {
        val items = getWatchNext().filterNot { it.stableKey == item.stableKey }.toMutableList()
        items.add(0, item)
        saveItems(key(KEY_WATCH_NEXT), items.take(50))
    }

    fun removeFromWatchNext(item: IptvItem) {
        saveItems(key(KEY_WATCH_NEXT), getWatchNext().filterNot { it.stableKey == item.stableKey })
    }

    fun isInWatchNext(item: IptvItem): Boolean = getWatchNext().any { it.stableKey == item.stableKey }

    fun updateWatchRecord(kind: String, stableKey: String, positionMs: Long? = null, durationMs: Long? = null, completed: Boolean? = null, watchedCount: Int? = null): IptvItem? {
        val storageKey = when (kind) {
            "progress" -> key(KEY_PROGRESS)
            "history" -> key(KEY_HISTORY)
            "live" -> key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY)
            "watchNext" -> key(KEY_WATCH_NEXT)
            "watchlist" -> key(KEY_WATCHLIST)
            else -> return null
        }
        val items = readItems(storageKey).toMutableList()
        val index = items.indexOfFirst { it.stableKey == stableKey }
        if (index < 0) return null
        val original = items[index]
        val safeDuration = durationMs ?: original.durationMs
        val safePosition = positionMs ?: original.positionMs
        val updated = original.copy(
            positionMs = safePosition.coerceAtLeast(0L),
            durationMs = safeDuration.coerceAtLeast(0L),
            completed = completed ?: original.completed,
            watchedCount = watchedCount?.coerceAtLeast(0) ?: original.watchedCount,
            lastWatchedAtMs = System.currentTimeMillis()
        )
        items[index] = updated
        saveItems(storageKey, items)
        return updated
    }

    fun deleteWatchRecord(kind: String, stableKey: String): Boolean {
        val storageKey = when (kind) {
            "progress" -> key(KEY_PROGRESS)
            "history" -> key(KEY_HISTORY)
            "live" -> key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY)
            "watchNext" -> key(KEY_WATCH_NEXT)
            "watchlist" -> key(KEY_WATCHLIST)
            else -> return false
        }
        val items = readItems(storageKey)
        val updated = items.filterNot { it.stableKey == stableKey }
        if (updated.size == items.size) return false
        saveItems(storageKey, updated)
        return true
    }

    fun setRating(item: IptvItem, rating: Int) {
        val safeRating = rating.coerceIn(-1, 1)
        val ratings = readRatings().toMutableMap()
        if (safeRating == 0) ratings.remove(item.stableKey) else ratings[item.stableKey] = safeRating
        prefs.edit().putString(key(KEY_RATINGS), JSONObject(ratings.mapValues { it.value }).toString()).apply()
    }

    fun getRating(item: IptvItem): Int = readRatings()[item.stableKey] ?: 0

    fun getRatingsSnapshot(): Map<String, Int> = readRatings()

    fun getItemProgress(stableKey: String): Long {
        val all = readItems(key(KEY_PROGRESS)) + readItems(key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY))
        return all.find { it.stableKey == stableKey }?.positionMs ?: 0L
    }

    fun saveProgress(item: IptvItem, positionMs: Long, durationMs: Long) {
        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        val safeDuration = durationMs.coerceAtLeast(0L)
        val completed = safeDuration > 0L && positionMs >= safeDuration * 0.9
        val progressItem = item.copy(
            positionMs = positionMs.coerceAtLeast(0L),
            durationMs = safeDuration,
            lastWatchedAtMs = now,
            completed = completed,
            watchedCount = item.watchedCount + if (completed) 1 else 0
        )

        if (item.contentType == ContentType.LIVE) {
            val liveItems = readItems(key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY)).filterNot { it.stableKey == item.stableKey }.toMutableList()
            liveItems.add(progressItem)
            saveItems(key(KEY_LIVE_HISTORY), liveItems.takeLast(100))
        } else {
            val progressItems = readItems(key(KEY_PROGRESS)).filterNot { it.stableKey == item.stableKey }.toMutableList()
            progressItems.add(progressItem)
            saveItems(key(KEY_PROGRESS), progressItems.takeLast(200))
        }

        val historyItems = readItems(key(KEY_HISTORY)).filterNot { it.stableKey == item.stableKey }.toMutableList()
        historyItems.add(progressItem)
        saveItems(key(KEY_HISTORY), historyItems.takeLast(300))
    }

    fun buildSnapshot(userId: String, serverUsername: String? = null): JSONObject {
        return JSONObject()
            .put("eventId", UUID.randomUUID().toString())
            .put("userId", serverUserId(userId, serverUsername))
            .put("profileId", serverProfileId(serverUsername))
            .put("generatedAt", System.currentTimeMillis())
            .put("watchlist", JSONArray(getWatchlist().map(::itemToJson)))
            .put("watchNext", JSONArray(getWatchNext().map(::itemToJson)))
            .put("progress", JSONArray(getContinueWatching().map(::itemToJson)))
            .put("finishEpisodes", JSONArray(getFinishEpisodes().map(::itemToJson)))
            .put("history", JSONArray(getHistory().map(::itemToJson)))
    }

    fun buildWatchEvent(userId: String, item: IptvItem, positionMs: Long, durationMs: Long, serverUsername: String? = null): JSONObject {
        return JSONObject()
            .put("eventId", UUID.randomUUID().toString())
            .put("userId", serverUserId(userId, serverUsername))
            .put("profileId", serverProfileId(serverUsername))
            .put("eventType", if (durationMs > 0 && positionMs >= durationMs * 0.9) "complete" else "progress")
            .put("item", itemToJson(item))
            .put("positionMs", positionMs)
            .put("durationMs", durationMs)
            .put("createdAt", System.currentTimeMillis())
    }

    private fun serverProfileId(serverUsername: String?): String = profileId()

    private fun serverUserId(localUserId: String, serverUsername: String?): String = localUserId

    private fun readItems(key: String): List<IptvItem> {
        val raw = prefs.getString(key, "[]") ?: "[]"
        val array = JSONArray(raw)
        val items = mutableListOf<IptvItem>()
        for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
            val obj = array.optJSONObject(index) ?: continue
            items.add(itemFromJson(obj))
        }
        return items
    }

    private fun saveItems(key: String, items: List<IptvItem>) {
        memoryCache[key] = items
        prefs.edit().putString(key, JSONArray(items.map(::itemToJson)).toString()).apply()
    }

    private fun readRatings(): Map<String, Int> {
        val raw = prefs.getString(key(KEY_RATINGS), "{}") ?: "{}"
        val obj = JSONObject(raw)
        val ratings = mutableMapOf<String, Int>()
        obj.keys().forEach { stableKey ->
            val rating = obj.optInt(stableKey, 0)
            if (rating == -1 || rating == 1) ratings[stableKey] = rating
        }
        return ratings
    }

    companion object {
        private const val KEY_WATCHLIST = "watchlist"
        private const val KEY_WATCH_NEXT = "watchNext"
        private const val KEY_PROGRESS = "progress"
        private const val KEY_HISTORY = "history"
        private const val KEY_LIVE_HISTORY = "liveHistory"
        private const val KEY_RATINGS = "ratings"

        fun itemToJson(item: IptvItem): JSONObject {
            return JSONObject()
                .put("id", item.id)
                .put("streamId", item.streamId)
                .put("title", item.title)
                .put("description", item.description)
                .put("categoryId", item.categoryId)
                .put("categoryName", item.categoryName)
                .put("coverUrl", item.coverUrl)
                .put("backdropUrl", item.backdropUrl)
                .put("streamUrl", item.streamUrl)
                .put("containerExtension", item.containerExtension)
                .put("rating", item.rating)
                .put("year", item.year)
                .put("contentType", item.contentType.name)
                .put("actionKey", item.actionKey)
                .put("durationMs", item.durationMs)
                .put("positionMs", item.positionMs)
                .put("lastWatchedAtMs", item.lastWatchedAtMs)
                .put("addedAtMs", item.addedAtMs)
                .put("watchedCount", item.watchedCount)
                .put("completed", item.completed)
                .put("metadataProvider", item.metadataProvider)
                .put("metadataId", item.metadataId)
                .put("serverStableKey", item.serverStableKey)
                .put("traktSlug", item.traktSlug)
                .put("traktType", item.traktType)
                .put("imdbId", item.imdbId)
                .put("tmdbId", item.tmdbId)
                .put("genres", JSONArray(item.genres))
                .put("seasonNumber", item.seasonNumber)
                .put("episodeNumber", item.episodeNumber)
                .put("parentSeriesId", item.parentSeriesId)
                .put("parentSeriesTitle", item.parentSeriesTitle)
                .put("sourceLabel", item.sourceLabel)
                .put("subtitleUrl", item.subtitleUrl)
                .put("providerAccountId", item.providerAccountId)
        }

        fun itemFromJson(obj: JSONObject): IptvItem {
            val genresArray = obj.optJSONArray("genres") ?: JSONArray()
            val genres = mutableListOf<String>()
            for (index in 0 until genresArray.length()) {
                genresArray.optString(index).takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(genres::add)
            }

            fun optIntNullable(name: String): Int? = if (obj.has(name) && !obj.isNull(name)) obj.optInt(name) else null

            return IptvItem(
                id = obj.optLong("id", 0L),
                streamId = obj.optString("streamId", ""),
                title = obj.optString("title", ""),
                description = obj.optString("description", ""),
                categoryId = obj.optString("categoryId", null),
                categoryName = obj.optString("categoryName", null),
                coverUrl = obj.optString("coverUrl", null),
                backdropUrl = obj.optString("backdropUrl", null),
                streamUrl = obj.optString("streamUrl", null),
                containerExtension = obj.optString("containerExtension", null),
                rating = obj.optString("rating", null),
                year = obj.optString("year", null),
                contentType = runCatching { ContentType.valueOf(obj.optString("contentType", ContentType.MOVIE.name)) }.getOrDefault(ContentType.MOVIE),
                actionKey = obj.optString("actionKey", null),
                durationMs = obj.optLong("durationMs", 0L),
                positionMs = obj.optLong("positionMs", 0L),
                lastWatchedAtMs = obj.optLong("lastWatchedAtMs", 0L),
                addedAtMs = obj.optLong("addedAtMs", 0L),
                watchedCount = obj.optInt("watchedCount", 0),
                completed = obj.optBoolean("completed", false),
                metadataProvider = obj.optString("metadataProvider", null),
                metadataId = obj.optString("metadataId", null),
                serverStableKey = obj.optString("serverStableKey", null),
                traktSlug = obj.optString("traktSlug", null),
                traktType = obj.optString("traktType", null),
                imdbId = obj.optString("imdbId", null),
                tmdbId = obj.optString("tmdbId", null),
                genres = genres,
                seasonNumber = optIntNullable("seasonNumber"),
                episodeNumber = optIntNullable("episodeNumber"),
                parentSeriesId = obj.optString("parentSeriesId", null),
                parentSeriesTitle = obj.optString("parentSeriesTitle", null),
                sourceLabel = obj.optString("sourceLabel", null),
                subtitleUrl = obj.optString("subtitleUrl", null),
                providerAccountId = obj.optString("providerAccountId", null)
            )
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/model/EpgModels.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model

import java.io.Serializable

data class EpgProgram(
    val channelStableKey: String,
    val channelTitle: String,
    val programTitle: String,
    val description: String = "",
    val startTimeMs: Long,
    val endTimeMs: Long,
    val source: String = "Xtream"
) : Serializable {
    val isLiveNow: Boolean
        get() {
            val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
            return startTimeMs <= now && now < endTimeMs
        }

    val progressPercent: Int
        get() {
            val duration = (endTimeMs - startTimeMs).coerceAtLeast(1L)
            val elapsed = (System.currentTimeMillis() - startTimeMs).coerceIn(0L, duration)
            return ((elapsed * 100L) / duration).toInt().coerceIn(0, 100)
        }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/model/IptvModels.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model

import java.io.Serializable

enum class ContentType : Serializable {
    LIVE,
    MOVIE,
    SERIES,
    EPISODE,
    ACTION
}

data class IptvCredentials(
    val serverUrl: String,
    val username: String,
    val password: String,
    val syncServerUrl: String? = null,
    val syncServerUsername: String? = null,
    val syncServerPassword: String? = null,
    val syncServerToken: String? = null,
    val traktClientId: String? = null,
    val traktClientSecret: String? = null,
    val traktAccessToken: String? = null,
    val traktRefreshToken: String? = null,
    val userId: String
) : Serializable

data class UserProfile(
    val id: String,
    val name: String,
    val isKidsProfile: Boolean = false
) : Serializable

data class IptvCategory(
    val categoryId: String,
    val categoryName: String,
    val contentType: ContentType
) : Serializable

data class IptvItem(
    var id: Long = 0,
    var streamId: String = "",
    var title: String = "",
    var description: String = "",
    var categoryId: String? = null,
    var categoryName: String? = null,
    var coverUrl: String? = null,
    var backdropUrl: String? = null,
    var streamUrl: String? = null,
    var containerExtension: String? = null,
    var rating: String? = null,
    var year: String? = null,
    var contentType: ContentType = ContentType.MOVIE,
    var actionKey: String? = null,
    var durationMs: Long = 0L,
    var positionMs: Long = 0L,
    var lastWatchedAtMs: Long = 0L,
    var addedAtMs: Long = 0L,
    var watchedCount: Int = 0,
    var completed: Boolean = false,
    var metadataProvider: String? = null,
    var metadataId: String? = null,
    var serverStableKey: String? = null,
    var traktSlug: String? = null,
    var traktType: String? = null,
    var imdbId: String? = null,
    var tmdbId: String? = null,
    var genres: List<String> = emptyList(),
    var seasonNumber: Int? = null,
    var episodeNumber: Int? = null,
    var parentSeriesId: String? = null,
    var parentSeriesTitle: String? = null,
    var sourceLabel: String? = null,
    var subtitleUrl: String? = null,
    var providerAccountId: String? = null
) : Serializable {
    val stableKey: String
        get() {
            if (!serverStableKey.isNullOrBlank()) return serverStableKey.orEmpty()
            val providerPrefix = providerAccountId?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { "$it:" }.orEmpty()
            return when {
                contentType == ContentType.EPISODE && !parentSeriesId.isNullOrBlank() ->
                    "${providerPrefix}EPISODE:$parentSeriesId:${seasonNumber ?: 0}:${episodeNumber ?: 0}:$streamId"
                else -> "${providerPrefix}${contentType.name}:$streamId"
            }
        }

    val progressPercent: Int
        get() = if (durationMs > 0L) ((positionMs * 100L) / durationMs).coerceIn(0L, 100L).toInt() else 0

    val isPlayable: Boolean
        get() = contentType != ContentType.ACTION && !streamUrl.isNullOrBlank()
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model

import java.io.Serializable

data class SocialRoom(
    val id: String,
    val roomType: String, // watchParty, discussion, direct
    val catalogItemId: String? = null,
    val title: String,
    val lastMessage: String? = null,
    val updatedAt: Long = 0L,
    val unreadCount: Int = 0
) : Serializable

data class SocialMessage(
    val id: String,
    val clientMessageId: String? = null,
    val roomId: String,
    val senderUserId: String,
    val senderDisplayName: String,
    val messageType: String, // text, mediaShare, listShare, system
    val text: String,
    val createdAt: Long,
    val sharePayload: String? = null // JSON string of shared item
) : Serializable

data class SocialUser(
    val id: String,
    val displayName: String,
    val username: String? = null,
    val avatarUrl: String? = null,
    val status: String? = null,
    val lastSeenAt: Long = 0L
) : Serializable

data class WatchPresence(
    val id: String,
    val roomId: String?,
    val catalogKey: String,
    val catalogTitle: String,
    val catalogType: String? = null,
    val positionMs: Long = 0L,
    val durationMs: Long = 0L,
    val playbackState: String = "watching",
    val deviceName: String? = null,
    val lastHeartbeatAt: Long = 0L,
    val user: SocialUser? = null
) : Serializable

data class SocialFriendship(
    val id: String,
    val status: String,
    val direction: String,
    val otherUser: SocialUser?
) : Serializable

data class ViewingPartyInvite(
    val id: String,
    val status: String,
    val user: SocialUser?
) : Serializable

data class ViewingParty(
    val id: String,
    val title: String,
    val status: String,
    val scheduledFor: Long = 0L,
    val catalogKey: String? = null,
    val catalogTitle: String,
    val catalogType: String? = null,
    val room: SocialRoom?,
    val createdBy: SocialUser?,
    val invites: List<ViewingPartyInvite> = emptyList()
) : Serializable

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/AiSyncClient.kt
