package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext
import okhttp3.HttpUrl.Companion.toHttpUrlOrNull
import okhttp3.MediaType.Companion.toMediaType
import okhttp3.OkHttpClient
import okhttp3.Request
import okhttp3.RequestBody.Companion.toRequestBody
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import okhttp3.Credentials

class AiSyncClient(
    private val syncServerUrl: String?,
    private val syncServerUsername: String? = null,
    private val syncServerPassword: String? = null,
    private val syncServerToken: String? = null,
    private val client: OkHttpClient = OkHttpClient.Builder().build()
) {
    private val jsonMediaType = "application/json; charset=utf-8".toMediaType()

    fun isConfigured(): Boolean = NetworkPolicy.isAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)

    suspend fun postWatchSnapshot(snapshot: JSONObject): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        postJson("/api/iptv/watch-snapshot", snapshot)
    }

    suspend fun postWatchEvent(event: JSONObject): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        postJson("/api/iptv/watch-event", event)
    }

    suspend fun checkConnection(): Result<ServerAuthStatus> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val request = requestBuilder(base + "/api/auth/check").get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val body = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                val user = body.optJSONObject("user")
                ServerAuthStatus(
                    ok = body.optBoolean("ok", false),
                    username = user?.optNullableString("username"),
                    displayName = user?.optNullableString("displayName"),
                    isAdmin = user?.optBoolean("isAdmin", false) == true,
                    tmdbLinked = user?.optBoolean("tmdbLinked", false) == true,
                    tmdbUsername = user?.optNullableString("tmdbUsername")
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun startPairing(deviceName: String): Result<PairingStart> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val payload = JSONObject().put("deviceName", deviceName)
            val request = Request.Builder()
                .url("$base/api/pairing/start")
                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val body = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                PairingStart(
                    deviceCode = body.optString("deviceCode"),
                    pairingUrl = body.optString("pairingUrl"),
                    qrPayload = body.optNullableString("qrPayload"),
                    expiresAt = body.optNullableString("expiresAt"),
                    pollIntervalSeconds = body.optInt("pollIntervalSeconds", 2).coerceIn(1, 10)
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getPairingStatus(deviceCode: String): Result<PairingStatus> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val url = "$base/api/pairing/status".toHttpUrlOrNull()
                ?.newBuilder()
                ?.addQueryParameter("deviceCode", deviceCode)
                ?.build()
                ?: error("Invalid AI sync server URL")
            val request = Request.Builder().url(url).get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful && response.code != 404) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val body = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                PairingStatus(
                    status = body.optString("status", "pending"),
                    syncServerUrl = body.optNullableString("syncServerUrl"),
                    syncServerUsername = body.optNullableString("syncServerUsername"),
                    syncServerToken = body.optNullableString("syncServerToken"),
                    displayName = body.optNullableString("displayName"),
                    expiresAt = body.optNullableString("expiresAt")
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun postIptvCredentials(credentials: IptvCredentials, profileId: String? = null): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val payload = JSONObject()
            .put("serverUrl", credentials.serverUrl)
            .put("username", credentials.username)
            .put("password", credentials.password)
            .put("androidUserId", credentials.userId)
            .putNullable("profileId", profileId)
        postJson("/api/iptv/credentials", payload)
    }

    suspend fun getLatestIptvCredentials(): Result<SyncedIptvCredentials> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/iptv/credentials/latest").get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                val bodyText = response.body?.string() ?: "{}"
                if (!response.isSuccessful) {
                    val serverMessage = runCatching { JSONObject(bodyText).optNullableString("error") }.getOrNull()
                    error(serverMessage ?: "AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                }
                val credential = JSONObject(bodyText).optJSONObject("credential")
                    ?: error("No IPTV credentials have been synced to this AI server account yet.")
                SyncedIptvCredentials(
                    serverUrl = credential.optString("iptvServerUrl"),
                    username = credential.optString("iptvUsername"),
                    password = credential.optString("iptvPassword"),
                    profileId = credential.optNullableString("profileId"),
                    updatedAt = credential.optNullableString("updatedAt")
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun postCatalogMetadata(items: List<IptvItem>): Result<Int> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            var saved = 0
            items.asSequence()
                .filter { it.title.isNotBlank() && it.contentType != ContentType.ACTION }
                .chunked(100)
                .forEach { chunk ->
                    val payload = JSONObject().put("items", JSONArray(chunk.map(::safeCatalogJson)))
                    val response = postJsonObject("/api/iptv/catalog-metadata", payload)
                    saved += response.optInt("saved", chunk.size)
                }
            saved
        }
    }

    suspend fun getRecommendations(
        profileId: String,
        mood: String = "any",
        contentType: String = "any",
        query: String? = null,
        useWebSearch: Boolean = false,
        limit: Int = 40
    ): Result<List<IptvItem>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val payload = JSONObject()
                .put("profileId", profileId)
                .put("mood", mood.ifBlank { "any" })
                .put("contentType", contentType.ifBlank { "any" })
                .put("limit", limit.coerceIn(1, 50))
                .put("useWebSearch", useWebSearch)
            if (!query.isNullOrBlank()) payload.put("query", query)
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/ai/recommendations")
                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            val primary = client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
                } else {
                    null
                }
            }
            if (primary != null) {
                primary
            } else {
                val fallbackUrl = "$base/api/iptv/recommendations".toHttpUrlOrNull()
                    ?.newBuilder()
                    ?.addQueryParameter("profileId", profileId)
                    ?.build()
                    ?: error("Invalid AI sync server URL")
                val fallbackRequest = requestBuilder(fallbackUrl.toString()).get().build()
                client.newCall(fallbackRequest).execute().use { response ->
                    if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                    parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
                }
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getWatchItems(profileId: String, kind: String, limit: Int = 200): Result<List<IptvItem>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val url = "$base/api/catalog/watch".toHttpUrlOrNull()
                ?.newBuilder()
                ?.addQueryParameter("profileId", profileId)
                ?.addQueryParameter("kind", kind)
                ?.addQueryParameter("limit", limit.toString())
                ?.build()
                ?: error("Invalid AI sync server URL")
            val request = requestBuilder(url.toString()).get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getTmdbCollection(collection: String, type: ContentType?, limit: Int = 40): Result<List<IptvItem>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val tmdbType = when (type) {
                null -> "all"
                ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.EPISODE -> "tv"
                ContentType.MOVIE -> "movie"
                else -> "all"
            }
            val url = "$base/api/catalog/external/tmdb/$collection".toHttpUrlOrNull()
                ?.newBuilder()
                ?.addQueryParameter("type", tmdbType)
                ?.addQueryParameter("limit", limit.toString())
                ?.build()
                ?: error("Invalid AI sync server URL")
            val request = requestBuilder(url.toString()).get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getTmdbWatchlist(limit: Int = 40): Result<List<IptvItem>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val url = "$base/api/users/me/tmdb/watchlist".toHttpUrlOrNull()
                ?.newBuilder()
                ?.addQueryParameter("type", "all")
                ?.addQueryParameter("limit", limit.toString())
                ?.build()
                ?: error("Invalid AI sync server URL")
            val request = requestBuilder(url.toString()).get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun requestTmdbToken(): Result<TmdbRequestToken> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/users/me/tmdb/request-token").get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val body = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                TmdbRequestToken(
                    requestToken = body.optString("request_token"),
                    authenticationUrl = body.optString("authentication_url")
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun completeTmdbLink(requestToken: String): Result<ServerAuthStatus> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val payload = JSONObject().put("requestToken", requestToken)
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/users/me/tmdb/create-session")
                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val user = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}").optJSONObject("user")
                ServerAuthStatus(
                    ok = true,
                    username = user?.optNullableString("username"),
                    displayName = user?.optNullableString("displayName"),
                    isAdmin = user?.optBoolean("isAdmin", false) == true,
                    tmdbLinked = !user?.optNullableString("tmdbUsername").isNullOrBlank(),
                    tmdbUsername = user?.optNullableString("tmdbUsername")
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun unlinkTmdb(): Result<ServerAuthStatus> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/users/me/tmdb/unlink")
                .post(JSONObject().toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val user = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}").optJSONObject("user")
                ServerAuthStatus(
                    ok = true,
                    username = user?.optNullableString("username"),
                    displayName = user?.optNullableString("displayName"),
                    isAdmin = user?.optBoolean("isAdmin", false) == true,
                    tmdbLinked = false,
                    tmdbUsername = user?.optNullableString("tmdbUsername")
                )
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getIgnoredStableKeys(profileId: String): Result<Set<String>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val url = "$base/api/iptv/preferences".toHttpUrlOrNull()
                ?.newBuilder()
                ?.addQueryParameter("profileId", profileId)
                ?.build()
                ?: error("Invalid AI sync server URL")
            val request = requestBuilder(url.toString()).get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val body = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                val array = body.optJSONArray("ignoredStableKeys") ?: JSONArray()
                val keys = mutableSetOf<String>()
                for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
                    array.optString(index).takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(keys::add)
                }
                keys
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun saveCatalogPreference(profileId: String, item: IptvItem, rating: Int? = null, ignored: Boolean? = null): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val payload = JSONObject()
            .put("profileId", profileId)
            .put("stableKeys", JSONArray(listOf(item.stableKey)))
            .put("items", JSONArray(listOf(safeCatalogJson(item))))
        if (rating != null) payload.put("rating", rating)
        if (ignored != null) payload.put("ignored", ignored)
        postJson("/api/iptv/preferences", payload)
    }

                .build()
            
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getExplanation(profileId: String, catalogItemId: String): Result<String> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)

                .put("profileId", profileId)
                .put("catalogItemId", catalogItemId)
            
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/ai/explain")
                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val obj = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                obj.optString("reason", "No explanation available.")
            }
        }
    }

                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getTrendingDiscussions(): Result<List<JSONObject>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/social/discussions").get().build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                val body = response.body?.string() ?: "{}"
                val array = JSONObject(body).optJSONArray("discussions") ?: JSONArray()
                val list = mutableListOf<JSONObject>()
                for (i in 0 until array.length()) list.add(array.getJSONObject(i))
                list
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun sendRecommendationFeedback(
        profileId: String,

            "/api/ai/feedback",
            JSONObject()
                .put("profileId", profileId)
                .put("catalogItemId", catalogItemId)
                .put("action", action)
                .putNullable("mode", mode)
        )
    }

    suspend fun getAdminSummary(): Result<JSONObject> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {

            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)

            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                val text = response.body?.string() ?: "{}"
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error(JSONObject(text).optNullableString("error") ?: "Admin summary returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                JSONObject(text)
            }
        }
    }

    suspend fun getCatalogQualityReport(): Result<JSONObject> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {

            }

    suspend fun sendWatchPartyControl(roomId: String, action: String, positionMs: Long, durationMs: Long): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        postJson(
            "/api/social/rooms/$roomId/control",

    suspend fun naturalSearch(profileId: String, query: String, limit: Int = 40): Result<List<IptvItem>> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val payload = JSONObject()
                .put("profileId", profileId)
                .put("query", query)
                .put("limit", limit.coerceIn(1, 50))
            
            val request = requestBuilder("$base/api/ai/natural-search")
                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
                parseItems(JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}"))
            }
        }
    }

    private fun parseItems(root: JSONObject): List<IptvItem> {
        val array = root.optJSONArray("items") ?: return emptyList()
        val items = mutableListOf<IptvItem>()
        for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
            val obj = array.optJSONObject(index) ?: continue
            // Some responses might nest the item
            val itemObj = obj.optJSONObject("catalogItem") ?: obj
            items.add(
                IptvItem(
                    id = index.toLong(),
                    streamId = itemObj.optString("streamId", ""),
                    title = itemObj.optString("title", "Recommended"),
                    description = itemObj.optString("description", ""),
                    categoryId = itemObj.optNullableString("categoryId"),
                    categoryName = itemObj.optNullableString("categoryName") ?: itemObj.optNullableString("category"),
                    coverUrl = itemObj.optNullableString("coverUrl"),
                    backdropUrl = itemObj.optNullableString("backdropUrl"),
                    streamUrl = itemObj.optNullableString("streamUrl"),
                    containerExtension = itemObj.optNullableString("containerExtension"),
                    rating = itemObj.optNullableString("rating"),
                    year = itemObj.optNullableString("year"),
                    contentType = parseContentType(itemObj.optString("contentType", itemObj.optString("type", ContentType.MOVIE.name))),
                    metadataProvider = itemObj.optNullableString("metadataProvider"),
                    metadataId = itemObj.optNullableString("metadataId"),
                    serverStableKey = itemObj.optNullableString("stableKey"),
                    traktSlug = itemObj.optNullableString("traktSlug"),
                    traktType = itemObj.optNullableString("traktType"),
                    imdbId = itemObj.optNullableString("imdbId"),
                    tmdbId = itemObj.optNullableString("tmdbId"),
                    genres = parseGenres(itemObj),
                    seasonNumber = itemObj.optIntNullable("seasonNumber"),
                    episodeNumber = itemObj.optIntNullable("episodeNumber"),
                    parentSeriesId = itemObj.optNullableString("parentSeriesId"),
                    parentSeriesTitle = itemObj.optNullableString("parentSeriesTitle"),
                    positionMs = obj.optLong("positionMs", 0L),
                    durationMs = obj.optLong("durationMs", itemObj.optLong("durationMs", 0L)),
                    completed = obj.optBoolean("completed", false),
                    watchedCount = obj.optInt("playCount", 0),
                    providerAccountId = itemObj.optNullableString("providerAccountId"),
                    sourceLabel = obj.optNullableString("reason")
                        ?: obj.optNullableString("aiReason")
                        ?: watchSourceLabel(obj)
                        ?: itemObj.optNullableString("sourceLabel")
                )
            )
        }
        return items
    }

    private fun parseGenres(itemObj: JSONObject): List<String> {
        val array = itemObj.optJSONArray("genres") ?: itemObj.optJSONArray("genre") ?: JSONArray()
        val genres = mutableListOf<String>()
        for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
            array.optString(index).takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(genres::add)
        }
        return genres
    }

    private fun watchSourceLabel(obj: JSONObject): String? {
        return when (obj.optString("kind")) {
            "watchlist" -> "AI Server Watchlist"
            "history" -> "AI Server History"
            "progress" -> "AI Server Progress"
            else -> null
        }
    }

    private fun postJson(path: String, payload: JSONObject): Result<Unit> {
        return runCatching {
            val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
            val request = requestBuilder(base + path)
                .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
                .build()
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
            }
        }
    }

    private fun postJsonObject(path: String, payload: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val base = NetworkPolicy.requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(syncServerUrl)
        val request = requestBuilder(base + path)
            .post(payload.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()
        client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
            if (!response.isSuccessful) error("AI sync server returned HTTP ${response.code}")
            return JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
        }
    }

    private fun safeCatalogJson(item: IptvItem): JSONObject {
        return JSONObject()
            .put("stableKey", item.stableKey)
            .put("streamId", item.streamId)
            .putNullable("providerAccountId", item.providerAccountId)
            .put("title", item.title)
            .put("description", item.description)
            .putNullable("categoryId", item.categoryId)
            .putNullable("categoryName", item.categoryName)
            .putNullable("coverUrl", item.coverUrl)
            .putNullable("backdropUrl", item.backdropUrl)
            .put("contentType", item.contentType.name)
            .putNullable("rating", item.rating)
            .putNullable("year", item.year)
            .putNullable("metadataProvider", item.metadataProvider)
            .putNullable("metadataId", item.metadataId)
            .putNullable("traktSlug", item.traktSlug)
            .putNullable("traktType", item.traktType)
            .putNullable("imdbId", item.imdbId)
            .putNullable("tmdbId", item.tmdbId)
            .put("genres", JSONArray(item.genres))
    }

    private fun parseContentType(value: String): ContentType {
        return when (value.lowercase()) {
            "live" -> ContentType.LIVE
            "series" -> ContentType.SERIES
            "episode" -> ContentType.EPISODE
            "action" -> ContentType.ACTION
            else -> ContentType.MOVIE
        }
    }

    private fun JSONObject.putNullable(name: String, value: String?): JSONObject {
        return put(name, value ?: JSONObject.NULL)
    }

    private fun JSONObject.optNullableString(name: String): String? {
        return if (has(name) && !isNull(name)) optString(name).takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } else null
    }

    private fun JSONObject.optIntNullable(name: String): Int? {
        return if (has(name) && !isNull(name)) optInt(name) else null
    }

    private fun requestBuilder(url: String): Request.Builder {
        val builder = Request.Builder().url(url)
        if (!syncServerToken.isNullOrBlank()) {
            builder.header("Authorization", "Bearer $syncServerToken")
        } else if (!syncServerUsername.isNullOrBlank() && !syncServerPassword.isNullOrBlank()) {
            builder.header("Authorization", Credentials.basic(syncServerUsername, syncServerPassword))
        }
        return builder
    }

    data class ServerAuthStatus(
        val ok: Boolean,
        val username: String?,
        val displayName: String?,
        val isAdmin: Boolean,
        val tmdbLinked: Boolean = false,
        val tmdbUsername: String? = null
    )

    data class TmdbRequestToken(
        val requestToken: String,
        val authenticationUrl: String
    )

    data class PairingStart(
        val deviceCode: String,
        val pairingUrl: String,
        val qrPayload: String?,
        val expiresAt: String?,
        val pollIntervalSeconds: Int
    )

    data class PairingStatus(
        val status: String,
        val syncServerUrl: String?,
        val syncServerUsername: String?,
        val syncServerToken: String?,
        val displayName: String?,
        val expiresAt: String?
    )

    data class SyncedIptvCredentials(
        val serverUrl: String,
        val username: String,
        val password: String,
        val profileId: String?,
        val updatedAt: String?
    )
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/NetworkPolicy.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import okhttp3.HttpUrl.Companion.toHttpUrlOrNull

object NetworkPolicy {
    fun isAllowedControlPlaneUrl(raw: String?): Boolean {
        val url = raw?.trim()?.trimEnd('/')?.toHttpUrlOrNull() ?: return false
        if (url.isHttps) return true
        if (url.scheme != "http") return false
        return isLocalHost(url.host)
    }

    fun requireAllowedControlPlaneUrl(raw: String?): String {
        val normalized = raw?.trim()?.trimEnd('/').orEmpty()
        require(isAllowedControlPlaneUrl(normalized)) {
            "Remote sync and social servers must use HTTPS. Plain HTTP is allowed only on localhost or a private LAN."
        }
        return normalized
    }

    private fun isLocalHost(host: String): Boolean {
        val value = host.lowercase()
        if (value == "localhost" || value == "127.0.0.1" || value == "::1") return true
        if (value.startsWith("10.")) return true
        if (value.startsWith("192.168.")) return true
        if (value.startsWith("172.")) {
            val second = value.substringAfter("172.").substringBefore('.').toIntOrNull()
            if (second != null && second in 16..31) return true
        }
        return value.endsWith(".local")
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/SocialApiClient.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import android.util.Log
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialFriendship
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialMessage
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialRoom
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialUser
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ViewingParty
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ViewingPartyInvite
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.WatchPresence
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.objects
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.optCleanString
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext
import okhttp3.*
import okhttp3.HttpUrl.Companion.toHttpUrlOrNull
import okhttp3.MediaType.Companion.toMediaType
import okhttp3.RequestBody.Companion.toRequestBody
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.text.SimpleDateFormat
import java.util.Locale
import java.util.TimeZone
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit

class SocialApiClient(
    private val settings: SocialSettings,
    private val client: OkHttpClient = OkHttpClient.Builder()
        .connectTimeout(15, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
        .readTimeout(15, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
        .build()
) {
    private val jsonMediaType = "application/json; charset=utf-8".toMediaType()

    suspend fun checkHealth(): Boolean = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext false
        val request = Request.Builder().url("$url/health").get().build()
        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { it.isSuccessful }
        }.getOrDefault(false)
    }

    suspend fun getSessionToken(): String? = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext null
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/session")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .get()
            .build()
        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "").optString("token")
                } else null
            }
        }.getOrNull()
    }

    suspend fun getRooms(catalogItemId: String? = null, roomType: String? = null): List<SocialRoom> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val baseUrl = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val urlBuilder = "$baseUrl/api/social/rooms".toHttpUrlOrNull()?.newBuilder() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        if (catalogItemId != null) urlBuilder.addQueryParameter("catalogItemId", catalogItemId)
        if (roomType != null) urlBuilder.addQueryParameter("roomType", roomType)

        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url(urlBuilder.build())
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .get()
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    val array = root.optJSONArray("rooms") ?: JSONArray()
                    array.objects().map { parseRoom(it) }
                } else emptyList()
            }
        }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
    }

    suspend fun getUsers(): List<SocialUser> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/users")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .get()
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    val array = root.optJSONArray("users") ?: JSONArray()
                    array.objects().map { parseUser(it) }
                } else emptyList()
            }
        }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
    }

    suspend fun getFriends(): List<SocialFriendship> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/friends")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .get()
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    val array = root.optJSONArray("friendships") ?: JSONArray()
                    array.objects().map { parseFriendship(it) }
                } else emptyList()
            }
        }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
    }

    suspend fun requestFriend(userId: String): SocialFriendship? = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext null
        val body = JSONObject().put("userId", userId)
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/friends")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}").optJSONObject("friendship")?.let(::parseFriendship)
                } else null
            }
        }.getOrNull()
    }

    suspend fun getCurrentViewers(item: IptvItem): List<WatchPresence> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val baseUrl = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val url = "$baseUrl/api/social/watching".toHttpUrlOrNull()?.newBuilder()
            ?.addQueryParameter("catalogKey", item.stableKey)
            ?.build() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url(url)
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .get()
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    val array = root.optJSONArray("viewers") ?: JSONArray()
                    array.objects().map { parseWatchPresence(it) }
                } else emptyList()
            }
        }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
    }

    suspend fun updateWatchPresence(item: IptvItem, roomId: String? = null, positionMs: Long = 0L, durationMs: Long = 0L): WatchPresence? = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext null
        val body = JSONObject().apply {
            put("catalogKey", item.stableKey)
            put("catalogTitle", item.title)
            put("catalogType", item.contentType.name.lowercase(Locale.US))
            put("roomId", roomId)
            put("positionMs", positionMs)
            put("durationMs", durationMs)
            put("playbackState", "watching")
            put("deviceName", android.os.Build.MODEL ?: "Android TV")
        }
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/watching")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}").optJSONObject("presence")?.let(::parseWatchPresence)
                } else null
            }
        }.getOrNull()
    }

    suspend fun createViewingParty(item: IptvItem, title: String, scheduledForIso: String? = null, inviteUserIds: List<String> = emptyList()): ViewingParty? = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext null
        val body = JSONObject().apply {
            put("catalogKey", item.stableKey)
            put("title", title)
            put("scheduledFor", scheduledForIso)
            put("inviteUserIds", JSONArray(inviteUserIds))
        }
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/parties")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}").optJSONObject("party")?.let(::parseViewingParty)
                } else null
            }
        }.getOrNull()
    }

    suspend fun createRoom(roomType: String, catalogItemId: String?, title: String): SocialRoom? = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext null
        val body = JSONObject().apply {
            put("roomType", roomType)
            put("catalogItemId", catalogItemId)
            put("title", title)
        }
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/rooms")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    root.optJSONObject("room")?.let(::parseRoom) ?: parseRoom(root)
                }
                else null
            }
        }.getOrNull()
    }

    suspend fun getMessages(roomId: String, limit: Int = 50): List<SocialMessage> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/rooms/$roomId/messages?limit=$limit")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .get()
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    val array = root.optJSONArray("messages") ?: JSONArray()
                    array.objects().map { parseMessage(it) }
                } else emptyList()
            }
        }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
    }

    suspend fun sendMessage(roomId: String, text: String, clientMessageId: String): SocialMessage? = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext null
        val body = JSONObject().apply {
            put("text", text)
            put("clientMessageId", clientMessageId)
        }
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/rooms/$roomId/messages")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (response.isSuccessful) {
                    val root = JSONObject(response.body?.string() ?: "{}")
                    root.optJSONObject("message")?.let(::parseMessage) ?: parseMessage(root)
                }
                else null
            }
        }.getOrNull()
    }


    suspend fun sendWatchPartyControl(roomId: String, action: String, positionMs: Long = 0L, durationMs: Long = 0L): Boolean = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext false
        val body = JSONObject().apply {
            put("action", action)
            put("positionMs", positionMs)
            put("durationMs", durationMs)
        }
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/rooms/$roomId/control")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()
        runCatching { client.newCall(request).execute().use { it.isSuccessful } }.getOrDefault(false)
    }

    suspend fun shareMedia(roomId: String, item: IptvItem, text: String?): Boolean = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val url = settings.getServerUrl() ?: return@withContext false
        val body = JSONObject().apply {
            put("roomId", roomId)
            put("catalogItemId", item.stableKey)
            put("text", text ?: "")
            put("metadata", JSONObject().apply {
                put("title", item.title)
                put("type", item.contentType.name)
                put("year", item.year)
                put("posterUrl", item.coverUrl)
                put("backdropUrl", item.backdropUrl)
                put("description", item.description)
                put("rating", item.rating)
            })
        }
        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url("$url/api/social/share/media")
            .header("Authorization", buildAuthHeader())
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(jsonMediaType))
            .build()

        runCatching {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { it.isSuccessful }
        }.getOrDefault(false)
    }

    private fun buildAuthHeader(): String {
        val name = settings.getDisplayName() ?: "AndroidTV"
        val token = settings.getToken() ?: ""
        // Simple auth for now, adjust if server expects something else
        return Credentials.basic(name, token)
    }

    private fun parseRoom(obj: JSONObject) = SocialRoom(
        id = obj.optString("id"),
        roomType = obj.optString("roomType"),
        catalogItemId = obj.optCleanString("catalogItemId"),
        title = obj.optString("title"),
        lastMessage = obj.optCleanString("lastMessage") ?: obj.optCleanString("lastMessagePreview"),
        updatedAt = parseTimestamp(obj.opt("lastMessageAt")) ?: parseTimestamp(obj.opt("updatedAt")) ?: 0L,
        unreadCount = obj.optInt("unreadCount")
    )

    private fun parseMessage(obj: JSONObject) = SocialMessage(
        id = obj.optString("id"),
        clientMessageId = obj.optCleanString("clientMessageId"),
        roomId = obj.optString("roomId"),
        senderUserId = obj.optString("senderUserId"),
        senderDisplayName = obj.optString("senderDisplayName"),
        messageType = obj.optString("messageType"),
        text = obj.optString("text"),
        createdAt = parseTimestamp(obj.opt("createdAt")) ?: 0L,
        sharePayload = obj.optJSONObject("sharePayload")?.toString()
    )

    private fun parseUser(obj: JSONObject) = SocialUser(
        id = obj.optString("id"),
        displayName = obj.optCleanString("displayName") ?: obj.optCleanString("username") ?: "Viewer",
        username = obj.optCleanString("username"),
        avatarUrl = obj.optCleanString("avatarUrl"),
        status = obj.optCleanString("status"),
        lastSeenAt = parseTimestamp(obj.opt("lastSeenAt")) ?: 0L
    )

    private fun parseWatchPresence(obj: JSONObject) = WatchPresence(
        id = obj.optString("id"),
        roomId = obj.optCleanString("roomId"),
        catalogKey = obj.optString("catalogKey"),
        catalogTitle = obj.optString("catalogTitle"),
        catalogType = obj.optCleanString("catalogType"),
        positionMs = obj.optLong("positionMs"),
        durationMs = obj.optLong("durationMs"),
        playbackState = obj.optString("playbackState", "watching"),
        deviceName = obj.optCleanString("deviceName"),
        lastHeartbeatAt = parseTimestamp(obj.opt("lastHeartbeatAt")) ?: 0L,
        user = obj.optJSONObject("user")?.let(::parseUser)
    )

    private fun parseFriendship(obj: JSONObject) = SocialFriendship(
        id = obj.optString("id"),
        status = obj.optString("status"),
        direction = obj.optString("direction"),
        otherUser = obj.optJSONObject("otherUser")?.let(::parseUser)
    )

    private fun parseViewingParty(obj: JSONObject) = ViewingParty(
        id = obj.optString("id"),
        title = obj.optString("title"),
        status = obj.optString("status"),
        scheduledFor = parseTimestamp(obj.opt("scheduledFor")) ?: 0L,
        catalogKey = obj.optCleanString("catalogKey"),
        catalogTitle = obj.optString("catalogTitle"),
        catalogType = obj.optCleanString("catalogType"),
        room = obj.optJSONObject("room")?.let(::parseRoom),
        createdBy = obj.optJSONObject("createdBy")?.let(::parseUser),
        invites = (obj.optJSONArray("invites") ?: JSONArray()).objects().map {
            ViewingPartyInvite(
                id = it.optString("id"),
                status = it.optString("status"),
                user = it.optJSONObject("user")?.let(::parseUser)
            )
        }
    )

    private fun parseTimestamp(value: Any?): Long? {
        return when (value) {
            is Number -> value.toLong()
            is String -> value.toLongOrNull() ?: runCatching { isoDateFormat.parse(value)?.time }.getOrNull()
            else -> null
        }
    }

    companion object {
        private val isoDateFormat = SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSS'Z'", Locale.US).apply {
            timeZone = TimeZone.getTimeZone("UTC")
        }
    }
}

================================================================================
// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/SocialWebSocketClient.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import android.util.Log
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialMessage
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.optCleanString
import okhttp3.OkHttpClient
import okhttp3.Request
import okhttp3.Response
import okhttp3.WebSocket
import okhttp3.WebSocketListener
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.text.SimpleDateFormat
import java.util.Locale
import java.util.TimeZone
import java.util.concurrent.Executors
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledFuture
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit
import kotlin.math.min

class SocialWebSocketClient(
    private val settings: SocialSettings,
    private val onMessageReceived: (SocialMessage) -> Unit,
    private val onStatusChanged: (Boolean) -> Unit
) {
    private val client = OkHttpClient.Builder()
        .readTimeout(0, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)
        .pingInterval(20, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
        .build()
    private val scheduler = Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor { runnable ->
        Thread(runnable, "social-websocket-reconnect").apply { isDaemon = true }
    }
    private var webSocket: WebSocket? = null
    private var currentRoomId: String? = null
    private var sessionToken: String? = null
    private var reconnectAttempt = 0
    private var reconnectFuture: ScheduledFuture<*>? = null
    @Volatile private var closedByUser = false
    @Volatile private var connected = false

    fun connect(token: String) {
        sessionToken = token
        closedByUser = false
        reconnectFuture?.cancel(false)
        openSocket()
    }

    private fun openSocket() {
        val token = sessionToken ?: return
        val baseUrl = settings.getServerUrl()?.takeIf { NetworkPolicy.isAllowedControlPlaneUrl(it) } ?: return
        val wsUrl = baseUrl.replaceFirst("http://", "ws://").replaceFirst("https://", "wss://") +
            "/ws/social?token=${java.net.URLEncoder.encode(token, Charsets.UTF_8.name())}"
        webSocket?.cancel()
        webSocket = client.newWebSocket(Request.Builder().url(wsUrl).build(), listener)
    }

    private val listener = object : WebSocketListener() {
        override fun onOpen(webSocket: WebSocket, response: Response) {
            Log.i(TAG, "WebSocket connected")
            connected = true
            reconnectAttempt = 0
            onStatusChanged(true)
            currentRoomId?.let(::joinRoom)
        }

        override fun onMessage(webSocket: WebSocket, text: String) {
            runCatching {
                val json = JSONObject(text)
                if (json.optString("type") == "message" || json.optString("type") == "messageCreated") {
                    val msgObj = json.optJSONObject("data") ?: json.optJSONObject("message") ?: return@runCatching
                    onMessageReceived(
                        SocialMessage(
                            id = msgObj.optString("id"),
                            clientMessageId = msgObj.optCleanString("clientMessageId"),
                            roomId = msgObj.optString("roomId"),
                            senderUserId = msgObj.optString("senderUserId"),
                            senderDisplayName = msgObj.optString("senderDisplayName"),
                            messageType = msgObj.optString("messageType"),
                            text = msgObj.optString("text"),
                            createdAt = parseTimestamp(msgObj.opt("createdAt")) ?: 0L,
                            sharePayload = msgObj.optJSONObject("sharePayload")?.toString()
                        )
                    )
                }
            }.onFailure { Log.e(TAG, "Error parsing WebSocket message", it) }
        }

        override fun onClosing(webSocket: WebSocket, code: Int, reason: String) {
            connected = false
            onStatusChanged(false)
            webSocket.close(code, reason)
        }

        override fun onClosed(webSocket: WebSocket, code: Int, reason: String) {
            connected = false
            onStatusChanged(false)
            scheduleReconnect()
        }

        override fun onFailure(webSocket: WebSocket, error: Throwable, response: Response?) {
            Log.w(TAG, "WebSocket failure: ${error.message}")
            connected = false
            onStatusChanged(false)
            scheduleReconnect()
        }
    }

    private fun scheduleReconnect() {
        if (closedByUser || sessionToken.isNullOrBlank()) return
        reconnectFuture?.cancel(false)
        reconnectAttempt += 1
        val delaySeconds = min(60L, 1L shl min(reconnectAttempt, 6))
        reconnectFuture = scheduler.schedule({
            if (!closedByUser) openSocket()
        }, delaySeconds, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
    }

    fun joinRoom(roomId: String) {
        currentRoomId = roomId
        sendEvent(JSONObject().put("type", "joinRoom").put("roomId", roomId))
    }

    fun leaveRoom(roomId: String) {
        if (currentRoomId == roomId) currentRoomId = null
        sendEvent(JSONObject().put("type", "leaveRoom").put("roomId", roomId))
    }

    fun sendMessage(roomId: String, text: String, clientMessageId: String): Boolean {
        return sendEvent(
            JSONObject()
                .put("type", "sendMessage")
                .put("roomId", roomId)
                .put("text", text)
                .put("clientMessageId", clientMessageId)
        )
    }

    private fun sendEvent(event: JSONObject): Boolean {
        return connected && webSocket?.send(event.toString()) == true
    }

    fun disconnect() {
        closedByUser = true
        sessionToken = null
        reconnectFuture?.cancel(false)
        reconnectFuture = null
        connected = false
        onStatusChanged(false)
        webSocket?.close(1000, "App closed")
        webSocket = null
    }

    private fun parseTimestamp(value: Any?): Long? {
        return when (value) {
            is Number -> value.toLong()
            is String -> value.toLongOrNull() ?: runCatching { isoDateFormat.parse(value)?.time }.getOrNull()
            else -> null
        }
    }

    companion object {
        private const val TAG = "SocialWS"
        private val isoDateFormat = SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSS'Z'", Locale.US).apply {
            timeZone = TimeZone.getTimeZone("UTC")
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/TmdbApiClient.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext
import okhttp3.HttpUrl.Companion.toHttpUrl
import okhttp3.OkHttpClient
import okhttp3.Request
import org.json.JSONObject

class TmdbApiClient(
    private val apiKey: String?,
    private val client: OkHttpClient = OkHttpClient.Builder().build()
) {
    fun isConfigured(): Boolean = !apiKey.isNullOrBlank()

    suspend fun enrichItems(items: List<IptvItem>, maxItems: Int = 40): List<IptvItem> {
        if (!isConfigured()) return items
        return withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
            items.mapIndexed { index, item ->
                if (index < maxItems) runCatching { enrichItemBlocking(item) }.getOrDefault(item) else item
            }
        }
    }

    private fun enrichItemBlocking(item: IptvItem): IptvItem {
        if (item.contentType != ContentType.MOVIE && item.contentType != ContentType.SERIES) return item

        val cleanTitle = cleanTitle(item.title)
        if (cleanTitle.isBlank()) return item

        val mediaType = if (item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES) "tv" else "movie"
        val searchUrl = buildSearchUrl(mediaType, cleanTitle, item.year)
        val root = JSONObject(execute(searchUrl))
        val results = root.optJSONArray("results") ?: return item
        if (results.length() == 0) return item

        val match = results.optJSONObject(0) ?: return item
        val title = match.optString(if (mediaType == "tv") "name" else "title", item.title).ifBlank { item.title }
        val overview = match.optString("overview", "").ifBlank { item.description }
        val posterPath = match.optString("poster_path", "").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() && it != "null" }
        val backdropPath = match.optString("backdrop_path", "").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() && it != "null" }
        val voteAverage = match.optDouble("vote_average", 0.0)
        val tmdbYear = extractYear(match.optString(if (mediaType == "tv") "first_air_date" else "release_date", ""))
        val tmdbId = match.optLong("id", 0L).takeIf { it > 0L }?.toString()

        return item.copy(
            title = title,
            description = overview,
            coverUrl = posterPath?.let { imageUrl("w500", it) } ?: item.coverUrl,
            backdropUrl = backdropPath?.let { imageUrl("w1280", it) } ?: item.backdropUrl,
            rating = if (voteAverage > 0.0) String.format("%.1f", voteAverage) else item.rating,
            year = tmdbYear ?: item.year,
            metadataProvider = "TMDB",
            metadataId = tmdbId
        )
    }

    private fun buildSearchUrl(mediaType: String, query: String, year: String?): String {
        val builder = "https://api.themoviedb.org/3/search/$mediaType".toHttpUrl().newBuilder()
            .addQueryParameter("api_key", apiKey)
            .addQueryParameter("query", query)
            .addQueryParameter("include_adult", "false")
            .addQueryParameter("language", "en-US")
            .addQueryParameter("page", "1")

        year?.takeIf { it.matches(Regex("\\d{4}")) }?.let {
            if (mediaType == "tv") builder.addQueryParameter("first_air_date_year", it)
            else builder.addQueryParameter("primary_release_year", it)
        }

        return builder.build().toString()
    }

    private fun execute(url: String): String {
        val request = Request.Builder().url(url).get().build()
        client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
            if (!response.isSuccessful) error("TMDB returned HTTP ${response.code}")
            return response.body?.string() ?: error("Empty TMDB response")
        }
    }

    private fun imageUrl(size: String, path: String): String {
        return "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/$size${if (path.startsWith("/")) path else "/$path"}"
    }

    private fun extractYear(date: String): String? {
        return Regex("^(\\d{4})").find(date)?.groupValues?.getOrNull(1)
    }

    private fun cleanTitle(raw: String): String {
        return raw
            .replace(Regex("\\[[^]]*]"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\([^)]*\\)"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\b(19|20)\\d{2}\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\b(4k|uhd|fhd|hd|sd|1080p|720p|2160p|x264|x265|hevc|h264|h265|bluray|web[- ]?dl)\\b", RegexOption.IGNORE_CASE), " ")
            .replace(Regex("[._-]+"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\s+"), " ")
            .trim()
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/TraktApiClient.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.objects
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.optCleanString
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.delay
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext
import okhttp3.HttpUrl.Companion.toHttpUrl
import okhttp3.MediaType.Companion.toMediaType
import okhttp3.OkHttpClient
import okhttp3.Request
import okhttp3.RequestBody.Companion.toRequestBody
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject

class TraktApiClient(
    private val credentials: IptvCredentials,
    private val client: OkHttpClient = OkHttpClient.Builder().build()
) {
    data class DeviceCode(
        val deviceCode: String,
        val userCode: String,
        val verificationUrl: String,
        val expiresInSeconds: Int,
        val intervalSeconds: Int
    )

    data class TokenResponse(
        val accessToken: String,
        val refreshToken: String?,
        val expiresInSeconds: Int
    )

    fun isConfigured(): Boolean = !credentials.traktClientId.isNullOrBlank()
    fun isUserLinked(): Boolean = isConfigured() && !credentials.traktAccessToken.isNullOrBlank()

    suspend fun getTrendingMovies(limit: Int = 30): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (!isConfigured()) return@withContext emptyList()
        getArray("/movies/trending", mapOf("limit" to limit.toString(), "extended" to "full"))
            .objects()
            .mapIndexedNotNull { index, obj -> parseTraktMedia(index.toLong(), obj.optJSONObject("movie"), ContentType.MOVIE, "Trending on Trakt") }
    }

    suspend fun getTrendingShows(limit: Int = 30): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (!isConfigured()) return@withContext emptyList()
        getArray("/shows/trending", mapOf("limit" to limit.toString(), "extended" to "full"))
            .objects()
            .mapIndexedNotNull { index, obj -> parseTraktMedia(index.toLong(), obj.optJSONObject("show"), ContentType.SERIES, "Trending on Trakt") }
    }

    suspend fun search(query: String, limit: Int = 40): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (!isConfigured() || query.isBlank()) return@withContext emptyList()
        getArray("/search/movie,show", mapOf("query" to query, "limit" to limit.toString(), "extended" to "full"))
            .objects()
            .mapIndexedNotNull { index, obj ->
                val movie = obj.optJSONObject("movie")
                val show = obj.optJSONObject("show")
                when {
                    movie != null -> parseTraktMedia(index.toLong(), movie, ContentType.MOVIE, "Trakt Search")
                    show != null -> parseTraktMedia(index.toLong(), show, ContentType.SERIES, "Trakt Search")
                    else -> null
                }
            }
    }

    suspend fun enrichItems(items: List<IptvItem>, maxItems: Int = 40): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (!isConfigured()) return@withContext items
        items.mapIndexed { index, item ->
            if (index >= maxItems || item.contentType == ContentType.LIVE || item.contentType == ContentType.ACTION) item else enrichItem(item)
        }
    }

    suspend fun getUserWatchlist(limit: Int = 40): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (!isUserLinked()) return@withContext emptyList()
        getArray("/sync/watchlist", mapOf("extended" to "full"))
            .objects()
            .take(limit)
            .mapIndexedNotNull { index, obj ->
                val movie = obj.optJSONObject("movie")
                val show = obj.optJSONObject("show")
                when {
                    movie != null -> parseTraktMedia(index.toLong(), movie, ContentType.MOVIE, "Trakt Watchlist")
                    show != null -> parseTraktMedia(index.toLong(), show, ContentType.SERIES, "Trakt Watchlist")
                    else -> null
                }
            }
    }

    suspend fun syncWatchlistItem(item: IptvItem): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            if (!isUserLinked()) return@runCatching
            val body = JSONObject()
            val ids = traktIds(item)
            when (item.contentType) {
                ContentType.MOVIE -> body.put("movies", JSONArray().put(JSONObject().put("ids", ids)))
                ContentType.SERIES -> body.put("shows", JSONArray().put(JSONObject().put("ids", ids)))
                else -> return@runCatching
            }
            post("/sync/watchlist", body)
        }
    }

    suspend fun syncHistoryItem(item: IptvItem): Result<Unit> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        runCatching {
            if (!isUserLinked()) return@runCatching
            val ids = traktIds(item)
            val body = JSONObject()
            when (item.contentType) {
                ContentType.MOVIE -> body.put("movies", JSONArray().put(JSONObject().put("ids", ids)))
                ContentType.EPISODE -> body.put("episodes", JSONArray().put(JSONObject().put("ids", ids)))
                else -> return@runCatching
            }
            post("/sync/history", body)
        }
    }

    suspend fun requestDeviceCode(): DeviceCode = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (credentials.traktClientId.isNullOrBlank()) error("Trakt Client ID is required.")
        val payload = JSONObject().put("client_id", credentials.traktClientId)
        val response = postRaw("/oauth/device/code", payload, authenticated = false)
        DeviceCode(
            deviceCode = response.optString("device_code"),
            userCode = response.optString("user_code"),
            verificationUrl = response.optString("verification_url", "https://trakt.tv/activate"),
            expiresInSeconds = response.optInt("expires_in", 600),
            intervalSeconds = response.optInt("interval", 5).coerceAtLeast(5)
        )
    }

    suspend fun pollDeviceToken(deviceCode: DeviceCode, maxPolls: Int = 80): TokenResponse = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (credentials.traktClientId.isNullOrBlank() || credentials.traktClientSecret.isNullOrBlank()) {
            error("Trakt Client ID and Client Secret are required for device linking.")
        }
        val startedAt = System.currentTimeMillis()
        repeat(maxPolls) {
            val elapsedSeconds = ((System.currentTimeMillis() - startedAt) / 1000L).toInt()
            if (elapsedSeconds >= deviceCode.expiresInSeconds) error("Trakt device code expired. Start linking again.")
            delay(deviceCode.intervalSeconds * 1000L)
            val payload = JSONObject()
                .put("code", deviceCode.deviceCode)
                .put("client_id", credentials.traktClientId)
                .put("client_secret", credentials.traktClientSecret)
            val result = runCatching { postRaw("/oauth/device/token", payload, authenticated = false) }
            val obj = result.getOrNull()
            if (obj != null && obj.optString("access_token").isNotBlank()) {
                return@withContext TokenResponse(
                    accessToken = obj.optString("access_token"),
                    refreshToken = obj.optString("refresh_token", null),
                    expiresInSeconds = obj.optInt("expires_in", 0)
                )
            }
        }
        error("Trakt linking timed out. Try again.")
    }

    private fun enrichItem(item: IptvItem): IptvItem {
        val query = cleanTitle(item.title)
        if (query.isBlank()) return item
        val type = when (item.contentType) {
            ContentType.MOVIE -> "movie"
            ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.EPISODE -> "show"
            else -> return item
        }
        val results = getArray("/search/$type", mapOf("query" to query, "limit" to "1", "extended" to "full")).objects()
        val wrapper = results.firstOrNull() ?: return item
        val media = wrapper.optJSONObject(type) ?: return item
        val parsed = parseTraktMedia(item.id, media, item.contentType, "Trakt") ?: return item
        return item.copy(
            description = parsed.description.ifBlank { item.description },
            rating = parsed.rating ?: item.rating,
            year = parsed.year ?: item.year,
            metadataProvider = "Trakt",
            metadataId = parsed.metadataId,
            traktSlug = parsed.traktSlug,
            traktType = parsed.traktType,
            imdbId = parsed.imdbId,
            tmdbId = parsed.tmdbId,
            genres = parsed.genres.ifEmpty { item.genres },
            sourceLabel = parsed.sourceLabel,
            coverUrl = parsed.coverUrl ?: item.coverUrl,
            backdropUrl = parsed.backdropUrl ?: item.backdropUrl,
            addedAtMs = item.addedAtMs
        )
    }

    private fun parseTraktMedia(id: Long, media: JSONObject?, contentType: ContentType, source: String): IptvItem? {
        if (media == null) return null
        val ids = media.optJSONObject("ids") ?: JSONObject()
        val rating = media.optDouble("rating", -1.0).takeIf { it >= 0.0 }?.let { String.format("%.1f", it) }
        val genres = media.optJSONArray("genres")?.let { array ->
            val values = mutableListOf<String>()
            for (index in 0 until array.length()) array.optString(index).takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let(values::add)
            values
        } ?: emptyList()

        return IptvItem(
            id = id,
            streamId = ids.optString("trakt", ids.optString("slug", "trakt_$id")),
            title = media.optCleanString("title") ?: "Untitled",
            description = media.optCleanString("overview") ?: "",
            rating = rating,
            year = media.optInt("year", 0).takeIf { it > 0 }?.toString(),
            contentType = contentType,
            metadataProvider = "Trakt",
            metadataId = ids.optString("trakt", null),
            traktSlug = ids.optString("slug", null),
            traktType = if (contentType == ContentType.MOVIE) "movie" else "show",
            imdbId = ids.optString("imdb", null),
            tmdbId = ids.optString("tmdb", null),
            genres = genres,
            sourceLabel = source,
            coverUrl = media.optCleanString("poster") ?: media.optCleanString("thumb"),
            backdropUrl = media.optCleanString("fanart") ?: media.optCleanString("background")
        )
    }

    private fun traktIds(item: IptvItem): JSONObject {
        val ids = JSONObject()
        item.metadataId?.toIntOrNull()?.let { ids.put("trakt", it) }
        item.traktSlug?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { ids.put("slug", it) }
        item.imdbId?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { ids.put("imdb", it) }
        item.tmdbId?.toIntOrNull()?.let { ids.put("tmdb", it) }
        if (ids.length() == 0) ids.put("slug", cleanTitle(item.title).lowercase().replace(Regex("[^a-z0-9]+"), "-").trim('-'))
        return ids
    }

    private fun cleanTitle(title: String): String {
        return title
            .replace(Regex("\\[[^]]*]"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\([^)]*\\)"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("(?i)\\b(4k|uhd|fhd|hd|sd|hdr|x264|x265|hevc|bluray|web[- ]?dl)\\b"), " ")
            .replace(Regex("\\s+"), " ")
            .trim()
    }

    private fun getArray(path: String, params: Map<String, String> = emptyMap()): JSONArray {
        val url = buildUrl(path, params)
        val request = baseRequest(url).get().build()
        client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
            if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Trakt returned HTTP ${response.code}")
            return JSONArray(response.body?.string() ?: "[]")
        }
    }

    private fun post(path: String, body: JSONObject): JSONObject = postRaw(path, body, authenticated = true)

    private fun postRaw(path: String, body: JSONObject, authenticated: Boolean): JSONObject {
        val requestBuilder = if (authenticated) baseRequest(buildUrl(path)) else unauthenticatedRequest(buildUrl(path))
        val request = requestBuilder
            .post(body.toString().toRequestBody(JSON_MEDIA_TYPE))
            .build()
        client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
            val raw = response.body?.string().orEmpty()
            if (!response.isSuccessful) error("Trakt returned HTTP ${response.code}: $raw")
            return if (raw.isBlank()) JSONObject() else JSONObject(raw)
        }
    }

    private fun buildUrl(path: String, params: Map<String, String> = emptyMap()): String {
        val builder = "https://api.trakt.tv${path}".toHttpUrl().newBuilder()
        params.forEach { (key, value) -> builder.addQueryParameter(key, value) }
        return builder.build().toString()
    }

    private fun baseRequest(url: String): Request.Builder {
        val builder = unauthenticatedRequest(url)
            .header("trakt-api-key", credentials.traktClientId.orEmpty())
        credentials.traktAccessToken?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { token ->
            builder.header("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
        }
        return builder
    }

    private fun unauthenticatedRequest(url: String): Request.Builder {
        return Request.Builder()
            .url(url)
            .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
            .header("trakt-api-version", "2")
    }

    companion object {
        private val JSON_MEDIA_TYPE = "application/json; charset=utf-8".toMediaType()
    }
}
