// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/remote/XtreamApiClient.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCategory
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.EpgProgram
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.objects
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.optCleanString
import android.util.Log
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext
import okhttp3.HttpUrl.Companion.toHttpUrl
import okhttp3.OkHttpClient
import okhttp3.Request
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream
import java.net.ProtocolException
import java.net.Socket
import java.net.URL
import java.security.MessageDigest
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit

class XtreamApiClient(
    private val credentials: IptvCredentials,
    private val client: OkHttpClient = OkHttpClient.Builder()
        .connectTimeout(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
        .readTimeout(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
        .writeTimeout(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
        .retryOnConnectionFailure(true)
        .addNetworkInterceptor { chain ->
            // Many IPTV servers return corrupted GZIP or mislabeled encoding.
            // Forcing identity and removing server-side content-encoding can bypass buggy decompression.
            val request = chain.request().newBuilder()
                .header("Accept-Encoding", "identity")
                .build()
            val response = chain.proceed(request)
            if (response.header("Content-Encoding") != null) {
                response.newBuilder().removeHeader("Content-Encoding").build()
            } else {
                response
            }
        }
        .build()
) {
    companion object {
        private const val TAG = "XtreamApiClient"
        private const val USER_AGENT = "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/119.0.0.0 Safari/537.36"
    }

    private val providerAccountId: String by lazy {
        val identity = "${credentials.serverUrl.trim().trimEnd('/').lowercase()}|${credentials.username.trim().lowercase()}"
        MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256")
            .digest(identity.toByteArray(Charsets.UTF_8))
            .joinToString("") { "%02x".format(it) }
            .take(20)
    }

    suspend fun validateLogin(): Boolean = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val response = requestJsonObject(null)
        val userInfo = response.optJSONObject("user_info") ?: return@withContext false
        val auth = userInfo.opt("auth")?.toString()
        auth == "1" || auth.equals("true", ignoreCase = true)
    }

    suspend fun getCategories(contentType: ContentType): List<IptvCategory> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val action = when (contentType) {
            ContentType.LIVE -> "get_live_categories"
            ContentType.MOVIE -> "get_vod_categories"
            ContentType.SERIES -> "get_series_categories"
            ContentType.EPISODE, ContentType.ACTION -> return@withContext emptyList()
        }
        requestJsonArray(action).objects().mapNotNull { obj ->
            val id = obj.optCleanString("category_id") ?: return@mapNotNull null
            IptvCategory(
                categoryId = id,
                categoryName = obj.optCleanString("category_name") ?: "Category $id",
                contentType = contentType
            )
        }
    }

    suspend fun getItems(contentType: ContentType, category: IptvCategory? = null, limit: Int? = 50): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val action = when (contentType) {
            ContentType.LIVE -> "get_live_streams"
            ContentType.MOVIE -> "get_vod_streams"
            ContentType.SERIES -> "get_series"
            ContentType.EPISODE, ContentType.ACTION -> return@withContext emptyList()
        }
        val params = buildMap {
            if (category != null) put("category_id", category.categoryId)
        }
        val items = requestJsonArray(action, params).objects()
            .mapIndexed { index, obj -> parseItem(index.toLong(), obj, contentType, category) }
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.addedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase() })
        if (limit == null) items else items.take(limit)
    }

    suspend fun getVodInfo(vodId: String): JSONObject = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        val response = requestJsonObject("get_vod_info", mapOf("vod_id" to vodId))
        // Basic subtitle extraction if available in the response
        val info = response.optJSONObject("info")
        val subs = info?.optString("subtitles")
        if (!subs.isNullOrBlank()) {
             Log.d(TAG, "Found subtitles for $vodId: $subs")
        }
        response
    }

    suspend fun getSeriesInfo(seriesId: String): JSONObject = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        requestJsonObject("get_series_info", mapOf("series_id" to seriesId))
    }

    suspend fun getSeriesEpisodes(series: IptvItem): List<IptvItem> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (series.streamId.isBlank()) return@withContext emptyList()
        val response = requestJsonObject("get_series_info", mapOf("series_id" to series.streamId))
        val episodesObj = response.optJSONObject("episodes") ?: return@withContext emptyList()
        val items = mutableListOf<IptvItem>()
        val seasonKeys = episodesObj.keys()
        while (seasonKeys.hasNext()) {
            val seasonKey = seasonKeys.next()
            val seasonNumber = seasonKey.toIntOrNull() ?: continue
            val episodes = episodesObj.optJSONArray(seasonKey) ?: continue
            for (index in 0 until episodes.length()) {
                val obj = episodes.optJSONObject(index) ?: continue
                val episodeId = obj.optCleanString("id") ?: obj.optCleanString("episode_id") ?: continue
                val extension = obj.optCleanString("container_extension") ?: "mp4"
                val episodeNumber = obj.optInt("episode_num", index + 1)
                val title = obj.optCleanString("title") ?: "S${seasonNumber}E${episodeNumber}"
                val info = obj.optJSONObject("info") ?: JSONObject()
                items.add(
                    IptvItem(
                        id = items.size.toLong(),
                        streamId = episodeId,
                        title = "S${seasonNumber}E${episodeNumber} • $title",
                        description = info.optCleanString("plot") ?: obj.optCleanString("plot") ?: series.description,
                        categoryId = series.categoryId,
                        categoryName = series.categoryName,
                        coverUrl = info.optCleanString("movie_image") ?: series.coverUrl,
                        backdropUrl = series.backdropUrl,
                        streamUrl = buildStreamUrl("series", episodeId, extension),
                        containerExtension = extension,
                        rating = info.optCleanString("rating") ?: series.rating,
                        year = series.year,
                        contentType = ContentType.EPISODE,
                        metadataProvider = series.metadataProvider,
                        metadataId = series.metadataId,
                        traktSlug = series.traktSlug,
                        traktType = "episode",
                        imdbId = series.imdbId,
                        tmdbId = series.tmdbId,
                        genres = series.genres,
                        seasonNumber = seasonNumber,
                        episodeNumber = episodeNumber,
                        parentSeriesId = series.streamId,
                        parentSeriesTitle = series.title,
                        sourceLabel = "Xtream Episode",
                        addedAtMs = series.addedAtMs,
                        providerAccountId = providerAccountId
                    )
                )
            }
        }
        items.sortedWith(compareBy<IptvItem> { it.seasonNumber ?: 0 }.thenBy { it.episodeNumber ?: 0 })
    }


    suspend fun getShortEpg(channel: IptvItem, limit: Int = 6): List<EpgProgram> = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
        if (channel.contentType != ContentType.LIVE || channel.streamId.isBlank()) return@withContext emptyList()
        val response = requestJsonObject(
            "get_short_epg",
            mapOf("stream_id" to channel.streamId, "limit" to limit.coerceIn(1, 12).toString())
        )
        val array = response.optJSONArray("epg_listings") ?: response.optJSONArray("listings") ?: JSONArray()
        val programs = mutableListOf<EpgProgram>()
        for (index in 0 until array.length()) {
            val obj = array.optJSONObject(index) ?: continue
            val start = parseEpgTime(obj.optCleanString("start_timestamp") ?: obj.optCleanString("start") ?: obj.optCleanString("startTime"))
            val end = parseEpgTime(obj.optCleanString("stop_timestamp") ?: obj.optCleanString("end") ?: obj.optCleanString("endTime"))
            if (start <= 0L || end <= start) continue
            programs.add(
                EpgProgram(
                    channelStableKey = channel.stableKey,
                    channelTitle = channel.title,
                    programTitle = decodeMaybeBase64(obj.optCleanString("title") ?: obj.optCleanString("name") ?: "Program"),
                    description = decodeMaybeBase64(obj.optCleanString("description") ?: ""),
                    startTimeMs = start,
                    endTimeMs = end,
                    source = "Xtream"
                )
            )
        }
        programs
    }

    private fun parseEpgTime(raw: String?): Long {
        val numeric = raw?.toLongOrNull() ?: return 0L
        return if (numeric > 9_999_999_999L) numeric else numeric * 1000L
    }

    private fun decodeMaybeBase64(value: String): String {
        if (value.isBlank()) return value
        return runCatching {
            val decoded = android.util.Base64.decode(value, android.util.Base64.DEFAULT).toString(Charsets.UTF_8).trim()
            if (decoded.count { it.isLetterOrDigit() } >= 2) decoded else value
        }.getOrDefault(value)
    }

    private fun parseItem(index: Long, obj: JSONObject, contentType: ContentType, category: IptvCategory?): IptvItem {
        val streamId = when (contentType) {
            ContentType.SERIES -> obj.optCleanString("series_id") ?: ""
            else -> obj.optCleanString("stream_id") ?: ""
        }
        val extension = obj.optCleanString("container_extension") ?: "mp4"
        val streamUrl = when (contentType) {
            ContentType.LIVE -> buildStreamUrl("live", streamId, "ts")
            ContentType.MOVIE -> buildStreamUrl("movie", streamId, extension)
            ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.EPISODE, ContentType.ACTION -> null
        }
        val description = obj.optCleanString("plot")
            ?: obj.optCleanString("description")
            ?: listOfNotNull(obj.optCleanString("rating")?.let { "Rating: $it" }, obj.optCleanString("year")).joinToString(" • ")

        return IptvItem(
            id = index,
            streamId = streamId,
            title = obj.optCleanString("name") ?: obj.optCleanString("title") ?: "Untitled",
            description = description ?: "",
            categoryId = obj.optCleanString("category_id") ?: category?.categoryId,
            categoryName = category?.categoryName ?: obj.optCleanString("category_name"),
            coverUrl = obj.optCleanString("stream_icon") ?: obj.optCleanString("cover") ?: obj.optCleanString("cover_big"),
            backdropUrl = obj.optJSONArray("backdrop_path")?.optString(0) ?: obj.optCleanString("cover_big") ?: obj.optCleanString("cover"),
            streamUrl = streamUrl,
            containerExtension = extension,
            rating = obj.optCleanString("rating"),
            year = obj.optCleanString("year") ?: obj.optCleanString("releaseDate"),
            contentType = contentType,
            sourceLabel = "Xtream",
            addedAtMs = parseAddedAtMs(obj),
            providerAccountId = providerAccountId
        )
    }

    private fun parseAddedAtMs(obj: JSONObject): Long {
        val raw = obj.optCleanString("added")
            ?: obj.optCleanString("added_at")
            ?: obj.optCleanString("last_modified")
            ?: return 0L
        val numeric = raw.toLongOrNull() ?: return 0L
        return if (numeric > 9_999_999_999L) numeric else numeric * 1000L
    }

    private fun buildStreamUrl(kind: String, streamId: String, extension: String): String {
        return "${credentials.serverUrl.trimEnd('/')}/$kind/${credentials.username}/${credentials.password}/$streamId.$extension"
    }

    private fun buildApiUrl(action: String?, params: Map<String, String> = emptyMap()): String {
        val builder = credentials.serverUrl.trimEnd('/').plus("/player_api.php").toHttpUrl().newBuilder()
            .addQueryParameter("username", credentials.username)
            .addQueryParameter("password", credentials.password)
        if (!action.isNullOrBlank()) builder.addQueryParameter("action", action)
        params.forEach { (key, value) -> builder.addQueryParameter(key, value) }
        return builder.build().toString()
    }

    private fun execute(url: String, retryCount: Int = 0): String {
        if (url.startsWith("http://", ignoreCase = true)) {
            runCatching { return executeRawHttp(url) }
                .onFailure { Log.w(TAG, "Lenient raw HTTP read failed; falling back to OkHttp for ${redactUrl(url)}: ${it.message}") }
        }

        val request = Request.Builder()
            .url(url)
            .header("User-Agent", USER_AGENT)
            .header("Accept", "application/json")
            .header("Accept-Encoding", "identity") // Disable transparent GZIP to avoid corruption errors
            .header("Connection", "close")
            .get()
            .build()
        
        try {
            client.newCall(request).execute().use { response ->
                if (!response.isSuccessful) {
                    val errorMsg = "IPTV server returned HTTP ${response.code} for URL: ${redactUrl(url)}"
                    Log.e(TAG, errorMsg)
                    
                    if (response.code >= 500 && retryCount < 2) {
                        Log.w(TAG, "Retrying request due to server error ${response.code} (attempt ${retryCount + 1})")
                        Thread.sleep(1000L * (retryCount + 1))
                        return execute(url, retryCount + 1)
                    }

                    Log.e(TAG, "Response Headers: ${response.headers}")
                    val bodyPreview = try { response.peekBody(1024).string() } catch (e: Exception) { "unavailable" }
                    Log.e(TAG, "Response Body (first 1024 bytes): $bodyPreview")
                    error(errorMsg)
                }
                return response.body?.string() ?: error("Empty IPTV server response")
            }
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            if (retryCount < 2) {
                Log.w(TAG, "Retrying request due to exception: ${e.message} (attempt ${retryCount + 1})")
                Thread.sleep(1000L * (retryCount + 1))
                return execute(url, retryCount + 1)
            }
            if (shouldUseRawHttpFallback(url, e)) {
                Log.w(TAG, "Using lenient raw HTTP fallback for malformed IPTV response: ${redactUrl(url)}")
                return executeRawHttp(url)
            }
            Log.e(TAG, "Error executing request to ${redactUrl(url)} after $retryCount retries", e)
            throw e
        }
    }

    private fun shouldUseRawHttpFallback(url: String, error: Exception): Boolean {
        val message = error.message.orEmpty()
        return url.startsWith("http://", ignoreCase = true) &&
            (error is ProtocolException ||
                message.contains("chunk", ignoreCase = true) ||
                message.contains("unexpected end of stream", ignoreCase = true) ||
                message.contains("Expected leading", ignoreCase = true))
    }

    private fun executeRawHttp(url: String): String {
        val parsed = URL(url)
        val host = parsed.host
        val port = if (parsed.port != -1) parsed.port else 80
        val path = parsed.file.ifBlank { "/" }
        val request = buildString {
            append("GET ").append(path).append(" HTTP/1.1\r\n")
            append("Host: ").append(host).append("\r\n")
            append("User-Agent: ").append(USER_AGENT).append("\r\n")
            append("Accept: application/json\r\n")
            append("Accept-Encoding: identity\r\n")
            append("Connection: close\r\n\r\n")
        }

        Socket(host, port).use { socket ->
            socket.soTimeout = 60_000
            socket.getOutputStream().write(request.toByteArray(Charsets.UTF_8))
            val raw = ByteArrayOutputStream()
            val buffer = ByteArray(16 * 1024)
            val input = socket.getInputStream()
            while (true) {
                val read = input.read(buffer)
                if (read == -1) break
                raw.write(buffer, 0, read)
            }
            val response = raw.toString(Charsets.UTF_8.name())
            val headerEnd = response.indexOf("\r\n\r\n")
            if (headerEnd == -1) error("Malformed IPTV server response")

            val headers = response.substring(0, headerEnd)
            val body = response.substring(headerEnd + 4)
            val status = headers.lineSequence().firstOrNull().orEmpty()
            if (!status.contains(" 200 ")) error("IPTV server returned $status for URL: ${redactUrl(url)}")

            return if (headers.contains("Transfer-Encoding: chunked", ignoreCase = true)) {
                decodeChunkedLeniently(body)
            } else {
                trimToJson(body)
            }
        }
    }

    private fun decodeChunkedLeniently(rawBody: String): String {
        if (rawBody.trimStart().startsWith("[") || rawBody.trimStart().startsWith("{")) return trimToJson(rawBody)

        val decoded = StringBuilder()
        var position = 0
        while (position < rawBody.length) {
            while (position < rawBody.length && (rawBody[position] == '\r' || rawBody[position] == '\n')) position++
            val lineEnd = rawBody.indexOf("\r\n", position)
            if (lineEnd == -1) break
            val sizeLine = rawBody.substring(position, lineEnd).substringBefore(";").trim()
            val size = sizeLine.toIntOrNull(16)
            if (size == null) return trimToJson(decoded.append(rawBody.substring(position)).toString())
            position = lineEnd + 2
            if (size == 0) break
            val end = (position + size).coerceAtMost(rawBody.length)
            decoded.append(rawBody, position, end)
            position = end
        }
        return trimToJson(decoded.toString())
    }

    private fun trimToJson(value: String): String {
        val startArray = value.indexOf('[').takeIf { it >= 0 } ?: Int.MAX_VALUE
        val startObject = value.indexOf('{').takeIf { it >= 0 } ?: Int.MAX_VALUE
        val start = minOf(startArray, startObject)
        return if (start == Int.MAX_VALUE) value.trim() else value.substring(start).trim()
    }

    private fun redactUrl(url: String): String {
        return runCatching {
            val parsed = url.toHttpUrl()
            parsed.newBuilder()
                .setQueryParameter("username", "***")
                .setQueryParameter("password", "***")
                .build()
                .toString()
        }.getOrDefault(url)
    }

    private fun requestJsonObject(action: String?, params: Map<String, String> = emptyMap()): JSONObject {
        return JSONObject(execute(buildApiUrl(action, params)))
    }

    private fun requestJsonArray(action: String, params: Map<String, String> = emptyMap()): JSONArray {
        return JSONArray(execute(buildApiUrl(action, params)))
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/sync/CatalogRefreshScheduler.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.sync

import android.content.Context
import androidx.work.Constraints
import androidx.work.ExistingPeriodicWorkPolicy
import androidx.work.NetworkType
import androidx.work.PeriodicWorkRequestBuilder
import androidx.work.WorkManager
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit

object CatalogRefreshScheduler {
    private const val UNIQUE_PERIODIC_WORK = "catalog_refresh_periodic"

    fun schedule(context: Context) {
        val intervalDays = CredentialStore(context).getSyncIntervalDays().coerceIn(1, 30)
        val constraints = Constraints.Builder()
            .setRequiredNetworkType(NetworkType.CONNECTED)
            .build()
        val request = PeriodicWorkRequestBuilder<CatalogRefreshWorker>(intervalDays.toLong(), TimeUnit.DAYS)
            .setConstraints(constraints)
            .build()
        WorkManager.getInstance(context.applicationContext).enqueueUniquePeriodicWork(
            UNIQUE_PERIODIC_WORK,
            ExistingPeriodicWorkPolicy.UPDATE,
            request
        )
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/sync/CatalogRefreshWorker.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.sync

import android.content.Context
import androidx.work.CoroutineWorker
import androidx.work.Data
import androidx.work.ExistingWorkPolicy
import androidx.work.OneTimeWorkRequestBuilder
import androidx.work.WorkManager
import androidx.work.WorkerParameters
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CategorySyncStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CleanCatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCategory
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient

class CatalogRefreshWorker(
    appContext: Context,
    workerParams: WorkerParameters
) : CoroutineWorker(appContext, workerParams) {
    override suspend fun doWork(): Result {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(applicationContext).get() ?: return Result.failure(progressData("No IPTV login saved."))
        val profile = ProfileStore(applicationContext).getCurrentProfile()
        val catalogStore = CatalogStore(applicationContext)
        val categorySyncStore = CategorySyncStore(applicationContext)
        val cleanCatalogStore = CleanCatalogStore(applicationContext)
        val apiClient = XtreamApiClient(credentials)
        val aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken)

        return runCatching {
            updateProgress("Starting catalog refresh...")
            val counts = mutableMapOf<ContentType, Int>()
            for (contentType in listOf(ContentType.MOVIE, ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.LIVE)) {
                val label = label(contentType)
                updateProgress("Refreshing $label...")
                catalogStore.markRefreshAttempt(contentType)
                val items = loadCleanXtream(apiClient, categorySyncStore, cleanCatalogStore, contentType, profile.isKidsProfile) { message ->
                    updateProgress(message)
                }
                catalogStore.replaceType(contentType, items)
                catalogStore.markSynced(contentType)
                val savedCount = catalogStore.countItems(contentType)
                counts[contentType] = savedCount
                updateProgress("Saved $savedCount $label.")
                if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured() && items.isNotEmpty()) {
                    updateProgress("Syncing $savedCount $label to server...")
                    runCatching {
                        kotlinx.coroutines.withTimeout(30000L) {
                            aiSyncClient.postCatalogMetadata(items)
                        }
                    }.onFailure { error ->
                        updateProgress("Server sync skipped: ${error.message}")
                    }
                }
            }
            updateProgress("Catalog refreshed.")
            Result.success(
                Data.Builder()
                    .putString(KEY_MESSAGE, "Catalog refreshed.")
                    .putInt(KEY_MOVIES, counts[ContentType.MOVIE] ?: 0)
                    .putInt(KEY_SERIES, counts[ContentType.SERIES] ?: 0)
                    .putInt(KEY_LIVE, counts[ContentType.LIVE] ?: 0)
                    .build()
            )
        }.getOrElse { error ->
            Result.failure(progressData(error.message ?: "Catalog refresh failed."))
        }
    }

    private suspend fun updateProgress(message: String) {
        if (isStopped) return
        runCatching { setProgress(progressData(message)) }
    }

    private suspend fun loadCleanXtream(
        apiClient: XtreamApiClient,
        categorySyncStore: CategorySyncStore,
        cleanCatalogStore: CleanCatalogStore,
        contentType: ContentType,
        isKids: Boolean,
        onProgress: suspend (String) -> Unit
    ): List<IptvItem> {
        val label = label(contentType)
        onProgress("Loading $label categories...")
        val enabledCategories = categorySyncStore.getEnabledCategoryIds(contentType)
        val categoriesConfigured = categorySyncStore.isConfigured(contentType)
        val categories = runCatching { apiClient.getCategories(contentType) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
        val categoriesById = categories.associateBy { it.categoryId }

        if (categoriesConfigured && enabledCategories.isEmpty()) return emptyList()
        val rawItems = if (enabledCategories.isNotEmpty()) {
            val allItems = mutableListOf<IptvItem>()
            val categoryIds = enabledCategories.toList()
            for (index in categoryIds.indices) {
                if (isStopped) break
                val catId = categoryIds[index]
                val category = categoriesById[catId] ?: IptvCategory(catId, "Category $catId", contentType)
                onProgress("Refreshing $label: ${category.categoryName} (${index + 1}/${categoryIds.size})")
                val catItems = runCatching { 
                    apiClient.getItems(contentType, category, limit = null)
                }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
                allItems.addAll(catItems)
                onProgress("Refreshing $label: ${allItems.size} items loaded...")
            }
            allItems
        } else {
            onProgress("Refreshing $label: Downloading all (this may take a while)...")
            runCatching { apiClient.getItems(contentType, limit = null) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
        }

        return rawItems.map { item ->
            if (!item.categoryName.isNullOrBlank() || item.categoryId.isNullOrBlank()) item else item.copy(categoryName = categoriesById[item.categoryId]?.categoryName)
        }.filter { item ->
            !cleanCatalogStore.shouldHide(item.title, item.categoryName) && (!isKids || cleanCatalogStore.isKidsSafe(item.categoryName, item.title))
        }
    }

    private fun label(contentType: ContentType): String {
        return when (contentType) {
            ContentType.MOVIE -> "movies"
            ContentType.SERIES -> "series"
            ContentType.LIVE -> "live channels"
            ContentType.EPISODE -> "episodes"
            ContentType.ACTION -> "items"
        }
    }

    private fun progressData(message: String): Data = Data.Builder().putString(KEY_MESSAGE, message).build()

    companion object {
        const val UNIQUE_WORK_NAME = "catalog_refresh"
        const val KEY_MESSAGE = "message"
        const val KEY_MOVIES = "movies"
        const val KEY_SERIES = "series"
        const val KEY_LIVE = "live"

        fun enqueue(context: Context) {
            val request = OneTimeWorkRequestBuilder<CatalogRefreshWorker>().build()
            WorkManager.getInstance(context.applicationContext)
                .enqueueUniqueWork(UNIQUE_WORK_NAME, ExistingWorkPolicy.REPLACE, request)
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/sync/SyncOutboxStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.sync

import android.content.Context
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.io.File
import java.util.UUID

class SyncOutboxStore(context: Context) {
    private val file = File(context.applicationContext.filesDir, "sync_outbox.jsonl")

    fun enqueue(kind: String, payload: JSONObject): String = synchronized(LOCK) {
        val eventId = payload.optString("eventId").ifBlank { UUID.randomUUID().toString() }
        payload.put("eventId", eventId)
        val record = Record(eventId, kind, payload.toString(), System.currentTimeMillis(), 0)
        val records = readAll().filterNot { it.id == eventId } + record
        writeAll(records.takeLast(MAX_EVENTS))
        eventId
    }

    fun pending(limit: Int = 50): List<Record> = synchronized(LOCK) {
        readAll().sortedBy { it.createdAt }.take(limit.coerceIn(1, 200))
    }

    fun markComplete(id: String) = synchronized(LOCK) {
        writeAll(readAll().filterNot { it.id == id })
    }

    fun markFailed(id: String) = synchronized(LOCK) {
        writeAll(readAll().map { if (it.id == id) it.copy(attempts = it.attempts + 1) else it })
    }

    fun size(): Int = synchronized(LOCK) { readAll().size }

    private fun readAll(): List<Record> {
        if (!file.exists()) return emptyList()
        return file.useLines { lines ->
            lines.mapNotNull { line ->
                runCatching {
                    val obj = JSONObject(line)
                    Record(
                        id = obj.getString("id"),
                        kind = obj.getString("kind"),
                        payload = obj.getString("payload"),
                        createdAt = obj.optLong("createdAt", 0L),
                        attempts = obj.optInt("attempts", 0)
                    )
                }.getOrNull()
            }.toList()
        }
    }

    private fun writeAll(records: List<Record>) {
        val temp = File(file.parentFile, "${file.name}.tmp")
        temp.bufferedWriter().use { writer ->
            records.forEach { record ->
                writer.append(
                    JSONObject()
                        .put("id", record.id)
                        .put("kind", record.kind)
                        .put("payload", record.payload)
                        .put("createdAt", record.createdAt)
                        .put("attempts", record.attempts)
                        .toString()
                )
                writer.newLine()
            }
        }
        if (!temp.renameTo(file)) {
            temp.copyTo(file, overwrite = true)
            temp.delete()
        }
    }

    data class Record(
        val id: String,
        val kind: String,
        val payload: String,
        val createdAt: Long,
        val attempts: Int
    )

    companion object {
        const val KIND_WATCH_EVENT = "watch_event"
        const val KIND_WATCH_SNAPSHOT = "watch_snapshot"
        private const val MAX_EVENTS = 1_000
        private val LOCK = Any()
    }
}

class SyncOutboxWorker(

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/admin/AdminDashboardActivity.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.admin

import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.ScrollView
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import org.json.JSONObject

class AdminDashboardActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var container: LinearLayout

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        val scroll = ScrollView(this).apply { setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background); isFillViewport = true }
        container = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 36), TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 36))
        }
        scroll.addView(container)
        setContentView(scroll)
        renderLoading()
        loadAdminSummary()
    }

    override fun onDestroy() { scope.cancel(); super.onDestroy() }

    private fun renderLoading() {
        container.removeAllViews()
        container.addView(title("Admin Dashboard"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help("Loading server health, usage, sessions, and maintenance data\u2026"), TvUi.matchWrap())
    }

    private fun loadAdminSummary() {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(this).getAny()
        val client = AiSyncClient(credentials?.syncServerUrl, credentials?.syncServerUsername, credentials?.syncServerPassword, credentials?.syncServerToken)
        if (credentials == null || !client.isConfigured()) {
            container.addView(help("Configure the AI server and pair this device first."), TvUi.matchWrap())
            return
        }
        scope.launch {
            val result = client.getAdminSummary()
            val json = result.getOrNull()
            if (json == null) {
                Toast.makeText(this@AdminDashboardActivity, result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "Admin summary failed", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                container.addView(help("Admin summary failed. This account may not be an admin."), TvUi.matchWrap())
                return@launch
            }
            renderSummary(json)
        }
    }

    private fun renderSummary(json: JSONObject) {
        container.removeAllViews()
        container.addView(title("Admin Dashboard"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Refresh") { renderLoading(); loadAdminSummary() }, fieldParams())
        val sections = listOf("overview", "users", "devices", "catalog", "ai", "social", "sync", "security")
        sections.forEach { key ->
            val value = json.optJSONObject(key)
            if (value != null) addJsonPanel(key.replaceFirstChar(Char::titlecase), value)
        }
    }

    private fun addJsonPanel(label: String, obj: JSONObject) {
        val panel = TvUi.verticalPanel(this)
        panel.addView(section(label), TvUi.matchWrap())
        val text = obj.toString(2)
        panel.addView(help(text), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(panel, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this))
    }

    private fun fieldParams(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply { setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 10)) }
    private fun title(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 34f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); gravity = Gravity.START; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 12)) }
    private fun section(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 20f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 8), 0, TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 8)) }
    private fun help(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(0xFFDDDDDD.toInt()); textSize = 14f; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@AdminDashboardActivity, 8)); setTextIsSelectable(true) }
}
