// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/ai/AiModesActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.ai

import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.ScrollView
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogInsightEngine
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class AiModesActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var container: LinearLayout
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var credentialStore: CredentialStore
    private lateinit var profileStore: ProfileStore

    private val modes = listOf(
        "quality" to "Best available quality",
        "short" to "Something short",
        "family" to "Family safe",
        "hidden" to "Hidden gems",
        "new" to "New to my library",
        "comfort" to "Comfort viewing",
        "action" to "High action"
    )

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(this)
        credentialStore = CredentialStore(this)
        profileStore = ProfileStore(this)
        val scroll = ScrollView(this).apply { setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background); isFillViewport = true }
        container = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 36), TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 36))
        }
        scroll.addView(container)
        setContentView(scroll)
        renderHome()
    }

    override fun onDestroy() { scope.cancel(); super.onDestroy() }

    private fun renderHome() {
        container.removeAllViews()
        container.addView(title("AI Recommendation Modes"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help("Recommendations are candidate-first: the app starts from your playable local catalog, then asks the server AI to rerank when available."), TvUi.matchWrap())
        modes.forEach { (mode, label) -> container.addView(TvUi.button(this, label) { loadMode(mode, label) }, fieldParams()) }
    }

    private fun loadMode(mode: String, label: String) {
        container.removeAllViews()
        container.addView(title(label), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Back to modes") { renderHome() }, fieldParams())
        val localItems = CatalogInsightEngine.smartPicks(catalogStore.getAllItems(), mode, 40)
        val credentials = credentialStore.getAny()
        val client = AiSyncClient(credentials?.syncServerUrl, credentials?.syncServerUsername, credentials?.syncServerPassword, credentials?.syncServerToken)
        if (credentials != null && client.isConfigured()) {
            Toast.makeText(this, "Loading AI rerank\u2026", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            scope.launch {
                val serverItems = client.getRecommendations(
                    profileId = ProfileStore(this@AiModesActivity).getCurrentProfile().id,
                    mood = if (mode in listOf("action", "family", "short")) mode else "any",
                    contentType = "any",
                    query = "Recommendation mode: $label. Only choose from available local catalog candidates.",
                    limit = 30
                ).getOrDefault(emptyList())
                val merged = if (serverItems.isNotEmpty()) serverItems else localItems
                renderItems(label, merged, source = if (serverItems.isNotEmpty()) "Server AI rerank" else "Local fallback")
            }
        } else {
            renderItems(label, localItems, source = "Local fallback")
        }
    }

    private fun renderItems(label: String, items: List<IptvItem>, source: String) {
        container.removeAllViews()
        container.addView(title(label), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help(source), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Back to modes") { renderHome() }, fieldParams())
        if (items.isEmpty()) container.addView(help("No playable items matched this mode."), TvUi.matchWrap())
        items.forEach { item ->
            val panel = TvUi.verticalPanel(this)
            panel.addView(section(item.title), TvUi.matchWrap())
            panel.addView(help(listOfNotNull(item.year, item.rating?.let { "\u2605 $it" }, item.sourceLabel).joinToString(" \u2022 ")), TvUi.matchWrap())
            panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Open details") { openDetails(item) }, fieldParams())
            panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Less like this") { sendFeedback(item, "less_like_this") }, fieldParams())
            container.addView(panel, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this))
        }
    }

    private fun sendFeedback(item: IptvItem, action: String) {
        val credentials = credentialStore.getAny() ?: return
        val client = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) return
        scope.launch {
            client.sendRecommendationFeedback(profileStore.getCurrentProfile().id, item.stableKey, action, "ai_modes")
            Toast.makeText(this@AiModesActivity, "Feedback saved.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    private fun openDetails(item: IptvItem) = startActivity(Intent(this, DetailsActivity::class.java).putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item))
    private fun fieldParams(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply { setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 10)) }
    private fun title(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 34f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); gravity = Gravity.START; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 12)) }
    private fun section(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 20f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 8), 0, TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 8)) }
    private fun help(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(0xFFDDDDDD.toInt()); textSize = 14f; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@AiModesActivity, 8)) }
}

================================================================================
// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/browse/CategoryGridFragment.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.browse

import android.app.AlertDialog
import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Color
import android.graphics.Typeface
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.view.LayoutInflater
import android.view.View
import android.view.ViewGroup
import android.widget.EditText
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.core.content.ContextCompat
import androidx.lifecycle.lifecycleScope
import androidx.leanback.app.VerticalGridSupportFragment
import androidx.leanback.widget.ArrayObjectAdapter
import androidx.leanback.widget.OnItemViewClickedListener
import androidx.leanback.widget.VerticalGridPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher.isDisplayPlayable
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.WatchRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.CardPresenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.Job
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext
import kotlinx.coroutines.yield

class CategoryGridFragment : VerticalGridSupportFragment(), androidx.leanback.app.BrowseSupportFragment.MainFragmentAdapterProvider {
    private lateinit var mAdapter: ArrayObjectAdapter
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var watchRepository: WatchRepository
    private lateinit var credentialStore: CredentialStore
    private lateinit var profileStore: ProfileStore
    private lateinit var aiSyncClient: AiSyncClient
    private var filterSortButton: TextView? = null
    private var activeFiltersView: TextView? = null
    private var resultCountView: TextView? = null
    
    private var currentMode: String? = null
    private var selectedCategory: String? = null
    private var textFilter = ""
    private var sortMode = SortMode.NAME
    private var isLoaded = false
    private var refreshJob: Job? = null

    private val mMainFragmentAdapter = object : androidx.leanback.app.BrowseSupportFragment.MainFragmentAdapter<CategoryGridFragment>(this) {
        override fun setExpand(expand: Boolean) {
            super.setExpand(expand)
            // expand is true when the main fragment is expanded (sidebar is closed/focus moved to grid)
            if (expand && !isLoaded) {
                refresh()
            }
        }
    }

    override fun getMainFragmentAdapter(): androidx.leanback.app.BrowseSupportFragment.MainFragmentAdapter<*> {
        return mMainFragmentAdapter
    }

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(requireContext())
        watchRepository = WatchRepository(requireContext())
        credentialStore = CredentialStore(requireContext())
        profileStore = ProfileStore(requireContext())
        val credentials = credentialStore.get()
        aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(credentials?.syncServerUrl, credentials?.syncServerUsername, credentials?.syncServerPassword, credentials?.syncServerToken)

        currentMode = arguments?.getString(LibraryBrowseActivity.EXTRA_MODE)
        selectedCategory = arguments?.getString(EXTRA_TITLE)
        
        // Remove title to avoid overlap as requested
        title = null

        val gridPresenter = VerticalGridPresenter()
        gridPresenter.numberOfColumns = calculateColumnCount()
        setGridPresenter(gridPresenter)

        val itemPresenter = CardPresenter(
            if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_LIVE) CardPresenter.CardStyle.LANDSCAPE else CardPresenter.CardStyle.POSTER,
            ::showItemActions
        )
        mAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(itemPresenter)
        adapter = mAdapter
        mAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = "Opening library...", sourceLabel = "Items will continue loading in the background.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))

        onItemViewClickedListener = OnItemViewClickedListener { _, item, _, _ ->
            if (item is IptvItem) {
                if (item.contentType == ContentType.ACTION) {
                    return@OnItemViewClickedListener
                } else {
                    val intent = Intent(requireContext(), DetailsActivity::class.java)
                    intent.putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item)
                    startActivity(intent)
                }
            }
        }

        // We don't call refresh() here anymore. 
        // It will be called by MainFragmentAdapter when the user clicks/navigates into the grid.
    }

    override fun onViewCreated(view: View, savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onViewCreated(view, savedInstanceState)
        view.post {
            if (!isLoaded && refreshJob == null) refresh()
        }
    }

    override fun onCreateView(inflater: LayoutInflater, container: ViewGroup?, savedInstanceState: Bundle?): View {
        val gridView = super.onCreateView(inflater, container, savedInstanceState)
        val context = requireContext()
        val root = LinearLayout(context).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background)
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(context, 36), TvUi.dp(context, 24), TvUi.dp(context, 36), 0)
        }

        val controls = LinearLayout(context).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
            setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(context, 14))
        }

        val categoryTitle = TextView(context).apply {
            text = selectedCategory?.substringBefore(" (") ?: "All Content"
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            textSize = 22f
            typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
            maxLines = 1
        }
        activeFiltersView = TextView(context).apply {
            setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.tile_text_secondary))
            textSize = 14f
            maxLines = 1
            setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(context, 4), 0, 0)
        }
        val titleStack = LinearLayout(context).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            addView(categoryTitle, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            addView(activeFiltersView, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
        }
        resultCountView = TextView(context).apply {
            setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.tile_text_secondary))
            textSize = 15f
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL or Gravity.END
        }
        filterSortButton = controlButton("Filter & Sort").apply { setOnClickListener { showFilterSortDialog() } }

        controls.addView(titleStack, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1f))
        controls.addView(resultCountView, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(TvUi.dp(context, 190), TvUi.dp(context, 64)).apply {
            setMargins(0, 0, TvUi.dp(context, 14), 0)
        })
        controls.addView(filterSortButton, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(TvUi.dp(context, 260), TvUi.dp(context, 64)))
        root.addView(controls, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
        root.addView(gridView, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, 0, 1f))
        updateControls()
        return root
    }

    fun showControlsDialog() {
        showFilterSortDialog()
    }

    private fun showFilterSortDialog() {
        val context = requireContext()
        var pendingSort = sortMode
        val panel = LinearLayout(context).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(context, 22), TvUi.dp(context, 8), TvUi.dp(context, 22), 0)
        }
        val input = TvUi.input(context, "Search title or description").apply {
            setSingleLine(true)
            setText(textFilter)
        }
        panel.addView(TvUi.helperText(context, "Search within this category, then choose how results should be ordered."))
        panel.addView(input, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
        panel.addView(TvUi.sectionTitle(context, "Sort"))

        SortMode.values().forEach { mode ->
            val option = controlButton(if (mode == sortMode) "${mode.label} selected" else mode.label).apply {
                gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
                setPadding(TvUi.dp(context, 18), 0, TvUi.dp(context, 18), 0)
                setOnClickListener {
                    pendingSort = mode
                    for (index in 3 until panel.childCount) {
                        val child = panel.getChildAt(index) as? TextView
                        val childMode = SortMode.values().getOrNull(index - 3)
                        child?.text = if (childMode == pendingSort) "${childMode.label} selected" else childMode?.label.orEmpty()
                    }
                }
            }
            panel.addView(option, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, 58).apply {
                setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(context, 8))
            })
        }

        AlertDialog.Builder(context)
            .setTitle("Filter & Sort")
            .setView(panel)
            .setPositiveButton("Apply") { _, _ ->
                textFilter = input.text.toString().trim()
                sortMode = pendingSort
                refresh()
            }
            .setNeutralButton("Clear") { _, _ ->
                textFilter = ""
                sortMode = SortMode.NAME
                refresh()
            }
            .setNegativeButton(android.R.string.cancel, null)
            .show()
    }

    private fun refresh() {
        refreshJob?.cancel()
        refreshJob = lifecycleScope.launch {
            showLoadingItem("Loading items...")
            loadItemsInBackground()
        }
    }

    private suspend fun loadItemsInBackground() {
        if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_AI_PICKS) {
            refreshAiPicks()
            return
        }
        if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST || currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_RECENT) {
            refreshServerBackedWatchItems()
            return
        }
        val base = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
            when (currentMode) {
                LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_RECENT -> watchRepository.getHistory()
                LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST -> watchRepository.getWatchlist()
                LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_LIVE -> catalogItemsForSelectedCategory(ContentType.LIVE)
                LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_SHOWS -> catalogItemsForSelectedCategory(ContentType.SERIES)
                else -> catalogItemsForSelectedCategory(ContentType.MOVIE)
            }
        }
        
        val sorted = withContext(Dispatchers.Default) {
            val isAllContent = selectedCategory?.startsWith("All ") == true || selectedCategory == null
            val selectedName = selectedCategory?.substringBefore(" (").orEmpty()
            val filtered = base.filter { item ->
                val specialMatch = when (selectedName) {
                    "Recently Added" -> item.addedAtMs > 0L
                    "4K / UHD" -> isUltraHd(item)
                    "Playable Only" -> item.isDisplayPlayable()
                    else -> null
                }
                val catMatch = specialMatch ?: (isAllContent || item.categoryName?.equals(selectedName, ignoreCase = true) == true)
                val textMatch = textFilter.isBlank() || item.title.contains(textFilter, ignoreCase = true) || item.description.contains(textFilter, ignoreCase = true)
                catMatch && textMatch
            }

            when (sortMode) {
                SortMode.NAME -> filtered.sortedBy { it.title.lowercase() }
                SortMode.RATING -> filtered.sortedByDescending { it.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0 }
                SortMode.YEAR -> filtered.sortedByDescending { it.year?.toIntOrNull() ?: 0 }
                SortMode.ADDED -> filtered.sortedByDescending { it.addedAtMs }
            }
        }

        if (sorted.isEmpty()) {
            mAdapter.clear()
            val message = if (textFilter.isBlank()) {
                "No items in this category"
            } else {
                "No results for \"$textFilter\""
            }
            mAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = message, sourceLabel = "Try clearing filters or choosing another category.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
        } else {
            showItemsInChunks(sorted)
        }
        updateControls(sorted.size)
        isLoaded = true
    }

    private suspend fun refreshServerBackedWatchItems() {
        val local = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
            when (currentMode) {
                LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST -> watchRepository.matchWatchlistItems(catalogStore.getAllItems())
                else -> watchRepository.getHistory()
            }
        }
        val credentials = credentialStore.get()
        val base = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
            if (credentials != null && aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
                val kind = if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST) "watchlist" else "history"
                aiSyncClient.getWatchItems(serverProfileId(credentials), kind).getOrDefault(local)
            } else {
                local
            }
        }
        val matchedBase = if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST) {
            val catalog = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { catalogStore.getAllItems() }
            withContext(Dispatchers.Default) {
                base.mapNotNull { item ->
                    if (item.isDisplayPlayable()) item else CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(catalog, item)?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(item, it) }
                }
            }
        } else {
            base.filter { it.isDisplayPlayable() }
        }
        showFilteredItems(matchedBase, if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST) "No watchlist items found" else "No history found")
    }

    private suspend fun refreshAiPicks() {
        val credentials = credentialStore.get()
        if (credentials == null || !aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            showItems(emptyList(), "AI server is not configured")
            return
        }
        val localCatalog = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { catalogStore.getAllItems() }
        val recommendations = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
            aiSyncClient.getRecommendations(serverProfileId(credentials)).getOrDefault(emptyList())
        }
        val items = withContext(Dispatchers.Default) {
            recommendations.map { recommendation ->
                CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(localCatalog, recommendation)
                    ?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(recommendation, it).copy(sourceLabel = recommendation.sourceLabel ?: "AI Pick - Playable") }
                    ?: recommendation.copy(sourceLabel = recommendation.sourceLabel ?: "AI Pick - Not in catalog")
            }.distinctBy { it.stableKey }
        }
        showItems(items, "No AI picks yet")
    }

    private suspend fun showItems(items: List<IptvItem>, emptyTitle: String) {
        val isAllContent = selectedCategory?.startsWith("All AI Picks") == true || selectedCategory == null
        val selectedType = selectedCategory?.substringBefore(" (")
        val filtered = items.filter { item ->
            val typeMatch = isAllContent || contentTypeLabel(item.contentType).equals(selectedType, ignoreCase = true)
            val textMatch = textFilter.isBlank() || item.title.contains(textFilter, ignoreCase = true) || item.description.contains(textFilter, ignoreCase = true)
            typeMatch && textMatch
        }
        if (filtered.isEmpty()) {
            mAdapter.clear()
            mAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = emptyTitle, sourceLabel = "Refresh catalog/watch data, then try AI Picks again.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
        } else {
            showItemsInChunks(filtered)
        }
        updateControls(filtered.size)
        isLoaded = true
    }

    private fun contentTypeLabel(contentType: ContentType): String {
        return contentType.name.lowercase().replaceFirstChar(Char::titlecase)
    }

    private suspend fun showFilteredItems(items: List<IptvItem>, emptyTitle: String) {
        val isAllContent = selectedCategory?.startsWith("All ") == true || selectedCategory == null
        val selectedName = selectedCategory?.substringBefore(" (")
        val filtered = items.filter { item ->
            val itemGroup = item.categoryName ?: item.contentType.name.lowercase().replaceFirstChar(Char::titlecase)
            val specialMatch = when (selectedName) {
                "Recently Added" -> item.addedAtMs > 0L
                "4K / UHD" -> isUltraHd(item)
                "Playable Only" -> item.isDisplayPlayable()
                else -> null
            }
            val catMatch = specialMatch ?: (isAllContent || itemGroup.equals(selectedName, ignoreCase = true))
            val textMatch = textFilter.isBlank() || item.title.contains(textFilter, ignoreCase = true) || item.description.contains(textFilter, ignoreCase = true)
            catMatch && textMatch
        }
        val sorted = when (sortMode) {
            SortMode.NAME -> filtered.sortedBy { it.title.lowercase() }
            SortMode.RATING -> filtered.sortedByDescending { it.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0 }
            SortMode.YEAR -> filtered.sortedByDescending { it.year?.toIntOrNull() ?: 0 }
            SortMode.ADDED -> filtered.sortedByDescending { it.addedAtMs }
        }
        if (sorted.isEmpty()) {
            mAdapter.clear()
            mAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = emptyTitle, sourceLabel = "Sync this profile or add items on the AI server dashboard.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
        } else {
            showItemsInChunks(sorted)
        }
        updateControls(sorted.size)
        isLoaded = true
    }

    private suspend fun showItemsInChunks(items: List<IptvItem>) {
        mAdapter.clear()
        val firstBatch = items.take(INITIAL_RENDER_LIMIT)
        mAdapter.addAll(0, firstBatch)
        updateControls(firstBatch.size)
        if (items.size <= INITIAL_RENDER_LIMIT) return
        items.drop(INITIAL_RENDER_LIMIT).chunked(BACKGROUND_RENDER_CHUNK_SIZE).forEach { chunk ->
            yield()
            mAdapter.addAll(mAdapter.size(), chunk)
            updateControls(mAdapter.size())
        }
    }

    private fun showItemActions(item: IptvItem) {
        if (item.contentType == ContentType.ACTION) return
        val options = arrayOf(
            if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) "Remove from Watchlist" else "Add to Watchlist",
            if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) "Clear Like" else "Like",
            if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) "Clear Dislike" else "Dislike",
            "Ignore in Catalogue"
        )
        AlertDialog.Builder(requireContext())
            .setTitle(item.title)
            .setItems(options) { _, which ->
                when (which) {
                    0 -> toggleWatchlist(item)
                    1 -> rateItem(item, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) 0 else 1)
                    2 -> rateItem(item, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) 0 else -1)
                    3 -> ignoreItem(item)
                }
            }
            .show()
    }

    private fun toggleWatchlist(item: IptvItem) {
        if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) {
            watchRepository.removeFromWatchlist(item)
            android.widget.Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Removed from watchlist", android.widget.Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST) {
                refresh()
            }
        } else {
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                val savedItem = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
                    watchRepository.addToWatchlist(item, catalogStore.getAllItems())
                }
                val message = if (savedItem.isPlayable && !item.isPlayable) "Added to watchlist and matched to stream" else "Added to watchlist"
                android.widget.Toast.makeText(requireContext(), message, android.widget.Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST) {
                    refresh()
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private fun rateItem(item: IptvItem, rating: Int) {
        watchRepository.setRating(item, rating)
        val credentials = credentialStore.get()
        if (credentials != null && aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            lifecycleScope.launch { aiSyncClient.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(credentials), item, rating = rating) }
        }
    }

    private fun ignoreItem(item: IptvItem) {
        catalogStore.ignoreItem(item)
        val credentials = credentialStore.get()
        if (credentials != null && aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            lifecycleScope.launch { aiSyncClient.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(credentials), item, ignored = true) }
        }
        refresh()
    }

    private fun serverProfileId(credentials: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials): String {
        val localProfileId = profileStore.getCurrentProfile().id
        val owner = credentials.syncServerUsername?.trim()?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: return localProfileId
        return "$owner:$localProfileId"
    }

    private fun controlButton(label: String): TextView {
        return TextView(requireContext()).apply {
            text = label
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            textSize = 16f
            typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            includeFontPadding = false
            TvUi.applyFocusableTile(this)
        }
    }

    private fun updateControls(resultCount: Int? = null) {
        filterSortButton?.text = if (textFilter.isBlank() && sortMode == SortMode.NAME) "Filter & Sort" else "Edit Filters"
        val filterLabel = if (textFilter.isBlank()) "No search filter" else "Search: $textFilter"
        activeFiltersView?.text = "$filterLabel  |  Sort: ${sortMode.label}"
        resultCountView?.text = resultCount?.let { "$it items" }.orEmpty()
    }

    private fun catalogItems(contentType: ContentType): List<IptvItem> {
        return catalogStore.getItems(contentType)
    }

    private fun catalogItemsForSelectedCategory(contentType: ContentType): List<IptvItem> {
        val selectedName = selectedCategory?.substringBefore(" (").orEmpty()
        val isAllContent = selectedCategory?.startsWith("All ") == true || selectedCategory == null
        val isSpecial = selectedName == "Recently Added" || selectedName == "4K / UHD" || selectedName == "Playable Only"
        return if (isAllContent || isSpecial) {
            catalogStore.getItems(contentType)
        } else {
            catalogStore.getItems(contentType, selectedName)
        }
    }

    private fun showLoadingItem(message: String) {
        mAdapter.clear()
        mAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = message, sourceLabel = "This will continue in the background.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
        updateControls()
    }

    private fun isUltraHd(item: IptvItem): Boolean {
        val text = listOf(item.title, item.categoryName.orEmpty(), item.sourceLabel.orEmpty()).joinToString(" ").lowercase()
        return text.contains("4k") || text.contains("uhd") || text.contains("2160")
    }

    private fun calculateColumnCount(): Int {
        val widthDp = resources.configuration.screenWidthDp
        val targetWidth = if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_LIVE) 300 else 220
        return (widthDp / targetWidth).coerceIn(if (currentMode == LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_LIVE) 3 else 4, 6)
    }

    private enum class SortMode(val label: String) {
        NAME("Name"),
        RATING("Rating"),
        YEAR("Year"),
        ADDED("Recently Added")
    }

    companion object {
        const val EXTRA_TITLE = "title"
        private const val ACTION_FILTER = "grid_filter"
        private const val ACTION_SORT = "grid_sort"
        private const val INITIAL_RENDER_LIMIT = 80
        private const val BACKGROUND_RENDER_CHUNK_SIZE = 80

        fun newInstance(mode: String?, title: String?): CategoryGridFragment {
            return CategoryGridFragment().apply {
                arguments = Bundle().apply {
                    putString(LibraryBrowseActivity.EXTRA_MODE, mode)
                    putString(EXTRA_TITLE, title)
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

================================================================================
// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/browse/LibraryBrowseActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.browse

import android.os.Bundle
import androidx.core.content.ContextCompat
import androidx.fragment.app.Fragment
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import androidx.lifecycle.lifecycleScope
import androidx.leanback.app.BrowseSupportFragment
import androidx.leanback.widget.ArrayObjectAdapter
import androidx.leanback.widget.HeaderItem
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRow
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRowPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.PageRow
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.WatchRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.GridItemPresenter
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext

class LibraryBrowseActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        title = "" // Clear activity title to prevent overlap
        val mode = intent.getStringExtra(EXTRA_MODE) ?: MODE_MOVIES
        if (savedInstanceState == null) {
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(android.R.id.content, LibraryBrowseFragment.newInstance(mode))
                .commit()
        }
    }

    class LibraryBrowseFragment : BrowseSupportFragment() {
        private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
        private lateinit var watchRepository: WatchRepository
        private lateinit var credentialStore: CredentialStore
        private lateinit var profileStore: ProfileStore
        private lateinit var aiSyncClient: AiSyncClient

        private val mode: String
            get() = arguments?.getString(EXTRA_MODE) ?: MODE_MOVIES

        override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
            catalogStore = CatalogStore(requireContext())
            watchRepository = WatchRepository(requireContext())
            credentialStore = CredentialStore(requireContext())
            profileStore = ProfileStore(requireContext())
            val credentials = credentialStore.get()
            aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(credentials?.syncServerUrl, credentials?.syncServerUsername, credentials?.syncServerPassword, credentials?.syncServerToken)
            setupUI()
            setupFragmentFactory()
            loadCategories()
        }

        private fun setupUI() {
            title = null // Clear title to prevent overlap
            badgeDrawable = null // Remove badge to clear top right area
            headersState = HEADERS_ENABLED
            isHeadersTransitionOnBackEnabled = true
            brandColor = ContextCompat.getColor(requireContext(), R.color.fastlane_background)
        }

        private fun setupFragmentFactory() {
            mainFragmentRegistry.registerFragment(PageRow::class.java, object : FragmentFactory<Fragment>() {
                override fun createFragment(rowObj: Any?): Fragment {
                    val row = rowObj as PageRow
                    return CategoryGridFragment.newInstance(mode, row.headerItem.name)
                }
            })
        }

        private fun loadCategories() {
            val rowsAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter())
            adapter = loadingRows("Loading library...")
            
            if (mode == MODE_AI_PICKS) {
                lifecycleScope.launch { loadAiPickCategories(rowsAdapter) }
                return
            }

            if (mode == MODE_WATCHLIST || mode == MODE_RECENT) {
                lifecycleScope.launch { loadServerBackedCategories(rowsAdapter) }
                return
            }

            rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(0, allContentTitle())))
            adapter = rowsAdapter

            lifecycleScope.launch {
                val contentType = selectedContentType()
                val totalCount = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
                    contentType?.let(catalogStore::countItems) ?: baseItems().size
                }

                if (totalCount == 0) {
                    val emptyAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
                    val hint = "Refresh the catalog and wait for the saved count to finish."
                    emptyAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = "No content loaded", sourceLabel = hint, contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                    adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                        add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "Library"), emptyAdapter))
                    }
                    return@launch
                }

                val specialCounts = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
                    contentType?.let(catalogStore::getSpecialCounts)
                }
                if (specialCounts != null) {
                    rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(10_001, "Recently Added (${specialCounts.recentlyAdded})")))
                    rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(10_002, "4K / UHD (${specialCounts.ultraHd})")))
                    rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(10_003, "Playable Only (${specialCounts.playable})")))
                }

                val categories = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
                    contentType?.let(catalogStore::getCategoryCounts) ?: baseItems().groupingBy { it.categoryName ?: "Uncategorized" }.eachCount()
                }.toSortedMap()

                var index = 1L
                categories.forEach { (name, count) ->
                    rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(index++, "$name ($count)")))
                }

                adapter = rowsAdapter
            }
        }

        private fun catalogItems(contentType: ContentType) = catalogStore.getItems(contentType)

        private fun selectedContentType(): ContentType? {
            return when (mode) {
                MODE_LIVE -> ContentType.LIVE
                MODE_SHOWS -> ContentType.SERIES
                MODE_MOVIES -> ContentType.MOVIE
                else -> null
            }
        }

        private fun baseItems(): List<IptvItem> {
            return when (mode) {
                MODE_RECENT -> watchRepository.getHistory()
                MODE_WATCHLIST -> watchRepository.getWatchlist()
                MODE_LIVE -> catalogItems(ContentType.LIVE)
                MODE_SHOWS -> catalogItems(ContentType.SERIES)
                MODE_AI_PICKS -> emptyList()
                else -> catalogItems(ContentType.MOVIE)
            }
        }

        private suspend fun loadServerBackedCategories(rowsAdapter: ArrayObjectAdapter) {
            val base = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { serverBackedItems() }
            rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(0, "${allContentTitle()} (${base.size})")))
            if (base.isEmpty()) {
                val emptyAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
                val title = if (mode == MODE_WATCHLIST) "No watchlist items found" else "No history found"
                val hint = if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
                    "Sync this profile or add items on the AI server dashboard."
                } else {
                    "Add AI Sync Server settings, then sync watch data."
                }
                emptyAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = title, sourceLabel = hint, contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                    add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, if (mode == MODE_WATCHLIST) "Watchlist" else "History"), emptyAdapter))
                }
                return
            }

            withContext(Dispatchers.Default) {
                base.groupBy { it.categoryName ?: it.contentType.name.lowercase().replaceFirstChar(Char::titlecase) }.toSortedMap()
            }
                .forEach { (name, items) ->
                    rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(rowsAdapter.size().toLong(), "$name (${items.size})")))
                }
            adapter = rowsAdapter
        }

        private suspend fun serverBackedItems(): List<IptvItem> {
            val local = baseItems()
            if (!aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) return local
            val credentials = credentialStore.get() ?: return local
            val kind = if (mode == MODE_WATCHLIST) "watchlist" else "history"
            return aiSyncClient.getWatchItems(serverProfileId(credentials), kind)
                .getOrDefault(local)
        }

        private fun allContentTitle(): String {
            return when (mode) {
                MODE_RECENT -> "All History"
                MODE_WATCHLIST -> "All Watchlist"
                MODE_LIVE -> "All Channels"
                MODE_SHOWS -> "All Shows"
                else -> "All Content"
            }
        }

        private suspend fun loadAiPickCategories(rowsAdapter: ArrayObjectAdapter) {
            val credentials = credentialStore.get()
            if (credentials == null || !aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
                val emptyAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
                emptyAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = "AI server is not configured", sourceLabel = "Add AI Sync Server settings, then refresh recommendations.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                    add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "AI Picks"), emptyAdapter))
                }
                return
            }
            val picks = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) {
                aiSyncClient.getRecommendations(serverProfileId(credentials)).getOrDefault(emptyList())
            }
            rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(0, "All AI Picks (${picks.size})")))
            if (picks.isEmpty()) {
                val emptyAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
                emptyAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = "No AI picks yet", sourceLabel = "Upload catalog/watch data or use AI Picks on the server dashboard.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                    add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "AI Picks"), emptyAdapter))
                }
                return
            }
            withContext(Dispatchers.Default) {
                picks.groupBy { it.contentType.name.lowercase().replaceFirstChar(Char::titlecase) }.toSortedMap()
            }
                .forEach { (name, items) ->
                    rowsAdapter.add(PageRow(HeaderItem(rowsAdapter.size().toLong(), "$name (${items.size})")))
                }
            adapter = rowsAdapter
        }

        private fun loadingRows(message: String): ArrayObjectAdapter {
            val emptyAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
            emptyAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = message, sourceLabel = "You can keep navigating while this loads.", contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
            return ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "Library"), emptyAdapter))
            }
        }

        private fun serverProfileId(credentials: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials): String {
            val localProfileId = profileStore.getCurrentProfile().id
            val owner = credentials.syncServerUsername?.trim()?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: return localProfileId
            return "$owner:$localProfileId"
        }

        companion object {
            fun newInstance(mode: String): LibraryBrowseFragment {
                return LibraryBrowseFragment().apply {
                    arguments = Bundle().apply { putString(EXTRA_MODE, mode) }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    companion object {
        const val EXTRA_MODE = "mode"
        const val MODE_RECENT = "recent"
        const val MODE_WATCHLIST = "watchlist"
        const val MODE_LIVE = "live"
        const val MODE_MOVIES = "movies"
        const val MODE_SHOWS = "shows"
        const val MODE_AI_PICKS = "aiPicks"
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/categories/CategoryManagementActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.categories

import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.text.Editable
import android.text.TextWatcher
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.CheckBox
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.ProgressBar
import android.widget.ScrollView
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CategorySyncStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCategory
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class CategoryManagementActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var categorySyncStore: CategorySyncStore
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var contentLayout: LinearLayout
    private val checkBoxes = mutableMapOf<ContentType, MutableList<Pair<IptvCategory, CheckBox>>>()

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        categorySyncStore = CategorySyncStore(this)
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(this)

        val scrollView = ScrollView(this).apply {
            setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background)
            isFillViewport = true
        }
        contentLayout = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@CategoryManagementActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CategoryManagementActivity, 36), TvUi.dp(this@CategoryManagementActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CategoryManagementActivity, 36))
        }
        scrollView.addView(contentLayout)
        setContentView(scrollView)

        buildHeader()
        loadCategories()
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        scope.cancel()
        super.onDestroy()
    }

    private fun buildHeader() {
        contentLayout.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = "Manage Categories"
            textSize = 34f
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
        }, TvUi.centeredPanelParams(this))

        contentLayout.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = "Choose which IPTV categories are allowed to refresh into Home. Use All Categories to return to provider defaults."
            textSize = 16f
            setTextColor(Color.LTGRAY)
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            setPadding(0, 10, 0, 22)
        }, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this, bottomMarginDp = 22))
    }

    private fun loadCategories() {
        val loadingView = ProgressBar(this)
        contentLayout.addView(loadingView)
        val credentials = CredentialStore(this).get()
        if (credentials == null) {
            contentLayout.removeView(loadingView)
            showMessage("Login details are missing.")
            return
        }

        scope.launch {
            val api = XtreamApiClient(credentials)
            val result = runCatching {
                listOf(ContentType.MOVIE, ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.LIVE)
                    .associateWith { type -> api.getCategories(type) }
            }
            contentLayout.removeViews(2, contentLayout.childCount - 2)

            val categoriesByType = result.getOrNull()
            if (categoriesByType == null) {
                showMessage(result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "Could not load categories.")
                return@launch
            }
            if (categoriesByType.values.all { it.isEmpty() }) {
                showMessage("No provider categories were returned. Check IPTV login details or try refreshing later.")
                return@launch
            }

            categoriesByType.forEach { (type, categories) -> addCategorySection(type, categories) }
            addActions()
        }
    }

    private fun addCategorySection(type: ContentType, categories: List<IptvCategory>) {
        val title = when (type) {
            ContentType.MOVIE -> "Movies"
            ContentType.SERIES -> "TV Shows"
            ContentType.LIVE -> "Live TV"
            else -> type.name
        }
        val sectionPanel = TvUi.verticalPanel(this)
        contentLayout.addView(sectionPanel, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this, bottomMarginDp = 18))

        sectionPanel.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = title
            textSize = 24f
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            setPadding(0, 0, 0, 8)
        }, TvUi.matchWrap())

        val configured = categorySyncStore.isConfigured(type)
        val enabledIds = categorySyncStore.getEnabledCategoryIds(type)
        val pairs = mutableListOf<Pair<IptvCategory, CheckBox>>()
        val countText = TextView(this).apply {
            textSize = 14f
            setTextColor(Color.LTGRAY)
            setPadding(0, 0, 0, 8)
        }
        sectionPanel.addView(countText, TvUi.matchWrap())

        val searchInput = TvUi.input(this, "Search $title categories").apply {
            addTextChangedListener(object : TextWatcher {
                override fun beforeTextChanged(s: CharSequence?, start: Int, count: Int, after: Int) = Unit
                override fun afterTextChanged(s: Editable?) = Unit
                override fun onTextChanged(s: CharSequence?, start: Int, before: Int, count: Int) {
                    filterCategorySection(s?.toString().orEmpty(), pairs, countText)
                }
            })
        }
        sectionPanel.addView(searchInput, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply {
            setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@CategoryManagementActivity, 10))
        })

        val sectionActions = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
        }
        val selectAllButton = TvUi.button(this, "Select All") {}
        val clearButton = TvUi.button(this, "Clear") {}
        sectionActions.addView(selectAllButton, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1f).apply {
            setMargins(0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@CategoryManagementActivity, 8), 0)
        })
        sectionActions.addView(clearButton, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1f))
        sectionPanel.addView(sectionActions, TvUi.matchWrap())

        categories.sortedBy { it.categoryName.lowercase() }.forEach { category ->
            val checked = if (configured) enabledIds.contains(category.categoryId) else true
            val checkBox = CheckBox(this).apply {
                text = category.categoryName
                isChecked = checked
                textSize = 18f
                setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
                buttonTintList = android.content.res.ColorStateList.valueOf(Color.WHITE)
                setPadding(12, 8, 12, 8)
                setOnCheckedChangeListener { _, _ -> updateCount(countText, pairs) }
            }
            pairs.add(category to checkBox)
            sectionPanel.addView(checkBox, TvUi.matchWrap())
        }
        selectAllButton.setOnClickListener {
            pairs.filter { it.second.visibility == android.view.View.VISIBLE }.forEach { it.second.isChecked = true }
            updateCount(countText, pairs)
        }
        clearButton.setOnClickListener {
            pairs.filter { it.second.visibility == android.view.View.VISIBLE }.forEach { it.second.isChecked = false }
            updateCount(countText, pairs)
        }
        checkBoxes[type] = pairs
        updateCount(countText, pairs)
    }

    private fun addActions() {
        contentLayout.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Save Selected Categories", TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY) {
            saveSelected()
        }, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this, bottomMarginDp = 10))

        contentLayout.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Use All Categories") {
            useAllCategories()
        }, TvUi.centeredPanelParams(this))
    }

    private fun updateCount(label: TextView, pairs: List<Pair<IptvCategory, CheckBox>>) {
        val selected = pairs.count { it.second.isChecked }
        val visible = pairs.count { it.second.visibility == android.view.View.VISIBLE }
        label.text = if (visible == pairs.size) {
            "$selected of ${pairs.size} selected"
        } else {
            "$selected of ${pairs.size} selected | $visible shown"
        }
    }

    private fun filterCategorySection(query: String, pairs: List<Pair<IptvCategory, CheckBox>>, countText: TextView) {
        val cleaned = query.trim()
        pairs.forEach { (category, checkBox) ->
            checkBox.visibility = if (cleaned.isBlank() || category.categoryName.contains(cleaned, ignoreCase = true)) {
                android.view.View.VISIBLE
            } else {
                android.view.View.GONE
            }
        }
        updateCount(countText, pairs)
    }

    private fun saveSelected() {
        checkBoxes.forEach { (type, pairs) ->
            val knownIds = pairs.map { it.first.categoryId }.toSet()
            val enabledIds = pairs.filter { it.second.isChecked }.map { it.first.categoryId }.toSet()
            categorySyncStore.saveEnabledCategoryIds(type, enabledIds, knownIds)
        }
        catalogStore.clearCache()
        Toast.makeText(this, "Categories saved. Home will refresh with your selection.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        finish()
    }

    private fun useAllCategories() {
        android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(this)
            .setTitle("Use All Categories")
            .setMessage("Return Movies, TV Shows, and Live TV to provider defaults?")
            .setPositiveButton("Use All") { _, _ ->
                listOf(ContentType.MOVIE, ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.LIVE).forEach(categorySyncStore::clearContentType)
                catalogStore.clearCache()
                Toast.makeText(this, "All categories enabled.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                finish()
            }
            .setNegativeButton(android.R.string.cancel, null)
            .show()
    }

    private fun showMessage(message: String) {
        contentLayout.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = message
            textSize = 18f
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            setPadding(0, 24, 0, 0)
        }, TvUi.centeredPanelParams(this))
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/clean/CleanCatalogActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.clean

import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.Button
import android.widget.EditText
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CleanCatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi

class CleanCatalogActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private lateinit var cleanCatalogStore: CleanCatalogStore
    private lateinit var keywordsEditText: EditText

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        cleanCatalogStore = CleanCatalogStore(this)

        val root = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@CleanCatalogActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CleanCatalogActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CleanCatalogActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CleanCatalogActivity, 48))
            setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background)
        }

        val title = TextView(this).apply {
            text = getString(R.string.clean_catalog_title)
            textSize = 34f
            setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.WHITE)
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
        }
        root.addView(title, TvUi.centeredPanelParams(this, 760))

        val help = TextView(this).apply {
            text = "Hide clutter by keyword. This affects Home, Movies, Series, and Kids-safe profile filtering."
            textSize = 16f
            setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.LTGRAY)
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            setPadding(0, 10, 0, 22)
        }
        root.addView(help, TvUi.centeredPanelParams(this, 760))

        keywordsEditText = TvUi.input(this, getString(R.string.clean_catalog_hint)).apply {
            hint = getString(R.string.clean_catalog_hint)
            setSingleLine(false)
            minLines = 4
            setText(cleanCatalogStore.getHiddenKeywords().joinToString(", "))
        }
        root.addView(keywordsEditText, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this, 760, 10))

        val saveButton = TvUi.button(this, getString(R.string.save), TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY) { save() }
        root.addView(saveButton, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this, 760, 10))

        val resetButton = TvUi.button(this, "Reset Smart Defaults") {
            cleanCatalogStore.resetDefaults()
            keywordsEditText.setText(cleanCatalogStore.getHiddenKeywords().joinToString(", "))
        }
        root.addView(resetButton, TvUi.centeredPanelParams(this, 760))

        setContentView(root)
    }

    private fun save() {
        val keywords = keywordsEditText.text.toString()
            .split(",", "\n")
            .map { it.trim() }
            .filter { it.isNotBlank() }
            .toSet()
        cleanCatalogStore.saveHiddenKeywords(keywords)
        Toast.makeText(this, "Clean catalog filters saved.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        finish()
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/common/TvUi.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common

import android.content.Context
import android.graphics.Typeface
import android.graphics.drawable.GradientDrawable
import android.text.InputType
import android.view.Gravity
import android.view.View
import android.view.ViewGroup
import android.widget.Button
import android.widget.EditText
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.core.content.ContextCompat
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R

object TvUi {
    private const val FOCUS_SCALE = 1.055f
    private const val ANIMATION_MS = 150L

    enum class ButtonTone {
        PRIMARY,
        SECONDARY,
        DANGER
    }

    fun dp(context: Context, value: Int): Int = (value * context.resources.displayMetrics.density).toInt()

    fun tileBackground(context: Context, focused: Boolean, danger: Boolean = false): GradientDrawable {
        val color = when {
            danger && focused -> ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.accent_coral)
            danger -> 0xFF37201F.toInt()
            focused -> ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.tile_background_focused)
            else -> ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.tile_background)
        }
        return GradientDrawable().apply {
            cornerRadius = dp(context, 8).toFloat()
            setColor(color)
            setStroke(
                if (focused) dp(context, 2) else dp(context, 1),
                if (focused) ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.accent_gold) else ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.panel_stroke)
            )
        }
    }

    fun panelBackground(context: Context): GradientDrawable = GradientDrawable().apply {
        cornerRadius = dp(context, 8).toFloat()
        setColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.premium_panel))
        setStroke(dp(context, 1), ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.panel_stroke))
    }

    fun applyFocusableTile(view: View, danger: Boolean = false) {
        view.isFocusable = true
        view.isFocusableInTouchMode = true
        view.background = tileBackground(view.context, focused = false, danger = danger)
        view.setOnFocusChangeListener { focusedView, hasFocus ->
            focusedView.background = tileBackground(focusedView.context, focused = hasFocus, danger = danger)
            focusedView.animate()
                .scaleX(if (hasFocus) FOCUS_SCALE else 1f)
                .scaleY(if (hasFocus) FOCUS_SCALE else 1f)
                .translationZ(if (hasFocus) dp(focusedView.context, 10).toFloat() else 0f)
                .alpha(if (hasFocus) 1f else 0.94f)
                .setDuration(ANIMATION_MS)
                .start()
        }
    }

    fun sectionTitle(context: Context, text: String): TextView = TextView(context).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.text_primary))
        textSize = 21f
        typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
        letterSpacing = 0.02f
        setPadding(0, dp(context, 16), 0, dp(context, 8))
    }

    fun helperText(context: Context, text: String): TextView = TextView(context).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.text_secondary))
        textSize = 14f
        setLineSpacing(dp(context, 2).toFloat(), 1.0f)
        setPadding(0, 0, 0, dp(context, 10))
    }

    fun input(context: Context, hint: String, inputType: Int = InputType.TYPE_CLASS_TEXT): EditText {
        return EditText(context).apply {
            this.hint = hint
            this.inputType = inputType
            setSingleLine(true)
            minHeight = dp(context, 56)
            textSize = 15f
            setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.text_primary))
            setHintTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.text_muted))
            background = inputBackground(context, focused = false)
            setPadding(dp(context, 16), 0, dp(context, 16), 0)
            setOnFocusChangeListener { view, hasFocus ->
                view.background = inputBackground(context, focused = hasFocus)
                view.animate()
                    .translationZ(if (hasFocus) dp(context, 8).toFloat() else 0f)
                    .setDuration(ANIMATION_MS)
                    .start()
            }
        }
    }

    private fun inputBackground(context: Context, focused: Boolean): GradientDrawable = GradientDrawable().apply {
        cornerRadius = dp(context, 8).toFloat()
        setColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.card_background))
        setStroke(
            if (focused) dp(context, 2) else dp(context, 1),
            if (focused) ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.selected_background) else ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.panel_stroke)
        )
    }

    fun button(context: Context, text: String, tone: ButtonTone = ButtonTone.SECONDARY, onClick: () -> Unit): Button {
        val danger = tone == ButtonTone.DANGER
        return Button(context).apply {
            this.text = text
            minHeight = dp(context, 56)
            textSize = 15f
            typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
            isAllCaps = false
            setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.text_primary))
            background = tileBackground(context, focused = tone == ButtonTone.PRIMARY, danger = danger)
            setOnClickListener { onClick() }
            setOnFocusChangeListener { view, hasFocus ->
                view.background = tileBackground(context, focused = hasFocus || tone == ButtonTone.PRIMARY, danger = danger)
                view.animate()
                    .scaleX(if (hasFocus) FOCUS_SCALE else 1f)
                    .scaleY(if (hasFocus) FOCUS_SCALE else 1f)
                    .translationZ(if (hasFocus) dp(context, 10).toFloat() else 0f)
                    .setDuration(ANIMATION_MS)
                    .start()
            }
        }
    }

    fun styleButton(button: Button, tone: ButtonTone = ButtonTone.SECONDARY) {
        val context = button.context
        val danger = tone == ButtonTone.DANGER
        button.minHeight = dp(context, 56)
        button.textSize = 15f
        button.typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
        button.isAllCaps = false
        button.setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(context, R.color.text_primary))
        button.background = tileBackground(context, focused = tone == ButtonTone.PRIMARY, danger = danger)
        button.setOnFocusChangeListener { view, hasFocus ->
            view.background = tileBackground(context, focused = hasFocus || tone == ButtonTone.PRIMARY, danger = danger)
            view.animate()
                .scaleX(if (hasFocus) FOCUS_SCALE else 1f)
                .scaleY(if (hasFocus) FOCUS_SCALE else 1f)
                .translationZ(if (hasFocus) dp(context, 10).toFloat() else 0f)
                .setDuration(ANIMATION_MS)
                .start()
        }
    }

    fun row(context: Context): LinearLayout = LinearLayout(context).apply {
        orientation = LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL
        gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
    }

    fun verticalPanel(context: Context): LinearLayout = LinearLayout(context).apply {
        orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
        background = panelBackground(context)
        setPadding(dp(context, 24), dp(context, 20), dp(context, 24), dp(context, 20))
    }

    fun matchWrap(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams {
        return LinearLayout.LayoutParams(ViewGroup.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, ViewGroup.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
    }

    fun centeredPanelParams(context: Context, maxWidthDp: Int = 820): LinearLayout.LayoutParams {
        return LinearLayout.LayoutParams(
            dp(context, maxWidthDp),
            ViewGroup.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT
        ).apply {
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL
        }
    }

    fun centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(context: Context, maxWidthDp: Int = 820, bottomMarginDp: Int = 16): LinearLayout.LayoutParams {
        return centeredPanelParams(context, maxWidthDp).apply {
            setMargins(0, 0, 0, dp(context, bottomMarginDp))
        }
    }
}
