// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/details/DetailsDescriptionPresenter.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details

import androidx.leanback.widget.AbstractDetailsDescriptionPresenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem

class DetailsDescriptionPresenter : AbstractDetailsDescriptionPresenter() {
    override fun onBindDescription(viewHolder: ViewHolder, item: Any) {
        val iptvItem = item as IptvItem
        viewHolder.title.text = iptvItem.title
        viewHolder.subtitle.text = buildSubtitle(iptvItem)
        viewHolder.body.text = buildBody(iptvItem)
    }

    private fun buildSubtitle(item: IptvItem): String {
        return listOfNotNull(
            item.year,
            item.rating?.let { "★ $it" },
            item.genres.takeIf { it.isNotEmpty() }?.take(3)?.joinToString(", "),
            item.metadataProvider,
            item.sourceLabel
        ).joinToString(" • ")
    }

    private fun buildBody(item: IptvItem): String {
        val overview = item.description.ifBlank { "No description available yet." }
        val progress = if (item.progressPercent > 0) "\n\nProgress: ${item.progressPercent}% watched" else ""
        val ids = listOfNotNull(
            item.traktSlug?.let { "Trakt: $it" },
            item.imdbId?.let { "IMDb: $it" },
            item.tmdbId?.let { "TMDB: $it" }
        ).joinToString(" • ").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { "\n\n$it" }.orEmpty()
        return overview + progress + ids
    }
}

================================================================================
// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/details/VideoDetailsFragment.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details

import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Bitmap
import android.graphics.drawable.Drawable
import android.os.Bundle
import android.app.AlertDialog
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.core.content.ContextCompat
import androidx.leanback.app.DetailsSupportFragment
import androidx.leanback.app.DetailsSupportFragmentBackgroundController
import androidx.leanback.widget.Action
import androidx.leanback.widget.ArrayObjectAdapter
import androidx.leanback.widget.ClassPresenterSelector
import androidx.leanback.widget.DetailsOverviewRow
import androidx.leanback.widget.FullWidthDetailsOverviewRowPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.FullWidthDetailsOverviewSharedElementHelper
import androidx.leanback.widget.HeaderItem
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRow
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRowPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.OnActionClickedListener
import androidx.leanback.widget.OnItemViewClickedListener
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.Row
import androidx.leanback.widget.RowPresenter
import com.bumptech.glide.Glide
import com.bumptech.glide.request.target.SimpleTarget
import com.bumptech.glide.request.transition.Transition
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher.isDisplayPlayable
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.WatchRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.TraktApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.CardPresenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.playback.PlaybackActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.series.SeriesHubActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.serializableExtra
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext

class VideoDetailsFragment : DetailsSupportFragment() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var detailsBackground: DetailsSupportFragmentBackgroundController
    private lateinit var presenterSelector: ClassPresenterSelector
    private lateinit var rowAdapter: ArrayObjectAdapter
    private lateinit var watchRepository: WatchRepository
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var aiSyncClient: AiSyncClient
    private lateinit var socialSettings: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
    private lateinit var socialRepository: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialRepository
    private var selectedItem: IptvItem? = null
    private var episodesLoadedFor: String? = null

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        detailsBackground = DetailsSupportFragmentBackgroundController(this)
        watchRepository = WatchRepository(requireContext())
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(requireContext())
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()
        aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(credentials?.syncServerUrl, credentials?.syncServerUsername, credentials?.syncServerPassword, credentials?.syncServerToken)
        socialSettings = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings(requireContext())
        socialRepository = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialRepository(com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient(socialSettings), socialSettings)

        val intentItem = requireActivity().intent.serializableExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, IptvItem::class.java)
        if (intentItem == null) {
            requireActivity().finish()
            return
        }

        presenterSelector = ClassPresenterSelector()
        rowAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(presenterSelector)
        adapter = rowAdapter

        scope.launch {
            val item = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                if (intentItem.isPlayable) {
                    intentItem
                } else {
                    CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(catalogStore.getAllItems(), intentItem)
                        ?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(intentItem, it) }
                        ?: intentItem
                }
            }
            selectedItem = item
            
            // Refresh progress from repository
            item.positionMs = watchRepository.getItemProgress(item.stableKey)

            setupDetailsOverviewRow(item)
            setupDetailsOverviewRowPresenter(item)
            setupRows(item)
            initializeBackground(item)
            loadVodExtras(item)
        }

        onItemViewClickedListener = OnItemViewClickedListener { _, clicked, _, _ ->
            if (clicked is IptvItem) play(clicked)
        }
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        scope.cancel()
        super.onDestroy()
    }

    private fun initializeBackground(item: IptvItem) {
        detailsBackground.enableParallax()
        val imageModel = (item.backdropUrl ?: item.coverUrl)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        if (imageModel == null) {
            detailsBackground.coverBitmap = null
            return
        }
        Glide.with(requireContext())
            .asBitmap()
            .centerCrop()
            .error(R.drawable.default_background)
            .load(imageModel)
            .into(object : SimpleTarget<Bitmap>() {
                override fun onResourceReady(resource: Bitmap, transition: Transition<in Bitmap>?) {
                    detailsBackground.coverBitmap = resource
                    rowAdapter.notifyArrayItemRangeChanged(0, rowAdapter.size())
                }
            })
    }

    private fun setupDetailsOverviewRow(item: IptvItem) {
        val row = DetailsOverviewRow(item)
        row.imageDrawable = ContextCompat.getDrawable(requireContext(), R.drawable.movie)
        val imageModel = (item.coverUrl ?: item.backdropUrl)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        if (imageModel != null) {
            Glide.with(requireContext())
                .load(imageModel)
                .centerCrop()
                .error(R.drawable.movie)
                .into(object : SimpleTarget<Drawable>(posterWidth(), posterHeight()) {
                    override fun onResourceReady(resource: Drawable, transition: Transition<in Drawable>?) {
                        row.imageDrawable = resource
                        rowAdapter.notifyArrayItemRangeChanged(0, rowAdapter.size())
                    }
                })
        }

        row.actionsAdapter = buildActions(item)
        rowAdapter.add(row)
    }

    private fun setupDetailsOverviewRowPresenter(item: IptvItem) {
        val detailsPresenter = FullWidthDetailsOverviewRowPresenter(DetailsDescriptionPresenter())
        detailsPresenter.backgroundColor = ContextCompat.getColor(requireContext(), R.color.details_panel)
        val sharedElementHelper = FullWidthDetailsOverviewSharedElementHelper()
        sharedElementHelper.setSharedElementEnterTransition(requireActivity(), DetailsActivity.SHARED_ELEMENT_NAME)
        detailsPresenter.setListener(sharedElementHelper)
        detailsPresenter.isParticipatingEntranceTransition = true
        detailsPresenter.onActionClickedListener = OnActionClickedListener { action ->
            when (action.id) {
                ACTION_PLAY -> play(item)
                ACTION_EPISODES -> openSeriesHub(item)
                ACTION_WATCH_NEXT -> toggleWatchNext(item)
                ACTION_WATCHLIST -> toggleWatchlist(item)
                ACTION_SYNC -> syncItem(item)
                ACTION_SOCIAL_WATCH -> startWatchTogether(item)
                ACTION_SOCIAL_DISCUSS -> openDiscussion(item)
                ACTION_SOCIAL_SHARE -> shareItem(item)
                ACTION_LIKE -> rateItem(item, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) 0 else 1)
                ACTION_DISLIKE -> rateItem(item, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) 0 else -1)
                ACTION_IGNORE -> ignoreItem(item)
            }
        }
        presenterSelector.addClassPresenter(DetailsOverviewRow::class.java, detailsPresenter)
    }

    private fun posterWidth(): Int = (resources.displayMetrics.density * 320).toInt()

    private fun posterHeight(): Int = (resources.displayMetrics.density * 480).toInt()

    private fun setupRows(item: IptvItem) {
        presenterSelector.addClassPresenter(ListRow::class.java, ListRowPresenter())
        if (item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES) loadEpisodes(item)
        
        loadSimilarItems(item)
        loadExplanation(item)
        loadTrendingDiscussions()
    }

    private fun loadTrendingDiscussions() {
        if (!aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) return
        scope.launch {
            val result = aiSyncClient.getTrendingDiscussions()
            val discussions = result.getOrNull()
            if (!discussions.isNullOrEmpty()) {
                val rowAdapterDiscussions = ArrayObjectAdapter(com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.GridItemPresenter())
                discussions.take(10).forEach { obj ->
                    val title = obj.optString("title", "Discussion")
                    val id = obj.optString("id")
                    rowAdapterDiscussions.add(IptvItem(title = title, actionKey = "SOCIAL_ROOM_$id", contentType = ContentType.ACTION, sourceLabel = "Trending Discussion"))
                }
                rowAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(35, "Trending Discussions"), rowAdapterDiscussions))
            }
        }
    }

    private fun loadSimilarItems(item: IptvItem) {
        if (!aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) return
        val profile = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get() ?: return
        scope.launch {
            val result = aiSyncClient.getSimilarItems(profile.userId, item.stableKey)
            val similar = result.getOrNull()
            val playableSimilar = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                val catalog = catalogStore.getAllItems()
                similar.orEmpty().mapNotNull { candidate ->
                    if (candidate.isDisplayPlayable()) {
                        candidate
                    } else {
                        CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(catalog, candidate)?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(candidate, it) }
                    }
                }.distinctBy { it.stableKey }
            }
            if (playableSimilar.isNotEmpty()) {
                val rowAdapterSimilar = ArrayObjectAdapter(CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.POSTER))
                playableSimilar.forEach { rowAdapterSimilar.add(it) }
                rowAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(33, "Similar to ${item.title}"), rowAdapterSimilar))
            }
        }
    }

    private fun loadVodExtras(item: IptvItem) {
        if (item.contentType != ContentType.MOVIE || item.streamId.isBlank()) return
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get() ?: return
        scope.launch {
            val subUrl = runCatching {
                XtreamApiClient(credentials)
                    .getVodInfo(item.streamId)
                    .optJSONObject("info")
                    ?.optString("subtitles")
            }.getOrNull()
            if (!subUrl.isNullOrBlank()) item.subtitleUrl = subUrl
        }
    }

    private fun loadExplanation(item: IptvItem) {
        if (!aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) return
        val profile = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get() ?: return
        scope.launch {
            val result = aiSyncClient.getExplanation(profile.userId, item.stableKey)
            val reason = result.getOrNull()
            if (!reason.isNullOrBlank()) {
                val rowAdapterReason = ArrayObjectAdapter(com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.GridItemPresenter())
                rowAdapterReason.add(IptvItem(title = "Why Recommended?", sourceLabel = reason, contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                rowAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(34, "AI Insight"), rowAdapterReason))
            }
        }
    }

    private fun loadEpisodes(series: IptvItem) {
        if (episodesLoadedFor == series.stableKey) return
        episodesLoadedFor = series.stableKey
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get() ?: return
        scope.launch {
            val episodes = runCatching { XtreamApiClient(credentials).getSeriesEpisodes(series) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
            if (episodes.isEmpty()) {
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), getString(R.string.series_not_ready), Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                return@launch
            }
            val rowAdapterEpisodes = ArrayObjectAdapter(CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.LANDSCAPE))
            episodes.take(60).forEach { rowAdapterEpisodes.add(it) }
            rowAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(22, "Episodes"), rowAdapterEpisodes))
        }
    }

    private fun toggleWatchlist(item: IptvItem) {
        scope.launch {
            if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) {
                withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.removeFromWatchlist(item) }
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Removed from watchlist.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            } else {
                val savedItem = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.addToWatchlist(item, catalogStore.getAllItems()) }
                val message = if (savedItem.isPlayable && !item.isPlayable) "Added to watchlist and matched to stream." else "Added to watchlist."
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), message, Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()?.let { credentials ->
                    scope.launch { TraktApiClient(credentials).syncWatchlistItem(savedItem) }
                }
            }
            refreshActions(item)
        }
    }

    private fun toggleWatchNext(item: IptvItem) {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()
        scope.launch {
            if (watchRepository.isInWatchNext(item)) {
                withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.removeFromWatchNext(item) }
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Removed from Watch Next.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            } else {
                withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.addToWatchNext(item) }
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Added to Watch Next.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                if (credentials != null && aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
                    scope.launch { aiSyncClient.addToWatchNext(credentials.userId, item.stableKey) }
                }
            }
            refreshActions(item)
        }
    }

    private fun refreshActions(item: IptvItem) {
        val row = rowAdapter.get(0) as? DetailsOverviewRow ?: return
        row.actionsAdapter = buildActions(item)
        rowAdapter.notifyArrayItemRangeChanged(0, 1)
    }

    private fun buildActions(item: IptvItem): ArrayObjectAdapter {
        val actions = ArrayObjectAdapter()
        val playLabel = when {
            item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES -> "Episodes"
            item.positionMs > 0 -> getString(R.string.resume)
            else -> getString(R.string.play)
        }
        actions.add(Action(ACTION_PLAY, playLabel))
        if (item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES) actions.add(Action(ACTION_EPISODES, "Series Hub"))

        val watchNextLabel = if (watchRepository.isInWatchNext(item)) "Remove Watch Next" else "Add Watch Next"
        actions.add(Action(ACTION_WATCH_NEXT, watchNextLabel))

        val watchlistLabel = if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) "Remove Watchlist" else "Add Watchlist"
        actions.add(Action(ACTION_WATCHLIST, watchlistLabel))
        actions.add(Action(ACTION_LIKE, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) "Clear Like" else "Like"))
        actions.add(Action(ACTION_DISLIKE, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) "Clear Dislike" else "Dislike"))
        actions.add(Action(ACTION_IGNORE, "Ignore"))
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()
        val canSync = aiSyncClient.isConfigured() || credentials?.let { TraktApiClient(it).isUserLinked() } == true

        if (socialSettings.isConfigured()) {
            actions.add(Action(ACTION_SOCIAL_WATCH, "Watch Together"))
            actions.add(Action(ACTION_SOCIAL_DISCUSS, "Discussion"))
            actions.add(Action(ACTION_SOCIAL_SHARE, "Share"))
        }
        if (canSync) actions.add(Action(ACTION_SYNC, getString(R.string.sync_now)))
        return actions
    }

    private fun openSeriesHub(item: IptvItem) {
        if (item.contentType != ContentType.SERIES) {
            loadEpisodes(item)
            return
        }
        startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), SeriesHubActivity::class.java).putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item))
    }

    private fun play(item: IptvItem) {
        if (item.contentType == ContentType.SERIES) {
            openSeriesHub(item)
            return
        }
        if (item.streamUrl.isNullOrBlank()) {
            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "This Trakt item is not matched to an IPTV stream yet. Search the catalog or open a matched item.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
            return
        }
        val intent = Intent(requireContext(), PlaybackActivity::class.java)
        intent.putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item)
        startActivity(intent)
    }

    private fun rateItem(item: IptvItem, rating: Int) {
        watchRepository.setRating(item, rating)
        Toast.makeText(requireContext(), when (rating) {
            1 -> "Marked as liked."
            -1 -> "Marked as disliked."
            else -> "Rating cleared."
        }, Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()
        if (credentials != null && aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            scope.launch { aiSyncClient.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(credentials), item, rating = rating) }
        }
        refreshActions(item)
    }

    private fun ignoreItem(item: IptvItem) {
        catalogStore.ignoreItem(item)
        Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Ignored in catalogue.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()
        if (credentials != null && aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            scope.launch { aiSyncClient.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(credentials), item, ignored = true) }
        }
        requireActivity().finish()
    }

    private fun serverProfileId(credentials: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials): String {
        val localProfileId = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore(requireContext()).getCurrentProfile().id
        val owner = credentials.syncServerUsername?.trim()?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: return localProfileId
        return "$owner:$localProfileId"
    }

    private fun syncItem(item: IptvItem) {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(requireContext()).get()
        if (credentials == null) return
        val event = watchRepository.buildWatchEvent(credentials.userId, item, item.positionMs, item.durationMs, credentials.syncServerUsername)
        scope.launch {
            if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) aiSyncClient.postWatchEvent(event)
            val traktClient = TraktApiClient(credentials)
            if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) traktClient.syncWatchlistItem(item)
            if (item.completed || item.progressPercent >= 90) traktClient.syncHistoryItem(item)
            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Sync requested.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    private fun startWatchTogether(item: IptvItem) {
        val intent = Intent(requireContext(), PlaybackActivity::class.java)
        intent.putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item)
        intent.putExtra("SHOW_CHAT", true)
        startActivity(intent)
    }

    private fun openDiscussion(item: IptvItem) {
        scope.launch {
            val room = socialRepository.getWatchPartyRoom(item)
            if (room != null) {
                val intent = Intent(requireContext(), com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social.SocialChatActivity::class.java)
                intent.putExtra("ROOM_ID", room.id)
                startActivity(intent)
            } else {
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Could not open discussion room.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            }
        }
    }

    private fun shareItem(item: IptvItem) {
        scope.launch {
            val rooms = socialRepository.getInboxRooms()
            if (rooms.isEmpty()) {
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "No social rooms found to share to.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                return@launch
            }
            val labels = rooms.map { it.title }.toTypedArray()
            AlertDialog.Builder(requireContext())
                .setTitle("Share to...")
                .setItems(labels) { _, which ->
                    val selectedRoom = rooms[which]
                    scope.launch {
                        val result = socialRepository.shareMedia(selectedRoom.id, item, "Check this out!")
                        if (result != null) {
                            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Shared to ${selectedRoom.title}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                        } else {
                            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Failed to share.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                        }
                    }
                }
                .setNegativeButton(android.R.string.cancel, null)
                .show()
        }
    }

    companion object {
        private const val ACTION_PLAY = 1L
        private const val ACTION_WATCHLIST = 2L
        private const val ACTION_SYNC = 3L
        private const val ACTION_EPISODES = 4L
        private const val ACTION_WATCH_NEXT = 5L
        private const val ACTION_SOCIAL_WATCH = 6L
        private const val ACTION_SOCIAL_DISCUSS = 7L
        private const val ACTION_SOCIAL_SHARE = 8L
        private const val ACTION_LIKE = 9L
        private const val ACTION_DISLIKE = 10L
        private const val ACTION_IGNORE = 11L
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/insights/CatalogInsightsActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.insights

import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.ScrollView
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogInsightEngine
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity

class CatalogInsightsActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var container: LinearLayout

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(this)
        val scroll = ScrollView(this).apply {
            setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background)
            isFillViewport = true
        }
        container = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 36), TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 36))
        }
        scroll.addView(container)
        setContentView(scroll)
        render()
    }

    private fun render() {
        container.removeAllViews()
        val items = catalogStore.getAllItems()
        val quality = CatalogInsightEngine.qualityReport(items)
        val duplicates = CatalogInsightEngine.duplicateGroups(items)
        val lowQuality = quality.filter { it.score < 55 }.take(40)
        val average = if (quality.isEmpty()) 0 else quality.map { it.score }.average().toInt()

        container.addView(title("Catalog Insights"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help("${quality.size} items analyzed \u2022 Average quality $average/100 \u2022 ${duplicates.size} duplicate groups"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Hide lower-quality duplicates", TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY) { hideLowerQualityDuplicates(duplicates) }, fieldParams())

        container.addView(section("Duplicate groups needing review"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        if (duplicates.isEmpty()) container.addView(help("No likely duplicates found."), TvUi.matchWrap())
        duplicates.take(30).forEach { group -> duplicatePanel(group) }

        container.addView(section("Lowest quality items"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        if (lowQuality.isEmpty()) container.addView(help("No low-quality items found."), TvUi.matchWrap())
        lowQuality.forEach { insight -> qualityPanel(insight) }
    }

    private fun duplicatePanel(group: CatalogInsightEngine.DuplicateGroup) {
        val panel = TvUi.verticalPanel(this)
        panel.addView(section("${group.title} (${group.items.size})"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        panel.addView(help("Best: ${group.best.item.title} \u2022 ${group.best.score}/100 grade ${group.best.grade}"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        group.items.forEach { insight ->
            panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "${insight.score}/100 ${insight.grade} \u2022 ${insight.item.title}") { openDetails(insight.item) }, fieldParams())
        }
        panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Hide all but best") {
            group.items.filter { it.item.stableKey != group.best.item.stableKey }.forEach { catalogStore.ignoreItem(it.item) }
            Toast.makeText(this, "Hidden ${group.items.size - 1} duplicate item(s).", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            render()
        }, fieldParams())
        container.addView(panel, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this))
    }

    private fun qualityPanel(insight: CatalogInsightEngine.QualityInsight) {
        val panel = TvUi.verticalPanel(this)
        panel.addView(section("${insight.score}/100 ${insight.grade} \u2022 ${insight.item.title}"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        panel.addView(help((insight.issues.ifEmpty { listOf("No major issues") }).joinToString(" \u2022 ")), TvUi.matchWrap())
        panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Open details") { openDetails(insight.item) }, fieldParams())
        panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Ignore item") {
            catalogStore.ignoreItem(insight.item)
            Toast.makeText(this, "Ignored ${insight.item.title}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            render()
        }, fieldParams())
        container.addView(panel, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this))
    }

    private fun hideLowerQualityDuplicates(groups: List<CatalogInsightEngine.DuplicateGroup>) {
        var hidden = 0
        groups.forEach { group ->
            group.items.filter { it.item.stableKey != group.best.item.stableKey }.forEach {
                catalogStore.ignoreItem(it.item)
                hidden += 1
            }
        }
        Toast.makeText(this, "Hidden $hidden lower-quality duplicate item(s).", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        render()
    }

    private fun openDetails(item: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem) {
        startActivity(Intent(this, DetailsActivity::class.java).putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item))
    }

    private fun fieldParams(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply {
        setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 10))
    }

    private fun title(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
        textSize = 34f
        setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD)
        gravity = Gravity.START
        setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 12))
    }

    private fun section(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
        textSize = 20f
        setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD)
        setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 12), 0, TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 8))
    }

    private fun help(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(0xFFDDDDDD.toInt())
        textSize = 15f
        setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@CatalogInsightsActivity, 10))
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/live/LiveGuideActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.live

import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.ScrollView
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.epg.EpgStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.EpgProgram
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.playback.PlaybackActivity
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import java.text.DateFormat
import java.util.Date

class LiveGuideActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var epgStore: EpgStore
    private lateinit var container: LinearLayout

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(this)
        epgStore = EpgStore(this)
        val scroll = ScrollView(this).apply { setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background); isFillViewport = true }
        container = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 36), TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 36))
        }
        scroll.addView(container)
        setContentView(scroll)
        render(loadFresh = false)
    }

    override fun onDestroy() { scope.cancel(); super.onDestroy() }

    private fun render(loadFresh: Boolean) {
        container.removeAllViews()
        val channels = catalogStore.getItems(ContentType.LIVE).take(120)
        container.addView(title("Live TV Guide"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help("${channels.size} channels \u2022 Select a program or channel to start playback."), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Refresh Now/Next EPG", TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY) { refreshEpg(channels) }, fieldParams())

        if (channels.isEmpty()) {
            container.addView(help("No live channels loaded. Refresh the catalog first."), TvUi.matchWrap())
            return
        }
        val byCategory = channels.groupBy { it.categoryName ?: "Live Channels" }.toSortedMap()
        byCategory.forEach { (category, categoryChannels) ->
            container.addView(section(category), TvUi.matchWrap())
            categoryChannels.take(40).forEach { channel -> channelPanel(channel) }
        }
        if (loadFresh) refreshEpg(channels)
    }

    private fun channelPanel(channel: IptvItem) {
        val panel = TvUi.verticalPanel(this)
        panel.addView(section(channel.title), TvUi.matchWrap())
        val programs = epgStore.getNowNext(channel.stableKey).ifEmpty { fallbackProgram(channel) }
        programs.take(4).forEach { program ->
            val liveMarker = if (program.isLiveNow) "LIVE ${program.progressPercent}% \u2022 " else ""
            panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "$liveMarker${time(program.startTimeMs)}\u2013${time(program.endTimeMs)}  ${program.programTitle}") { play(channel) }, fieldParams())
            if (program.description.isNotBlank()) panel.addView(help(program.description.take(160)), TvUi.matchWrap())
        }
        panel.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Channel details") { openDetails(channel) }, fieldParams())
        container.addView(panel, TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this))
    }

    private fun refreshEpg(channels: List<IptvItem>) {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(this).get()
        if (credentials == null) {
            Toast.makeText(this, "IPTV credentials are missing.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
            return
        }
        Toast.makeText(this, "Refreshing now/next for ${channels.take(40).size} channels\u2026", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        scope.launch {
            val api = XtreamApiClient(credentials)
            var saved = 0
            channels.take(40).forEach { channel ->
                val programs = runCatching { api.getShortEpg(channel, 4) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
                if (programs.isNotEmpty()) {
                    epgStore.save(programs)
                    saved += programs.size
                }
            }
            Toast.makeText(this@LiveGuideActivity, "Saved $saved EPG programs.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
            render(loadFresh = false)
        }
    }

    private fun fallbackProgram(channel: IptvItem): List<EpgProgram> {
        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        val start = now - (now % (30 * 60 * 1000L))
        return listOf(EpgProgram(channel.stableKey, channel.title, "Live: ${channel.title}", "No provider EPG data cached yet.", start, start + 30 * 60 * 1000L, "Generated"))
    }

    private fun play(item: IptvItem) = startActivity(Intent(this, PlaybackActivity::class.java).putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item))
    private fun openDetails(item: IptvItem) = startActivity(Intent(this, DetailsActivity::class.java).putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item))
    private fun time(ms: Long): String = DateFormat.getTimeInstance(DateFormat.SHORT).format(Date(ms))

    private fun fieldParams(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply { setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 10)) }
    private fun title(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 34f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); gravity = Gravity.START; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 12)) }
    private fun section(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 20f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 8), 0, TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 8)) }
    private fun help(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(0xFFDDDDDD.toInt()); textSize = 14f; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@LiveGuideActivity, 8)) }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/login/LoginActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.login

import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Bitmap
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Build
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.View
import android.widget.Button
import android.widget.EditText
import android.widget.ImageView
import android.widget.ProgressBar
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.TraktApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.sync.CatalogRefreshScheduler
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.MainActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.web.AndroidHostedWebServer
import com.google.zxing.BarcodeFormat
import com.google.zxing.qrcode.QRCodeWriter
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class LoginActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var credentialStore: CredentialStore
    private lateinit var serverUrlEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var usernameEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var passwordEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var traktClientIdEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var traktClientSecretEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var traktAccessTokenEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var traktRefreshTokenEditText: EditText
    private lateinit var loginButton: Button
    private lateinit var linkTraktButton: Button
    private lateinit var traktHelpButton: Button
    private lateinit var progressBar: ProgressBar
    private lateinit var messageTextView: TextView
    private lateinit var traktDeviceTextView: TextView
    private lateinit var webServerQrImageView: ImageView
    private lateinit var webServerUrlTextView: TextView

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        setContentView(R.layout.activity_login)
        credentialStore = CredentialStore(this)

        val access = AndroidHostedWebServer.start(this)

        serverUrlEditText = findViewById(R.id.serverUrlEditText)
        usernameEditText = findViewById(R.id.usernameEditText)
        passwordEditText = findViewById(R.id.passwordEditText)
        traktClientIdEditText = findViewById(R.id.traktClientIdEditText)
        traktClientSecretEditText = findViewById(R.id.traktClientSecretEditText)
        traktAccessTokenEditText = findViewById(R.id.traktAccessTokenEditText)
        traktRefreshTokenEditText = findViewById(R.id.traktRefreshTokenEditText)
        loginButton = findViewById(R.id.loginButton)
        linkTraktButton = findViewById(R.id.linkTraktButton)
        traktHelpButton = findViewById(R.id.traktHelpButton)
        progressBar = findViewById(R.id.loginProgressBar)
        messageTextView = findViewById(R.id.loginMessageTextView)
        traktDeviceTextView = findViewById(R.id.traktDeviceTextView)
        webServerQrImageView = findViewById(R.id.webServerQrImageView)
        webServerUrlTextView = findViewById(R.id.webServerUrlTextView)

        webServerUrlTextView.text = access.url
        webServerQrImageView.setImageBitmap(createQrBitmap(access.url, 560))

        styleLoginControls()

        credentialStore.getAny()?.let { saved ->
            serverUrlEditText.setText(saved.serverUrl)
            usernameEditText.setText(saved.username)
            passwordEditText.setText(saved.password)
            traktClientIdEditText.setText(saved.traktClientId.orEmpty())
            traktClientSecretEditText.setText(saved.traktClientSecret.orEmpty())
            traktAccessTokenEditText.setText(saved.traktAccessToken.orEmpty())
            traktRefreshTokenEditText.setText(saved.traktRefreshToken.orEmpty())
        }

        loginButton.setOnClickListener { login() }
        linkTraktButton.setOnClickListener { linkTraktDevice() }
        traktHelpButton.setOnClickListener { showTraktHelp() }
    }

    private fun styleLoginControls() {
        TvUi.styleButton(loginButton, TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY)
        TvUi.styleButton(linkTraktButton)
        TvUi.styleButton(traktHelpButton)
        listOf(
            serverUrlEditText,
            usernameEditText,
            passwordEditText,
            traktClientIdEditText,
            traktClientSecretEditText,
            traktAccessTokenEditText,
            traktRefreshTokenEditText
        ).forEach { input ->
            val currentHint = input.hint
            val currentType = input.inputType
            input.background = TvUi.input(this, currentHint?.toString().orEmpty(), currentType).background
            input.setPadding(TvUi.dp(this, 16), 0, TvUi.dp(this, 16), 0)
        }
    }

    private fun showTraktHelp() {
        android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(this)
            .setTitle("How to Connect Trakt")
            .setMessage("1. On a phone or computer, create a free account at trakt.tv.\n" +
                    "2. In Trakt, open Settings, then API Applications, then add a new app.\n" +
                    "3. Name it AI IPTV Viewer and use http://localhost as the redirect URI.\n" +
                    "4. Copy the Client ID and Client Secret into this screen.\n" +
                    "5. Select Link Trakt on This TV, open the shown web address, and enter the code.\n" +
                    "6. Press Login to save IPTV and Trakt details.\n\n" +
                    "You can also log in using a phone: scan the QR code above to open the web dashboard, then navigate to Settings.")
            .setPositiveButton("Got it", null)
            .show()
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        scope.cancel()
        super.onDestroy()
    }

    private fun currentCredentials(requireIptv: Boolean): IptvCredentials? {
        val serverUrl = serverUrlEditText.text.toString().trim()
        val username = usernameEditText.text.toString().trim()
        val password = passwordEditText.text.toString().trim()
        val traktClientId = traktClientIdEditText.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktClientSecret = traktClientSecretEditText.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktAccessToken = traktAccessTokenEditText.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktRefreshToken = traktRefreshTokenEditText.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }

        if (requireIptv && (serverUrl.isBlank() || username.isBlank() || password.isBlank())) {
            messageTextView.text = getString(R.string.login_required_fields)
            return null
        }

        val saved = credentialStore.getAny()
        return IptvCredentials(
            serverUrl = serverUrl,
            username = username,
            password = password,
            syncServerUrl = saved?.syncServerUrl,
            syncServerUsername = saved?.syncServerUsername,
            syncServerPassword = saved?.syncServerPassword,
            syncServerToken = saved?.syncServerToken,
            traktClientId = traktClientId,
            traktClientSecret = traktClientSecret,
            traktAccessToken = traktAccessToken,
            traktRefreshToken = traktRefreshToken,
            userId = credentialStore.getOrCreateUserId()
        )
    }

    private fun createQrBitmap(value: String, size: Int = 512): Bitmap {
        val matrix = QRCodeWriter().encode(value, BarcodeFormat.QR_CODE, size, size)
        val pixels = IntArray(size * size)
        for (y in 0 until size) {
            for (x in 0 until size) {
                pixels[y * size + x] = if (matrix[x, y]) Color.BLACK else Color.WHITE
            }
        }
        return Bitmap.createBitmap(size, size, Bitmap.Config.ARGB_8888).apply {
            setPixels(pixels, 0, size, 0, 0, size, size)
        }
    }

    private fun login() {
        val credentials = currentCredentials(requireIptv = true) ?: return

        credentialStore.save(credentials)
        CatalogRefreshScheduler.schedule(this)

        loginButton.isEnabled = false
        linkTraktButton.isEnabled = false
        progressBar.visibility = View.VISIBLE
        messageTextView.text = getString(R.string.checking_iptv_login)

        scope.launch {
            val result = runCatching { XtreamApiClient(credentials).validateLogin() }
            progressBar.visibility = View.GONE
            loginButton.isEnabled = true
            linkTraktButton.isEnabled = true

            if (result.getOrDefault(false)) {
                startActivity(Intent(this@LoginActivity, MainActivity::class.java))
                finish()
            } else {
                messageTextView.text = result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: getString(R.string.login_failed)
            }
        }
    }

    private fun linkTraktDevice() {
        val baseCredentials = currentCredentials(requireIptv = false) ?: return
        if (baseCredentials.traktClientId.isNullOrBlank() || baseCredentials.traktClientSecret.isNullOrBlank()) {
            traktDeviceTextView.text = getString(R.string.trakt_link_missing_keys)
            return
        }

        linkTraktButton.isEnabled = false
        loginButton.isEnabled = false
        progressBar.visibility = View.VISIBLE
        traktDeviceTextView.text = getString(R.string.trakt_link_starting)

        scope.launch {
            val result = runCatching {
                val client = TraktApiClient(baseCredentials)
                val deviceCode = client.requestDeviceCode()
                traktDeviceTextView.text = getString(R.string.trakt_link_code, deviceCode.verificationUrl, deviceCode.userCode)
                client.pollDeviceToken(deviceCode)
            }

            progressBar.visibility = View.GONE
            linkTraktButton.isEnabled = true
            loginButton.isEnabled = true

            val token = result.getOrNull()
            if (token != null) {
                traktAccessTokenEditText.setText(token.accessToken)
                traktRefreshTokenEditText.setText(token.refreshToken.orEmpty())
                traktDeviceTextView.text = getString(R.string.trakt_link_success)
                messageTextView.text = getString(R.string.trakt_link_success_save)

                currentCredentials(requireIptv = false)?.let { credentialStore.save(it); CatalogRefreshScheduler.schedule(this@LoginActivity) }
            } else {
                traktDeviceTextView.text = result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: getString(R.string.trakt_link_failed)
            }
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/main/CardPresenter.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main

import android.graphics.drawable.Drawable
import android.view.ViewGroup
import androidx.core.content.ContextCompat
import androidx.leanback.widget.ImageCardView
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import com.bumptech.glide.Glide
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher.isDisplayPlayable
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem

class CardPresenter(
    private val cardStyle: CardStyle = CardStyle.POSTER,
    private val onLongClickListener: ((IptvItem) -> Unit)? = null
) : Presenter() {
    enum class CardStyle {
        POSTER,
        LANDSCAPE,
        COMPACT
    }

    private var defaultCardImage: Drawable? = null
    private var defaultBackgroundColor: Int = 0
    private var selectedBackgroundColor: Int = 0

    override fun onCreateViewHolder(parent: ViewGroup): ViewHolder {
        defaultBackgroundColor = ContextCompat.getColor(parent.context, R.color.card_background)
        selectedBackgroundColor = ContextCompat.getColor(parent.context, R.color.card_background_raised)
        defaultCardImage = ContextCompat.getDrawable(parent.context, R.drawable.movie)

        val cardView = object : ImageCardView(parent.context) {
            override fun setSelected(selected: Boolean) {
                updateCardBackgroundColor(this, selected)
                animate()
                    .scaleX(if (selected) 1.045f else 1f)
                    .scaleY(if (selected) 1.045f else 1f)
                    .translationZ(if (selected) 22f else 0f)
                    .alpha(if (selected) 1f else 0.95f)
                    .setDuration(140L)
                    .start()
                super.setSelected(selected)
            }
        }
        cardView.isFocusable = true
        cardView.isFocusableInTouchMode = true
        updateCardBackgroundColor(cardView, false)

        if (onLongClickListener != null) {
            cardView.setOnLongClickListener {
                val item = cardView.tag as? IptvItem
                if (item != null) {
                    onLongClickListener.invoke(item)
                    true
                } else false
            }
        }

        return ViewHolder(cardView)
    }

    override fun onBindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder, item: Any?) {
        val iptvItem = item as IptvItem
        val cardView = viewHolder.view as ImageCardView
        cardView.tag = iptvItem
        cardView.titleText = iptvItem.title
        cardView.contentText = secondaryText(iptvItem)
        cardView.badgeImage = if (iptvItem.contentType != ContentType.ACTION && !iptvItem.isDisplayPlayable()) {
            ContextCompat.getDrawable(viewHolder.view.context, R.drawable.ic_unmatched_stream)
        } else {
            null
        }
        val (width, height) = dimensions(iptvItem)
        cardView.setMainImageDimensions(width, height)
        val imageModel = (iptvItem.coverUrl ?: iptvItem.backdropUrl)?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        if (imageModel == null) {
            cardView.mainImage = defaultCardImage
        } else {
            Glide.with(viewHolder.view.context)
                .load(imageModel)
                .centerCrop()
                .transition(com.bumptech.glide.load.resource.drawable.DrawableTransitionOptions.withCrossFade(160))
                .error(defaultCardImage)
                .into(cardView.mainImageView!!)
        }
    }

    override fun onUnbindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder) {
        val cardView = viewHolder.view as ImageCardView
        cardView.badgeImage = null
        cardView.mainImage = null
    }

    private fun dimensions(item: IptvItem): Pair<Int, Int> {
        return when (cardStyle) {
            CardStyle.LANDSCAPE -> 480 to 270
            CardStyle.COMPACT -> 330 to 165
            CardStyle.POSTER -> if (item.contentType == ContentType.LIVE) 480 to 270 else 320 to 480
        }
    }

    private fun secondaryText(item: IptvItem): String {
        if (item.completed) return "Watched"
        if (item.positionMs > 0 && item.durationMs > 0) return "Resume: ${item.progressPercent}%"
        if (item.contentType != ContentType.ACTION && !item.isDisplayPlayable()) {
            return when {
                item.sourceLabel?.contains("Trakt", ignoreCase = true) == true -> "Trakt only - no stream"
                item.sourceLabel?.contains("AI", ignoreCase = true) == true -> "AI pick - not matched"
                else -> "No playable stream"
            }
        }
        val base = when (item.contentType) {
            ContentType.LIVE -> listOfNotNull("Playable", item.categoryName ?: item.sourceLabel).joinToString(" - ")
            ContentType.MOVIE -> listOfNotNull("Playable", shortRatingText(item).ifBlank { null }).joinToString(" - ")
            ContentType.SERIES -> listOfNotNull("Series details", shortRatingText(item).ifBlank { null }).joinToString(" - ")
            ContentType.EPISODE -> listOfNotNull(item.parentSeriesTitle, item.seasonNumber?.let { "S$it" }, item.episodeNumber?.let { "E$it" }).joinToString(" ")
            ContentType.ACTION -> item.sourceLabel.orEmpty()
        }
        return base.ifBlank {
            when (item.contentType) {
                ContentType.LIVE -> "Live TV"
                ContentType.MOVIE -> "Movie"
                ContentType.SERIES -> "Series"
                ContentType.EPISODE -> "Episode"
                ContentType.ACTION -> ""
            }
        }
    }

    private fun shortRatingText(item: IptvItem): String {
        return listOfNotNull(item.year, item.rating?.let { "Rating $it" }).joinToString("  ")
    }

    private fun updateCardBackgroundColor(view: ImageCardView, selected: Boolean) {
        val color = if (selected) selectedBackgroundColor else defaultBackgroundColor
        view.setBackgroundColor(color)
        view.setInfoAreaBackgroundColor(color)
        view.foreground = if (selected) {
            android.graphics.drawable.GradientDrawable().apply {
                setColor(android.graphics.Color.TRANSPARENT)
                cornerRadius = 8f
                setStroke(4, ContextCompat.getColor(view.context, R.color.accent_gold))
            }
        } else {
            null
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/main/GridItemPresenter.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main

import android.graphics.Color
import android.graphics.Typeface
import android.view.Gravity
import android.view.ViewGroup
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi

class GridItemPresenter(private val width: Int = 430, private val height: Int = 118) : Presenter() {
    override fun onCreateViewHolder(parent: ViewGroup): ViewHolder {
        val view = LinearLayout(parent.context).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(parent.context, 28), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 18), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 28), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 18))
        }
        view.layoutParams = ViewGroup.MarginLayoutParams(TvUi.dp(parent.context, width), TvUi.dp(parent.context, height)).apply {
            val margin = TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8)
            setMargins(margin, margin, margin, margin)
        }
        TvUi.applyFocusableTile(view)
        view.addView(TextView(parent.context).apply {
            id = android.R.id.text1
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            textSize = 17f
            typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            maxLines = 2
            includeFontPadding = false
        }, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
        view.addView(TextView(parent.context).apply {
            id = android.R.id.text2
            setTextColor(0xFFC6D3E1.toInt())
            textSize = 13f
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            maxLines = 2
            includeFontPadding = false
            setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), 0, 0)
        }, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
        return ViewHolder(view)
    }

    override fun onBindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder, item: Any?) {
        val iptvItem = item as? IptvItem
        val title = iptvItem?.title ?: item.toString()
        val subtitle = iptvItem?.sourceLabel.orEmpty()
        val view = viewHolder.view as LinearLayout
        val isDanger = iptvItem?.actionKey == "logout"
        TvUi.applyFocusableTile(view, danger = isDanger)
        view.findViewById<TextView>(android.R.id.text1).text = title
        view.findViewById<TextView>(android.R.id.text2).apply {
            text = subtitle
            visibility = if (subtitle.isBlank()) android.view.View.GONE else android.view.View.VISIBLE
        }
    }

    override fun onUnbindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder) = Unit
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main

import android.content.Intent
import android.os.Bundle
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.login.LoginActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.sync.CatalogRefreshScheduler

class MainActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        CatalogRefreshScheduler.schedule(this)
        if (!CredentialStore(this).hasCredentials()) {
            startActivity(Intent(this, LoginActivity::class.java))
            finish()
            return
        }
        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)
        if (savedInstanceState == null) {
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(R.id.main_browse_fragment, MainFragment())
                .commitNow()
        }
    }
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main

import android.content.Intent

import com.bumptech.glide.Glide

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogMatcher

class MainFragment : BrowseSupportFragment() {
    private val handler = Handler(Looper.getMainLooper())
    private lateinit var backgroundManager: BackgroundManager
    private lateinit var metrics: DisplayMetrics
    private var defaultBackground: Drawable? = null
    private var backgroundTimer: Timer? = null
    private var backgroundUri: String? = null

    private lateinit var credentialStore: CredentialStore
    private lateinit var watchRepository: WatchRepository
    private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
    private lateinit var categorySyncStore: CategorySyncStore
    private lateinit var cleanCatalogStore: CleanCatalogStore
    private lateinit var profileStore: ProfileStore
    private lateinit var homeSettings: ProfileHomeSettings
    private lateinit var socialSettings: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
    private lateinit var socialRepository: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialRepository
    private lateinit var credentials: IptvCredentials
    private lateinit var apiClient: XtreamApiClient
    private lateinit var aiSyncClient: AiSyncClient
    private lateinit var traktApiClient: TraktApiClient
    private var rowsLoaded = false
    private var lastCategoryVersion = 0L
    private var loadRowsJob: Job? = null
    private var backgroundRefreshQueued = false

    override fun onActivityCreated(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onActivityCreated(savedInstanceState)
        credentialStore = CredentialStore(requireContext())
        val savedCredentials = credentialStore.get()
        if (savedCredentials == null) {
            startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), LoginActivity::class.java))
            requireActivity().finish()
            return
        }
        credentials = savedCredentials
        profileStore = ProfileStore(requireContext())
        homeSettings = ProfileHomeSettings(requireContext())
        watchRepository = WatchRepository(requireContext())
        catalogStore = CatalogStore(requireContext())
        categorySyncStore = CategorySyncStore(requireContext())
        lastCategoryVersion = categorySyncStore.getVersion()
        cleanCatalogStore = CleanCatalogStore(requireContext())
        socialSettings = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings(requireContext())
        socialRepository = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialRepository(com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient(socialSettings), socialSettings)
        apiClient = XtreamApiClient(credentials)
        aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken)
        traktApiClient = TraktApiClient(credentials)

        prepareBackgroundManager()
        setupUIElements()
        loadRows()
        setupEventListeners()
        observeRefreshWorker()
    }

    private fun observeRefreshWorker() {
        WorkManager.getInstance(requireContext())
            .getWorkInfosForUniqueWorkLiveData(CatalogRefreshWorker.UNIQUE_WORK_NAME)
            .observe(viewLifecycleOwner) { workInfos ->
                val info = workInfos.firstOrNull() ?: return@observe
                val message = info.progress.getString(CatalogRefreshWorker.KEY_MESSAGE)
                    ?: info.outputData.getString(CatalogRefreshWorker.KEY_MESSAGE)
                
                if (info.state == WorkInfo.State.RUNNING) {
                    backgroundRefreshQueued = true
                    if (!message.isNullOrBlank()) updateLoadingStatus(message)
                } else if (info.state.isFinished) {
                    backgroundRefreshQueued = false
                    if (info.state == WorkInfo.State.SUCCEEDED) {
                        val movies = info.outputData.getInt(CatalogRefreshWorker.KEY_MOVIES, 0)
                        val series = info.outputData.getInt(CatalogRefreshWorker.KEY_SERIES, 0)
                        val live = info.outputData.getInt(CatalogRefreshWorker.KEY_LIVE, 0)
                        if (rowsLoaded && !message.isNullOrBlank()) {
                             Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Catalog refreshed: $movies movies, $series series, $live live.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                             loadRows(forceRefresh = false)
                        }
                    } else if (info.state == WorkInfo.State.FAILED) {
                        val error = message ?: "Catalog refresh failed."
                        if (rowsLoaded) Toast.makeText(requireContext(), error, Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                    }
                    clearLoadingStatus()
                    setupUIElements() // Reset title
                }
            }
    }

    override fun onResume() {
        super.onResume()
        if (::credentials.isInitialized) {
            credentialStore.get()?.let { saved ->
                if (saved != credentials) {
                    credentials = saved
                    apiClient = XtreamApiClient(credentials)
                    aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken)
                    traktApiClient = TraktApiClient(credentials)
                    loadRows()
                    return
                }
            }
            val categoryVersion = categorySyncStore.getVersion()
            if (categoryVersion != lastCategoryVersion) {
                lastCategoryVersion = categoryVersion
                startBackgroundCatalogRefresh()
                loadRows(forceRefresh = false)
                return
            }
            if (!rowsLoaded) loadRows()
        }
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        backgroundTimer?.cancel()
        super.onDestroy()
    }

    private fun prepareBackgroundManager() {
        backgroundManager = BackgroundManager.getInstance(requireActivity())
        backgroundManager.attach(requireActivity().window)
        defaultBackground = ContextCompat.getDrawable(requireContext(), R.drawable.default_background)
        metrics = resources.displayMetrics
    }

    private fun setupUIElements() {
        val profile = profileStore.getCurrentProfile()
        title = "${getString(R.string.browse_title)} • ${profile.name}"
        headersState = HEADERS_ENABLED
        isHeadersTransitionOnBackEnabled = true
        brandColor = ContextCompat.getColor(requireContext(), R.color.fastlane_background)
        searchAffordanceColor = ContextCompat.getColor(requireContext(), R.color.search_opaque)
        badgeDrawable = ContextCompat.getDrawable(requireContext(), R.drawable.ic_app_icon)
    }

    private fun loadRows(forceRefresh: Boolean = false) {
        loadRowsJob?.cancel()
        if (!rowsLoaded) {
            adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                add(statusRow(if (forceRefresh) "Refreshing catalog..." else getString(R.string.loading_catalog)))
            }
        } else if (forceRefresh) {
            updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog in background...")
        }

        loadRowsJob = viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
            setupUIElements()
            val rows = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter())
            val posterPresenter = CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.POSTER, ::onItemLongClicked)
            val landscapePresenter = CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.LANDSCAPE, ::onItemLongClicked)
            val compactPresenter = CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.COMPACT)
            val currentProfile = profileStore.getCurrentProfile()
            val isKids = currentProfile.isKidsProfile

            rows.add(buildPrimaryNavRow())

            val continueWatching = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.getContinueWatching() }
            if (continueWatching.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(1, getString(R.string.continue_watching), continueWatching, posterPresenter))

            val cachedCatalog = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { catalogStore.getAllItems() }
            val localWatchNext = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.getWatchNext() }

            if (localWatchlist.isNotEmpty() && isHomeRowEnabled(currentProfile.id, ProfileHomeSettings.HomeRow.WATCHLIST)) rows.add(buildItemRow(5, getString(R.string.watchlist), localWatchlist, posterPresenter))

            val recentLive = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { watchRepository.getRecentlyWatchedLive() }
            if (recentLive.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(10, getString(R.string.recent_live), recentLive, landscapePresenter))
