    private suspend fun loadHomeDiscoveryRows(
        rows: ArrayObjectAdapter,
        posterPresenter: CardPresenter,
        compactPresenter: CardPresenter,
        currentProfile: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.UserProfile,
        cachedCatalog: List<IptvItem>,
        movies: List<IptvItem>,
        series: List<IptvItem>
    ) {
        syncIgnoredCatalogPreferences()

        if (isHomeRowEnabled(currentProfile.id, ProfileHomeSettings.HomeRow.AI)) {
            val serverRecommendations = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeRecommendationsWithLocalCatalog(aiSyncClient.getRecommendations(serverProfileId()).getOrDefault(emptyList()), cachedCatalog)
            }
            if (serverRecommendations.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(11_001, "AI Watch Next", serverRecommendations, posterPresenter))
        }

        val traktWatchlist = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
            runCatching { traktApiClient.getUserWatchlist(40) }
                .getOrDefault(emptyList())
                .mapNotNull { item ->
                    CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(cachedCatalog, item)
                        ?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(item, it).copy(sourceLabel = "Trakt Watchlist - Available") }
                }
        }
        if (traktWatchlist.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(6, getString(R.string.trakt_watchlist), traktWatchlist, posterPresenter))

        if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            val tmdbWatchlist = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeWithLocalCatalog(aiSyncClient.getTmdbWatchlist(40).getOrDefault(emptyList()), cachedCatalog, "TMDb Watchlist")
            }
            if (tmdbWatchlist.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(14, "TMDb Watchlist", tmdbWatchlist, posterPresenter))

            val tmdbPopularMovies = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeWithLocalCatalog(aiSyncClient.getTmdbCollection("popular", ContentType.MOVIE, 40).getOrDefault(emptyList()), movies, "TMDb Popular")
            }
            if (tmdbPopularMovies.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(15, "TMDb Popular Movies", tmdbPopularMovies, posterPresenter))

            val tmdbTopRatedMovies = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeWithLocalCatalog(aiSyncClient.getTmdbCollection("top_rated", ContentType.MOVIE, 40).getOrDefault(emptyList()), movies, "TMDb Top Rated")
            }
            if (tmdbTopRatedMovies.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(16, "TMDb Top Rated Movies", tmdbTopRatedMovies, posterPresenter))

            val tmdbTopRatedSeries = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeWithLocalCatalog(aiSyncClient.getTmdbCollection("top_rated", ContentType.SERIES, 40).getOrDefault(emptyList()), series, "TMDb Top Rated")
            }
            if (tmdbTopRatedSeries.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(17, "TMDb Top Rated Series", tmdbTopRatedSeries, posterPresenter))
        }

        if (isHomeRowEnabled(currentProfile.id, ProfileHomeSettings.HomeRow.TRENDING)) {
            val trendingMovies = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeWithLocalCatalog(runCatching { traktApiClient.getTrendingMovies(40) }.getOrDefault(emptyList()), movies, "Trakt Trending")
            }
            if (trendingMovies.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(7, getString(R.string.trending_movies), trendingMovies, posterPresenter))

            val trendingShows = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                mergeWithLocalCatalog(runCatching { traktApiClient.getTrendingShows(40) }.getOrDefault(emptyList()), series, "Trakt Trending")
            }
            if (trendingShows.isNotEmpty()) rows.add(buildItemRow(8, getString(R.string.trending_series), trendingShows, posterPresenter))
        }

        if (socialSettings.isConfigured()) {
            val socialRooms = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { socialRepository.getInboxRooms() }
            if (socialRooms.isNotEmpty()) {
                val socialAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(compactPresenter)
                socialRooms.forEach { room ->
                    socialAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = room.title, contentType = ContentType.ACTION, actionKey = "SOCIAL_ROOM_${room.id}", sourceLabel = room.lastMessage ?: "Discussion"))
                }
                rows.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(12, "Social Discussions"), socialAdapter))
            }
            rows.add(buildSocialNavRow(compactPresenter))
        }
    }

    private suspend fun syncIgnoredCatalogPreferences() {
        if (!aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) return
        aiSyncClient.getIgnoredStableKeys(serverProfileId())
            .onSuccess { keys ->
                withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                    catalogStore.setServerIgnoredStableKeys(keys)
                }
            }
            .onFailure { error -> Log.w("MainFragment", "Could not sync ignored catalog preferences", error) }
    }

    private fun serverProfileId(): String {
        val localProfileId = profileStore.getCurrentProfile().id
        val owner = credentials.syncServerUsername?.trim()?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: return localProfileId
        return "$owner:$localProfileId"
    }

    private suspend fun loadSmartCatalog(contentType: ContentType, limit: Int, isKids: Boolean, forceRefresh: Boolean = false): List<IptvItem> {
        val label = catalogTypeLabel(contentType)
        val interval = credentialStore.getSyncIntervalDays()
        val cached = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
            catalogStore.getItems(contentType)
        }
        val isExpired = catalogStore.isCacheExpired(contentType, interval)
        val refreshAttemptExpired = catalogStore.isRefreshAttemptExpired(contentType, interval)
        
        if (!forceRefresh && cached.isNotEmpty() && (!isExpired || !refreshAttemptExpired)) {
            Log.d("MainFragment", "Loading $contentType from cache (refresh interval $interval days)")
            return cached.take(limit)
        }

        if (!forceRefresh) {
            if (!backgroundRefreshQueued && refreshAttemptExpired) {
                backgroundRefreshQueued = true
                CatalogRefreshWorker.enqueue(requireContext())
                updateLoadingStatus("Catalog refresh queued in background.")
            }
            return cached.take(limit)
        }

        Log.d("MainFragment", "Cache expired or empty for $contentType, fetching from server...")
        updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog: loading $label...")
        catalogStore.markRefreshAttempt(contentType)
        val items = loadCleanXtream(contentType, fetchLimit = null, isKids) { message ->
            updateLoadingStatus(message)
        }
        if (items.isNotEmpty()) {
            updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog: saving ${items.size} $label...")
            withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                catalogStore.replaceType(contentType, items)
                catalogStore.markSynced(contentType)
            }
            val savedCount = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) { catalogStore.countItems(contentType) }
            updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog: saved $savedCount $label.")
            if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
                updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog: syncing ${items.size} $label to server...")
                aiSyncClient.postCatalogMetadata(items)
            }
            updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog: $savedCount $label ready.")
        } else if (cached.isNotEmpty()) {
            Log.w("MainFragment", "Server refresh returned no $contentType items; keeping stale cache")
            return cached.take(limit)
        }
        return items.take(limit)
    }

    private suspend fun loadCleanXtream(
        contentType: ContentType,
        fetchLimit: Int?,
        isKids: Boolean,
        onProgress: (String) -> Unit = {}
    ): List<IptvItem> {
        val label = catalogTypeLabel(contentType)
        val enabledCategories = categorySyncStore.getEnabledCategoryIds(contentType)
        val categoriesConfigured = categorySyncStore.isConfigured(contentType)
        onProgress("Refreshing catalog: loading $label categories...")
        val categories = runCatching { apiClient.getCategories(contentType) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
        val categoriesById = categories.associateBy { it.categoryId }
        
        if (categoriesConfigured && enabledCategories.isEmpty()) {
            onProgress("Refreshing catalog: no $label categories enabled.")
            return emptyList()
        }

        if (enabledCategories.isNotEmpty()) {
            val allItems = mutableListOf<IptvItem>()
            val categoryIds = enabledCategories.toList()
            for (index in categoryIds.indices) {
                val catId = categoryIds[index]
                val category = categoriesById[catId] ?: com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCategory(catId, "Category $catId", contentType)
                onProgress("Refreshing catalog: $label category ${index + 1}/${categoryIds.size}...")
                val catItems = runCatching { 
                    apiClient.getItems(contentType, category, limit = fetchLimit)
                }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
                allItems.addAll(catItems)
                onProgress("Refreshing catalog: ${allItems.size} $label loaded...")
                if (fetchLimit != null && allItems.size >= fetchLimit * 2) break
            }
            return allItems.filter { item ->
                !cleanCatalogStore.shouldHide(item.title, item.categoryName) && (!isKids || cleanCatalogStore.isKidsSafe(item.categoryName, item.title))
            }
        }

        // Fallback to general fetch if no categories enabled (or first run)
        onProgress("Refreshing catalog: downloading all $label...")
        val items = runCatching { apiClient.getItems(contentType, limit = fetchLimit) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
        onProgress("Refreshing catalog: ${items.size} $label downloaded...")
        return items.map { item ->
            if (!item.categoryName.isNullOrBlank() || item.categoryId.isNullOrBlank()) item else item.copy(categoryName = categoriesById[item.categoryId]?.categoryName)
        }.filter { item ->
            !cleanCatalogStore.shouldHide(item.title, item.categoryName) && (!isKids || cleanCatalogStore.isKidsSafe(item.categoryName, item.title))
        }
    }

    private fun updateLoadingStatus(message: String) {
        handler.post {
            title = message
            val currentAdapter = adapter as? ArrayObjectAdapter ?: return@post
            
            // Try to find status row at the very top (id 999 for active progress)
            var statusRowIndex = -1
            for (i in 0 until currentAdapter.size()) {
                val row = currentAdapter.get(i) as? ListRow
                if (row?.headerItem?.id == 999L) {
                    statusRowIndex = i
                    break
                }
            }

            if (statusRowIndex != -1) {
                val row = currentAdapter.get(statusRowIndex) as ListRow
                val rowAdapter = row.adapter as ArrayObjectAdapter
                rowAdapter.clear()
                rowAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = message, contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                currentAdapter.notifyArrayItemRangeChanged(statusRowIndex, 1)
            } else {
                // If the app just loaded, rowsLoaded might be false, but adapter might already have items
                val rowAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
                rowAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = message, contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
                val insertIndex = if (currentAdapter.size() > 0) 1 else 0 // After "Start Here" if possible
                currentAdapter.add(insertIndex, ListRow(HeaderItem(999L, "Current Task"), rowAdapter))
            }
        }
    }

    private fun clearLoadingStatus() {
        handler.post {
            val currentAdapter = adapter as? ArrayObjectAdapter ?: return@post
            for (i in 0 until currentAdapter.size()) {
                val row = currentAdapter.get(i) as? ListRow
                if (row?.headerItem?.id == 999L) {
                    currentAdapter.remove(row)
                    break
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private fun catalogTypeLabel(contentType: ContentType): String {
        return when (contentType) {
            ContentType.MOVIE -> "movies"
            ContentType.SERIES -> "series"
            ContentType.LIVE -> "live channels"
            ContentType.EPISODE -> "episodes"
            ContentType.ACTION -> "items"
        }
    }

    private fun isHomeRowEnabled(profileId: String, row: ProfileHomeSettings.HomeRow): Boolean {
        return homeSettings.isRowEnabled(profileId, row)
    }

    private fun mergeWithLocalCatalog(discovery: List<IptvItem>, local: List<IptvItem>, source: String): List<IptvItem> {
        if (discovery.isEmpty()) return emptyList()
        return discovery.mapNotNull { discoveryItem ->
            CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(local, discoveryItem)
                ?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(discoveryItem, it).copy(sourceLabel = "$source - Available") }
        }.distinctBy { it.stableKey }
    }

    private fun mergeRecommendationsWithLocalCatalog(recommendations: List<IptvItem>, local: List<IptvItem>): List<IptvItem> {
        return recommendations.map { recommendation ->
            CatalogMatcher.matchPlayableLocalCatalog(local, recommendation)
                ?.let { CatalogMatcher.mergePlayableMatch(recommendation, it).copy(sourceLabel = recommendation.sourceLabel ?: "AI Pick - Playable") }
                ?: recommendation.copy(sourceLabel = recommendation.sourceLabel ?: "AI Pick - Not in catalog")
        }.distinctBy { it.stableKey }
    }

    private fun buildItemRow(id: Long, title: String, items: List<IptvItem>, cardPresenter: CardPresenter): ListRow {
        val rowAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(cardPresenter)
        items.forEach { rowAdapter.add(it) }
        return ListRow(HeaderItem(id, title), rowAdapter)
    }

    }

    private fun buildLastRefreshLabel(): String {
        val lastSync = listOf(ContentType.MOVIE, ContentType.SERIES, ContentType.LIVE)
            .map { catalogStore.getLastSyncedAt(it) }
            .filter { it > 0L }
            .minOrNull()
        return if (lastSync == null) {
            "Catalog Not Refreshed"
        } else {
            "Last Refresh: ${DateFormat.getDateTimeInstance(DateFormat.SHORT, DateFormat.SHORT).format(Date(lastSync))}"
        }
    }

    private fun setupEventListeners() {
        setOnSearchClickedListener { startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), SearchActivity::class.java)) }
        onItemViewClickedListener = ItemViewClickedListener()
        onItemViewSelectedListener = ItemViewSelectedListener()
    }

    private fun onItemLongClicked(item: IptvItem) {
        if (item.contentType == ContentType.ACTION) return
        val options = mutableListOf<String>()
        options.add(if (watchRepository.isInWatchNext(item)) "Remove from Watch Next" else "Add to Watch Next")
        options.add(if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) "Remove from Watchlist" else "Add to Watchlist")
        options.add(if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) "Clear Like" else "Like")
        options.add(if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) "Clear Dislike" else "Dislike")
        options.add("Ignore in Catalogue")
        
        AlertDialog.Builder(requireContext())
            .setTitle(item.title)
            .setItems(options.toTypedArray()) { _, which ->
                when (which) {
                    0 -> {
                        if (watchRepository.isInWatchNext(item)) {
                            watchRepository.removeFromWatchNext(item)
                            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Removed from Watch Next", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                        } else {
                            watchRepository.addToWatchNext(item)
                            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Added to Watch Next", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                        }
                        loadRows()
                    }
                    1 -> {
                        if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) {
                            watchRepository.removeFromWatchlist(item)
                            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Removed from watchlist", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                            loadRows()
                        } else {
                            viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
                                val savedItem = withContext(kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers.IO) {
                                    watchRepository.addToWatchlist(item, catalogStore.getAllItems())
                                }
                                val message = if (savedItem.isPlayable && !item.isPlayable) "Added to watchlist and matched to stream" else "Added to watchlist"
                                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), message, Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                                loadRows()
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    2 -> rateItem(item, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) 0 else 1)
                    3 -> rateItem(item, if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) 0 else -1)
                    4 -> ignoreItem(item)
                }
            }
            .show()
    }

    private fun rateItem(item: IptvItem, rating: Int) {
        watchRepository.setRating(item, rating)
        Toast.makeText(requireContext(), when (rating) {
            1 -> "Marked as liked"
            -1 -> "Marked as disliked"
            else -> "Rating cleared"
        }, Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
                aiSyncClient.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(), item, rating = rating)
            }
        }
    }

    private fun ignoreItem(item: IptvItem) {
        catalogStore.ignoreItem(item)
        Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Ignored in catalogue", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
                aiSyncClient.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(), item, ignored = true)
            }
        }
        loadRows()
    }

    private inner class ItemViewClickedListener : OnItemViewClickedListener {
        override fun onItemClicked(itemViewHolder: Presenter.ViewHolder, item: Any, rowViewHolder: RowPresenter.ViewHolder, row: Row) {
            if (item is IptvItem && item.contentType == ContentType.ACTION) {
                handleAction(item.actionKey)
                return
            }
            if (item is IptvItem) {
                val intent = Intent(requireContext(), DetailsActivity::class.java)
                intent.putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item)
                val imageView = (itemViewHolder.view as? ImageCardView)?.mainImageView
                val bundle = if (imageView != null) ActivityOptionsCompat.makeSceneTransitionAnimation(requireActivity(), imageView, DetailsActivity.SHARED_ELEMENT_NAME).toBundle() else null
                startActivity(intent, bundle)
            }
        }
    }

    private fun handleAction(actionKey: String?) {
        if (actionKey?.startsWith("SOCIAL_ROOM_") == true) {
            val roomId = actionKey.removePrefix("SOCIAL_ROOM_")
            startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social.SocialChatActivity::class.java).putExtra("ROOM_ID", roomId))
            return
        }
        when (actionKey) {
            ACTION_SYNC -> syncNow()
            ACTION_SYNC_INTERVAL -> showCatalogRefreshDialog()
            ACTION_REFRESH -> {
                startBackgroundCatalogRefresh()
            }
            ACTION_SEARCH -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), SearchActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_BROWSE_RECENT -> openBrowse(LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_RECENT)
            ACTION_BROWSE_LIVE -> openBrowse(LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_LIVE)
            ACTION_BROWSE_MOVIES -> openBrowse(LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_MOVIES)
            ACTION_BROWSE_SHOWS -> openBrowse(LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_SHOWS)
            ACTION_BROWSE_WATCHLIST -> openBrowse(LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_WATCHLIST)
            ACTION_BROWSE_AI_PICKS -> openBrowse(LibraryBrowseActivity.MODE_AI_PICKS)
            ACTION_LIVE_GUIDE -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), LiveGuideActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_AI_MODES -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), AiModesActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_CATALOG_INSIGHTS -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), CatalogInsightsActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_ADMIN_DASHBOARD -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), AdminDashboardActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_CATEGORIES -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), CategoryManagementActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_PROFILES -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), ProfilesActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_CLEAN -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), CleanCatalogActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_SETTINGS -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), SettingsActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_ANDROID_WEBSERVER -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), AndroidWebServerActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_SOCIAL_INBOX -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social.SocialInboxActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_EDIT_LOGIN -> startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), LoginActivity::class.java))
            ACTION_LOGOUT -> confirmLogout()
        }
    }

    private fun confirmLogout() {
        AlertDialog.Builder(requireContext())
            .setTitle(getString(R.string.logout))
            .setMessage("Clear saved IPTV login details and return to the login screen?")
            .setPositiveButton(getString(R.string.logout)) { _, _ ->
                credentialStore.clear()
                startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), LoginActivity::class.java))
                requireActivity().finish()
            }
            .setNegativeButton(android.R.string.cancel, null)
            .show()
    }

    private fun openBrowse(mode: String) {
        try {
            startActivity(Intent(requireContext(), LibraryBrowseActivity::class.java).putExtra(LibraryBrowseActivity.EXTRA_MODE, mode))
        } catch (error: ActivityNotFoundException) {
            Log.e("MainFragment", "Library browse activity is missing from the installed manifest.", error)
            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Browse screen is not available in this build. Reinstall the latest APK.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        }
    }

    private fun showCatalogRefreshDialog() {
        val choices = intArrayOf(1, 2, 3, 5, 7)
        val labels = choices.map { days ->
            if (days == 1) "Every day" else "Every $days days"
        }.toTypedArray()
        val currentIndex = choices.indexOf(credentialStore.getSyncIntervalDays()).coerceAtLeast(0)
        AlertDialog.Builder(requireContext())
            .setTitle("Catalog Refresh")
            .setSingleChoiceItems(labels, currentIndex) { dialog, which ->
                val days = choices[which]
                credentialStore.setSyncIntervalDays(days)
                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Catalog will refresh every $days day${if (days == 1) "" else "s"}.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                dialog.dismiss()
                loadRows(forceRefresh = false)
            }
            .setNegativeButton(android.R.string.cancel, null)
            .show()
    }

    private fun startBackgroundCatalogRefresh() {
        Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Refreshing catalog in background.", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        updateLoadingStatus("Refreshing catalog in background...")
        CatalogRefreshWorker.enqueue(requireContext())
    }

    private fun syncNow() {
        if (!aiSyncClient.isConfigured() && !traktApiClient.isUserLinked()) {
            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Configure AI Sync Server or Trakt access token.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
            return
        }
        viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
            if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) aiSyncClient.postWatchSnapshot(watchRepository.buildSnapshot(credentials.userId, credentials.syncServerUsername))
            val watchlist = watchRepository.getWatchlist()
            watchlist.take(20).forEach { traktApiClient.syncWatchlistItem(it) }
            Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Sync requested for current profile.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        }
    }

    private inner class ItemViewSelectedListener : OnItemViewSelectedListener {
        override fun onItemSelected(itemViewHolder: Presenter.ViewHolder?, item: Any?, rowViewHolder: RowPresenter.ViewHolder, row: Row) {
            if (item is IptvItem) {
                backgroundUri = item.backdropUrl ?: item.coverUrl
                startBackgroundTimer()
            }
        }
    }

    private fun updateBackground(uri: String?) {
        if (uri.isNullOrBlank()) {
            backgroundManager.drawable = defaultBackground
            return
        }
        Glide.with(requireContext())
            .load(uri)
            .centerCrop()
            .error(defaultBackground)
            .into(object : CustomTarget<Drawable>(metrics.widthPixels, metrics.heightPixels) {
                override fun onResourceReady(resource: Drawable, transition: Transition<in Drawable>?) {
                    backgroundManager.drawable = resource
                }
                override fun onLoadCleared(placeholder: Drawable?) {
                }
            })
        backgroundTimer?.cancel()
    }

    private fun startBackgroundTimer() {
        backgroundTimer?.cancel()
        backgroundTimer = Timer()
        backgroundTimer?.schedule(object : TimerTask() {
            override fun run() {
                handler.post { updateBackground(backgroundUri) }
            }
        }, 280L)
    }

    companion object {
        private const val ACTION_SYNC = "sync"
        private const val ACTION_SYNC_INTERVAL = "syncInterval"
        private const val ACTION_REFRESH = "refresh"
        private const val ACTION_EDIT_LOGIN = "editLogin"
        private const val ACTION_LOGOUT = "logout"
        private const val ACTION_SEARCH = "search"
        private const val ACTION_BROWSE_RECENT = "browseRecent"
        private const val ACTION_BROWSE_LIVE = "browseLive"
        private const val ACTION_BROWSE_MOVIES = "browseMovies"
        private const val ACTION_BROWSE_SHOWS = "browseShows"
        private const val ACTION_BROWSE_WATCHLIST = "browseWatchlist"
        private const val ACTION_BROWSE_AI_PICKS = "browseAiPicks"
        private const val ACTION_CATEGORIES = "categories"
        private const val ACTION_PROFILES = "profiles"
        private const val ACTION_CLEAN = "clean"
        private const val ACTION_SETTINGS = "settings"
        private const val ACTION_ANDROID_WEBSERVER = "androidWebServer"
        private const val ACTION_SOCIAL_INBOX = "socialInbox"
        private const val ACTION_SOCIAL_PEOPLE = "socialPeople"
        private const val ACTION_LIVE_GUIDE = "liveGuide"
        private const val ACTION_AI_MODES = "aiModes"
        private const val ACTION_CATALOG_INSIGHTS = "catalogInsights"
        private const val ACTION_ADMIN_DASHBOARD = "adminDashboard"
    }
}

class PlaybackActivity : FragmentActivity() {

    private val progressRunnable = object : Runnable {
        override fun run() {
            saveProgressLocally()
            handler.postDelayed(this, PROGRESS_SAVE_INTERVAL_MS)
        }
    }

    private val hideWatchPartyHintRunnable = Runnable {
        findViewById<android.view.View>(R.id.watchPartyHint)?.visibility = android.view.View.GONE

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        window.addFlags(WindowManager.LayoutParams.FLAG_KEEP_SCREEN_ON)
        setContentView(R.layout.activity_player)

        watchRepository = WatchRepository(this)
        credentialStore = CredentialStore(this)
        val credentials = credentialStore.getAny()
        aiSyncClient = AiSyncClient(
            credentials?.syncServerUrl,
            credentials?.syncServerUsername,
            credentials?.syncServerPassword,
            credentials?.syncServerToken
        )
        traktApiClient = credentials?.let(::TraktApiClient)
            ?: TraktApiClient(IptvCredentials("", "", "", userId = ""))
        socialSettings = SocialSettings(this)
        outboxStore = SyncOutboxStore(this)
        item = intent.serializableExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, IptvItem::class.java)

        if (item?.streamUrl.isNullOrBlank()) {
            Toast.makeText(this, "This item does not have a playable stream.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
            finish()
            return
        }

        resumePositionMs = savedInstanceState?.getLong(STATE_POSITION_MS)
            ?: item?.let { watchRepository.getItemProgress(it.stableKey) }
            ?: 0L
        playWhenReady = savedInstanceState?.getBoolean(STATE_PLAY_WHEN_READY, true) ?: true
        isSocialPanelVisible = savedInstanceState?.getBoolean(STATE_SOCIAL_VISIBLE, false) ?: false
    }

    override fun onStart() {
        super.onStart()
        initializePlayer()
        handler.removeCallbacks(progressRunnable)
        handler.postDelayed(progressRunnable, PROGRESS_SAVE_INTERVAL_MS)
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        capturePlayerState()
        outState.putLong(STATE_POSITION_MS, resumePositionMs)
        outState.putBoolean(STATE_PLAY_WHEN_READY, playWhenReady)
        outState.putBoolean(STATE_SOCIAL_VISIBLE, isSocialPanelVisible)
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
    }

    private fun initializePlayer() {
        if (player != null) return
        val currentItem = item ?: return
        val streamUrl = currentItem.streamUrl ?: return
        val selector = DefaultTrackSelector(this)
        trackSelector = selector
        val loadControl = DefaultLoadControl.Builder()
            .setBufferDurationsMs(
                if (currentItem.contentType == ContentType.LIVE) 8_000 else 20_000,
                if (currentItem.contentType == ContentType.LIVE) 30_000 else 90_000,
                1_500,
                3_000
            )
            .setPrioritizeTimeOverSizeThresholds(true)
            .build()
        val playerView = findViewById<PlayerView>(R.id.playerView)
        player = ExoPlayer.Builder(this)
            .setTrackSelector(selector)
            .setLoadControl(loadControl)
            .setSeekBackIncrementMs(10_000)
            .setSeekForwardIncrementMs(10_000)
            .build()
            .also { exoPlayer ->
                playerView.player = exoPlayer
                exoPlayer.setMediaItem(buildMediaItem(currentItem, streamUrl))
                if (resumePositionMs > MIN_RESUME_POSITION_MS && currentItem.contentType != ContentType.LIVE) {
                    exoPlayer.seekTo(resumePositionMs)
                }
                exoPlayer.playWhenReady = playWhenReady
                exoPlayer.addListener(playerListener)
                exoPlayer.prepare()
            }

    }

    private fun buildMediaItem(currentItem: IptvItem, streamUrl: String): MediaItem {
        val builder = MediaItem.Builder().setUri(streamUrl)
        currentItem.subtitleUrl?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { subtitleUrl ->
            val mime = when {
                subtitleUrl.endsWith(".vtt", ignoreCase = true) -> MimeTypes.TEXT_VTT
                subtitleUrl.endsWith(".ttml", ignoreCase = true) -> MimeTypes.APPLICATION_TTML
                else -> MimeTypes.APPLICATION_SUBRIP
            }
            builder.setSubtitleConfigurations(
                listOf(
                    MediaItem.SubtitleConfiguration.Builder(android.net.Uri.parse(subtitleUrl))
                        .setMimeType(mime)
                        .setSelectionFlags(C.SELECTION_FLAG_DEFAULT)
                        .build()
                )
            )
        }
        return builder.build()
    }

    private val playerListener = object : Player.Listener {
        override fun onPlaybackStateChanged(playbackState: Int) {
            when (playbackState) {
                Player.STATE_READY -> retryCount = 0
                Player.STATE_ENDED -> {
                    saveProgressLocally()
                    enqueueWatchEvent()
                }
            }
        }

        override fun onPlayerError(error: PlaybackException) {
            if (retryCount < MAX_AUTOMATIC_RETRIES) {
                retryCount += 1
                val delayMs = 1_000L shl (retryCount - 1)
                showWatchPartyHint("Playback interrupted. Retrying in ${delayMs / 1000}s\u2026")
                handler.postDelayed({ player?.prepare(); player?.play() }, delayMs)
            } else {
                Toast.makeText(
                    this@PlaybackActivity,
                    "Playback failed: ${error.errorCodeName}. Press play to retry.",
                    Toast.LENGTH_LONG
                ).show()
                findViewById<PlayerView>(R.id.playerView).showController()
            }
        }
    }

    override fun onKeyDown(keyCode: Int, event: KeyEvent?): Boolean {
        val currentPlayer = player ?: return super.onKeyDown(keyCode, event)
        when (keyCode) {
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_DPAD_CENTER,
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_ENTER,
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_MEDIA_PLAY_PAUSE -> {
                if (currentPlayer.playerError != null) {
                    retryCount = 0
                    currentPlayer.prepare()
                    currentPlayer.play()
                } else if (currentPlayer.isPlaying) currentPlayer.pause() else currentPlayer.play()
                playerView().showController()
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_DPAD_LEFT, KeyEvent.KEYCODE_MEDIA_REWIND -> {
                currentPlayer.seekBack()
                playerView().showController()
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_DPAD_RIGHT -> {
                if (!isSocialPanelVisible && socialSettings.isConfigured() && event?.isLongPress == true) {
                    toggleSocialPanel(true)
                    return true
                }
                if (!isSocialPanelVisible) {
                    currentPlayer.seekForward()
                    playerView().showController()
                    return true
                }
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_MEDIA_FAST_FORWARD -> {
                currentPlayer.seekForward()
                playerView().showController()
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_DPAD_UP -> {
                if (item?.contentType != ContentType.LIVE) {
                    safeSeek(currentPlayer.currentPosition + 60_000)
                    return true
                }
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_DPAD_DOWN -> {
                if (item?.contentType != ContentType.LIVE) {
                    safeSeek(currentPlayer.currentPosition - 60_000)
                    return true
                }
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_INFO, KeyEvent.KEYCODE_I -> {
                playerView().showController()
                if (socialSettings.isConfigured()) showWatchPartyHint("Press C to toggle group chat")
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_C -> {
                if (socialSettings.isConfigured() && item?.contentType != ContentType.LIVE) {
                    toggleSocialPanel(!isSocialPanelVisible)
                    return true
                }
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_BACK -> {
                if (isSocialPanelVisible) {
                    toggleSocialPanel(false)
                    return true
                }
                if (playerView().isControllerFullyVisible) {
                    playerView().hideController()
                    return true
                }
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_CAPTIONS, KeyEvent.KEYCODE_S -> {
                showTrackSelection(C.TRACK_TYPE_TEXT, "Select Subtitles")
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_M, KeyEvent.KEYCODE_MENU, KeyEvent.KEYCODE_A -> {
                showTrackSelection(C.TRACK_TYPE_AUDIO, "Select Audio")
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_L -> {
                rateCurrentItem(1)
                return true
            }
            KeyEvent.KEYCODE_D -> {
                rateCurrentItem(-1)
                return true
            }
        }
        return super.onKeyDown(keyCode, event)
    }

    private fun safeSeek(targetMs: Long) {
        val currentPlayer = player ?: return
        val duration = currentPlayer.duration
        val upperBound = if (duration == C.TIME_UNSET || duration <= 0L) Long.MAX_VALUE else duration
        currentPlayer.seekTo(targetMs.coerceIn(0L, upperBound))
        playerView().showController()
    }

    private fun rateCurrentItem(rating: Int) {
        val currentItem = item ?: return
        val currentRating = watchRepository.getRating(currentItem)
        val nextRating = if (currentRating == rating) 0 else rating
        watchRepository.setRating(currentItem, nextRating)
        Toast.makeText(
            this,
            when (nextRating) {
                1 -> "Marked as liked"
                -1 -> "Marked as disliked"
                else -> "Rating cleared"
            },
            Toast.LENGTH_SHORT
        ).show()

    private fun serverProfileId(credentials: IptvCredentials): String {
        return ProfileStore(this).getCurrentProfile().id
    }

    private fun showTrackSelection(trackType: Int, title: String) {
        val currentPlayer = player ?: return
        TrackSelectionDialogBuilder(this, title, currentPlayer, trackType).build().show()
    }

    private fun toggleSocialPanel(show: Boolean) {
        if (!socialSettings.isConfigured()) return
        isSocialPanelVisible = show
        val panel = findViewById<android.view.View>(R.id.socialPanel)
        panel.visibility = if (show) android.view.View.VISIBLE else android.view.View.GONE
        findViewById<android.view.View>(R.id.watchPartyHint).visibility = android.view.View.GONE
        if (show) {
            val currentItem = item ?: return
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(R.id.socialPanel, com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social.ChatPanelFragment.newInstance(currentItem))
                .commit()
            panel.requestFocus()
        } else {
            playerView().requestFocus()
            showWatchPartyHint("Press C to reopen group chat")
        }
    }

    private fun showWatchPartyHint(text: String) {
        val hint = findViewById<android.widget.TextView>(R.id.watchPartyHint)
        hint.text = text
        hint.visibility = android.view.View.VISIBLE
        handler.removeCallbacks(hideWatchPartyHintRunnable)
        handler.postDelayed(hideWatchPartyHintRunnable, 6_000L)
    }

    private fun playerView(): PlayerView = findViewById(R.id.playerView)

    override fun onStop() {
        capturePlayerState()
        saveProgressLocally()
        enqueueWatchEvent()
        handler.removeCallbacks(progressRunnable)
        handler.removeCallbacks(hideWatchPartyHintRunnable)
        releasePlayer()
        super.onStop()
    }

    private fun capturePlayerState() {
        player?.let {
            resumePositionMs = it.currentPosition.coerceAtLeast(0L)
            playWhenReady = it.playWhenReady
        }
    }

    private fun releasePlayer() {
        playerView().player = null
        player?.removeListener(playerListener)
        player?.release()
        player = null
        trackSelector = null
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        scope.cancel()
        super.onDestroy()
    }

    private fun saveProgressLocally() {
        val currentItem = item ?: return
        val currentPlayer = player ?: return
        val duration = currentPlayer.duration.takeIf { it != C.TIME_UNSET && it > 0L } ?: 0L
        watchRepository.saveProgress(currentItem, currentPlayer.currentPosition.coerceAtLeast(0L), duration)
    }

    private fun enqueueWatchEvent() {
        val currentItem = item ?: return
        val credentials = credentialStore.getAny() ?: return
        val currentPlayer = player
        val position = currentPlayer?.currentPosition?.coerceAtLeast(0L) ?: resumePositionMs
        val duration = currentPlayer?.duration?.takeIf { it != C.TIME_UNSET && it > 0L }
            ?: currentItem.durationMs.coerceAtLeast(0L)
        if (position <= 0L && currentItem.contentType != ContentType.LIVE) return
        val completed = duration > 0L && position >= duration * 0.9
        if (kotlin.math.abs(position - lastEnqueuedPositionMs) < 1_000L && completed == lastEnqueuedCompleted) return
        lastEnqueuedPositionMs = position
        lastEnqueuedCompleted = completed

        if (aiSyncClient.isConfigured()) {
            val event = watchRepository.buildWatchEvent(
                userId = credentials.userId,
                item = currentItem,
                positionMs = position,
                durationMs = duration,
                serverUsername = credentials.syncServerUsername
            )
            outboxStore.enqueue(SyncOutboxStore.KIND_WATCH_EVENT, event)
            SyncOutboxWorker.enqueue(this)
        }

        if (completed && traktApiClient.isUserLinked() && currentItem.contentType != ContentType.LIVE) {
            scope.launch { traktApiClient.syncHistoryItem(currentItem) }
        }
    }

    companion object {
        const val EXTRA_SHOW_CHAT = "SHOW_CHAT"
        private const val STATE_POSITION_MS = "position_ms"
        private const val STATE_PLAY_WHEN_READY = "play_when_ready"
        private const val STATE_SOCIAL_VISIBLE = "social_visible"
        private const val MIN_RESUME_POSITION_MS = 5_000L
        private const val PROGRESS_SAVE_INTERVAL_MS = 15_000L
        private const val MAX_AUTOMATIC_RETRIES = 3
    }
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.profiles

import android.graphics.Color
import android.graphics.Typeface
import android.view.Gravity
import android.view.ViewGroup
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.UserProfile
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi

class ProfilePresenter : Presenter() {
    override fun onCreateViewHolder(parent: ViewGroup): ViewHolder {
        val view = TextView(parent.context)
        view.layoutParams = ViewGroup.MarginLayoutParams(TvUi.dp(parent.context, 360), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 180)).apply {
            setMargins(TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8))
        }
        view.gravity = Gravity.CENTER
        view.textSize = 24f
        view.typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
        view.setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
        TvUi.applyFocusableTile(view)
        return ViewHolder(view)
    }

    override fun onBindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder, item: Any?) {
        (viewHolder.view as TextView).text = when (item) {
            is UserProfile -> if (item.isKidsProfile) "${item.name}\nKids" else item.name
            is IptvItem -> "+\n${item.title}"
            else -> item.toString()
        }
    }

    override fun onUnbindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder) = Unit
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/profiles/ProfilesActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.profiles

import android.os.Bundle
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import androidx.leanback.app.BrowseSupportFragment
import androidx.leanback.widget.ArrayObjectAdapter
import androidx.leanback.widget.HeaderItem
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRow
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRowPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.OnItemViewClickedListener
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileHomeSettings
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.UserProfile
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.CardPresenter

class ProfilesActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        if (savedInstanceState == null) {
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(android.R.id.content, ProfilesFragment())
                .commitNow()
        }
    }

    class ProfilesFragment : BrowseSupportFragment() {
        private lateinit var profileStore: ProfileStore
        private lateinit var homeSettings: ProfileHomeSettings

        override fun onActivityCreated(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onActivityCreated(savedInstanceState)
            profileStore = ProfileStore(requireContext())
            homeSettings = ProfileHomeSettings(requireContext())
            title = getString(R.string.profile_title)
            headersState = HEADERS_DISABLED
            brandColor = resources.getColor(R.color.fastlane_background, null)
            loadRows()
            onItemViewClickedListener = OnItemViewClickedListener { _, item, _, _ ->
                when (item) {
                    is UserProfile -> {
                        profileStore.setCurrentProfile(item)
                        Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Switched to ${item.name}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                        requireActivity().finish()
                    }
                    is IptvItem -> {
                        when {
                            item.actionKey == ACTION_ADD_GUEST -> {
                                val newProfile = profileStore.addProfile("Guest")
                                profileStore.setCurrentProfile(newProfile)
                                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "Added Guest profile", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                                requireActivity().finish()
                            }
                            item.actionKey?.startsWith(ACTION_TOGGLE_PREFIX) == true -> {
                                val rowName = item.actionKey!!.removePrefix(ACTION_TOGGLE_PREFIX)
                                val row = runCatching { ProfileHomeSettings.HomeRow.valueOf(rowName) }.getOrNull() ?: return@OnItemViewClickedListener
                                val enabled = homeSettings.toggleRow(profileStore.getCurrentProfile().id, row)
                                Toast.makeText(requireContext(), "${row.label} ${if (enabled) "shown" else "hidden"} on Home", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                                loadRows()
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        private fun loadRows() {
            val rows = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter())
            val adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ProfilePresenter())
            profileStore.getProfiles().forEach { adapter.add(it) }
            adapter.add(IptvItem(title = getString(R.string.add_guest_profile), contentType = ContentType.ACTION, actionKey = ACTION_ADD_GUEST))
            rows.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(1, getString(R.string.profiles)), adapter))
            val currentProfile = profileStore.getCurrentProfile()
            val homeAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.COMPACT))
            ProfileHomeSettings.HomeRow.values().forEach { row ->
                val enabled = homeSettings.isRowEnabled(currentProfile.id, row)
                homeAdapter.add(
                    IptvItem(
                        title = if (enabled) "Hide ${row.label}" else "Show ${row.label}",
                        sourceLabel = "Home row for ${currentProfile.name}",
                        contentType = ContentType.ACTION,
                        actionKey = ACTION_TOGGLE_PREFIX + row.name
                    )
                )
            }
            rows.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(2, "Home Rows"), homeAdapter))
            this.adapter = rows
        }

        companion object {
            private const val ACTION_ADD_GUEST = "addGuest"
            private const val ACTION_TOGGLE_PREFIX = "toggleHome:"
        }
    }
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.search

import android.content.Intent
import android.os.Bundle
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import androidx.leanback.app.SearchSupportFragment
import androidx.leanback.widget.ArrayObjectAdapter
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRow
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRowPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.HeaderItem
import androidx.leanback.widget.OnItemViewClickedListener
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.Row
import androidx.leanback.widget.RowPresenter
import androidx.lifecycle.lifecycleScope
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.TraktApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.CardPresenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.GridItemPresenter
import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
import kotlinx.coroutines.Job
import kotlinx.coroutines.delay
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import kotlinx.coroutines.withContext

class SearchActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        if (savedInstanceState == null) {
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(android.R.id.content, UniversalSearchFragment())
                .commitNow()
        }
    }

    class UniversalSearchFragment : SearchSupportFragment(), SearchSupportFragment.SearchResultProvider {
        private lateinit var rowsAdapter: ArrayObjectAdapter
        private lateinit var catalogStore: CatalogStore
        private var lastQuery: String = ""
        private var searchJob: Job? = null

        override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
            catalogStore = CatalogStore(requireContext())
            rowsAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter())
            setSearchResultProvider(this)
            setOnItemViewClickedListener(OnItemViewClickedListener { _, item, _, _ ->
                if (item is IptvItem && item.contentType != ContentType.ACTION) {
                    val intent = Intent(requireContext(), DetailsActivity::class.java)
                    intent.putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item)
                    startActivity(intent)
                }
            })
        }

        override fun getResultsAdapter(): ArrayObjectAdapter = rowsAdapter

        override fun onQueryTextChange(newQuery: String): Boolean {
            runSearch(newQuery)
            return true
        }

        override fun onQueryTextSubmit(query: String): Boolean {
            runSearch(query)
            return true
        }

        private fun runSearch(query: String) {
            val cleaned = query.trim()
            if (cleaned == lastQuery) return
            lastQuery = cleaned
            searchJob?.cancel()
            rowsAdapter.clear()
            if (cleaned.length < 2) {
                addStatusRow("Type at least 2 characters", "Search movies, shows, channels, and metadata.")
                return
            }
            addStatusRow("Searching \"$cleaned\"", "Results will update as sources respond.")

            searchJob = lifecycleScope.launch {
                delay(250)
                rowsAdapter.clear()
                val localMatches = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { catalogStore.search(cleaned) }
                addLocalRows(localMatches)

                val credentials = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { CredentialStore(requireContext()).get() }
                if (credentials == null && localMatches.isEmpty()) {
                    addStatusRow("No results", "Check login settings or try a different search.")
                    return@launch
                }
                if (credentials != null) {
                    val aiClient = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken)
                    if (aiClient.isConfigured()) {
                        val aiMatches = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { aiClient.naturalSearch(credentials.userId, cleaned).getOrDefault(emptyList()) }
                        if (aiMatches.isNotEmpty()) {
                            val aiAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.POSTER))
                            aiMatches.forEach { aiAdapter.add(it) }
                            rowsAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "AI Smart Search"), aiAdapter))
                        }
                    }

                    val traktMatches = withContext(Dispatchers.IO) { runCatching { TraktApiClient(credentials).search(cleaned, 40) }.getOrDefault(emptyList()) }
                    if (traktMatches.isNotEmpty()) {
                        val traktAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(CardPresenter(CardPresenter.CardStyle.POSTER))
                        traktMatches.forEach { traktAdapter.add(it) }
                        rowsAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(2, "Trakt Search"), traktAdapter))
                    }
                    if (rowsAdapter.size() == 0) {
                        addStatusRow("No results for \"$cleaned\"", "Try fewer words or check catalog sync settings.")
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        private fun addLocalRows(localMatches: List<IptvItem>) {
            val groups = listOf(
                ContentType.MOVIE to "IPTV Movies",
                ContentType.SERIES to "IPTV Shows",
                ContentType.LIVE to "IPTV Live"
            )
            groups.forEach { (type, label) ->
                val items = localMatches.filter { it.contentType == type }
                if (items.isNotEmpty()) {
                    val style = if (type == ContentType.LIVE) CardPresenter.CardStyle.LANDSCAPE else CardPresenter.CardStyle.POSTER
                    val localAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(CardPresenter(style))
                    items.forEach { localAdapter.add(it) }
                    rowsAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(type.ordinal.toLong() + 1L, "$label (${items.size})"), localAdapter))
                }
            }
        }

        private fun addStatusRow(title: String, subtitle: String) {
            val adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
            adapter.add(IptvItem(title = title, sourceLabel = subtitle, contentType = ContentType.ACTION))
            rowsAdapter.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(99, "Search"), adapter))
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/series/SeriesHubActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.series

import android.content.Intent
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.ScrollView
import android.widget.TextView
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.WatchRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.playback.PlaybackActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.serializableExtra
import kotlinx.coroutines.MainScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.cancel
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class SeriesHubActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    private val scope = MainScope()
    private lateinit var container: LinearLayout
    private lateinit var watchRepository: WatchRepository
    private var series: IptvItem? = null

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        watchRepository = WatchRepository(this)
        series = intent.serializableExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, IptvItem::class.java)
        val scroll = ScrollView(this).apply { setBackgroundResource(R.drawable.default_background); isFillViewport = true }
        container = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 36), TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 36))
        }
        scroll.addView(container)
        setContentView(scroll)
        loadEpisodes()
    }

    override fun onDestroy() { scope.cancel(); super.onDestroy() }

    private fun loadEpisodes() {
        val currentSeries = series ?: run { finish(); return }
        container.removeAllViews()
        container.addView(title(currentSeries.title), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help("Loading seasons and episode progress\u2026"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        val credentials = CredentialStore(this).get()
        if (credentials == null) {
            container.addView(help("IPTV credentials are missing."), TvUi.matchWrap())
            return
        }
        scope.launch {
            val episodes = runCatching { XtreamApiClient(credentials).getSeriesEpisodes(currentSeries) }.getOrDefault(emptyList())
            if (episodes.isEmpty()) {
                Toast.makeText(this@SeriesHubActivity, "No episodes returned for this series.", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                return@launch
            }
            renderEpisodes(episodes)
        }
    }

    private fun renderEpisodes(episodes: List<IptvItem>) {
        container.removeAllViews()
        val currentSeries = series ?: return
        val nextEpisode = episodes.firstOrNull { watchRepository.getItemProgress(it.stableKey) <= 0L }
            ?: episodes.firstOrNull { !it.completed }
            ?: episodes.first()
        container.addView(title(currentSeries.title), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(help("${episodes.mapNotNull { it.seasonNumber }.distinct().size} seasons \u2022 ${episodes.size} episodes"), TvUi.matchWrap())
        container.addView(TvUi.button(this, "Play next: ${nextEpisode.title}", TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY) { play(nextEpisode) }, fieldParams())

        episodes.groupBy { it.seasonNumber ?: 0 }.toSortedMap().forEach { (season, seasonEpisodes) ->
            container.addView(section(if (season > 0) "Season $season" else "Episodes"), TvUi.matchWrap())
            seasonEpisodes.sortedBy { it.episodeNumber ?: 0 }.forEach { episode ->
                val progress = watchRepository.getItemProgress(episode.stableKey)
                val label = buildString {
                    append(episode.title)
                    if (progress > 0L) append(" \u2022 ${progress / 60000}m watched")
                }
                container.addView(TvUi.button(this, label) { play(episode) }, fieldParams())
            }
        }
    }

    private fun play(item: IptvItem) = startActivity(Intent(this, PlaybackActivity::class.java).putExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item))
    private fun fieldParams(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply { setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 10)) }
    private fun title(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 34f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); gravity = Gravity.START; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 12)) }
    private fun section(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(Color.WHITE); textSize = 20f; setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD); setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 8), 0, TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 8)) }
    private fun help(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply { this.text = text; setTextColor(0xFFDDDDDD.toInt()); textSize = 14f; setPadding(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@SeriesHubActivity, 8)) }
}

            panel.addView(button("Test Social Connection") { testSocialConnection() }, fieldParams())
        })

        container.addView(settingsPanel("Save Changes") { panel ->
            panel.addView(button(getString(R.string.save), TvUi.ButtonTone.PRIMARY) { saveSettings(showMessage = true) }, fieldParams())
        })
        progressBar = ProgressBar(this).apply { visibility = View.GONE }
        container.addView(progressBar, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply {
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL
            topMargin = TvUi.dp(this@SettingsActivity, 18)
        })
        messageView = TextView(this).apply {
            setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(this@SettingsActivity, android.R.color.white))
            textSize = 16f
            setPadding(0, 18, 0, 0)
        }
        container.addView(messageView)

        return scrollView
    }

    private fun settingsPanel(title: String, helper: String? = null, build: (LinearLayout) -> Unit): LinearLayout {
        return TvUi.verticalPanel(this).apply {
            addView(section(title), TvUi.matchWrap())
            if (!helper.isNullOrBlank()) addView(help(helper), TvUi.matchWrap())
            build(this)
            layoutParams = TvUi.centeredPanelParamsWithBottomMargin(this@SettingsActivity)
        }
    }

    private fun fieldParams(): LinearLayout.LayoutParams {
        return LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT).apply {
            setMargins(0, 0, 0, TvUi.dp(this@SettingsActivity, 10))
        }
    }

    private fun bindSavedValues() {
        val credentials = credentialStore.get()
        iptvUrlInput.setText(credentials?.serverUrl.orEmpty())
        iptvUsernameInput.setText(credentials?.username.orEmpty())
        iptvPasswordInput.setText(credentials?.password.orEmpty())
        serverUrlInput.setText(credentials?.syncServerUrl ?: CredentialStore.DEFAULT_SYNC_SERVER_URL)
        serverUsernameInput.setText(credentials?.syncServerUsername.orEmpty())
        serverPasswordInput.setText(credentials?.syncServerPassword.orEmpty())
        pairedServerToken = credentials?.syncServerToken
        traktClientIdInput.setText(credentials?.traktClientId.orEmpty())
        traktClientSecretInput.setText(credentials?.traktClientSecret.orEmpty())
        traktAccessTokenInput.setText(credentials?.traktAccessToken.orEmpty())
        traktRefreshTokenInput.setText(credentials?.traktRefreshToken.orEmpty())
        refreshDaysInput.setText(credentialStore.getSyncIntervalDays().toString())
        socialUrlInput.setText(socialSettings.getServerUrl().orEmpty())
        socialNameInput.setText(socialSettings.getDisplayName().orEmpty())
        socialTokenInput.setText(socialSettings.getToken().orEmpty())
    }

    private fun currentCredentials(): IptvCredentials? {
        val iptvUrl = iptvUrlInput.text.toString().trim()
        val iptvUsername = iptvUsernameInput.text.toString().trim()
        val iptvPassword = iptvPasswordInput.text.toString().trim()
        if (iptvUrl.isBlank() || iptvUsername.isBlank() || iptvPassword.isBlank()) {
            val msg = getString(R.string.login_required_fields)
            messageView.text = msg
            Toast.makeText(this, msg, Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
            return null
        }
        return IptvCredentials(
            serverUrl = iptvUrl,
            username = iptvUsername,
            password = iptvPassword,
            syncServerUrl = serverUrlInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            syncServerUsername = serverUsernameInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            syncServerPassword = serverPasswordInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            syncServerToken = pairedServerToken,
            traktClientId = traktClientIdInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            traktClientSecret = traktClientSecretInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            traktAccessToken = traktAccessTokenInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            traktRefreshToken = traktRefreshTokenInput.text.toString().trim().takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
            userId = credentialStore.getOrCreateUserId()
        )
    }

    private fun saveSettings(showMessage: Boolean): IptvCredentials? {
        val credentials = currentCredentials() ?: return null
        credentialStore.save(credentials)
        credentialStore.setSyncIntervalDays(refreshDaysInput.text.toString().toIntOrNull()?.coerceIn(1, 30) ?: 3)
        CatalogRefreshScheduler.schedule(this)
        socialSettings.setServerUrl(socialUrlInput.text.toString())
        socialSettings.setDisplayName(socialNameInput.text.toString())
        socialSettings.setToken(socialTokenInput.text.toString())
        if (showMessage) messageView.text = "Settings saved."
        return credentials
    }

    private fun syncWatchNow() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        if (!AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken).isConfigured()) {
            messageView.text = "Configure a secure AI server first."
            return
        }
        val snapshot = WatchRepository(this).buildSnapshot(credentials.userId, credentials.syncServerUsername)
        SyncOutboxStore(this).enqueue(SyncOutboxStore.KIND_WATCH_SNAPSHOT, snapshot)
        SyncOutboxWorker.enqueue(this)
        messageView.text = "Watch sync queued. It will retry automatically if the server is unavailable."
    }

    private fun checkIptvLogin() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        setBusy(true, "Checking IPTV login...")
        scope.launch {
            val result = runCatching { XtreamApiClient(credentials).validateLogin() }
            setBusy(false, if (result.getOrDefault(false)) "IPTV login works." else result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: getString(R.string.login_failed))
        }
    }

    private fun checkServerConnection() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        setBusy(true, "Checking server connection...")
        scope.launch {
            val result = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken).checkConnection()
            val status = result.getOrNull()
            val message = if (status?.ok == true) {
                val name = status.displayName ?: status.username ?: credentials.syncServerUsername ?: "server user"
                val role = if (status.isAdmin) "admin" else "viewer"
                val tmdb = if (status.tmdbLinked) " TMDb linked${status.tmdbUsername?.let { " as $it" } ?: ""}." else " TMDb account not linked; server metadata can still work if TMDb is configured there."
                "Server login works as $name ($role).$tmdb"
            } else {
                result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "Server did not respond successfully."
            }
            setBusy(false, message)
        }
    }

    private fun startServerPairing() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        if (credentials.syncServerUrl.isNullOrBlank()) {
            setBusy(false, "Enter the AI server URL first.")
            return
        }
        setBusy(true, "Starting device pairing...")
        scope.launch {
            val client = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken)
            val start = client.startPairing("${Build.MANUFACTURER} ${Build.MODEL}".trim()).getOrElse { error ->
                setBusy(false, error.message ?: "Could not start pairing.")
                return@launch
            }
            setBusy(true, "Open ${start.pairingUrl} and enter code ${start.deviceCode}. Waiting for approval...")
            repeat(PAIRING_POLL_LIMIT) {
                delay(start.pollIntervalSeconds * 1000L)
                val status = client.getPairingStatus(start.deviceCode).getOrNull()
                when (status?.status) {
                    "approved" -> {
                        val token = status.syncServerToken
                        val username = status.syncServerUsername
                        if (token.isNullOrBlank() || username.isNullOrBlank()) {
                            setBusy(false, "Pairing approved, but the server did not return a device token.")
                            return@launch
                        }
                        pairedServerToken = token
                        serverUrlInput.setText(status.syncServerUrl ?: credentials.syncServerUrl.orEmpty())
                        serverUsernameInput.setText(username)
                        serverPasswordInput.setText("")
                        val pairedCredentials = credentials.copy(
                            syncServerUrl = status.syncServerUrl ?: credentials.syncServerUrl,
                            syncServerUsername = username,
                            syncServerPassword = null,
                            syncServerToken = token
                        )
                        credentialStore.save(pairedCredentials)
                        CatalogRefreshScheduler.schedule(this@SettingsActivity)
                        setBusy(false, "Paired as ${status.displayName ?: username}. Server token saved.")
                        return@launch
                    }
                    "expired" -> {
                        setBusy(false, "Pairing code expired. Start pairing again.")
                        return@launch
                    }
                    "cancelled" -> {
                        setBusy(false, "Pairing was cancelled.")
                        return@launch
                    }
                }
            }
            setBusy(false, "Pairing timed out. Start pairing again when you are ready.")
        }
    }

    private fun startTmdbLink() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        setBusy(true, "Requesting TMDb approval link...")
        scope.launch {
            val result = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken).requestTmdbToken()
            val token = result.getOrNull()
            if (token == null || token.requestToken.isBlank() || token.authenticationUrl.isBlank()) {
                setBusy(false, result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "Could not start TMDb link.")
                return@launch
            }
            pendingTmdbRequestToken = token.requestToken
            try {
                startActivity(Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(token.authenticationUrl)))
                setBusy(false, "Approve TMDb in the browser, then return here and choose Complete TMDb Link.")
            } catch (error: ActivityNotFoundException) {
                setBusy(false, "Open this TMDb approval URL manually: ${token.authenticationUrl}")
            }
        }
    }

    private fun completeTmdbLink() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        val token = pendingTmdbRequestToken
        if (token.isNullOrBlank()) {
            setBusy(false, "Start TMDb linking first so this screen has a request token.")
            return
        }
        setBusy(true, "Completing TMDb link...")
        scope.launch {
            val result = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken).completeTmdbLink(token)
            val status = result.getOrNull()
            if (status?.tmdbLinked == true) {
                pendingTmdbRequestToken = null
                setBusy(false, "TMDb linked${status.tmdbUsername?.let { " as $it" } ?: ""}.")
            } else {
                setBusy(false, result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "TMDb link was not completed.")
            }
        }
    }

    private fun unlinkTmdb() {
        val credentials = saveSettings(showMessage = false) ?: return
        setBusy(true, "Unlinking TMDb...")
        scope.launch {
            val result = AiSyncClient(credentials.syncServerUrl, credentials.syncServerUsername, credentials.syncServerPassword, credentials.syncServerToken).unlinkTmdb()
            pendingTmdbRequestToken = null
            setBusy(false, if (result.isSuccess) "TMDb account unlinked. Public metadata enrichment can still work from the server." else result.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "Could not unlink TMDb.")
        }
    }

    private fun testSocialConnection() {
        saveSettings(showMessage = false)
        setBusy(true, "Checking social server...")
        scope.launch {
            val apiClient = com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient(socialSettings)
            val healthy = apiClient.checkHealth()
            if (healthy) {
                val token = apiClient.getSessionToken()
                setBusy(false, if (token != null) "Social server connected and session active." else "Social server healthy but session failed.")
            } else {
                setBusy(false, "Social server unreachable.")
            }
        }
    }

    private fun setBusy(isBusy: Boolean, message: String) {
        progressBar.visibility = if (isBusy) View.VISIBLE else View.GONE
        messageView.text = message
        if (!isBusy && message.isNotBlank()) {
            Toast.makeText(this, message, Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
            scrollView.post { scrollView.fullScroll(View.FOCUS_DOWN) }
        }
    }

    private fun title(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(this@SettingsActivity, android.R.color.white))
        textSize = 34f
        setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD)
        setPadding(0, 0, 0, 20)
    }

    private fun section(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(ContextCompat.getColor(this@SettingsActivity, android.R.color.white))
        textSize = 20f
        setTypeface(typeface, android.graphics.Typeface.BOLD)
        setPadding(0, 24, 0, 8)
    }

    private fun help(text: String): TextView = TextView(this).apply {
        this.text = text
        setTextColor(0xFFDDDDDD.toInt())
        textSize = 14f
        setPadding(0, 0, 0, 8)
    }

    private fun input(hint: String, inputType: Int): EditText = TvUi.input(this, hint, inputType)

    private fun button(text: String, tone: TvUi.ButtonTone = TvUi.ButtonTone.SECONDARY, onClick: () -> Unit): Button =
        TvUi.button(this, text, tone, onClick)

    companion object {
        private const val PAIRING_POLL_LIMIT = 150
    }
}
