// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/social/ChatPanelFragment.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social

import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.LayoutInflater
import android.view.View
import android.view.ViewGroup
import android.view.inputmethod.EditorInfo
import android.widget.Button
import android.widget.EditText
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.fragment.app.Fragment
import androidx.lifecycle.lifecycleScope
import androidx.recyclerview.widget.LinearLayoutManager
import androidx.recyclerview.widget.RecyclerView
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialMessage
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.details.DetailsActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.util.serializableExtra
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.collectLatest
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class ChatPanelFragment : Fragment() {
    private lateinit var socialRepository: SocialRepository
    private lateinit var chatAdapter: ChatAdapter
    private lateinit var chatList: RecyclerView
    private lateinit var messageInput: EditText
    private lateinit var chatTitle: TextView
    private lateinit var chatStatus: TextView
    private var item: IptvItem? = null
    private var roomId: String? = null

    override fun onCreateView(inflater: LayoutInflater, container: ViewGroup?, savedInstanceState: Bundle?): View? {
        val view = inflater.inflate(R.layout.fragment_chat_panel, container, false)
        chatTitle = view.findViewById(R.id.chatTitle)
        chatStatus = view.findViewById(R.id.chatStatus)
        chatList = view.findViewById(R.id.chatList)
        messageInput = view.findViewById(R.id.messageInput)
        val sendButton = view.findViewById<Button>(R.id.sendButton)
        val quickLaughButton = view.findViewById<Button>(R.id.quickLaughButton)
        val quickWowButton = view.findViewById<Button>(R.id.quickWowButton)
        val quickRewindButton = view.findViewById<Button>(R.id.quickRewindButton)

        chatAdapter = ChatAdapter()
        chatList.adapter = chatAdapter
        chatList.layoutManager = LinearLayoutManager(requireContext()).apply { stackFromEnd = true }

        messageInput.setOnEditorActionListener { _, actionId, _ ->
            if (actionId == EditorInfo.IME_ACTION_SEND) {
                sendMessage()
                true
            } else false
        }
        sendButton.setOnClickListener { sendMessage() }
        quickLaughButton.setOnClickListener { sendQuickMessage("LOL") }
        quickWowButton.setOnClickListener { sendQuickMessage("Whoa") }
        quickRewindButton.setOnClickListener {
            roomId?.let { activeRoom ->
                viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch { socialRepository.sendWatchPartyControl(activeRoom, "rewind_request") }
            }
            sendQuickMessage("Rewind that?")
        }

        val settings = SocialSettings(requireContext())
        socialRepository = SocialRepository(SocialApiClient(settings), settings)
        item = arguments?.serializableExtra(DetailsActivity.ITEM, IptvItem::class.java)
        roomId = arguments?.getString("ROOM_ID")
        chatTitle.text = item?.title?.let { "Watching $it" } ?: "Watch Party"

        loadChat()
        return view
    }

    private fun loadChat() {
        val currentItem = item
        val currentRoomId = roomId

        viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
            chatStatus.text = "Connecting to watch room..."
            socialRepository.connect()

            if (currentRoomId != null) {
                roomId = currentRoomId
                if (currentItem != null) socialRepository.announceWatching(currentItem, currentRoomId)
                socialRepository.joinRoom(currentRoomId)
                val history = socialRepository.getMessages(currentRoomId)
                chatAdapter.setMessages(history)
                scrollToLatest()
                if (currentItem != null) updateViewerStatus(currentItem) else chatStatus.text = "Room ready"
            } else if (currentItem != null) {
                val room = socialRepository.getWatchPartyRoom(currentItem)
                if (room != null) {
                    roomId = room.id
                    chatTitle.text = room.title
                    socialRepository.announceWatching(currentItem, room.id)
                    socialRepository.joinRoom(room.id)
                    val history = socialRepository.getMessages(room.id)
                    chatAdapter.setMessages(history)
                    scrollToLatest()
                    updateViewerStatus(currentItem)
                } else {
                    chatStatus.text = "Could not open a watch room. Sync catalog to the server first."
                }
            }

            socialRepository.messages.collectLatest { message ->
                if (message.roomId == roomId) {
                    chatAdapter.addMessage(message)
                    scrollToLatest(smooth = true)
                }
            }
        }

        viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
            socialRepository.isConnected.collectLatest { connected ->
                val activeRoom = roomId != null
                chatStatus.text = when {
                    connected && activeRoom -> "Live chat connected"
                    connected -> "Connected. Opening room..."
                    activeRoom -> "Offline send available"
                    else -> "Opening room..."
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private suspend fun updateViewerStatus(currentItem: IptvItem) {
        val viewers = socialRepository.getCurrentViewers(currentItem)
        val otherViewers = viewers.mapNotNull { it.user?.displayName }.distinct()
        chatStatus.text = when (otherViewers.size) {
            0 -> "Group watch room ready"
            1 -> "Watching now with ${otherViewers.first()}"
            else -> "${otherViewers.size} viewers watching now"
        }
    }

    private fun sendMessage() {
        val text = messageInput.text.toString().trim()
        val currentRoomId = roomId
        if (text.isNotEmpty() && currentRoomId != null) {
            messageInput.text.clear()
            viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
                val sent = socialRepository.sendMessageReliable(currentRoomId, text)
                if (sent != null) {
                    chatAdapter.addMessage(sent)
                    scrollToLatest(smooth = true)
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private fun sendQuickMessage(text: String) {
        messageInput.setText(text)
        sendMessage()
    }

    private fun scrollToLatest(smooth: Boolean = false) {
        val target = chatAdapter.itemCount - 1
        if (target < 0) return
        if (smooth) chatList.smoothScrollToPosition(target) else chatList.scrollToPosition(target)
    }

    override fun onDestroyView() {
        roomId?.let { socialRepository.leaveRoom(it) }
        socialRepository.disconnect()
        super.onDestroyView()
    }

    companion object {
        fun newInstance(item: IptvItem): ChatPanelFragment {
            return ChatPanelFragment().apply {
                arguments = Bundle().apply { putSerializable(DetailsActivity.ITEM, item) }
            }
        }

        fun newInstance(roomId: String): ChatPanelFragment {
            return ChatPanelFragment().apply {
                arguments = Bundle().apply { putString("ROOM_ID", roomId) }
            }
        }
    }

    private class ChatAdapter : RecyclerView.Adapter<ChatViewHolder>() {
        private val messages = mutableListOf<SocialMessage>()

        fun setMessages(newMessages: List<SocialMessage>) {
            messages.clear()
            messages.addAll(newMessages)
            notifyDataSetChanged()
        }

        fun addMessage(message: SocialMessage) {
            messages.add(message)
            notifyItemInserted(messages.size - 1)
        }

        override fun onCreateViewHolder(parent: ViewGroup, viewType: Int): ChatViewHolder {
            val view = LayoutInflater.from(parent.context).inflate(R.layout.item_chat_message, parent, false)
            return ChatViewHolder(view)
        }

        override fun onBindViewHolder(holder: ChatViewHolder, position: Int) {
            val msg = messages[position]
            holder.senderName.text = msg.senderDisplayName
            holder.messageText.text = msg.text
        }

        override fun getItemCount() = messages.size
    }

    private class ChatViewHolder(view: View) : RecyclerView.ViewHolder(view) {
        val senderName: TextView = view.findViewById(R.id.senderName)
        val messageText: TextView = view.findViewById(R.id.messageText)
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/social/SocialChatActivity.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social

import android.os.Bundle
import android.widget.FrameLayout
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R

class SocialChatActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        val container = FrameLayout(this).apply {
            id = R.id.socialPanel // Reuse ID or use a generic one
        }
        setContentView(container)

        if (savedInstanceState == null) {
            val roomId = intent.getStringExtra("ROOM_ID")
            val fragment = ChatPanelFragment().apply {
                arguments = Bundle().apply {
                    putString("ROOM_ID", roomId)
                }
            }
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(container.id, fragment)
                .commit()
        }
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/ui/social/SocialInboxActivity.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social

import android.content.Intent
import android.os.Bundle
import androidx.core.content.ContextCompat
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import androidx.leanback.app.BrowseSupportFragment
import androidx.leanback.widget.ArrayObjectAdapter
import androidx.leanback.widget.HeaderItem
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRow
import androidx.leanback.widget.ListRowPresenter
import androidx.leanback.widget.OnItemViewClickedListener
import androidx.lifecycle.lifecycleScope
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialRoom
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.main.GridItemPresenter
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class SocialInboxActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        if (savedInstanceState == null) {
            supportFragmentManager.beginTransaction()
                .replace(android.R.id.content, SocialInboxFragment())
                .commitNow()
        }
    }

    class SocialInboxFragment : BrowseSupportFragment() {
        private lateinit var socialRepository: SocialRepository

        override fun onActivityCreated(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onActivityCreated(savedInstanceState)
            val settings = SocialSettings(requireContext())
            socialRepository = SocialRepository(SocialApiClient(settings), settings)
            
            title = "Social"
            headersState = HEADERS_ENABLED
            brandColor = ContextCompat.getColor(requireContext(), R.color.fastlane_background)
            
            loadRooms()
            
            onItemViewClickedListener = OnItemViewClickedListener { _, item, _, _ ->
                if (item is SocialRoom) {
                    val intent = Intent(requireContext(), SocialChatActivity::class.java)
                    intent.putExtra("ROOM_ID", item.id)
                    intent.putExtra("ROOM_TITLE", item.title)
                    startActivity(intent)
                }
            }
        }

        private fun loadRooms() {
            adapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter()).apply {
                add(statusRow("Loading social rooms", "Checking watch parties and discussions."))
            }
            viewLifecycleOwner.lifecycleScope.launch {
                val watchPartiesResult = runCatching { socialRepository.apiClient.getRooms(roomType = "watchParty") }
                val discussionsResult = runCatching { socialRepository.apiClient.getRooms(roomType = "discussion") }
                val watchParties = watchPartiesResult.getOrDefault(emptyList())
                val discussions = discussionsResult.getOrDefault(emptyList())
                
                val rows = ArrayObjectAdapter(ListRowPresenter())
                if (watchPartiesResult.isFailure && discussionsResult.isFailure) {
                    rows.add(statusRow("Could not load social rooms", watchPartiesResult.exceptionOrNull()?.message ?: "Check social server settings."))
                    adapter = rows
                    return@launch
                }
                
                if (watchParties.isNotEmpty()) {
                    rows.add(buildRoomRow(1, "Watch Parties", watchParties))
                }
                
                if (discussions.isNotEmpty()) {
                    rows.add(buildRoomRow(2, "Discussions", discussions))
                }
                
                if (watchParties.isEmpty() && discussions.isEmpty()) {
                    val emptyAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
                    emptyAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = "No social rooms yet", contentType = ContentType.ACTION, sourceLabel = "Start a watch discussion from a title detail page."))
                    rows.add(ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "Social"), emptyAdapter))
                }
                
                adapter = rows
            }
        }

        private fun buildRoomRow(id: Long, title: String, rooms: List<SocialRoom>): ListRow {
            val presenter = SocialRoomPresenter()
            val roomAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(presenter)
            rooms.forEach { roomAdapter.add(it) }
            return ListRow(HeaderItem(id, title), roomAdapter)
        }

        private fun statusRow(title: String, subtitle: String): ListRow {
            val statusAdapter = ArrayObjectAdapter(GridItemPresenter())
            statusAdapter.add(IptvItem(title = title, contentType = ContentType.ACTION, sourceLabel = subtitle))
            return ListRow(HeaderItem(0, "Status"), statusAdapter)
        }
    }
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.social

import android.graphics.Color
import android.graphics.Typeface
import android.view.Gravity
import android.view.ViewGroup
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.leanback.widget.Presenter
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.SocialRoom
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi

class SocialRoomPresenter : Presenter() {
    override fun onCreateViewHolder(parent: ViewGroup): ViewHolder {
        val view = LinearLayout(parent.context).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(parent.context, 20), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 14), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 20), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 14))
        }
        view.layoutParams = ViewGroup.MarginLayoutParams(TvUi.dp(parent.context, 400), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 140)).apply {
            setMargins(TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8), TvUi.dp(parent.context, 8))
        }
        TvUi.applyFocusableTile(view)
        
        view.addView(TextView(parent.context).apply {
            id = android.R.id.text1
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            textSize = 18f
            typeface = Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
            maxLines = 1
        })
        
        view.addView(TextView(parent.context).apply {
            id = android.R.id.text2
            setTextColor(Color.LTGRAY)
            textSize = 14f
            maxLines = 1
        })
        
        return ViewHolder(view)
    }

    override fun onBindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder, item: Any?) {
        val room = item as SocialRoom
        val view = viewHolder.view as LinearLayout
        view.findViewById<TextView>(android.R.id.text1).text = room.title
        view.findViewById<TextView>(android.R.id.text2).text = room.lastMessage ?: "Join discussion"
    }

    override fun onUnbindViewHolder(viewHolder: ViewHolder) {}
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.web

import android.graphics.Bitmap
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.text.InputType
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.ImageView
import android.widget.LinearLayout
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.fragment.app.FragmentActivity
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.R
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.ui.common.TvUi
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.web.AndroidHostedWebServer
import com.google.zxing.BarcodeFormat
import com.google.zxing.qrcode.QRCodeWriter

class AndroidWebServerActivity : FragmentActivity() {
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
        val access = AndroidHostedWebServer.start(this)

        val root = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 64), TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 48), TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 64), TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 48))
            setBackgroundColor(0xFF101820.toInt())
        }

        val qr = ImageView(this).apply {
            setImageBitmap(createQrBitmap(access.url))
            contentDescription = getString(R.string.android_webserver_qr_description)
            setBackgroundColor(Color.WHITE)
            setPadding(18, 18, 18, 18)
        }
        root.addView(qr, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(TvUi.dp(this, 320), TvUi.dp(this, 320)))

        val textPanel = LinearLayout(this).apply {
            orientation = LinearLayout.VERTICAL
            gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
            setPadding(TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 40), 0, 0, 0)
        }
        textPanel.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = getString(R.string.android_webserver_title)
            setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
            textSize = 30f
            typeface = android.graphics.Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD
        })
        textPanel.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = access.url
            setTextColor(0xFF53D6A5.toInt())
            textSize = 24f
            inputType = InputType.TYPE_TEXT_VARIATION_URI
            setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 20), 0, 0)
        })
        textPanel.addView(TextView(this).apply {
            text = getString(R.string.android_webserver_hint) + "\n\nPairing code: ${access.pairingCode}"
            setTextColor(0xFFC6D3E1.toInt())
            textSize = 18f
            setPadding(0, TvUi.dp(this@AndroidWebServerActivity, 20), 0, 0)
        })
        root.addView(textPanel, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1f))

        setContentView(root)
    }

    private fun createQrBitmap(value: String): Bitmap {
        val size = 720
        val matrix = QRCodeWriter().encode(value, BarcodeFormat.QR_CODE, size, size)
        val bitmap = Bitmap.createBitmap(size, size, Bitmap.Config.ARGB_8888)
        for (x in 0 until size) {
            for (y in 0 until size) {
                bitmap.setPixel(x, y, if (matrix[x, y]) Color.BLACK else Color.WHITE)
            }
        }
        return bitmap
    }
}

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.util

import android.content.Intent
import android.os.Build
import java.io.Serializable

@Suppress("DEPRECATION")
fun <T : Serializable> Intent.serializableExtra(key: String, clazz: Class<T>): T? {
    return if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= 33) {
        getSerializableExtra(key, clazz)
    } else {
        getSerializableExtra(key) as? T
    }
}

@Suppress("DEPRECATION")
fun <T : Serializable> android.os.Bundle.serializableExtra(key: String, clazz: Class<T>): T? {
    return if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= 33) {
        getSerializable(key, clazz)
    } else {
        getSerializable(key) as? T
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/util/JsonExtensions.kt

package com.example.aiiptvviewer.util

import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject

fun JSONObject.optCleanString(name: String): String? {
    val value = optString(name, "").trim()
    return value.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() && !it.equals("null", ignoreCase = true) }
}

fun JSONArray.objects(): List<JSONObject> {
    val result = mutableListOf<JSONObject>()
    for (index in 0 until length()) {
        val item = optJSONObject(index)
        if (item != null) result.add(item)
    }
    return result
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/web/AndroidHostedWebServer.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.web

import android.content.Context
import android.util.Log
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.AppVersion
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CatalogStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.CredentialStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.ProfileStore
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SocialSettings
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.WatchRepository
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvCredentials
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.AiSyncClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.SocialApiClient
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.remote.XtreamApiClient
import kotlinx.coroutines.runBlocking
import org.json.JSONArray
import org.json.JSONObject
import java.io.BufferedReader
import java.io.InputStreamReader
import java.net.Inet4Address
import java.net.NetworkInterface
import java.net.ServerSocket
import java.net.URLDecoder
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets
import java.util.Locale
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean
import kotlin.concurrent.thread

object AndroidHostedWebServer {
    private const val TAG = "AndroidHostedWebServer"
    private const val DEFAULT_PORT = 8787

    private val running = AtomicBoolean(false)
    private var serverSocket: ServerSocket? = null
    private var port: Int = DEFAULT_PORT
    private lateinit var appContext: Context

    val isRunning: Boolean
        get() = running.get()

    fun start(context: Context): AccessInfo {
        appContext = context.applicationContext
        if (running.get()) return accessInfo()

        val socket = openServerSocket()
        serverSocket = socket
        port = socket.localPort
        running.set(true)

        thread(name = "android-hosted-webserver", isDaemon = true) {
            while (running.get()) {
                try {
                    val client = socket.accept()
                    thread(name = "android-hosted-webserver-client", isDaemon = true) {
                        client.use { handleClient(it) }
                    }
                } catch (error: Exception) {
                    if (running.get()) Log.w(TAG, "Local webserver accept failed", error)
                }
            }
        }

        return accessInfo()
    }

    fun stop() {
        running.set(false)
        runCatching { serverSocket?.close() }
        serverSocket = null
    }

    fun accessInfo(): AccessInfo {
        val host = localIpAddress() ?: "127.0.0.1"
        val code = LocalWebAccessStore(appContext).pairingCode()
        return AccessInfo(host = host, port = port, url = "http://$host:$port/?code=$code", pairingCode = code)
    }

    private fun openServerSocket(): ServerSocket {
        for (candidate in DEFAULT_PORT..(DEFAULT_PORT + 10)) {
            val socket = runCatching { ServerSocket(candidate) }.getOrNull()
            if (socket != null) return socket
        }
        return ServerSocket(0)
    }

    private fun handleClient(client: java.net.Socket) {
        try {
            val request = readRequest(client)
            if (request == null) {
                writeJson(client, 400, JSONObject().put("error", "Invalid request"))
                return
            }

            val query = parseQuery(request.rawPath.substringAfter("?", ""))
            val path = request.rawPath.substringBefore("?")
            val accessStore = LocalWebAccessStore(appContext)
            val pairingAccepted = query["code"]?.equals(accessStore.pairingCode(), ignoreCase = true) == true
            val authorized = pairingAccepted || isAuthorized(request, query, accessStore.sessionToken())
            when {
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/" && authorized -> writeResponse(
                    client,
                    200,
                    "text/html; charset=utf-8",
                    dashboardHtml(),
                    if (pairingAccepted) mapOf("Set-Cookie" to sessionCookie(accessStore.sessionToken())) else emptyMap()
                )
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/" -> writeResponse(client, 401, "text/html; charset=utf-8", unlockHtml())
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/local-auth" -> {
                    val supplied = request.bodyJson().optString("code")
                    if (supplied.equals(accessStore.pairingCode(), ignoreCase = true)) {
                        writeResponse(
                            client,
                            200,
                            "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                            JSONObject().put("ok", true).toString(),
                            mapOf("Set-Cookie" to sessionCookie(accessStore.sessionToken()))
                        )
                    } else {
                        writeJson(client, 401, JSONObject().put("error", "Invalid pairing code"))
                    }
                }
                !authorized -> writeJson(client, 401, JSONObject().put("error", "Local dashboard authorization required"))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/status" -> writeJson(client, 200, statusJson())
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/dashboard" -> writeJson(client, 200, dashboardJson())
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/catalog" -> writeJson(client, 200, catalogJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/catalog/categories" -> writeJson(client, 200, catalogCategoriesJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/catalog/genres" -> writeJson(client, 200, catalogGenresJson(query))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/catalog/action" -> writeJson(client, 200, catalogActionJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/catalog/explain" -> writeJson(client, 200, catalogExplainJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/catalog/similar" -> writeJson(client, 200, catalogSimilarJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/search" -> writeJson(client, 200, searchJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/top-picks" -> writeJson(client, 200, topPicksJson())
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/watch" -> writeJson(client, 200, watchJson(query))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/watch/sync" -> writeJson(client, 200, syncWatchDataJson())
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/watch/update" -> writeJson(client, 200, updateWatchRecordJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/watch/delete" -> writeJson(client, 200, deleteWatchRecordJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/ai/recommendations" -> writeJson(client, 200, aiRecommendationsJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/ai/natural-search" -> writeJson(client, 200, aiNaturalSearchJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/tmdb" -> writeJson(client, 200, tmdbJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/tmdb/watchlist" -> writeJson(client, 200, tmdbWatchlistJson())
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/social/rooms" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialRoomsJson(query))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/social/messages" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialMessagesJson(query))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/social/messages" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialSendMessageJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/social/users" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialUsersJson())
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/social/friends" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialFriendsJson())
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/social/friends" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialRequestFriendJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/social/watching" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialWatchingJson(query))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/social/parties" -> writeJson(client, 200, socialCreatePartyJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/login" -> writeResponse(client, 200, "text/html; charset=utf-8", loginHtml())
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/settings/save" -> writeJson(client, 200, saveSettingsJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "GET" && path == "/api/settings/load" -> writeJson(client, 200, loadSettingsJson())
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/settings/test-connection" -> writeJson(client, 200, testAiConnectionJson(request.bodyJson()))
                request.method == "POST" && path == "/api/settings/test-iptv" -> writeJson(client, 200, testIptvConnectionJson(request.bodyJson()))
                else -> writeJson(client, 404, JSONObject().put("error", "Not found"))
            }
        } catch (error: Exception) {
            Log.w(TAG, "Local webserver request failed", error)
            writeJson(client, 500, JSONObject().put("error", error.message ?: "Request failed"))
        }
    }

    private fun isAuthorized(request: HttpRequest, query: Map<String, String>, sessionToken: String): Boolean {
        val bearer = request.headers["authorization"]
            ?.takeIf { it.startsWith("Bearer ", ignoreCase = true) }
            ?.substringAfter(' ')
            ?.trim()
        val headerToken = request.headers["x-aiiptv-token"]
        val cookieToken = request.headers["cookie"]
            ?.split(';')
            ?.map { it.trim() }
            ?.firstOrNull { it.startsWith("aiiptv_session=") }
            ?.substringAfter('=')
        val queryToken = query["token"]
        return listOf(bearer, headerToken, cookieToken, queryToken).any { it == sessionToken }
    }

    private fun sessionCookie(token: String): String {
        return "aiiptv_session=$token; Path=/; HttpOnly; SameSite=Strict; Max-Age=86400"
    }

    private fun unlockHtml(): String = """
        <!doctype html><html lang="en"><head><meta charset="utf-8"><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1">
        <title>Unlock AI IPTV Viewer</title><style>
        :root{color-scheme:dark;font-family:system-ui,sans-serif}body{margin:0;min-height:100vh;display:grid;place-items:center;background:#020617;color:#f8fafc}.card{width:min(440px,calc(100% - 32px));padding:28px;border:1px solid #334155;border-radius:18px;background:#0f172a}input,button{width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;padding:14px;border-radius:10px;font:inherit}input{background:#020617;color:white;border:1px solid #475569;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.14em}button{margin-top:12px;border:0;background:#38bdf8;color:#082f49;font-weight:800}p{color:#94a3b8}.error{color:#fca5a5;min-height:22px}</style></head>
        <body><form class="card" id="unlock"><h1>Unlock TV Dashboard</h1><p>Enter the pairing code shown on the TV. Access is limited to this device session.</p><input id="code" autocomplete="one-time-code" maxlength="8" autofocus><button>Unlock</button><div class="error" id="error"></div></form><script>
        document.querySelector('#unlock').addEventListener('submit',async(e)=>{e.preventDefault();const response=await fetch('/api/local-auth',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify({code:document.querySelector('#code').value.trim()})});if(response.ok){location.href='/';return;}const data=await response.json().catch(()=>({}));document.querySelector('#error').textContent=data.error||'Could not unlock dashboard';});
        </script></body></html>
    """.trimIndent()

    private fun readRequest(client: java.net.Socket): HttpRequest? {
        val reader = BufferedReader(InputStreamReader(client.getInputStream(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
        val requestLine = reader.readLine().orEmpty()
        val parts = requestLine.split(" ")
        if (parts.size < 2) return null

        val headers = mutableMapOf<String, String>()
        while (true) {
            val line = reader.readLine() ?: break
            if (line.isBlank()) break
            val name = line.substringBefore(":", "").lowercase(Locale.US)
            val value = line.substringAfter(":", "").trim()
            if (name.isNotBlank()) headers[name] = value
        }

        val contentLength = headers["content-length"]?.toIntOrNull()?.coerceAtLeast(0) ?: 0
        val body = if (contentLength > 0) {
            val chars = CharArray(contentLength)
            val read = reader.read(chars, 0, contentLength).coerceAtLeast(0)
            String(chars, 0, read)
        } else {
            ""
        }
        return HttpRequest(parts[0], parts[1], headers, body)
    }

    private fun writeJson(client: java.net.Socket, status: Int, body: JSONObject) {
        writeResponse(client, status, "application/json; charset=utf-8", body.toString())
    }

    private fun writeResponse(
        client: java.net.Socket,
        status: Int,
        contentType: String,
        body: String,
        extraHeaders: Map<String, String> = emptyMap()
    ) {
        val reason = when (status) {
            200 -> "OK"
            400 -> "Bad Request"
            401 -> "Unauthorized"
            403 -> "Forbidden"
            404 -> "Not Found"
            405 -> "Method Not Allowed"
            500 -> "Internal Server Error"
            else -> "Error"
        }
        val bytes = body.toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8)
        client.getOutputStream().use { output ->
            output.write("HTTP/1.1 $status $reason\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            output.write("Content-Type: $contentType\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            extraHeaders.forEach { (name, value) ->
                output.write("$name: $value\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            }
            output.write("X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            output.write("Referrer-Policy: no-referrer\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            output.write("Content-Length: ${bytes.size}\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            output.write("Cache-Control: no-store\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            output.write("Connection: close\r\n\r\n".toByteArray(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))
            output.write(bytes)
        }
    }

    private fun statusJson(): JSONObject {
        val catalogStore = CatalogStore(appContext)
        val profile = ProfileStore(appContext).getCurrentProfile()
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val aiConfigured = aiClient(credentials).isConfigured()
        return JSONObject()
            .put("ok", true)
            .put("service", "ai-iptv-viewer-android-webserver")
            .put("appVersionName", AppVersion.APP_VERSION_NAME)
            .put("appVersionCode", AppVersion.APP_VERSION_CODE)
            .put("webServerVersionName", AppVersion.ANDROID_WEBSERVER_VERSION_NAME)
            .put("webServerVersionCode", AppVersion.ANDROID_WEBSERVER_VERSION_CODE)
            .put("profile", profile.name)
            .put("profileId", profile.id)
            .put("url", accessInfo().url)
            .put("aiServerConfigured", aiConfigured)
            .put("aiServerUrl", credentials?.syncServerUrl ?: "")
            .put("counts", JSONObject()
                .put("movies", catalogStore.countItems(ContentType.MOVIE))
                .put("series", catalogStore.countItems(ContentType.SERIES))
                .put("live", catalogStore.countItems(ContentType.LIVE)))
    }

    private fun dashboardJson(): JSONObject {
        val catalogStore = CatalogStore(appContext)
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val localCatalog = catalogStore.getAllItems()
        return statusJson()
            .put("watch", JSONObject()
                .put("watchNext", watchRepository.getWatchNext().size)
                .put("watchlist", watchRepository.matchWatchlistItems(localCatalog).size)
                .put("progress", watchRepository.getContinueWatching().size)
                .put("history", watchRepository.getHistory().size))
            .put("topPicks", topPicksJson().optJSONArray("items") ?: JSONArray())
    }

    private fun catalogJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val catalogStore = CatalogStore(appContext)
        val type = query["type"]?.let(::contentTypeFromQuery)
        val limit = query["limit"]?.toIntOrNull()?.coerceIn(1, 800) ?: 240
        val offset = query["offset"]?.toIntOrNull()?.coerceAtLeast(0) ?: 0
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val watchedKeys = watchRepository.getHistory().filter { it.completed }.map { it.stableKey }.toSet()
        val inProgressKeys = watchRepository.getContinueWatching().map { it.stableKey }.toSet()
        val watchlistKeys = watchRepository.getWatchlist().map { it.stableKey }.toSet()
        val searchTokens = query["search"].orEmpty().lowercase(Locale.US).split(Regex("\\s+")).filter { it.isNotBlank() }
        val category = cleanOptionLabel(query["category"])
        val genre = cleanOptionLabel(query["genre"])
        val status = query["status"].orEmpty().ifBlank { "all" }
        val yearFrom = query["yearFrom"]?.toIntOrNull()
        val yearTo = query["yearTo"]?.toIntOrNull()
        val ratingFrom = query["ratingFrom"]?.toDoubleOrNull()?.takeIf { it > 0.0 }
        val sort = query["sort"].orEmpty().ifBlank { "rating" }

        val allItems = if (type == null) catalogStore.getAllItems() else catalogStore.getItems(type)
        val filtered = allItems
            .asSequence()
            .filter { item -> category.isNullOrBlank() || item.categoryName.equals(category, ignoreCase = true) }
            .filter { item -> genre.isNullOrBlank() || item.genres.any { it.equals(genre, ignoreCase = true) } || item.categoryName.equals(genre, ignoreCase = true) }
            .filter { item -> searchTokens.isEmpty() || searchTokens.all { token -> searchableText(item).contains(token) } }
            .filter { item ->
                val year = itemYear(item)
                (yearFrom == null || year == null || year >= yearFrom) && (yearTo == null || year == null || year <= yearTo)
            }
            .filter { item -> ratingFrom == null || (item.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0) >= ratingFrom }
            .filter { item ->
                when (status) {
                    "watched" -> watchedKeys.contains(item.stableKey)
                    "unwatched" -> !watchedKeys.contains(item.stableKey) && !inProgressKeys.contains(item.stableKey)
                    "inProgress" -> inProgressKeys.contains(item.stableKey)
                    "watchlist" -> watchlistKeys.contains(item.stableKey)
                    else -> true
                }
            }
            .toList()
            .sortedWith(catalogComparator(sort, watchedKeys, watchlistKeys))

        val pageItems = filtered.drop(offset).take(limit)
        val itemState = publicItemState(watchRepository)

        return JSONObject()
            .put("items", JSONArray(pageItems.map { publicItemJson(it, itemState) }))
            .put("count", filtered.size)
            .put("total", filtered.size)
            .put("offset", offset)
            .put("limit", limit)
            .put("hasMore", offset + limit < filtered.size)
    }

    private fun catalogCategoriesJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val type = query["type"]?.let(::contentTypeFromQuery)
        val items = type?.let { CatalogStore(appContext).getItems(it) } ?: CatalogStore(appContext).getAllItems()
        val categories = items
            .groupingBy { it.categoryName?.takeIf(String::isNotBlank) ?: "Uncategorized" }
            .eachCount()
            .toList()
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<Pair<String, Int>> { it.second }.thenBy { it.first.lowercase(Locale.US) })
            .map { (name, count) -> JSONObject().put("name", name).put("count", count) }
        return JSONObject().put("categories", JSONArray(categories))
    }

    private fun catalogGenresJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val type = query["type"]?.let(::contentTypeFromQuery)
        val items = type?.let { CatalogStore(appContext).getItems(it) } ?: CatalogStore(appContext).getAllItems()
        val counts = mutableMapOf<String, Int>()
        for (item in items) {
            val values = (item.genres + listOfNotNull(item.categoryName)).mapNotNull { it.takeIf(String::isNotBlank) }
            for (value in values) counts[value] = (counts[value] ?: 0) + 1
        }
        val genres = counts
            .toList()
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<Pair<String, Int>> { it.second }.thenBy { it.first.lowercase(Locale.US) })
            .map { (name, count) -> JSONObject().put("name", name).put("count", count) }
        return JSONObject().put("genres", JSONArray(genres))
    }

    private fun searchJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val q = query["q"].orEmpty().trim()
        val items = if (q.isBlank()) emptyList() else CatalogStore(appContext).search(q)
        val itemState = publicItemState(WatchRepository(appContext))
        return JSONObject()
            .put("query", q)
            .put("items", JSONArray(items.take(160).map { publicItemJson(it, itemState) }))
    }

    private fun topPicksJson(): JSONObject {
        val catalogStore = CatalogStore(appContext)
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val picks = sequenceOf(
            watchRepository.getWatchNext().map { it.copy(sourceLabel = it.sourceLabel ?: "Watch Next") },
            watchRepository.getContinueWatching().map { it.copy(sourceLabel = it.sourceLabel ?: "Continue Watching") },
            watchRepository.matchWatchlistItems(catalogStore.getAllItems()).map { it.copy(sourceLabel = it.sourceLabel ?: "Watchlist") },
            catalogStore.getRecentlyAdded(ContentType.MOVIE, 30).map { it.copy(sourceLabel = it.sourceLabel ?: "Recently Added Movie") },
            catalogStore.getRecentlyAdded(ContentType.SERIES, 30).map { it.copy(sourceLabel = it.sourceLabel ?: "Recently Added Series") }
        ).flatten()
            .filter { it.contentType != ContentType.ACTION }
            .distinctBy { it.stableKey }
            .take(140)
            .toList()

        val itemState = publicItemState(watchRepository)
        return JSONObject()
            .put("items", JSONArray(picks.map { publicItemJson(it, itemState) }))
            .put("count", picks.size)
    }

    private fun watchJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val kind = query["kind"].orEmpty().ifBlank { "watchlist" }
        val catalog = CatalogStore(appContext).getAllItems()
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val items = when (kind) {
            "watchNext" -> watchRepository.getWatchNext()
            "progress" -> watchRepository.getContinueWatching()
            "history" -> watchRepository.getHistory()
            "live" -> watchRepository.getRecentlyWatchedLive()
            else -> watchRepository.matchWatchlistItems(catalog)
        }.filter { item ->
            val search = query["search"].orEmpty().trim().lowercase(Locale.US)
            search.isBlank() || searchableText(item).contains(search)
        }
        val itemState = publicItemState(watchRepository)
        return JSONObject()
            .put("kind", kind)
            .put("items", JSONArray(items.map { watchRecordJson(kind, it, itemState) }))
            .put("count", items.size)
            .put("profile", ProfileStore(appContext).getCurrentProfile().let { JSONObject().put("id", it.id).put("name", it.name).put("kids", it.isKidsProfile) })
            .put("summary", watchSummaryJson(watchRepository, catalog))
    }

    private fun updateWatchRecordJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val kind = body.optString("kind").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("kind is required")
        val stableKey = body.optString("stableKey").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("stableKey is required")
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val primaryUpdate = watchRepository.updateWatchRecord(
            kind = kind,
            stableKey = stableKey,
            positionMs = body.optLongNullable("positionMs"),
            durationMs = body.optLongNullable("durationMs"),
            completed = body.optBooleanNullable("completed"),
            watchedCount = body.optIntNullable("watchedCount")
        )
        val fallbackUpdate = if (primaryUpdate == null && kind == "progress") {
            watchRepository.updateWatchRecord(
                kind = "live",
                stableKey = stableKey,
                positionMs = body.optLongNullable("positionMs"),
                durationMs = body.optLongNullable("durationMs"),
                completed = body.optBooleanNullable("completed"),
                watchedCount = body.optIntNullable("watchedCount")
            )
        } else {
            null
        }
        val updated = primaryUpdate ?: fallbackUpdate ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("Watch record not found")
        syncWatchSnapshot()
        return JSONObject()
            .put("ok", true)
            .put("message", "Watch record saved")
            .put("record", watchRecordJson(kind, updated, publicItemState(watchRepository)))
    }

    private fun deleteWatchRecordJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val kind = body.optString("kind").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("kind is required")
        val stableKey = body.optString("stableKey").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("stableKey is required")
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val deleted = watchRepository.deleteWatchRecord(kind, stableKey) || (kind == "progress" && watchRepository.deleteWatchRecord("live", stableKey))
        if (!deleted) throw IllegalArgumentException("Watch record not found")
        syncWatchSnapshot()
        return JSONObject().put("ok", true).put("message", "Watch record deleted")
    }

    private fun syncWatchDataJson(): JSONObject {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny() ?: throw IllegalStateException("No credentials saved on this Android app")
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) throw IllegalStateException("AI sync server is not configured")
        val snapshot = WatchRepository(appContext).buildSnapshot(credentials.userId, credentials.syncServerUsername)
        runBlocking { client.postWatchSnapshot(snapshot).getOrThrow() }
        return JSONObject().put("ok", true).put("message", "Watch data synced to central server")
    }

    private fun aiRecommendationsJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) throw IllegalStateException("AI sync server is not configured")
        val items = runBlocking {
            client.getRecommendations(
                profileId = serverProfileId(credentials),
                mood = body.optString("mood", "any"),
                contentType = body.optString("contentType", "any"),
                query = body.optString("query").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() },
                useWebSearch = body.optBoolean("useWebSearch", false),
                limit = body.optInt("limit", 40)
            ).getOrThrow()
        }
        return JSONObject().put("items", JSONArray(items.map { publicItemJson(it) })).put("count", items.size)
    }

    private fun aiNaturalSearchJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val query = body.optString("query").trim()
        if (query.isBlank()) return JSONObject().put("items", JSONArray()).put("count", 0)
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) throw IllegalStateException("AI sync server is not configured")
        val items = runBlocking { client.naturalSearch(serverProfileId(credentials), query, body.optInt("limit", 10)).getOrThrow() }
        return JSONObject().put("query", query).put("items", JSONArray(items.map { publicItemJson(it) })).put("count", items.size)
    }

    private fun tmdbJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) throw IllegalStateException("AI sync server is not configured")
        val collection = query["collection"] ?: "popular"
        val type = if (query["type"].equals("all", ignoreCase = true)) {
            null
        } else {
            contentTypeFromQuery(query["type"] ?: "movie") ?: ContentType.MOVIE
        }
        val limit = query["limit"]?.toIntOrNull()?.coerceIn(1, 300) ?: 80
        val items = runBlocking { client.getTmdbCollection(collection, type, limit).getOrThrow() }
        return JSONObject().put("items", JSONArray(items.map { publicItemJson(it) })).put("count", items.size)
    }

    private fun tmdbWatchlistJson(): JSONObject {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) throw IllegalStateException("AI sync server is not configured")
        val items = runBlocking { client.getTmdbWatchlist(80).getOrThrow() }
        return JSONObject().put("items", JSONArray(items.map { publicItemJson(it) })).put("count", items.size)
    }

    private fun catalogActionJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val item = localItemByKey(body.optString("catalogKey").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: body.optString("stableKey"))
        val action = body.optString("action").lowercase(Locale.US)
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val catalogStore = CatalogStore(appContext)
        val message = when (action) {
            "watchlist" -> {
                if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) {
                    watchRepository.removeFromWatchlist(item)
                    syncWatchSnapshot()
                    "Removed from watchlist"
                } else {
                    val savedItem = watchRepository.addToWatchlist(item, catalogStore.getAllItems())
                    syncWatchSnapshot()
                    if (savedItem.isPlayable && !item.isPlayable) "Added to watchlist and matched to stream" else "Added to watchlist"
                }
            }
            "watchnext" -> {
                if (watchRepository.isInWatchNext(item)) {
                    watchRepository.removeFromWatchNext(item)
                    syncWatchSnapshot()
                    "Removed from Watch Next"
                } else {
                    watchRepository.addToWatchNext(item)
                    syncWatchSnapshot()
                    "Added to Watch Next"
                }
            }
            "like" -> {
                val nextRating = if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) 0 else 1
                watchRepository.setRating(item, nextRating)
                syncCatalogPreference(item, rating = nextRating)
                if (nextRating == 1) "Marked as liked" else "Cleared like"
            }
            "dislike" -> {
                val nextRating = if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == -1) 0 else -1
                watchRepository.setRating(item, nextRating)
                syncCatalogPreference(item, rating = nextRating)
                if (nextRating == -1) "Marked as disliked" else "Cleared dislike"
            }
            "ignore" -> {
                catalogStore.ignoreItem(item)
                syncCatalogPreference(item, ignored = true)
                "Ignored in catalog"
            }
            else -> throw IllegalArgumentException("Unknown catalog action")
        }
        return JSONObject()
            .put("ok", true)
            .put("message", message)
            .put("item", publicItemJson(item, publicItemState(watchRepository)))
    }

    private fun catalogExplainJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val item = localItemByKey(query["catalogKey"] ?: query["stableKey"])
        val watchRepository = WatchRepository(appContext)
        val signals = mutableListOf<String>()
        if (watchRepository.isInWatchlist(item)) signals.add("saved to your watchlist")
        if (watchRepository.isInWatchNext(item)) signals.add("queued in Watch Next")
        if (watchRepository.getRating(item) == 1) signals.add("you liked it")
        if (item.progressPercent > 0) signals.add("${item.progressPercent}% watched")
        item.categoryName?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }?.let { signals.add("category: $it") }
        if (item.genres.isNotEmpty()) signals.add("genres: ${item.genres.take(3).joinToString(", ")}")
        if (!item.rating.isNullOrBlank()) signals.add("catalog rating ${item.rating}")
        val reason = if (signals.isEmpty()) {
            "This item is available in your Android catalog. Add ratings or watch progress to improve future signals."
        } else {
            "This item stands out because it is ${signals.joinToString(", ")}."
        }
        return JSONObject().put("title", item.title).put("reason", reason).put("signals", JSONArray(signals))
    }

    private fun catalogSimilarJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val item = localItemByKey(query["catalogKey"] ?: query["stableKey"])
        val limit = query["limit"]?.toIntOrNull()?.coerceIn(1, 40) ?: 12
        val sourceGenres = item.genres.map { it.lowercase(Locale.US) }.toSet()
        val sourceTokens = item.title.lowercase(Locale.US).split(Regex("\\W+")).filter { it.length > 3 }.toSet()
        val candidates = CatalogStore(appContext).getItems(item.contentType)
            .asSequence()
            .filterNot { it.stableKey == item.stableKey }
            .map { candidate ->
                val genreScore = candidate.genres.count { sourceGenres.contains(it.lowercase(Locale.US)) } * 4
                val categoryScore = if (!item.categoryName.isNullOrBlank() && item.categoryName.equals(candidate.categoryName, ignoreCase = true)) 5 else 0
                val tokenScore = candidate.title.lowercase(Locale.US).split(Regex("\\W+")).count { sourceTokens.contains(it) }
                val ratingScore = ((candidate.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0) / 2.0).toInt()
                candidate to (genreScore + categoryScore + tokenScore + ratingScore)
            }
            .filter { it.second > 0 }
            .sortedWith(compareByDescending<Pair<IptvItem, Int>> { it.second }.thenBy { it.first.title.lowercase(Locale.US) })
            .take(limit)
            .map { it.first.copy(sourceLabel = "Similar to ${item.title}") }
            .toList()
        val itemState = publicItemState(WatchRepository(appContext))
        return JSONObject().put("items", JSONArray(candidates.map { publicItemJson(it, itemState) })).put("count", candidates.size)
    }

    private fun socialClient(): SocialApiClient {
        val settings = SocialSettings(appContext)
        if (!settings.isConfigured()) throw IllegalStateException("Social server is not configured")
        return SocialApiClient(settings)
    }

    private fun localItemByKey(stableKey: String?): IptvItem {
        val key = stableKey?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("catalogKey is required")
        return CatalogStore(appContext).getAllItems().firstOrNull { it.stableKey == key }
            ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("Catalog item is not available on this Android device")
    }

    private fun socialRoomsJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val rooms = runBlocking {
            socialClient().getRooms(
                catalogItemId = query["catalogKey"] ?: query["catalogItemId"],
                roomType = query["roomType"]
            )
        }
        return JSONObject().put("rooms", JSONArray(rooms.map { room ->
            JSONObject()
                .put("id", room.id)
                .put("roomType", room.roomType)
                .put("catalogItemId", room.catalogItemId)
                .put("title", room.title)
                .put("lastMessage", room.lastMessage)
                .put("updatedAt", room.updatedAt)
                .put("unreadCount", room.unreadCount)
        }))
    }

    private fun socialMessagesJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val roomId = query["roomId"]?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("roomId is required")
        val messages = runBlocking { socialClient().getMessages(roomId, 80) }
        return JSONObject().put("messages", JSONArray(messages.map { message ->
            JSONObject()
                .put("id", message.id)
                .put("roomId", message.roomId)
                .put("senderDisplayName", message.senderDisplayName)
                .put("messageType", message.messageType)
                .put("text", message.text)
                .put("createdAt", message.createdAt)
                .put("sharePayload", message.sharePayload)
        }))
    }

    private fun socialSendMessageJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val roomId = body.optString("roomId").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("roomId is required")
        val text = body.optString("text").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("text is required")
        val sent = runBlocking { socialClient().sendMessage(roomId, text, "android-web-${System.currentTimeMillis()}") }
            ?: throw IllegalStateException("Message could not be sent")
        return JSONObject().put("message", JSONObject()
            .put("id", sent.id)
            .put("roomId", sent.roomId)
            .put("senderDisplayName", sent.senderDisplayName)
            .put("text", sent.text)
            .put("createdAt", sent.createdAt))
    }

    private fun socialUsersJson(): JSONObject {
        val users = runBlocking { socialClient().getUsers() }
        return JSONObject().put("users", JSONArray(users.map { user ->
            JSONObject()
                .put("id", user.id)
                .put("displayName", user.displayName)
                .put("username", user.username)
                .put("status", user.status)
                .put("lastSeenAt", user.lastSeenAt)
        }))
    }

    private fun socialFriendsJson(): JSONObject {
        val friendships = runBlocking { socialClient().getFriends() }
        return JSONObject().put("friendships", JSONArray(friendships.map { friendship ->
            JSONObject()
                .put("id", friendship.id)
                .put("status", friendship.status)
                .put("direction", friendship.direction)
                .put("otherUser", friendship.otherUser?.let { user ->
                    JSONObject().put("id", user.id).put("displayName", user.displayName).put("status", user.status)
                })
        }))
    }

    private fun socialRequestFriendJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val userId = body.optString("userId").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("userId is required")
        val friendship = runBlocking { socialClient().requestFriend(userId) }
            ?: throw IllegalStateException("Friend request could not be sent")
        return JSONObject().put("friendship", JSONObject()
            .put("id", friendship.id)
            .put("status", friendship.status)
            .put("direction", friendship.direction)
            .put("otherUser", friendship.otherUser?.let { JSONObject().put("id", it.id).put("displayName", it.displayName) }))
    }

    private fun socialWatchingJson(query: Map<String, String>): JSONObject {
        val item = localItemByKey(query["catalogKey"] ?: query["catalogItemId"])
        val viewers = runBlocking { socialClient().getCurrentViewers(item) }
        return JSONObject().put("viewers", JSONArray(viewers.map { viewer ->
            JSONObject()
                .put("roomId", viewer.roomId)
                .put("catalogKey", viewer.catalogKey)
                .put("catalogTitle", viewer.catalogTitle)
                .put("positionMs", viewer.positionMs)
                .put("durationMs", viewer.durationMs)
                .put("user", viewer.user?.let { user ->
                    JSONObject().put("id", user.id).put("displayName", user.displayName).put("status", user.status)
                })
        }))
    }

    private fun socialCreatePartyJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val item = localItemByKey(body.optString("catalogKey").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: body.optString("catalogItemId"))
        val title = body.optString("title").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: "Watch Party: ${item.title}"
        val inviteIds = body.optJSONArray("inviteUserIds")?.let { array ->
            (0 until array.length()).mapNotNull { index -> array.optString(index).takeIf(String::isNotBlank) }
        } ?: emptyList()
        val party = runBlocking { socialClient().createViewingParty(item, title, body.optString("scheduledFor").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }, inviteIds) }
            ?: throw IllegalStateException("Viewing party could not be created")
        return JSONObject().put("party", JSONObject()
            .put("id", party.id)
            .put("title", party.title)
            .put("status", party.status)
            .put("scheduledFor", party.scheduledFor)
            .put("catalogTitle", party.catalogTitle)
            .put("room", party.room?.let { room -> JSONObject().put("id", room.id).put("title", room.title) }))
    }

    private fun publicItemJson(item: IptvItem, state: PublicItemState = publicItemState(WatchRepository(appContext))): JSONObject {
        return JSONObject()
            .put("title", item.title)
            .put("description", item.description)
            .put("type", item.contentType.name.lowercase(Locale.US))
            .put("category", item.categoryName)
            .put("coverUrl", item.coverUrl)
            .put("backdropUrl", item.backdropUrl)
            .put("rating", item.rating)
            .put("year", item.year)
            .put("genres", JSONArray(item.genres))
            .put("sourceLabel", item.sourceLabel)
            .put("progressPercent", item.progressPercent)
            .put("positionMs", item.positionMs)
            .put("durationMs", item.durationMs)
            .put("completed", item.completed)
            .put("watchedCount", item.watchedCount)
            .put("metadataProvider", item.metadataProvider)
            .put("metadataId", item.metadataId)
            .put("imdbId", item.imdbId)
            .put("tmdbId", item.tmdbId)
            .put("stableKey", item.stableKey)
            .put("userRating", state.ratings[item.stableKey] ?: 0)
            .put("watchlisted", state.watchlistKeys.contains(item.stableKey))
            .put("watchNext", state.watchNextKeys.contains(item.stableKey))
    }

    private fun publicItemState(watchRepository: WatchRepository): PublicItemState {
        return PublicItemState(
            ratings = watchRepository.getRatingsSnapshot(),
            watchlistKeys = watchRepository.getWatchlist().map { it.stableKey }.toSet(),
            watchNextKeys = watchRepository.getWatchNext().map { it.stableKey }.toSet()
        )
    }

    private fun watchRecordJson(kind: String, item: IptvItem, state: PublicItemState): JSONObject {
        val progress = if (item.durationMs > 0L) (item.positionMs.toDouble() / item.durationMs.toDouble()).coerceIn(0.0, 1.0) else 0.0
        return JSONObject()
            .put("id", item.stableKey)
            .put("kind", kind)
            .put("progress", progress)
            .put("progressPercent", item.progressPercent)
            .put("positionMs", item.positionMs)
            .put("durationMs", item.durationMs)
            .put("completed", item.completed)
            .put("playCount", item.watchedCount)
            .put("updatedAt", item.lastWatchedAtMs)
            .put("createdAt", item.addedAtMs)
            .put("userRating", state.ratings[item.stableKey] ?: 0)
            .put("catalogItem", publicItemJson(item, state))
    }

    private fun watchSummaryJson(watchRepository: WatchRepository, catalog: List<IptvItem>): JSONObject {
        return JSONObject()
            .put("watchlist", watchRepository.matchWatchlistItems(catalog).size)
            .put("watchNext", watchRepository.getWatchNext().size)
            .put("progress", watchRepository.getContinueWatching().size)
            .put("history", watchRepository.getHistory().size)
            .put("live", watchRepository.getRecentlyWatchedLive().size)
    }

    private fun syncCatalogPreference(item: IptvItem, rating: Int? = null, ignored: Boolean? = null) {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny() ?: return
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) return
        runCatching {
            runBlocking {
                client.saveCatalogPreference(serverProfileId(credentials), item, rating = rating, ignored = ignored).getOrThrow()
            }
        }.onFailure { error ->
            Log.w(TAG, "Could not sync catalog preference", error)
        }
    }

    private fun syncWatchSnapshot() {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny() ?: return
        val client = aiClient(credentials)
        if (!client.isConfigured()) return
        runCatching {
            val snapshot = WatchRepository(appContext).buildSnapshot(credentials.userId, credentials.syncServerUsername)
            runBlocking { client.postWatchSnapshot(snapshot).getOrThrow() }
        }.onFailure { error ->
            Log.w(TAG, "Could not sync watch snapshot", error)
        }
    }

    private fun cleanOptionLabel(value: String?): String? {
        return value?.replace(Regex("\\s+\\(\\d+\\)$"), "")?.trim()?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
    }

    private fun searchableText(item: IptvItem): String {
        return listOf(
            item.title,
            item.description,
            item.categoryName.orEmpty(),
            item.year.orEmpty(),
            item.rating.orEmpty(),
            item.genres.joinToString(" "),
            item.sourceLabel.orEmpty(),
            item.parentSeriesTitle.orEmpty(),
            item.metadataProvider.orEmpty()
        ).joinToString(" ").lowercase(Locale.US)
    }

    private fun itemYear(item: IptvItem): Int? {
        val match = Regex("\\b(19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})\\b").find(listOf(item.year, item.title, item.description).filterNotNull().joinToString(" "))
        return match?.value?.toIntOrNull()
    }

    private fun catalogComparator(sort: String, watchedKeys: Set<String>, watchlistKeys: Set<String>): Comparator<IptvItem> {
        return when (sort) {
            "title" -> compareBy { it.title.lowercase(Locale.US) }
            "year" -> compareByDescending<IptvItem> { itemYear(it) ?: 0 }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase(Locale.US) }
            "added" -> compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.addedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase(Locale.US) }
            "watched" -> compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.lastWatchedAtMs }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase(Locale.US) }
            "watchlist" -> compareByDescending<IptvItem> { watchlistKeys.contains(it.stableKey) }.thenBy { it.title.lowercase(Locale.US) }
            else -> compareByDescending<IptvItem> { it.rating?.toDoubleOrNull() ?: 0.0 }
                .thenByDescending { watchedKeys.contains(it.stableKey) }
                .thenByDescending { it.addedAtMs }
                .thenBy { it.title.lowercase(Locale.US) }
        }
    }

    private fun aiClient(credentials: IptvCredentials?): AiSyncClient {
        return AiSyncClient(
            credentials?.syncServerUrl,
            credentials?.syncServerUsername,
            credentials?.syncServerPassword,
            credentials?.syncServerToken
        )
    }

    private fun serverProfileId(credentials: IptvCredentials?): String {
        val profileId = ProfileStore(appContext).getCurrentProfile().id
        val owner = credentials?.syncServerUsername?.trim()?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: return profileId
        return "$owner:$profileId"
    }

    private fun contentTypeFromQuery(value: String): ContentType? {
        return when (value.lowercase(Locale.US)) {
            "movie", "movies" -> ContentType.MOVIE
            "series", "show", "shows", "tv" -> ContentType.SERIES
            "live", "channel", "channels" -> ContentType.LIVE
            "episode", "episodes" -> ContentType.EPISODE
            else -> null
        }
    }

    private fun parseQuery(query: String): Map<String, String> {
        if (query.isBlank()) return emptyMap()
        return query.split("&")
            .mapNotNull { part ->
                val key = part.substringBefore("=", "").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: return@mapNotNull null
                val value = part.substringAfter("=", "")
                decode(key) to decode(value)
            }
            .toMap()
    }

    private fun decode(value: String): String {
        return URLDecoder.decode(value, StandardCharsets.UTF_8.name())
    }

    private fun localIpAddress(): String? {
        return NetworkInterface.getNetworkInterfaces().toList()
            .asSequence()
            .filter { it.isUp && !it.isLoopback }
            .flatMap { it.inetAddresses.toList().asSequence() }
            .filterIsInstance<Inet4Address>()
            .firstOrNull { !it.isLoopbackAddress }
            ?.hostAddress
    }

    private fun saveSettingsJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val iptvUrl = body.optString("iptvUrl").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: credentials?.serverUrl.orEmpty()
        val iptvUser = body.optString("iptvUser").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: credentials?.username.orEmpty()
        val iptvPass = body.optString("iptvPass").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: credentials?.password.orEmpty()
        val saved = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val aiUrl = body.optString("aiUrl").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.syncServerUrl
        val aiUser = body.optString("aiUser").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.syncServerUsername
        val aiPass = body.optString("aiPass").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.syncServerPassword
        val traktClientId = body.optString("traktClientId").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val traktSecret = body.optString("traktSecret").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }
        val savedCreds = credentials ?: IptvCredentials(
            serverUrl = "", username = "", password = "", userId = CredentialStore(appContext).getOrCreateUserId()
        )
        val updated = savedCreds.copy(
            serverUrl = iptvUrl, username = iptvUser, password = iptvPass,
            syncServerUrl = aiUrl ?: savedCreds.syncServerUrl,
            syncServerUsername = aiUser ?: savedCreds.syncServerUsername,
            syncServerPassword = aiPass ?: savedCreds.syncServerPassword,
            traktClientId = traktClientId ?: savedCreds.traktClientId,
            traktClientSecret = traktSecret ?: savedCreds.traktClientSecret
        )
        CredentialStore(appContext).save(updated)
        return JSONObject().put("ok", true).put("message", "Settings saved to device. Restart the app to apply changes.")
    }

    private fun loadSettingsJson(): JSONObject {
        val credentials = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        return JSONObject()
            .put("iptvUrl", credentials?.serverUrl.orEmpty())
            .put("iptvUser", credentials?.username.orEmpty())
            .put("iptvPass", "")
            .put("hasIptvPass", !credentials?.password.isNullOrBlank())
            .put("aiUrl", credentials?.syncServerUrl.orEmpty())
            .put("aiUser", credentials?.syncServerUsername.orEmpty())
            .put("aiPass", "")
            .put("hasAiPass", !credentials?.syncServerPassword.isNullOrBlank() || !credentials?.syncServerToken.isNullOrBlank())
            .put("traktClientId", credentials?.traktClientId.orEmpty())
            .put("traktSecret", "")
            .put("hasTraktSecret", !credentials?.traktClientSecret.isNullOrBlank())
    }

    private fun testIptvConnectionJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val saved = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val iptvUrl = body.optString("iptvUrl").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.serverUrl
        val iptvUser = body.optString("iptvUser").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.username
        val iptvPass = body.optString("iptvPass").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.password
        if (iptvUrl.isNullOrBlank() || iptvUser.isNullOrBlank() || iptvPass.isNullOrBlank()) {
            return JSONObject().put("ok", false).put("message", "Fill all IPTV fields")
        }
        val credentials = IptvCredentials(serverUrl = iptvUrl, username = iptvUser, password = iptvPass, userId = "")
        return try {
            val valid = runBlocking { XtreamApiClient(credentials).validateLogin() }
            if (valid) {
                JSONObject().put("ok", true).put("message", "IPTV server login works")
            } else {
                JSONObject().put("ok", false).put("message", "IPTV server returned invalid response")
            }
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            JSONObject().put("ok", false).put("message", e.message ?: "Connection failed")
        }
    }

    private fun testAiConnectionJson(body: JSONObject): JSONObject {
        val saved = CredentialStore(appContext).getAny()
        val aiUrl = body.optString("aiUrl").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.syncServerUrl
        val aiUser = body.optString("aiUser").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.syncServerUsername
        val aiPass = body.optString("aiPass").takeIf { it.isNotBlank() } ?: saved?.syncServerPassword
        if (aiUrl.isNullOrBlank()) {
            return JSONObject().put("ok", false).put("message", "AI server URL is required")
        }
        val client = AiSyncClient(aiUrl, aiUser, aiPass, null)
        return try {
            val status = runBlocking { client.checkConnection().getOrThrow() }
            val parts = mutableListOf<String>()
            parts.add(status.displayName ?: status.username ?: aiUser ?: "connected")
            if (status.isAdmin) parts.add("admin") else parts.add("viewer")
            parts.add("TMDb: ${if (status.tmdbLinked) "linked${status.tmdbUsername?.let { " ($it)" } ?: ""}" else "not linked"}")
            parts.joinToString(", ")
            JSONObject().put("ok", true).put("message", parts.joinToString(" \u00b7 "))
                .put("username", status.username)
                .put("displayName", status.displayName)
                .put("isAdmin", status.isAdmin)
                .put("tmdbLinked", status.tmdbLinked)
                .put("tmdbUsername", status.tmdbUsername)
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            val hint = when {
                e.message?.contains("401") == true -> "Invalid username or password"
                e.message?.contains("timed out") == true -> "Server unreachable (timeout)"
                e.message?.contains("refused") == true -> "Connection refused"
                else -> e.message ?: "Unknown error"
            }
            JSONObject().put("ok", false).put("message", hint)
        }
    }
