        </div>
        <script>
          const e = id => document.getElementById(id);
          const setBadge = (el, ok, text) => { el.innerHTML = ok ? '<span class="badge ok">\u2713 '+(text||'Connected')+'</span>' : text ? '<span class="badge err">\u2717 '+text+'</span>' : ''; };
          const showMsg = (el, ok, text) => { el.textContent = text; el.className = 'msg-box show '+(ok?'ok':'err'); };
          const hideMsg = el => { el.className = 'msg-box'; };

          async function load() {
            const data = await fetch('/api/settings/load').then(r=>r.json());
            e('iptvUrl').value = data.iptvUrl||'';
            e('iptvUser').value = data.iptvUser||'';
            e('iptvPass').value = data.iptvPass||'';
            e('aiUrl').value = data.aiUrl||'';
            e('aiUser').value = data.aiUser||'';
            e('aiPass').value = data.aiPass||'';
            e('traktClientId').value = data.traktClientId||'';
            e('traktSecret').value = data.traktSecret||'';
            if (data.aiUrl) testAiConnection();
          }

          async function testAiConnection() {
            const btn = e('testAiBtn'), badge = e('aiBadge'), msg = e('aiMsg'), details = e('aiDetails');
            const url = e('aiUrl').value.trim(), user = e('aiUser').value.trim(), pass = e('aiPass').value.trim();
            if (!url) { setBadge(badge, false, 'Enter URL first'); return; }
            btn.textContent = 'Testing...'; btn.disabled = true;
            hideMsg(msg); details.innerHTML = '';
            try {
              const res = await fetch('/api/settings/test-connection', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
                body: JSON.stringify({aiUrl:url, aiUser:user, aiPass:pass}) }).then(r=>r.json());
              if (res.ok) {
                setBadge(badge, true, 'Connected');
                showMsg(msg, true, res.message);
                if (res.username || res.displayName) {
                  let tags = '';
                  if (res.displayName) tags += '<span class="tag">'+res.displayName+'</span>';
                  if (res.username) tags += '<span class="tag">@'+res.username+'</span>';
                  if (res.isAdmin) tags += '<span class="tag" style="color:#fbbf24;background:rgba(251,191,36,.1)">admin</span>';
                  if (res.tmdbLinked) tags += '<span class="tag" style="color:#6ee7b7">TMDb: '+(res.tmdbUsername||'linked')+'</span>';
                  else tags += '<span class="tag">TMDb: not linked</span>';
                  details.innerHTML = tags;
                }
              } else {
                setBadge(badge, false, 'Failed');
                showMsg(msg, false, res.message);
              }
            } catch(e) {
              setBadge(badge, false, 'Error');
              showMsg(msg, false, 'Request failed: '+e.message);
            }
            btn.textContent = 'Test Connection'; btn.disabled = false;
          }

          e('testAiBtn').addEventListener('click', testAiConnection);

          e('testIptvBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const btn = e('testIptvBtn'), badge = e('iptvBadge'), msg = e('iptvMsg');
            const url = e('iptvUrl').value.trim(), user = e('iptvUser').value.trim(), pass = e('iptvPass').value.trim();
            if (!url||!user||!pass) { setBadge(badge, false, 'Fill all fields'); return; }
            btn.textContent = 'Testing...'; btn.disabled = true; hideMsg(msg);
            try {
              const res = await fetch('/api/settings/test-iptv', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
                body: JSON.stringify({iptvUrl:url, iptvUser:user, iptvPass:pass}) }).then(r=>r.json());
              if (res.ok) { setBadge(badge, true, 'OK'); showMsg(msg, true, 'IPTV server responded and login works'); }
              else { setBadge(badge, false, 'Failed'); showMsg(msg, false, res.message); }
            } catch(e) { setBadge(badge, false, 'Error'); showMsg(msg, false, e.message); }
            btn.textContent = 'Test IPTV'; btn.disabled = false;
          });

          e('saveBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const btn = e('saveBtn'), msg = e('saveMsg');
            const body = {
              iptvUrl: e('iptvUrl').value.trim(), iptvUser: e('iptvUser').value.trim(), iptvPass: e('iptvPass').value.trim(),
              aiUrl: e('aiUrl').value.trim(), aiUser: e('aiUser').value.trim(), aiPass: e('aiPass').value.trim(),
              traktClientId: e('traktClientId').value.trim(), traktSecret: e('traktSecret').value.trim()
            };
            btn.textContent = 'Saving...'; btn.disabled = true; hideMsg(msg);
            const data = await fetch('/api/settings/save', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify(body) }).then(r=>r.json());
            showMsg(msg, true, data.message||'Saved. Restart the app.');
            btn.textContent = 'Save Settings'; btn.disabled = false;
          });

          load();
        </script></body></html>
    """.trimIndent()

            @media (max-width: 650px) { .content { padding: 20px; } .stats { grid-template-columns: 1fr; } .nav { grid-template-columns: repeat(2,minmax(0,1fr)); } }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <div class="shell">
            <aside class="sidebar">
              <div class="brand"><div class="logo">AI</div><div><h1>AI IPTV Viewer</h1><p>Android-hosted dashboard</p></div></div>

            </aside>
            <main class="content">
              <div class="topbar"><div><div class="eyebrow">On-device webserver</div><h2 id="pageTitle">Dashboard</h2><p class="sub" id="pageSub">Browse the Android catalog, watch state, central AI picks, and TMDb discovery from your phone or computer.</p></div><button id="refreshBtn">Refresh</button></div>
              <section id="dashboardView">
                <div class="stats">
                  <div class="stat"><span>Movies</span><strong id="movieCount">0</strong></div>
                  <div class="stat"><span>Series</span><strong id="seriesCount">0</strong></div>

                  <div class="stat"><span>Watch Items</span><strong id="watchCount">0</strong></div>
                </div>
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>Top Picks</h3></div><div class="panelBody"><div id="dashboardCards" class="cards"></div></div></div>
              </section>
              <section id="catalogView" class="hidden">
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>Catalog</h3><span class="sub" id="catalogCount">0 items</span></div><div class="panelBody"><div class="catalogFilters"><input id="catalogSearch" type="search" placeholder="Search titles, categories, years"><select id="catalogType"><option value="">All types</option><option value="movie">Movies</option><option value="series">Series</option><option value="live">Live</option></select><select id="catalogCategory"><option value="">All categories</option></select><select id="catalogGenre"><option value="">All genres</option></select><select id="catalogStatus"><option value="all">All status</option><option value="unwatched">Unwatched</option><option value="watched">Watched</option><option value="inProgress">In progress</option><option value="watchlist">Watchlist</option></select></div><div class="rangeFilters"><input id="catalogYearFrom" inputmode="numeric" placeholder="Year from"><input id="catalogYearTo" inputmode="numeric" placeholder="Year to"><input id="catalogRatingFrom" inputmode="decimal" placeholder="Rating from"><select id="catalogSort"><option value="rating">Rating</option><option value="added">Recently added</option><option value="title">Title A-Z</option><option value="year">Newest year</option><option value="watched">Recently watched</option><option value="watchlist">Watchlist first</option></select><select id="catalogLimit"><option value="80" selected>80</option><option value="160">160</option><option value="320">320</option><option value="640">640</option></select><button id="catalogLoad">Load</button><button id="catalogClear">Clear</button></div><div id="catalogProgress" class="progressBar hidden"><div id="catalogProgressFill" class="progressFill"></div></div><p class="sub" id="catalogMeta"></p><div id="catalogCards" class="cards"></div><div class="toolbar compact"><button id="catalogMore" class="hidden">Load More</button></div><div id="catalogSentinel"></div></div></div>
              </section>
              <section id="watchView" class="hidden">
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>Watch Data</h3></div><div class="panelBody"><div class="toolbar"><input id="watchSearch" type="search" placeholder="Search titles or categories"><select id="watchKind"><option value="watchlist">Watchlist</option><option value="watchNext">Watch Next</option><option value="progress">Continue Watching</option><option value="history">History</option><option value="live">Recent Live</option></select><button id="watchLoad">Load</button></div><div id="watchSummary" class="stats"></div><p class="sub" id="watchMeta"></p><div id="watchCards" class="list"></div></div></div>
              </section>
              <section id="aiView" class="hidden">
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>AI Picks</h3></div><div class="panelBody"><div class="aiGrid"><textarea id="aiPrompt" placeholder="Ask for something, like: smart sci-fi that is not too long"></textarea><select id="aiMood"><option value="any">Any mood</option><option value="funny">Funny</option><option value="action">Action</option><option value="scary">Scary</option><option value="chill">Chill</option><option value="family">Family</option><option value="smart">Smart</option></select><select id="aiType"><option value="any">Any type</option><option value="movie">Movies</option><option value="series">Series</option><option value="live">Live</option></select><select id="aiLimit"><option value="5">5 picks</option><option value="10" selected>10 picks</option><option value="20">20 picks</option></select><button id="aiRun">Ask AI</button></div><p class="sub" id="aiMeta"></p><div id="aiCards" class="cards"></div></div></div>
              </section>
              <section id="tmdbView" class="hidden">
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>TMDb Discovery</h3></div><div class="panelBody"><div class="toolbar"><select id="tmdbCollection"><option value="popular">Popular</option><option value="top_rated">Top Rated</option><option value="trending">Trending</option><option value="watchlist">My TMDb Watchlist</option></select><select id="tmdbType"><option value="movie">Movies</option><option value="series">Series</option><option value="all">All</option></select><select id="tmdbLimit"><option value="40">40</option><option value="80" selected>80</option><option value="160">160</option><option value="300">300</option></select><button id="tmdbLoad">Load TMDb</button></div><p class="sub" id="tmdbMeta"></p><div id="tmdbCards" class="cards"></div></div></div>
              </section>
              <section id="socialView" class="hidden">
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>Social Chat</h3><button id="socialRefresh">Refresh</button></div><div class="panelBody"><div class="toolbar"><input id="socialCatalogKey" placeholder="Catalog key for same-title chat"><button id="socialFindWatching">Find Viewers</button><button id="socialCreateParty">Create Party</button></div><p class="sub" id="socialMeta">Open a room from the list, or use a catalog card's Chat button.</p><div class="toolbar"><select id="socialRoomSelect"></select><input id="socialMessage" placeholder="Message the room"><button id="socialSend">Send</button></div><div id="socialViewers" class="pillRow"></div><div id="socialMessages" class="list"></div></div></div>
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>People</h3></div><div class="panelBody"><div id="socialUsers" class="list"></div><h3>Friends</h3><div id="socialFriends" class="list"></div></div></div>
              </section>
              <section id="settingsView" class="hidden">
                <div class="panel"><div class="panelHead"><h3>Device Settings</h3><button id="settingsRefresh">Reload</button></div><div class="panelBody"><div class="toolbar compact"><button id="settingsLoad">Load Current</button><button id="settingsSave" class="primary">Save All</button></div><div class="catalogFilters" style="grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr"><input id="settingsIptvUrl" placeholder="IPTV Server URL"><input id="settingsIptvUser" placeholder="IPTV Username"><input id="settingsIptvPass" type="password" placeholder="IPTV Password"><input id="settingsAiUrl" placeholder="AI Server URL (optional)"><input id="settingsAiUser" placeholder="AI Server Username (optional)"><input id="settingsAiPass" type="password" placeholder="AI Server Password (optional)"><input id="settingsTraktClientId" placeholder="Trakt Client ID (optional)"><input id="settingsTraktSecret" type="password" placeholder="Trakt Client Secret (optional)"></div><p class="sub" id="settingsMeta">Fill in the fields and press Save All. Changes take effect after restarting the app.</p></div></div>
              </section>
            </main>
          </div>
          <div id="toast" class="toast"></div>
          <script>
            const state = { view: 'dashboard', catalogOffset: 0, catalogHasMore: false, catalogLoading: false };
            const viewText = {
              dashboard: ['Dashboard', 'Browse the Android catalog, watch state, central AI picks, and TMDb discovery from your phone or computer.'],
              catalog: ['Catalog', 'Search and filter the catalog cached on this Android device.'],
              watch: ['Watch Data', 'Review watchlist, watch next, progress, and history stored on this Android device.'],
              ai: ['AI Picks', 'Use the central server LLM from this Android-hosted dashboard.'],
              tmdb: ['TMDb', 'Use the central server TMDb connection for popular, top rated, trending, and linked watchlist rows.'],
              social: ['Social Chat', 'Chat through the central server while controlling the Android TV session from this browser.'],
              settings: ['Settings', 'Update IPTV, AI server, and Trakt credentials from your phone.']
            };
            function el(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
            function toast(message) { const node = el('toast'); node.textContent = message; node.classList.add('show'); setTimeout(() => node.classList.remove('show'), 3200); }
            async function json(url, options) {
              const response = await fetch(url, options);
              const data = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));
              if (!response.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || 'Request failed');
              return data;
            }
            function show(view) {
              state.view = view;
              document.querySelectorAll('[id$="View"]').forEach(node => node.classList.add('hidden'));
              el(view + 'View').classList.remove('hidden');
              document.querySelectorAll('.nav button').forEach(button => button.classList.toggle('active', button.dataset.view === view));
              el('pageTitle').textContent = viewText[view][0];
              el('pageSub').textContent = viewText[view][1];
              if (view === 'dashboard') loadDashboard();
              if (view === 'catalog') { loadCatalogOptions().catch(error => toast(error.message)); loadCatalog(true).catch(error => toast(error.message)); }
              if (view === 'watch') loadWatch();
              if (view === 'ai' && !el('aiCards').children.length) loadAi();
              if (view === 'tmdb' && !el('tmdbCards').children.length) loadTmdb();
              if (view === 'social') loadSocial();
              if (view === 'settings') loadSettings();
            }
            function itemCard(item) {
              const image = item.coverUrl || item.backdropUrl;
              const meta = [item.year, item.type, item.category, item.rating ? 'Rating ' + item.rating : ''].filter(Boolean).join(' - ');
              const badges = [item.sourceLabel, item.watchlisted ? 'Watchlist' : '', item.watchNext ? 'Watch Next' : '', item.userRating === 1 ? 'Liked' : '', item.userRating === -1 ? 'Disliked' : '', item.progressPercent ? item.progressPercent + '% watched' : '', item.metadataProvider].filter(Boolean);
              const actions = item.stableKey ? '<div class="pillRow"><button data-cat-action="watchlist" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.watchlisted ? 'Remove Watchlist' : 'Add Watchlist') + '</button><button data-cat-action="watchNext" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.watchNext ? 'Remove Next' : 'Watch Next') + '</button><button data-cat-action="like" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.userRating === 1 ? 'Clear Like' : 'Like') + '</button><button data-cat-action="dislike" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.userRating === -1 ? 'Clear Dislike' : 'Dislike') + '</button><button data-cat-action="ignore" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Ignore</button><button data-explain-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Why</button><button data-similar-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Similar</button><button data-chat-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Chat</button><button data-party-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Party</button></div>' : '';
              return '<article class="card" data-card-key="' + esc(item.stableKey || '') + '"><div class="art">' + (image ? '<img loading="lazy" decoding="async" src="' + esc(image) + '" alt="">' : esc(item.type || 'No artwork')) + '</div><div class="cardBody"><div class="title">' + esc(item.title || 'Untitled') + '</div><div class="meta">' + esc(meta) + '</div>' + (item.description ? '<div class="desc">' + esc(item.description) + '</div>' : '') + '<div class="pillRow">' + badges.slice(0, 5).map(b => '<span class="pill">' + esc(b) + '</span>').join('') + '</div>' + actions + '</div></article>';
            }
            function esc(value) { return String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c])); }
            function renderCards(id, items) { el(id).innerHTML = (items || []).map(itemCard).join('') || '<p class="sub">No items found.</p>'; }
            function renderWatchSummary(summary) {
              const rows = [
                ['Watchlist', summary.watchlist || 0],
                ['Watch Next', summary.watchNext || 0],
                ['Progress', summary.progress || 0],
                ['History', summary.history || 0]
              ];
              el('watchSummary').innerHTML = rows.map(row => '<div class="stat"><div class="label">' + esc(row[0]) + '</div><div class="value">' + esc(row[1]) + '</div></div>').join('');
            }
            function renderWatchRecord(record) {
              const item = record.catalogItem || {};
              const image = item.coverUrl || item.backdropUrl;
              const detail = record.kind === 'progress' || record.kind === 'live'
                ? 'Progress ' + Math.round((record.progress || 0) * 100) + '% - Completed: ' + (record.completed ? 'yes' : 'no')
                : record.kind === 'history'
                  ? 'Progress ' + Math.round((record.progress || 0) * 100) + '% - Plays: ' + (record.playCount || 0) + ' - Completed: ' + (record.completed ? 'yes' : 'no')
                  : 'Saved item';
              const editable = record.kind === 'watchlist' || record.kind === 'watchNext' ? '' :
                '<div class="toolbar compact"><input data-watch-position="' + esc(record.id) + '" inputmode="numeric" value="' + esc(record.positionMs || 0) + '" placeholder="Position ms"><input data-watch-duration="' + esc(record.id) + '" inputmode="numeric" value="' + esc(record.durationMs || 0) + '" placeholder="Duration ms"><input data-watch-play-count="' + esc(record.id) + '" inputmode="numeric" value="' + esc(record.playCount || 0) + '" placeholder="Plays"><select data-watch-completed="' + esc(record.id) + '"><option value="false"' + (!record.completed ? ' selected' : '') + '>Not done</option><option value="true"' + (record.completed ? ' selected' : '') + '>Done</option></select><button data-watch-save="' + esc(record.kind + '|' + record.id) + '">Save</button></div>';
              const itemActions = item.stableKey ? '<div class="pillRow"><button data-cat-action="watchlist" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.watchlisted ? 'Remove Watchlist' : 'Add Watchlist') + '</button><button data-cat-action="watchNext" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.watchNext ? 'Remove Next' : 'Watch Next') + '</button><button data-cat-action="like" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.userRating === 1 ? 'Clear Like' : 'Like') + '</button><button data-cat-action="dislike" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">' + esc(item.userRating === -1 ? 'Clear Dislike' : 'Dislike') + '</button><button data-cat-action="ignore" data-catalog-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Ignore</button><button data-explain-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Why</button><button data-similar-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Similar</button><button data-chat-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Chat</button><button data-party-key="' + esc(item.stableKey) + '">Party</button></div>' : '';
              return '<div class="row" data-watch-record="' + esc(record.id) + '"><div class="rowHead"><span>' + esc(item.title || 'Untitled') + '</span><button data-watch-delete="' + esc(record.kind + '|' + record.id) + '">Delete</button></div><div class="rowText">' + esc([item.type, item.year, item.category].filter(Boolean).join(' - ')) + '</div><div class="rowText">' + esc(detail) + '</div><div class="toolbar compact">' + (image ? '<img loading="lazy" decoding="async" src="' + esc(image) + '" alt="" style="width:56px;height:78px;object-fit:cover;border-radius:8px;">' : '') + '<span class="pill">Rating ' + esc(item.rating || 'n/a') + '</span><span class="pill">' + esc(item.userRating === 1 ? 'Liked' : item.userRating === -1 ? 'Disliked' : 'No rating') + '</span></div>' + editable + itemActions + '</div>';
            }
            function setCatalogLoading(loading, percent) {
              state.catalogLoading = loading;
              el('catalogProgress').classList.toggle('hidden', !loading);
              el('catalogProgressFill').style.width = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percent || 0)) + '%';
            }
            async function loadStatus() {
              const data = await json('/api/status');
              el('statusTitle').textContent = (data.profile || 'Android profile') + ' - App v' + (data.appVersionName || '?') + ' (' + (data.appVersionCode || '?') + ')';
              el('statusDetail').textContent = (data.aiServerConfigured ? 'Central AI/TMDb server connected: ' + data.aiServerUrl : 'Central AI/TMDb server is not configured.') + ' - Web v' + (data.webServerVersionName || '?') + ' (' + (data.webServerVersionCode || '?') + ')';
              el('statusUrl').textContent = data.url || '';
            }
            async function loadDashboard() {
              const data = await json('/api/dashboard');
              el('movieCount').textContent = data.counts.movies || 0;
              el('seriesCount').textContent = data.counts.series || 0;
              el('liveCount').textContent = data.counts.live || 0;
              const watch = data.watch || {};
              el('watchCount').textContent = (watch.watchNext || 0) + (watch.watchlist || 0) + (watch.progress || 0) + (watch.history || 0);
              renderCards('dashboardCards', data.topPicks || []);
              loadStatus();
            }
            async function loadCatalog(reset) {
              if (state.catalogLoading) return;
              if (reset) state.catalogOffset = 0;
              const limit = el('catalogLimit').value || '80';
              const params = new URLSearchParams({ limit: limit, offset: String(state.catalogOffset) });
              if (el('catalogSearch').value.trim()) params.set('search', el('catalogSearch').value.trim());
              if (el('catalogType').value) params.set('type', el('catalogType').value);
              if (el('catalogCategory').value) params.set('category', el('catalogCategory').value);
              if (el('catalogGenre').value) params.set('genre', el('catalogGenre').value);
              if (el('catalogStatus').value && el('catalogStatus').value !== 'all') params.set('status', el('catalogStatus').value);
              if (el('catalogYearFrom').value.trim()) params.set('yearFrom', el('catalogYearFrom').value.trim());
              if (el('catalogYearTo').value.trim()) params.set('yearTo', el('catalogYearTo').value.trim());
              if (Number(el('catalogRatingFrom').value.trim()) > 0) params.set('ratingFrom', el('catalogRatingFrom').value.trim());
              if (el('catalogSort').value) params.set('sort', el('catalogSort').value);
              setCatalogLoading(true, reset ? 20 : 55);
              try {
                const data = await json('/api/catalog?' + params.toString());
                const items = data.items || [];
                const total = data.total || data.count || 0;
                state.catalogHasMore = Boolean(data.hasMore);
                const shown = Math.min(state.catalogOffset + items.length, total);
                el('catalogMeta').textContent = shown + ' shown from ' + total + ' matching items';
                el('catalogCount').textContent = total + ' items';
                el('catalogProgressFill').style.width = (total ? Math.max(8, Math.round((shown / total) * 100)) : 100) + '%';
                if (state.catalogOffset > 0) {
                  el('catalogCards').insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', items.map(itemCard).join(''));
                } else {
                  renderCards('catalogCards', items);
                }
                el('catalogMore').classList.toggle('hidden', !state.catalogHasMore);
                state.catalogOffset += items.length;
              } finally {
                setTimeout(() => setCatalogLoading(false, 0), 180);
              }
            }
            async function loadCatalogOptions() {
              const type = el('catalogType').value;
              const suffix = type ? '?type=' + encodeURIComponent(type) : '';
              const [categories, genres] = await Promise.all([
                json('/api/catalog/categories' + suffix).catch(() => ({ categories: [] })),
                json('/api/catalog/genres' + suffix).catch(() => ({ genres: [] }))
              ]);
              el('catalogCategory').innerHTML = '<option value="">All categories</option>' + (categories.categories || []).map(item => '<option value="' + esc(item.name) + '">' + esc(item.name + ' (' + item.count + ')') + '</option>').join('');
              el('catalogGenre').innerHTML = '<option value="">All genres</option>' + (genres.genres || []).map(item => '<option value="' + esc(item.name) + '">' + esc(item.name + ' (' + item.count + ')') + '</option>').join('');
            }
            async function loadWatch() {
              const params = new URLSearchParams({ kind: el('watchKind').value });
              if (el('watchSearch').value.trim()) params.set('search', el('watchSearch').value.trim());
              const data = await json('/api/watch?' + params.toString());
              renderWatchSummary(data.summary || {});
              el('watchMeta').textContent = (data.items || []).length + ' ' + data.kind + ' records for ' + ((data.profile || {}).name || 'current profile');
              el('watchCards').innerHTML = (data.items || []).map(renderWatchRecord).join('') || '<p class="sub">No watch records found.</p>';
            }
            async function loadAi() {
              el('aiMeta').textContent = 'Asking the central server LLM...';
              const prompt = el('aiPrompt').value.trim();
              const endpoint = prompt ? '/api/ai/natural-search' : '/api/ai/recommendations';
              const limit = Number(el('aiLimit').value || 10);
              const body = prompt ? { query: prompt, limit: limit } : { mood: el('aiMood').value, contentType: el('aiType').value, limit: limit };
              try {
                const data = await json(endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(body) });
                el('aiMeta').textContent = (data.items || []).length + ' AI items';
                renderCards('aiCards', data.items || []);
              } catch (error) {
                el('aiMeta').textContent = error.message;
                renderCards('aiCards', []);
              }
            }
            async function loadTmdb() {
              const collection = el('tmdbCollection').value;
              const url = collection === 'watchlist' ? '/api/tmdb/watchlist' : '/api/tmdb?collection=' + encodeURIComponent(collection) + '&type=' + encodeURIComponent(el('tmdbType').value) + '&limit=' + encodeURIComponent(el('tmdbLimit').value || '80');
              el('tmdbMeta').textContent = 'Loading TMDb from central server...';
              try {
                const data = await json(url);
                el('tmdbMeta').textContent = (data.items || []).length + ' TMDb items';
                renderCards('tmdbCards', data.items || []);
              } catch (error) {
                el('tmdbMeta').textContent = error.message;
                renderCards('tmdbCards', []);
              }
            }
            async function loadSocial() {
              try {
                const [rooms, users, friends] = await Promise.all([json('/api/social/rooms'), json('/api/social/users'), json('/api/social/friends')]);
                el('socialRoomSelect').innerHTML = (rooms.rooms || []).map(room => '<option value="' + esc(room.id) + '">' + esc(room.title || room.id) + '</option>').join('');
                el('socialUsers').innerHTML = (users.users || []).map(user => '<div class="row"><div class="rowHead"><span>' + esc(user.displayName || user.username || 'Viewer') + '</span><button data-friend-user="' + esc(user.id) + '">Add</button></div><div class="rowText">' + esc(user.status || 'offline') + '</div></div>').join('') || '<p class="sub">No users found.</p>';
                el('socialFriends').innerHTML = (friends.friendships || []).map(friend => '<div class="row"><div class="rowHead"><span>' + esc((friend.otherUser || {}).displayName || 'Viewer') + '</span><span>' + esc(friend.status) + '</span></div></div>').join('') || '<p class="sub">No friends yet.</p>';
                el('socialMeta').textContent = (rooms.rooms || []).length + ' rooms available';
                if (el('socialRoomSelect').value) loadSocialMessages();
              } catch (error) {
                el('socialMeta').textContent = error.message;
              }
            }
            async function loadSocialMessages() {
              const roomId = el('socialRoomSelect').value;
              if (!roomId) return;
              const data = await json('/api/social/messages?roomId=' + encodeURIComponent(roomId));
              el('socialMessages').innerHTML = (data.messages || []).map(message => '<div class="row"><div class="rowHead"><span>' + esc(message.senderDisplayName || 'Viewer') + '</span><span>' + new Date(Number(message.createdAt || 0)).toLocaleTimeString() + '</span></div><div class="rowText">' + esc(message.text || '') + '</div></div>').join('') || '<p class="sub">No messages yet.</p>';
            }
            async function sendSocialMessage() {
              const roomId = el('socialRoomSelect').value;
              const text = el('socialMessage').value.trim();
              if (!roomId || !text) return;
              await json('/api/social/messages', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ roomId, text }) });
              el('socialMessage').value = '';
              await loadSocialMessages();
            }
            async function openSocialForCatalog(catalogKey) {
              show('social');
              el('socialCatalogKey').value = catalogKey;
              const rooms = await json('/api/social/rooms?catalogKey=' + encodeURIComponent(catalogKey) + '&roomType=watchParty');
              if (rooms.rooms && rooms.rooms.length) {
                await loadSocial();
                el('socialRoomSelect').value = rooms.rooms[0].id;
                await loadSocialMessages();
              }
              await findSocialViewers();
            }
            async function findSocialViewers() {
              const catalogKey = el('socialCatalogKey').value.trim();
              if (!catalogKey) return;
              const data = await json('/api/social/watching?catalogKey=' + encodeURIComponent(catalogKey));
              el('socialViewers').innerHTML = (data.viewers || []).map(viewer => '<span class="pill">' + esc(((viewer.user || {}).displayName || 'Viewer') + ' watching') + '</span>').join('') || '<span class="pill">No active viewers yet</span>';
            }
            async function createSocialParty(catalogKey) {
              const key = catalogKey || el('socialCatalogKey').value.trim();
              if (!key) return toast('Pick a catalog item first.');
              const data = await json('/api/social/parties', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ catalogKey: key }) });
              toast('Viewing party created.');
              await loadSocial();
              if (data.party && data.party.room) {
                el('socialRoomSelect').value = data.party.room.id;
                await loadSocialMessages();
              }
            }
            async function loadSettings() {
              try {
                const data = await json('/api/settings/load');
                el('settingsIptvUrl').value = data.iptvUrl || '';
                el('settingsIptvUser').value = data.iptvUser || '';
                el('settingsIptvPass').value = data.iptvPass || '';
                el('settingsAiUrl').value = data.aiUrl || '';
                el('settingsAiUser').value = data.aiUser || '';
                el('settingsAiPass').value = data.aiPass || '';
                el('settingsTraktClientId').value = data.traktClientId || '';
                el('settingsTraktSecret').value = data.traktSecret || '';
                el('settingsMeta').textContent = 'Settings loaded from device. Edit and press Save All.';
              } catch (error) {
                el('settingsMeta').textContent = error.message;
              }
            }
            async function saveSettings() {
              const body = {
                iptvUrl: el('settingsIptvUrl').value.trim(),
                iptvUser: el('settingsIptvUser').value.trim(),
                iptvPass: el('settingsIptvPass').value.trim(),
                aiUrl: el('settingsAiUrl').value.trim(),
                aiUser: el('settingsAiUser').value.trim(),
                aiPass: el('settingsAiPass').value.trim(),
                traktClientId: el('settingsTraktClientId').value.trim(),
                traktSecret: el('settingsTraktSecret').value.trim()
              };
              try {
                const data = await json('/api/settings/save', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(body) });
                toast(data.message || 'Settings saved.');
                el('settingsMeta').textContent = data.message || 'Settings saved to device.';
              } catch (error) {
                el('settingsMeta').textContent = error.message;
              }
            }
            async function runCatalogAction(button) {
              const catalogKey = button.dataset.catalogKey;
              const action = button.dataset.catAction;
              if (!catalogKey || !action) return;
              button.disabled = true;
              try {
                const data = await json('/api/catalog/action', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ catalogKey, action }) });
                toast(data.message || 'Catalog updated.');
                const card = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-card-key]')).find(node => node.dataset.cardKey === catalogKey);
                if (action === 'ignore') {
                  if (card) card.remove();
                  el('catalogMeta').textContent = el('catalogMeta').textContent.replace(/^\d+/, String(Math.max(0, el('catalogCards').children.length)));
                } else if (card && data.item) {
                  card.outerHTML = itemCard(data.item);
                }
              } catch (error) {
                toast(error.message);
              } finally {
                button.disabled = false;
              }
            }
            async function saveWatchRecord(kindAndId) {
              const parts = String(kindAndId || '').split('|');
              const kind = parts[0];
              const stableKey = parts.slice(1).join('|');
              if (!kind || !stableKey) return;
              const positionInput = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-watch-position]')).find(node => node.dataset.watchPosition === stableKey);
              const durationInput = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-watch-duration]')).find(node => node.dataset.watchDuration === stableKey);
              const playCountInput = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-watch-play-count]')).find(node => node.dataset.watchPlayCount === stableKey);
              const completedInput = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-watch-completed]')).find(node => node.dataset.watchCompleted === stableKey);
              const body = { kind, stableKey };
              if (positionInput) body.positionMs = Number(positionInput.value || 0);
              if (durationInput) body.durationMs = Number(durationInput.value || 0);
              if (playCountInput) body.watchedCount = Number(playCountInput.value || 0);
              if (completedInput) body.completed = completedInput.value === 'true';
              const data = await json('/api/watch/update', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(body) });
              toast(data.message || 'Watch record saved.');
              await loadWatch();
            }
            async function deleteWatchRecord(kindAndId) {
              const parts = String(kindAndId || '').split('|');
              const kind = parts[0];
              const stableKey = parts.slice(1).join('|');
              if (!kind || !stableKey) return;
              const data = await json('/api/watch/delete', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ kind, stableKey }) });
              toast(data.message || 'Watch record deleted.');
              await loadWatch();
            }
            async function explainCatalogItem(catalogKey) {
              const data = await json('/api/catalog/explain?catalogKey=' + encodeURIComponent(catalogKey));
              toast((data.title ? data.title + ': ' : '') + (data.reason || 'No explanation available.'));
            }
            async function loadSimilarCatalogItems(catalogKey) {
              const data = await json('/api/catalog/similar?catalogKey=' + encodeURIComponent(catalogKey) + '&limit=24');
              state.view = 'catalog';
              document.querySelectorAll('[id$="View"]').forEach(node => node.classList.add('hidden'));
              el('catalogView').classList.remove('hidden');
              document.querySelectorAll('.nav button').forEach(button => button.classList.toggle('active', button.dataset.view === 'catalog'));
              el('pageTitle').textContent = 'Catalog';
              el('pageSub').textContent = 'Search and filter the catalog cached on this Android device.';
              el('catalogMeta').textContent = (data.items || []).length + ' similar items';
              el('catalogCount').textContent = (data.items || []).length + ' items';
              state.catalogHasMore = false;
              state.catalogOffset = (data.items || []).length;
              renderCards('catalogCards', data.items || []);
              el('catalogMore').classList.add('hidden');
            }
            function debounce(fn, delay) {
              let timer = 0;
              return function () {
                clearTimeout(timer);
                timer = setTimeout(fn, delay);
              };
            }
            document.querySelectorAll('.nav button').forEach(button => button.addEventListener('click', () => show(button.dataset.view)));
            el('refreshBtn').addEventListener('click', () => show(state.view));
            el('catalogLoad').addEventListener('click', () => loadCatalog(true));
            el('catalogMore').addEventListener('click', () => loadCatalog(false));
            el('catalogClear').addEventListener('click', () => { el('catalogSearch').value = ''; el('catalogType').value = ''; el('catalogCategory').value = ''; el('catalogGenre').value = ''; el('catalogStatus').value = 'all'; el('catalogYearFrom').value = ''; el('catalogYearTo').value = ''; el('catalogRatingFrom').value = ''; el('catalogSort').value = 'rating'; el('catalogLimit').value = '80'; loadCatalogOptions().then(() => loadCatalog(true)); });
            el('catalogSearch').addEventListener('input', debounce(() => loadCatalog(true), 280));
            el('catalogType').addEventListener('change', () => loadCatalogOptions().then(() => loadCatalog(true)));
            el('catalogCategory').addEventListener('change', () => loadCatalog(true));
            el('catalogGenre').addEventListener('change', () => loadCatalog(true));
            el('catalogStatus').addEventListener('change', () => loadCatalog(true));
            el('catalogSort').addEventListener('change', () => loadCatalog(true));
            el('catalogLimit').addEventListener('change', () => loadCatalog(true));
            ['catalogYearFrom', 'catalogYearTo', 'catalogRatingFrom'].forEach(id => el(id).addEventListener('keydown', event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') loadCatalog(true); }));
            el('watchLoad').addEventListener('click', loadWatch);
            el('watchKind').addEventListener('change', loadWatch);
            el('watchSearch').addEventListener('input', loadWatch);
            el('settingsLoad').addEventListener('click', loadSettings);
            el('settingsSave').addEventListener('click', saveSettings);
            el('settingsRefresh').addEventListener('click', loadSettings);
            el('aiRun').addEventListener('click', loadAi);
            el('tmdbLoad').addEventListener('click', loadTmdb);
            el('tmdbCollection').addEventListener('change', loadTmdb);
            el('tmdbType').addEventListener('change', loadTmdb);
            el('tmdbLimit').addEventListener('change', loadTmdb);
            el('socialRefresh').addEventListener('click', loadSocial);
            el('socialRoomSelect').addEventListener('change', loadSocialMessages);
            el('socialSend').addEventListener('click', sendSocialMessage);
            el('socialMessage').addEventListener('keydown', event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') sendSocialMessage(); });
            el('socialFindWatching').addEventListener('click', findSocialViewers);
            el('socialCreateParty').addEventListener('click', () => createSocialParty());
            el('socialUsers').addEventListener('click', async event => {
              const button = event.target.closest('[data-friend-user]');
              if (!button) return;
              await json('/api/social/friends', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ userId: button.dataset.friendUser }) });
              toast('Friend request updated.');
              loadSocial();
            });
            document.body.addEventListener('click', event => {
              const chatButton = event.target.closest('[data-chat-key]');
              const partyButton = event.target.closest('[data-party-key]');
              const catalogActionButton = event.target.closest('[data-cat-action]');
              const watchSaveButton = event.target.closest('[data-watch-save]');
              const watchDeleteButton = event.target.closest('[data-watch-delete]');
              const explainButton = event.target.closest('[data-explain-key]');
              const similarButton = event.target.closest('[data-similar-key]');
              if (catalogActionButton) runCatalogAction(catalogActionButton);
              if (watchSaveButton) saveWatchRecord(watchSaveButton.dataset.watchSave).catch(error => toast(error.message));
              if (watchDeleteButton) deleteWatchRecord(watchDeleteButton.dataset.watchDelete).catch(error => toast(error.message));
              if (explainButton) explainCatalogItem(explainButton.dataset.explainKey).catch(error => toast(error.message));
              if (similarButton) loadSimilarCatalogItems(similarButton.dataset.similarKey).catch(error => toast(error.message));
              if (chatButton) openSocialForCatalog(chatButton.dataset.chatKey).catch(error => toast(error.message));
              if (partyButton) createSocialParty(partyButton.dataset.partyKey).catch(error => toast(error.message));
            });
            new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
              if (entries.some(entry => entry.isIntersecting) && state.view === 'catalog' && state.catalogHasMore && !state.catalogLoading) {
                loadCatalog(false).catch(error => toast(error.message));
              }
            }, { rootMargin: '700px 0px' }).observe(el('catalogSentinel'));
            loadDashboard().catch(error => toast(error.message));
          </script>
        </body>
        </html>
    """.trimIndent()

    private fun HttpRequest.bodyJson(): JSONObject {
        return if (body.isBlank()) JSONObject() else JSONObject(body)
    }

    private fun JSONObject.optLongNullable(name: String): Long? {
        return if (has(name) && !isNull(name)) optLong(name) else null
    }

    private fun JSONObject.optIntNullable(name: String): Int? {
        return if (has(name) && !isNull(name)) optInt(name) else null
    }

    private fun JSONObject.optBooleanNullable(name: String): Boolean? {
        return if (has(name) && !isNull(name)) optBoolean(name) else null
    }

    private data class HttpRequest(
        val method: String,
        val rawPath: String,
        val headers: Map<String, String>,
        val body: String
    )

    data class AccessInfo(
        val host: String,
        val port: Int,
        val url: String,
        val pairingCode: String
    )

    private data class PublicItemState(
        val ratings: Map<String, Int>,
        val watchlistKeys: Set<String>,
        val watchNextKeys: Set<String>
    )
}

// FILE: app/src/main/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/web/LocalWebAccessStore.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.web

import android.content.Context
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local.SecurePreferences
import java.security.SecureRandom
import android.util.Base64

class LocalWebAccessStore(context: Context) {
    private val prefs = SecurePreferences.open(context.applicationContext, "local_web_access")

    fun sessionToken(): String {
        val existing = prefs.getString(KEY_SESSION_TOKEN, null)
        if (!existing.isNullOrBlank()) return existing
        val bytes = ByteArray(32)
        SecureRandom().nextBytes(bytes)
        val token = Base64.encodeToString(bytes, Base64.URL_SAFE or Base64.NO_WRAP or Base64.NO_PADDING)
        prefs.edit().putString(KEY_SESSION_TOKEN, token).apply()
        return token
    }

    fun pairingCode(): String {
        val existing = prefs.getString(KEY_PAIRING_CODE, null)
        if (!existing.isNullOrBlank()) return existing
        val alphabet = "ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZ23456789"
        val random = SecureRandom()
        val code = buildString { repeat(8) { append(alphabet[random.nextInt(alphabet.length)]) } }
        prefs.edit().putString(KEY_PAIRING_CODE, code).apply()
        return code
    }

    fun rotate(): String {
        prefs.edit().remove(KEY_SESSION_TOKEN).remove(KEY_PAIRING_CODE).apply()
        sessionToken()
        return pairingCode()
    }

    companion object {
        private const val KEY_SESSION_TOKEN = "session_token"
        private const val KEY_PAIRING_CODE = "pairing_code"
    }
}

// FILE: app/src/test/java/com/example/aiiptvviewer/data/local/CatalogMatcherTest.kt
================================================================================
package com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.local

import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.ContentType
import com.example.aiiptvviewer.data.model.IptvItem
import org.junit.Assert.assertEquals
import org.junit.Assert.assertNotEquals
import org.junit.Assert.assertNotNull
import org.junit.Test

class CatalogMatcherTest {
    @Test
    fun normalizeTitleRemovesReleaseNoise() {
        assertEquals("blade runner", CatalogMatcher.normalizeTitle("Blade.Runner (1982) [2160p HEVC]"))
    }

    @Test
    fun providerIdentityPreventsStreamIdCollision() {
        val first = IptvItem(streamId = "42", title = "Movie", contentType = ContentType.MOVIE, providerAccountId = "provider-a")
        val second = IptvItem(streamId = "42", title = "Movie", contentType = ContentType.MOVIE, providerAccountId = "provider-b")
        assertNotEquals(first.stableKey, second.stableKey)
    }

    @Test
    fun matchesMetadataTitleToPlayableCatalog() {
        val local = IptvItem(
            streamId = "99",
            title = "The Matrix 4K HEVC",
            year = "1999",
            contentType = ContentType.MOVIE,
            streamUrl = "https://example.test/movie/99.mp4"
        )
        val metadata = IptvItem(
            streamId = "tmdb-603",
            title = "The Matrix",
            year = "1999",
            contentType = ContentType.MOVIE,
            tmdbId = "603"
        )
        assertNotNull(CatalogMatcher.findLocalCatalogMatch(listOf(local), metadata))
    }
}

  <div class="modalBackdrop hidden" id="itemModal">
    <div class="itemDialog p-6 md:p-8 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-800/80 rounded-3xl shadow-2xl">
      <div class="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-6">
        <div id="modalPoster" class="w-full md:w-60 flex-shrink-0"></div>
        <div class="flex-grow min-w-0 flex flex-col justify-between">

            <div class="flex items-center justify-between gap-4">

            <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm rounded-lg hover:btn-error" id="modalThumbDown">👎 Thumbs Down</button>

  <div class="toast" id="toast"></div>

  <script>
    var type = document.querySelector("#type");
    var category = document.querySelector("#category");
    var genre = document.querySelector("#genre");
    var statusFilter = document.querySelector("#status");
    var yearFrom = document.querySelector("#yearFrom");
    var yearTo = document.querySelector("#yearTo");
    var ratingFrom = document.querySelector("#ratingFrom");
    var sort = document.querySelector("#sort");
    var search = document.querySelector("#search");
    var profile = document.querySelector("#profile");
    var grid = document.querySelector("#grid");
    var summary = document.querySelector("#summary");
    var iptvCredentials = document.querySelector("#iptvCredentials");
    var watchKind = document.querySelector("#watchKind");
    var watchProfile = document.querySelector("#watchProfile");
    var watchSearch = document.querySelector("#watchSearch");
    var watchSummary = document.querySelector("#watchSummary");
    var watchList = document.querySelector("#watchList");
    var watchProfiles = document.querySelector("#watchProfiles");
    var sharedListTitle = document.querySelector("#sharedListTitle");
    var sharedListDescription = document.querySelector("#sharedListDescription");
    var usersSection = document.querySelector("#usersSection");
    var users = document.querySelector("#users");
    var loginCard = document.querySelector("#loginCard");
    var recommendRecipient = document.querySelector("#recommendRecipient");
    var recommendNote = document.querySelector("#recommendNote");
    var socialUsers = document.querySelector("#socialUsers");
    var socialRooms = document.querySelector("#socialRooms");
    var socialMessages = document.querySelector("#socialMessages");
    var sharedLists = document.querySelector("#sharedLists");
    var activeRoomTitle = document.querySelector("#activeRoomTitle");
    var socialMessage = document.querySelector("#socialMessage");
    var roomTitle = document.querySelector("#roomTitle");
    var itemModal = document.querySelector("#itemModal");
    var modalPoster = document.querySelector("#modalPoster");
    var modalType = document.querySelector("#modalType");
    var modalTitle = document.querySelector("#modalTitle");
    var modalMeta = document.querySelector("#modalMeta");
    var modalDescription = document.querySelector("#modalDescription");
    var modalDetails = document.querySelector("#modalDetails");
    var loginUsername = document.querySelector("#loginUsername");
    var registerDisplayName = document.querySelector("#registerDisplayName");
    var loginPassword = document.querySelector("#loginPassword");
    var loginStatus = document.querySelector("#loginStatus");
    var statusDot = document.querySelector("#statusDot");
    var toast = document.querySelector("#toast");
    var savedUsername = localStorage.getItem("serverUsername") || "";
    var savedPassword = localStorage.getItem("serverPassword") || "";
    var catalogById = {};
    var watchCatalogById = {};
    var socialUsersById = {};
    var socialRoomsById = {};
    var activeRoomId = "";
    var activeModalItemId = "";
    var watchProfileSummaries = [];
    loginUsername.value = savedUsername;
    loginPassword.value = savedPassword;

    function authHeaders(extra) {
      var username = loginUsername.value.trim();
      var password = loginPassword.value;
      var headers = Object.assign({}, extra || {});
      if (username && password) headers.Authorization = "Basic " + btoa(username + ":" + password);
      return headers;
    }

    async function apiFetch(url, options) {
      var opts = options || {};
      var response = await fetch(url, Object.assign({}, opts, { headers: authHeaders(opts.headers || {}) }));
      if (response.status === 401) {
        localStorage.removeItem("serverUsername");
        localStorage.removeItem("serverPassword");
        setConnected(false, "Enter a valid server username and password.");
      }
      return response;
    }

    function setConnected(ok, text) {
      loginStatus.textContent = text;
      statusDot.classList.toggle("ok", ok);
      loginCard.classList.toggle("connected", ok);
    }

    function showToast(message) {
      toast.textContent = message;
      toast.classList.add("show");
      clearTimeout(window.__toastTimer);
      window.__toastTimer = setTimeout(function () { toast.classList.remove("show"); }, 2500);
    }

    async function connect() {
      var response = await apiFetch("/api/auth/check");
      if (!response.ok) {
        var errorData = await response.json().catch(function () { return {}; });
        setConnected(false, errorData.error || "Login failed");
        return;
      }
      var data = await response.json();
      var user = data.user || {};
      localStorage.setItem("serverUsername", loginUsername.value.trim());
      localStorage.setItem("serverPassword", loginPassword.value);
      setConnected(true, "Connected as " + (user.displayName || user.username || loginUsername.value.trim()) + (user.isAdmin ? " (admin)" : ""));
      await loadMe();
      await refreshAll();
    }

    async function register() {
      var username = loginUsername.value.trim();
      var password = loginPassword.value;
      var displayName = registerDisplayName.value.trim();
      if (!username || !password) {
        setConnected(false, "Enter a username and password to register.");
        return;
      }

      var response = await fetch("/api/auth/register", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ username: username, password: password, displayName: displayName })
      });
      var data = await response.json().catch(function () { return {}; });
      if (!response.ok) {
        setConnected(false, data.error || "Registration failed");
        showToast(data.error || "Registration failed");
        return;
      }

      showToast(data.emailSent ? "Account created and email sent" : "Account created");
      await connect();
    }

    async function loadStats() {
      var response = await apiFetch("/api/dashboard/stats");

      var data = await response.json();
      var stats = data.stats || {};
      var cards = [
        { label: "Catalog Items", value: stats.catalogItems || 0, hint: (stats.movies || 0) + " movies &middot; " + (stats.series || 0) + " series &middot; " + (stats.live || 0) + " live" },
        { label: "Watch Signals", value: (stats.watchHistory || 0) + (stats.watchProgress || 0), hint: (stats.watchHistory || 0) + " history &middot; " + (stats.watchProgress || 0) + " progress" },
        { label: "Watchlist Items", value: stats.watchlistItems || 0, hint: (stats.profiles || 0) + " profiles" },
        { label: "AI Runs", value: stats.recommendationRuns || 0, hint: (stats.recommendations || 0) + " saved recommendations" },
        { label: "Server Version", value: data.versionName || "?", hint: "Code " + (data.versionCode || "?") }
      ];
      document.querySelector("#statsGrid").innerHTML = cards.map(function (card) {
        return '<div class="stat bg-slate-900/60 border border-slate-800/80 p-5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl flex flex-col justify-between min-h-[110px]">' +
          '<div class="text-xs uppercase font-bold tracking-wider text-slate-400">' + escapeHtml(card.label) + '</div>' +
          '<div class="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-black text-white tracking-tight my-1.5">' + escapeHtml(formatNumber(card.value)) + '</div>' +
          '<div class="text-xs text-slate-400/90 font-medium">' + escapeHtml(card.hint) + '</div>' +
          '</div>';
      }).join("");
    }

    async function loadIptvCredentials() {

      iptvCredentials.innerHTML = items.length ? items.map(function (item) {

          '<div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-sky-950/80 border border-sky-850 flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-sky-400 text-sm">IP</div>' +

app.post("/api/auth/register", authRateLimit, async (req, res) => {
  const existingUsers = await prisma.serverUser.count();
  if (existingUsers > 0 && !config.allowRegistration) {
    res.status(403).json({ error: "Registration is disabled. Ask the administrator to create or invite users." });
    return;
  }
  const username = String(req.body?.username ?? "").trim();
  const password = String(req.body?.password ?? "");
  const displayName = String(req.body?.displayName ?? username).trim();
  if (!username || password.length < 8) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Username and an 8+ character password are required." });
    return;
  }
  const user = await prisma.serverUser.create({ data: { username, passwordHash: hashPassword(password), displayName, isAdmin: existingUsers === 0 } }).catch(() => null);
  if (!user) {
    res.status(409).json({ error: "Username is already taken." });
    return;
  }
  if (username.includes("@")) {
    await sendMail({ to: username, subject: "AI IPTV account created", text: `Your AI IPTV account ${username} was created.` }).catch(() => false);
  }
  res.status(201).json({ user: { id: user.id, username: user.username, displayName: user.displayName, isAdmin: user.isAdmin } });
});

app.get("/api/auth/check", authRateLimit, requireServerUser, (_req, res) => {

// FILE: server/src/config.ts

import dotenv from "dotenv";
import { SERVER_VERSION_CODE, SERVER_VERSION_NAME } from "./version.js";

dotenv.config();

function numberFromEnv(name: string, fallback: number): number {
  const value = Number(process.env[name]);
  return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : fallback;
}

function booleanFromEnv(name: string, fallback = false): boolean {
  const value = process.env[name];
  if (value == null) return fallback;
  return value.toLowerCase() === "true";
}

function listFromEnv(name: string): string[] {
  return (process.env[name] ?? "")
    .split(",")
    .map((value) => value.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
}

const serverPassword = process.env.SERVER_PASSWORD ?? "";
const socialTokenSecret = process.env.SOCIAL_TOKEN_SECRET ?? serverPassword;

export const config = {
  nodeEnv: process.env.NODE_ENV ?? "development",
  serverVersionName: SERVER_VERSION_NAME,
  serverVersionCode: SERVER_VERSION_CODE,
  port: numberFromEnv("PORT", 3099),
  publicBaseUrl: process.env.PUBLIC_BASE_URL ?? "http://localhost:3099/",
  allowedOrigins: listFromEnv("ALLOWED_ORIGINS"),
  trustProxy: booleanFromEnv("TRUST_PROXY", false),
  allowRegistration: booleanFromEnv("ALLOW_REGISTRATION", false),
  serverUsername: process.env.SERVER_USERNAME ?? "",
  serverPassword,
  credentialEncryptionKey: process.env.CREDENTIAL_ENCRYPTION_KEY ?? "",
  openRouterApiKey: process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY ?? "",
  openRouterModel: process.env.OPENROUTER_MODEL ?? "deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash",
  openRouterBaseUrl: process.env.OPENROUTER_BASE_URL ?? "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1",
  openRouterAppName: process.env.OPENROUTER_APP_NAME ?? "AI IPTV Viewer",
  openRouterSiteUrl: process.env.OPENROUTER_SITE_URL ?? process.env.PUBLIC_BASE_URL ?? "http://localhost:3099/",
  tmdbApiKey: process.env.TMDB_API_KEY ?? process.env.TMDB_ACCESS_TOKEN ?? "",
  metadataEnrichmentEnabled: booleanFromEnv("METADATA_ENRICHMENT_ENABLED", true),
  aiLogPrompts: booleanFromEnv("AI_LOG_PROMPTS", false),
  aiMaxCandidates: numberFromEnv("AI_MAX_CANDIDATES", 50),
  aiMaxWebResults: numberFromEnv("AI_MAX_WEB_RESULTS", 10),
  aiRecommendationTimeoutMs: numberFromEnv("AI_RECOMMENDATION_TIMEOUT_MS", 45_000),
  socialTokenSecret,
  rateLimitWindowMs: numberFromEnv("RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS", 60_000),
  rateLimitMaxRequests: numberFromEnv("RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS", 180),
  authRateLimitMaxRequests: numberFromEnv("AUTH_RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS", 12),
  gmailUser: process.env.GMAIL_USER ?? "",
  gmailAppPassword: process.env.GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD ?? ""
};

export function validateProductionConfig(): void {
  if (config.nodeEnv !== "production") return;
  const errors: string[] = [];
  if (!config.publicBaseUrl.startsWith("https://")) errors.push("PUBLIC_BASE_URL must use HTTPS");
  if (!config.socialTokenSecret || config.socialTokenSecret.length < 32) errors.push("SOCIAL_TOKEN_SECRET must be at least 32 characters");
  if (!config.credentialEncryptionKey || config.credentialEncryptionKey.length < 32) errors.push("CREDENTIAL_ENCRYPTION_KEY must be at least 32 characters");
  if (config.allowedOrigins.length === 0) errors.push("ALLOWED_ORIGINS must be configured");
  if (errors.length) throw new Error(`Unsafe production configuration: ${errors.join("; ")}`);
}

function getLocalIpAddresses(): string[] {
  const nets = networkInterfaces();
  const addresses: string[] = [];
  for (const name of Object.keys(nets)) {
    for (const net of nets[name] ?? []) {
      const isIPv4 = net.family === "IPv4" || (net.family as unknown) === 4;
      if (isIPv4 && !net.internal) {
        addresses.push(net.address);
      }
    }
  }
  return addresses;
}

server.listen(config.port, () => {
  console.info(`AI IPTV Viewer server v${config.serverVersionName} (${config.serverVersionCode}) listening on port ${config.port}`);
  console.info(`  - Local:   http://localhost:${config.port}`);
  const localIps = getLocalIpAddresses();
  for (const ip of localIps) {
    console.info(`  - Network: http://${ip}:${config.port}`);
  }
  console.info(`Social WebSocket listening at /ws/social`);
});

// FILE: server/src/lib/recommendationPrompt.ts
================================================================================
import { config } from "../config.js";

export type PromptCandidate = {
  catalogItemId: string;
  title: string;
  type: string;
  year?: string | null;
  genre?: string[];
  category?: string | null;
  rating?: number | null;
};

export type PromptContext = {
  mood?: string;
  contentType?: string;
  genre?: string;
  query?: string;
  useWebSearch?: boolean;
  likedTitles: string[];
  watchHistoryTitles: string[];
  inProgressTitles: string[];
  watchlistTitles: string[];
  dislikedTitles: string[];
  ignoredTitles?: string[];
  candidates: PromptCandidate[];
  webSearchResults?: string[];
};

export function redactPromptText(value: string): string {
  return value
    .replace(/https?:\/\/\S+/gi, "[redacted-url]")
    .replace(/(password|token|secret|api[_-]?key)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/gi, "$1=[redacted]");
}

export function buildRecommendationPrompt(context: PromptContext): string {
  const payload = {
    task: "Recommend movies and TV shows for this viewer profile based on their full taste profile.",
    rules: [
      "Return valid JSON only matching the schema.",
      "Do not limit recommendations to candidateItems or the IPTV catalog. Recommend the best fit from movies and TV broadly.",
      "candidateItems are optional playable matches from the local IPTV catalog. Use them only to populate catalogItemId when the exact recommended title is present.",
      "If the best recommendation is not in candidateItems, set catalogItemId to null and still recommend it.",
      "Use likedTitles, watchHistoryTitles, inProgressTitles, and watchlistTitles as positive taste signals.",
      "Use dislikedTitles and ignoredTitles as negative taste signals and avoid close matches unless the user explicitly asks for them.",
      "Respect requestedMood, requestedGenre, requestedContentType, and naturalLanguageQuery from the page inputs when provided.",
      "When webSearchResults are present, use them as current discovery context, but do not invent facts not supported by the profile or snippets.",
      "Keep each reason short, specific, and based on taste similarity or the user's request."
    ],
    pagePreferences: {
      requestedMood: context.mood ?? "any",
      requestedGenre: context.genre ?? "any",
      requestedContentType: context.contentType ?? "any",
      naturalLanguageQuery: context.query ?? "",
      webSearchRequested: Boolean(context.useWebSearch)
    },
    requestedMood: context.mood ?? "any",
    requestedGenre: context.genre ?? "any",
    requestedContentType: context.contentType ?? "any",
    naturalLanguageQuery: context.query ?? "",
    likedTitles: context.likedTitles,
    watchHistoryTitles: context.watchHistoryTitles,
    inProgressTitles: context.inProgressTitles,
    watchlistTitles: context.watchlistTitles,
    dislikedTitles: context.dislikedTitles,
    ignoredTitles: context.ignoredTitles ?? [],
    candidateItems: context.candidates,
    webSearchResults: context.webSearchResults
  };

  const prompt = redactPromptText(JSON.stringify(payload));
  const maxCharacters = Math.max(4000, config.aiMaxCandidates * 420);
  return prompt.length > maxCharacters ? prompt.slice(0, maxCharacters) : prompt;
}

export function estimateTokens(text: string): number {
  return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
}

// FILE: server/src/lib/recommendationSchemas.ts

import { z } from "zod";

export const moodSchema = z.enum([
  "funny",
  "action",
  "scary",
  "chill",
  "dateNight",
  "family",
  "binge",
  "short",
  "smart",
  "any"
]);

export const contentTypeSchema = z.enum(["movie", "series", "episode", "live", "any"]);
export const recommendationModeSchema = z.enum(["quality", "short", "family", "hidden", "new", "comfort", "action", "any"]).default("any");

export const aiRecommendationRequestSchema = z.object({
  profileId: z.string().min(1),
  mood: moodSchema.default("any"),
  contentType: contentTypeSchema.default("any"),
  mode: recommendationModeSchema.optional(),
  limit: z.number().int().min(1).max(50).default(20),
  useWebSearch: z.boolean().default(false),
  genre: z.string().max(80).optional(),
  query: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  prompt: z.string().max(30000).optional()
});

export const explainRequestSchema = z.object({
  profileId: z.string().min(1),
  catalogItemId: z.string().min(1)
});

export const similarRequestSchema = z.object({
  profileId: z.string().min(1),
  catalogItemId: z.string().min(1),
  limit: z.number().int().min(1).max(50).default(20),
  useWebSearch: z.boolean().default(false)
});

export const recommendationFeedbackSchema = z.object({
  profileId: z.string().min(1),
  catalogItemId: z.string().min(1),
  action: z.string().min(1).max(80),
  mode: z.string().max(80).optional()
});

export const naturalSearchRequestSchema = z.object({
  profileId: z.string().min(1),
  query: z.string().min(1).max(500),
  limit: z.number().int().min(1).max(50).default(20),
  useWebSearch: z.boolean().default(false)
});

const aiStringSchema = z.preprocess((value) => {
  if (value == null) return value;
  return String(value);
}, z.string());

const aiNullableStringSchema = z.preprocess((value) => {
  if (value == null || value === "") return null;
  return String(value);
}, z.string().nullable());

const aiScoreSchema = z.preprocess((value) => {
  const numberValue = typeof value === "number" ? value : Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(numberValue)) return value;
  if (numberValue > 1 && numberValue <= 100) return numberValue / 100;
  return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, numberValue));
}, z.number().min(0).max(1));

const aiMatchedSignalsSchema = z.preprocess((value) => {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map((item) => String(item));
  if (value == null || value === "") return [];
  return [String(value)];
}, z.array(z.string()).default([]));

export const aiModelResponseSchema = z.object({
  summary: aiStringSchema.default("Recommendations based on your preferences."),
  recommendations: z.array(
    z.object({
      catalogItemId: aiNullableStringSchema.optional(),
      title: aiStringSchema,
      type: z.enum(["movie", "series", "episode", "live", "any"]).default("any"),
      year: aiNullableStringSchema.optional(),
      score: aiScoreSchema,
      reason: aiStringSchema,
      matchedSignals: aiMatchedSignalsSchema
    })
  )
});

export const interpretedFiltersSchema = z.object({
  contentType: contentTypeSchema.optional(),
  mood: moodSchema.optional(),
  maxDurationMinutes: z.number().int().positive().optional(),
  excludeCompleted: z.boolean().optional()
});

export type AiRecommendationRequest = z.infer<typeof aiRecommendationRequestSchema>;
export type SimilarRequest = z.infer<typeof similarRequestSchema>;
export type NaturalSearchRequest = z.infer<typeof naturalSearchRequestSchema>;
export type RecommendationFeedback = z.infer<typeof recommendationFeedbackSchema>;
export type AiModelResponse = z.infer<typeof aiModelResponseSchema>;

export const aiRecommendationSchemaDescription = `{
  "summary": "string explaining the choices",
  "recommendations": [
    {
      "catalogItemId": "matching catalogItemId if it appears in candidateItems, or null",
      "title": "the recommended movie or show title",
      "type": "movie, series, episode, or live",
      "year": "release year or null",
      "score": 0.0,
      "reason": "short user-facing reason based on taste similarity",
      "matchedSignals": ["signal"]
    }
  ]
}`;

// FILE: server/src/middleware/rateLimit.ts
================================================================================
import type { NextFunction, Request, Response } from "express";

interface Bucket {
  count: number;
  resetAt: number;
}

export function rateLimit(options: { windowMs: number; max: number; keyPrefix?: string }) {
  const buckets = new Map<string, Bucket>();
  return (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void => {
    const now = Date.now();
    if (buckets.size > 10_000) {
      for (const [key, bucket] of buckets) if (bucket.resetAt <= now) buckets.delete(key);
    }
    const key = `${options.keyPrefix ?? "default"}:${req.ip || req.socket.remoteAddress || "unknown"}`;
    const current = buckets.get(key);
    const bucket = !current || current.resetAt <= now ? { count: 0, resetAt: now + options.windowMs } : current;
    bucket.count += 1;
    buckets.set(key, bucket);
    res.setHeader("RateLimit-Limit", String(options.max));
    res.setHeader("RateLimit-Remaining", String(Math.max(0, options.max - bucket.count)));
    res.setHeader("RateLimit-Reset", String(Math.ceil(bucket.resetAt / 1000)));
    if (bucket.count > options.max) {
      res.setHeader("Retry-After", String(Math.max(1, Math.ceil((bucket.resetAt - now) / 1000))));
      res.status(429).json({ error: "Too many requests. Try again later." });
      return;
    }
    next();
  };
}

// FILE: server/src/middleware/requestContext.ts
================================================================================
import { randomUUID } from "node:crypto";
import type { NextFunction, Request, Response } from "express";

export function requestContext(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void {
  const requestId = req.header("x-request-id")?.slice(0, 100) || randomUUID();
  res.locals.requestId = requestId;
  res.setHeader("X-Request-Id", requestId);
  const startedAt = Date.now();
  res.on("finish", () => {
    console.info(JSON.stringify({
      level: "info",
      requestId,
      method: req.method,
      path: req.originalUrl,
      status: res.statusCode,
      durationMs: Date.now() - startedAt
    }));
  });
  next();
}

export function scopeProfileIds(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void {
  const authUserId = res.locals.authUser?.id as string | undefined;
  if (!authUserId) {
    next();
    return;
  }
  const scope = (value: unknown): string | undefined => {
    if (typeof value !== "string" || !value.trim()) return undefined;
    const raw = value.trim();
    if (raw.startsWith(`${authUserId}:`)) return raw;
    const localId = raw.includes(":") ? raw.substring(raw.lastIndexOf(":") + 1) : raw;
    return `${authUserId}:${localId}`;
  };
  const queryProfile = scope(req.query.profileId ?? req.query.userId);
  if (queryProfile) {
    req.query.profileId = queryProfile;
    if (req.query.userId != null) req.query.userId = authUserId;
  }
  if (req.body && typeof req.body === "object") {
    const body = req.body as Record<string, unknown>;
    const bodyProfile = scope(body.profileId ?? body.userId);
    if (bodyProfile) body.profileId = bodyProfile;
    if (body.userId != null) body.userId = authUserId;
  }
  next();
}
