// FILE: server/src/realtime/socialRealtime.ts
================================================================================
import type { IncomingMessage, Server } from "node:http";
import { WebSocketServer, type WebSocket } from "ws";
import { verifySocialToken } from "../services/socialTokenService.js";
import {
  createMessage,
  clearWatchPresence,
  ensureSocialUserByPayload,
  getActiveViewersForCatalog,
  joinRoom,
  leaveRoom,
  touchSocialUser,
  upsertWatchPresence,
  type SocialContext
} from "../services/socialService.js";

type ClientRecord = {
  socket: WebSocket;
  user: SocialContext;
  rooms: Set<string>;
};

const clients = new Map<WebSocket, ClientRecord>();
const rooms = new Map<string, Set<WebSocket>>();

function send(socket: WebSocket, payload: unknown): void {
  if (socket.readyState === socket.OPEN) {
    socket.send(JSON.stringify(payload));
  }
}

function safeString(value: unknown, maxLength: number): string | undefined {
  if (typeof value !== "string") return undefined;
  const trimmed = value.trim();
  return trimmed ? trimmed.slice(0, maxLength) : undefined;
}

function safeClientMessageId(value: unknown): string | undefined {
  return safeString(value, 128);
}

export function broadcastToRoom(roomId: string, payload: unknown, exceptSocket?: WebSocket): void {
  const sockets = rooms.get(roomId) ?? new Set<WebSocket>();
  for (const socket of sockets) {
    if (socket !== exceptSocket) send(socket, payload);
  }
}

export function broadcastSocialEvent(roomId: string, payload: unknown): void {
  broadcastToRoom(roomId, payload);
}

async function joinSocketRoom(client: ClientRecord, roomId: string): Promise<boolean> {
  if (client.rooms.has(roomId)) {
    await joinRoom(roomId, client.user.userId);
    return false;
  }

  client.rooms.add(roomId);
  if (!rooms.has(roomId)) rooms.set(roomId, new Set());
  rooms.get(roomId)!.add(client.socket);

  await joinRoom(roomId, client.user.userId);
  broadcastToRoom(roomId, { type: "userJoined", roomId, user: client.user }, client.socket);
  return true;
}

async function leaveSocketRoom(client: ClientRecord, roomId: string): Promise<void> {
  if (!client.rooms.has(roomId)) return;

  client.rooms.delete(roomId);
  rooms.get(roomId)?.delete(client.socket);
  await leaveRoom(roomId, client.user.userId);
  broadcastToRoom(roomId, { type: "userLeft", roomId, user: client.user }, client.socket);
}

function getToken(request: IncomingMessage): string | null {
  const host = request.headers.host ?? "localhost";
  const url = new URL(request.url ?? "/", `http://${host}`);
  const tokenFromQuery = url.searchParams.get("token");
  if (tokenFromQuery) return tokenFromQuery;

  const authHeader = request.headers.authorization ?? "";
  const [scheme, token] = authHeader.split(" ");
  if (scheme?.toLowerCase() === "bearer" && token) return token;
  return null;
}

function parseJsonEvent(raw: WebSocket.RawData): Record<string, unknown> | null {
  try {
    const parsed = JSON.parse(String(raw));
    return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" ? parsed as Record<string, unknown> : null;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

export function attachSocialWebSocket(server: Server): void {
  const wss = new WebSocketServer({ noServer: true });

  server.on("upgrade", (request, socket, head) => {
    const pathname = new URL(request.url ?? "/", `http://${request.headers.host ?? "localhost"}`).pathname;
    if (pathname !== "/ws/social") return;

    const token = getToken(request);
    const payload = token ? verifySocialToken(token) : null;
    if (!payload) {
      socket.write("HTTP/1.1 401 Unauthorized\r\nConnection: close\r\n\r\n");
      socket.destroy();
      return;
    }

    wss.handleUpgrade(request, socket, head, (ws) => wss.emit("connection", ws, request, payload));
  });

  wss.on("connection", async (socket: WebSocket, _request: IncomingMessage, payload: ReturnType<typeof verifySocialToken>) => {
    if (!payload) {
      socket.close(1008, "Unauthorized");
      return;
    }

    const user = await ensureSocialUserByPayload({
      userId: payload.userId,
      username: payload.username,
      displayName: payload.displayName
    });
    const client: ClientRecord = { socket, user, rooms: new Set() };
    clients.set(socket, client);
    send(socket, { type: "connected", user, serverTime: new Date().toISOString() });

    socket.on("message", async (raw) => {
      const event = parseJsonEvent(raw);
      if (!event) {
        send(socket, { type: "error", error: "Invalid JSON event" });
        return;
      }

      try {
        const roomId = safeString(event.roomId, 256);

        if (event.type === "ping") {
          send(socket, { type: "pong", serverTime: new Date().toISOString() });
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "joinRoom" && roomId) {
          await joinSocketRoom(client, roomId);
          send(socket, { type: "joinedRoom", roomId });
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "leaveRoom" && roomId) {
          await leaveSocketRoom(client, roomId);
          send(socket, { type: "leftRoom", roomId });
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "typing" && roomId) {
          if (!client.rooms.has(roomId)) await joinSocketRoom(client, roomId);
          broadcastToRoom(roomId, { type: "typing", roomId, user: client.user, at: new Date().toISOString() }, socket);
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "watchPresence") {
          const presence = await upsertWatchPresence(client.user.userId, {
            catalogItemId: safeString(event.catalogItemId, 256),
            catalogKey: safeString(event.catalogKey, 256),
            catalogTitle: safeString(event.catalogTitle, 240),
            catalogType: safeString(event.catalogType, 64),
            roomId,
            positionMs: typeof event.positionMs === "number" || typeof event.positionMs === "string" ? event.positionMs : 0,
            durationMs: typeof event.durationMs === "number" || typeof event.durationMs === "string" ? event.durationMs : 0,
            playbackState: safeString(event.playbackState, 64),
            deviceName: safeString(event.deviceName, 120)
          });
          if (presence.roomId) {
            await joinSocketRoom(client, presence.roomId);
            broadcastToRoom(presence.roomId, { type: "watchPresence", roomId: presence.roomId, presence }, client.socket);
            send(socket, { type: "watchPresence", roomId: presence.roomId, presence });
          }
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "stopWatching") {
          await clearWatchPresence(client.user.userId, safeString(event.catalogKey, 256));
          send(socket, { type: "stoppedWatching", catalogKey: safeString(event.catalogKey, 256) });
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "getCurrentViewers") {
          const catalogKey = safeString(event.catalogItemId, 256) ?? safeString(event.catalogKey, 256);
          if (!catalogKey) {
            send(socket, { type: "error", error: "catalogItemId or catalogKey is required" });
            return;
          }
          send(socket, { type: "currentViewers", catalogKey, viewers: await getActiveViewersForCatalog(catalogKey) });
          return;
        }

        if (event.type === "sendMessage" && roomId) {
          await joinSocketRoom(client, roomId);
          const message = await createMessage(roomId, client.user.userId, {
            clientMessageId: safeClientMessageId(event.clientMessageId),
            text: typeof event.text === "string" ? event.text : "",
            messageType: safeString(event.messageType, 64),
            sharePayload: event.sharePayload
          });
          const responseEvent = { type: "messageCreated", roomId, message };
          broadcastToRoom(roomId, responseEvent, socket);
          send(socket, responseEvent);
          return;
        }

        send(socket, { type: "error", error: `Unknown or invalid event type: ${String(event.type ?? "")}` });
      } catch (error) {
        send(socket, { type: "error", error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Event failed" });
      }
    });

    socket.on("close", async () => {
      clients.delete(socket);
      for (const roomId of client.rooms) rooms.get(roomId)?.delete(socket);
      await touchSocialUser(client.user.userId, "offline");
    });

    socket.on("error", () => {
      clients.delete(socket);
    });
  });
}

import { Router } from "express";
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";

adminRoutes.get("/summary", async (_req, res) => {
  const [users, profiles, catalogItems, movies, series, live, credentials, pairings, activePairings, watchHistory, watchProgress, recommendations, recommendationRuns, socialRooms, messages, auditEvents] = await Promise.all([
    prisma.serverUser.count(),
    prisma.profile.count(),
    prisma.catalogItem.count(),
    prisma.catalogItem.count({ where: { type: "movie" } }),
    prisma.catalogItem.count({ where: { type: "series" } }),
    prisma.catalogItem.count({ where: { type: "live" } }),
    prisma.iptvCredential.count(),
    prisma.devicePairing.count(),
    prisma.devicePairing.count({ where: { status: "approved" } }),
    prisma.watchHistory.count(),
    prisma.watchProgress.count(),
    prisma.recommendation.count(),
    prisma.recommendationRun.count(),
    prisma.chatRoom.count(),
    prisma.chatMessage.count(),
    prisma.adminAuditEvent.count().catch(() => 0)
  ]);
  const quality = await getQualityReport().catch(() => ({ summary: [], lowQuality: [] }));
  const duplicates = await getDuplicateGroups(20).catch(() => []);
  res.json({
    overview: { versionName: config.serverVersionName, versionCode: config.serverVersionCode, nodeEnv: config.nodeEnv, time: new Date().toISOString() },
    users: { users, profiles, credentials },
    devices: { pairings, activePairings },
    catalog: { catalogItems, movies, series, live, quality: quality.summary, duplicateGroups: duplicates.length },
    ai: { recommendations, recommendationRuns, model: config.openRouterModel, configured: Boolean(config.openRouterApiKey) },
    social: { socialRooms, messages },
    sync: { watchHistory, watchProgress },
    security: { allowedOrigins: config.allowedOrigins, registrationAllowed: config.allowRegistration, auditEvents }
  });
});

  res.json(result);
});

  res.json(result);
});

export const aiRoutes = Router();

function modelErrorStatus(error: unknown): number {
  const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "";
  if (
    message.includes("OPENROUTER_API_KEY") ||
    message.includes("OpenRouter returned HTTP") ||
    message.includes("OpenRouter request timed out") ||
    message.includes("OpenRouter returned invalid JSON")
  ) {
    return 503;
  }
  return 500;
}

aiRoutes.get("/capabilities", (_req, res) => {
  res.json({
    llm: {
      configured: Boolean(config.openRouterApiKey),
      provider: "OpenRouter",
      model: config.openRouterModel,
      baseUrl: config.openRouterBaseUrl,
      recommendations: true,
      naturalSearch: true,
      explanations: true
    },
    tmdb: {
      configured: Boolean(config.tmdbApiKey),
      metadataEnrichmentEnabled: config.metadataEnrichmentEnabled,
      collections: ["popular", "top_rated", "trending"],
      accountLinking: true
    }
  });
});

aiRoutes.post("/recommendations/prompt", async (req, res) => {
  const parsed = aiRecommendationRequestSchema.safeParse(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid recommendation request", details: parsed.error.flatten() });
    return;
  }
  const result = await previewAiRecommendationPrompt(parsed.data);
  res.json(result);
});

aiRoutes.post("/recommendations", async (req, res) => {
  const parsed = aiRecommendationRequestSchema.safeParse(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid recommendation request", details: parsed.error.flatten() });
    return;
  }
  try {
    const result = await getAiRecommendations(parsed.data);
    res.json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(modelErrorStatus(error)).json({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "AI recommendation failed" });
  }
});

    return;
  }
  try {
    res.json(await explainRecommendation(parsed.data.profileId, parsed.data.catalogItemId));
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(modelErrorStatus(error) === 503 ? 503 : 404).json({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Catalog item not found" });
  }
});

});

function queryString(value: unknown): string | undefined {
  return typeof value === "string" && value.trim() ? value.trim() : undefined;
}

function queryNumber(value: unknown): number | undefined {
  const parsed = Number(value);
  return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : undefined;
}

function itemYear(item: { year?: string | null; title?: string | null; description?: string | null }): number | null {
  const haystack = [item.year, item.title, item.description].filter(Boolean).join(" ");
  const match = haystack.match(/\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b/);
  if (!match) return null;
  const year = Number(match[1]);
  return Number.isFinite(year) ? year : null;
}

function safeJsonParse<T>(value: string | null | undefined, fallback: T): T {
  if (!value) return fallback;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(value) as T;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function itemGenres(item: { genreJson?: string | null; category?: string | null }): string[] {
  const genres = safeJsonParse<string[]>(item.genreJson, []);
  return [...genres, item.category].filter((value): value is string => Boolean(value));
}

function cleanOptionLabel(value: string | undefined): string | undefined {
  return value?.replace(/\s+\(\d+\)$/, "").trim();
}

type PublicCatalogItem = ReturnType<typeof toPublicCatalogItem> & Record<string, unknown>;
type CatalogPreferenceSummary = { catalogItemId: string; rating: number | null; ignored: boolean };

function normalizeMatchTitle(value: unknown): string {
  return String(value ?? "")
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\[[^\]]*]/g, " ")
    .replace(/\([^)]*\)/g, " ")
    .replace(/\b(4k|uhd|fhd|hd|sd|hdr|x264|x265|hevc|bluray|web[- ]?dl|multi|dubbed|subbed)\b/g, " ")
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, " ")
    .trim();
}

function catalogTypeForTmdb(type: unknown): string {
  const value = String(type ?? "").toLowerCase();
  return value === "tv" || value === "series" ? "series" : "movie";
}

function findCatalogMatch(tmdbItem: Record<string, unknown>, catalogItems: PublicCatalogItem[]): PublicCatalogItem | undefined {
  const tmdbId = queryString(tmdbItem.tmdbId) ?? queryString(tmdbItem.metadataId);
  const type = catalogTypeForTmdb(tmdbItem.type ?? tmdbItem.contentType);
  const title = normalizeMatchTitle(tmdbItem.title);
  const year = queryString(tmdbItem.year);

  if (tmdbId) {
    const idMatch = catalogItems.find((item) =>
      item.type === type &&
      (String(item.tmdbId ?? "") === tmdbId ||
        (String(item.metadataProvider ?? "").toLowerCase().includes("tmdb") && String(item.metadataId ?? "") === tmdbId))
    );
    if (idMatch) return idMatch;
  }

  return catalogItems.find((item) => {
    if (item.type !== type) return false;
    const itemTitle = normalizeMatchTitle(item.title);
    if (!itemTitle || itemTitle !== title) return false;
    if (!year || !item.year) return true;
    return String(item.year) === year;
  }) ?? catalogItems.find((item) => {
    if (item.type !== type) return false;
    const itemTitle = normalizeMatchTitle(item.title);
    return title.length >= 4 && itemTitle.length >= 4 && (itemTitle.includes(title) || title.includes(itemTitle));
  });
}

function splitMatchedTmdbItems(tmdbItems: Record<string, unknown>[], catalogItems: PublicCatalogItem[]) {
  const matched: Record<string, unknown>[] = [];
  const unmatched: Record<string, unknown>[] = [];
  const seenMatched = new Set<string>();

  for (const tmdbItem of tmdbItems) {
    const match = findCatalogMatch(tmdbItem, catalogItems);
    if (match) {
      const key = String(match.id ?? match.stableKey ?? `${match.type}:${match.title}`);
      if (!seenMatched.has(key)) {
        seenMatched.add(key);
        matched.push({
          ...match,
          description: queryString(match.description) ?? queryString(tmdbItem.description) ?? "",
          coverUrl: queryString(match.coverUrl) ?? queryString(tmdbItem.coverUrl),
          backdropUrl: queryString(match.backdropUrl) ?? queryString(tmdbItem.backdropUrl),
          tmdbId: queryString(match.tmdbId) ?? queryString(tmdbItem.tmdbId),
          metadataProvider: queryString(match.metadataProvider) ?? "TMDb",
          metadataId: queryString(match.metadataId) ?? queryString(tmdbItem.metadataId),
          sourceLabel: `${queryString(tmdbItem.sourceLabel) ?? "TMDb"} - Matched to IPTV`
        });
      }
    } else {
      unmatched.push({
        ...tmdbItem,
        sourceLabel: `${queryString(tmdbItem.sourceLabel) ?? "TMDb"} - Unmatched`
      });
    }
  }

  return { matched, unmatched, items: [...matched, ...unmatched] };
}

catalogRoutes.post("/metadata", async (req, res) => {
  const items = Array.isArray(req.body?.items) ? req.body.items as Record<string, unknown>[] : [];
  const saved: unknown[] = [];
  let enriched = 0;
  for (const item of items) {
    const savedItem = await upsertCatalogItem(item);
    saved.push(savedItem);
    if (enriched < 15) {
      const result = await enrichCatalogItemWithExternalMetadataIfNeeded(savedItem.id).catch(() => null);
      if (result) enriched += 1;
    }
  }
  res.json({ saved: saved.length, enriched });
});

catalogRoutes.get("/", async (req, res) => {
  const type = queryString(req.query.type);

      isBlocked: false,

          { category: { contains: search } },
          { year: { contains: search } }

    },
    select: safeCatalogSelect(),
    orderBy: [{ addedAt: "desc" }],
    take: 2000
  });

    prisma.watchHistory.findMany({ where: { profileId }, select: { catalogItemId: true, watchedAt: true, completed: true } }),
    prisma.watchProgress.findMany({ where: { profileId }, select: { catalogItemId: true, progress: true, completed: true, updatedAt: true } }),
    prisma.watchlistItem.findMany({ where: { profileId }, select: { catalogItemId: true, createdAt: true } })
  ]);
  const preferences = await prisma.userCatalogPreference.findMany({ where: { profileId }, select: { catalogItemId: true, rating: true, ignored: true } });
  const watchedIds = new Set(history.filter((item) => item.completed).map((item) => item.catalogItemId));
  const inProgressIds = new Set(progress.filter((item) => !item.completed && item.progress > 0).map((item) => item.catalogItemId));
  const watchlistIds = new Set(watchlist.map((item) => item.catalogItemId));

  for (const item of progress) recentWatchById.set(item.catalogItemId, Math.max(recentWatchById.get(item.catalogItemId) ?? 0, item.updatedAt.getTime()));

    const year = itemYear(item);
    if (yearFrom != null && year != null && year < yearFrom) return false;
    if (yearTo != null && year != null && year > yearTo) return false;
    if (genre && !itemGenres(item).some((value) => value.toLowerCase() === genre.toLowerCase())) return false;
    if (status === "watched" && !watchedIds.has(item.id)) return false;

    if (status === "inProgress" && !inProgressIds.has(item.id)) return false;
    if (status === "watchlist" && !watchlistIds.has(item.id)) return false;
    return true;
  });

  filtered.sort((left, right) => {
    if (sort === "title") return left.title.localeCompare(right.title);
    if (sort === "year") return (itemYear(right) ?? 0) - (itemYear(left) ?? 0);
    if (sort === "added") return right.addedAt.getTime() - left.addedAt.getTime();
    if (sort === "watched") return (recentWatchById.get(right.id) ?? 0) - (recentWatchById.get(left.id) ?? 0);
    if (sort === "watchlist") return Number(watchlistIds.has(right.id)) - Number(watchlistIds.has(left.id));
    return (right.rating ?? 0) - (left.rating ?? 0) || right.addedAt.getTime() - left.addedAt.getTime();
  });

  const items = filtered.slice(0, take).map((item) => {
    const publicItem = toPublicCatalogItem(item) as Record<string, unknown>;
    return {
      ...publicItem,
      watched: watchedIds.has(item.id),
      inProgress: inProgressIds.has(item.id),
      watchlisted: watchlistIds.has(item.id),
      userRating: preferenceById.get(item.id)?.rating ?? null,
      ignored: preferenceById.get(item.id)?.ignored ?? false
    };
  });
  res.json({ items, total: filtered.length, limit: take });
});

catalogRoutes.get("/genres", async (req, res) => {

    where: {
      isBlocked: false,
      ...(type ? { type } : {})
    },
    select: {
      genreJson: true,
      category: true
    },
    take: 5000
  });
  const counts = new Map<string, number>();
  for (const item of items) {
    for (const genre of itemGenres(item)) {
      counts.set(genre, (counts.get(genre) ?? 0) + 1);

    genres: [...counts.entries()]
      .sort((left, right) => right[1] - left[1] || left[0].localeCompare(right[0]))

  });
});

catalogRoutes.get("/external/tmdb/:collection", async (req, res) => {
  const collection = req.params.collection === "top_rated" ? "top_rated"
    : req.params.collection === "trending" ? "trending"
      : "popular";
  const rawType = queryString(req.query.type) ?? "movie";
  const type = rawType === "series" || rawType === "tv" ? "tv" : rawType === "all" ? "all" : "movie";
  const limit = Math.min(Number(req.query.limit ?? 40) || 40, 300);
  try {
    const items = await getTmdbCollection(collection, type, limit) as Record<string, unknown>[];
    const catalogTypes = type === "all" ? ["movie", "series"] : [type === "tv" ? "series" : "movie"];
    const catalogItems = (await prisma.catalogItem.findMany({
      where: { isBlocked: false, type: { in: catalogTypes } },
      select: safeCatalogSelect(),
      orderBy: [{ updatedAt: "desc" }],
      take: 5000
    })).map((item) => toPublicCatalogItem(item) as PublicCatalogItem);
    res.json(splitMatchedTmdbItems(items, catalogItems));
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(503).json({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "TMDB collection unavailable." });
  }
});

catalogRoutes.post("/enrich", async (req, res) => {
  const ids = Array.isArray(req.body?.catalogItemIds)
    ? req.body.catalogItemIds.map(String).map((id) => id.trim()).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 50)
    : [];
  const limit = Math.min(Number(req.body?.limit ?? 20) || 20, 50);
  const selectedIds = ids.length ? ids : (await prisma.catalogItem.findMany({
    where: { isBlocked: false },
    select: { id: true },
    orderBy: { updatedAt: "asc" },
    take: limit
  })).map((item) => item.id);

  const enriched: unknown[] = [];
  const failed: Array<{ id: string; error: string }> = [];
  for (const id of selectedIds) {
    try {
      enriched.push(await enrichCatalogItemWithExternalMetadata(id));
    } catch (error) {
      failed.push({ id, error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Could not enrich item" });
    }
  }
  res.json({ enriched, failed });
});

  }

catalogRoutes.get("/watch", async (req, res) => {
  const profileId = queryString(req.query.profileId) ?? "default";
  const kind = queryString(req.query.kind) ?? "watchlist";
  const search = queryString(req.query.search)?.toLowerCase() ?? "";
  const take = Math.min(Number(req.query.limit ?? 200) || 200, 500);
  const preferences = await prisma.userCatalogPreference.findMany({ where: { profileId }, select: { catalogItemId: true, rating: true, ignored: true } });
  const preferenceById = new Map<string, CatalogPreferenceSummary>(
    (preferences as CatalogPreferenceSummary[]).map((item) => [item.catalogItemId, item])
  );

  if (kind === "progress") {
    const rows = await prisma.watchProgress.findMany({
      where: { profileId },
      include: { catalogItem: { select: safeCatalogSelect() } },
      orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" },
      take
    });
    const items = rows
      .filter((row) => !preferenceById.get(row.catalogItemId)?.ignored)
      .filter((row) => !search || row.catalogItem.title.toLowerCase().includes(search) || (row.catalogItem.category ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(search))
      .map((row) => ({ id: row.id, kind, progress: row.progress, positionMs: row.positionMs, durationMs: row.durationMs, completed: row.completed, updatedAt: row.updatedAt, userRating: preferenceById.get(row.catalogItemId)?.rating ?? null, catalogItem: toPublicCatalogItem(row.catalogItem) }));
    res.json({ items });
    return;
  }

  if (kind === "history") {
    const rows = await prisma.watchHistory.findMany({
      where: { profileId },
      include: { catalogItem: { select: safeCatalogSelect() } },
      orderBy: { watchedAt: "desc" },
      take
    });
    const items = rows
      .filter((row) => !preferenceById.get(row.catalogItemId)?.ignored)
      .filter((row) => !search || row.catalogItem.title.toLowerCase().includes(search) || (row.catalogItem.category ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(search))
      .map((row) => ({ id: row.id, kind, progress: row.progress, completed: row.completed, playCount: row.playCount, watchedAt: row.watchedAt, userRating: preferenceById.get(row.catalogItemId)?.rating ?? null, catalogItem: toPublicCatalogItem(row.catalogItem) }));
    res.json({ items });
    return;
  }

  const rows = await prisma.watchlistItem.findMany({
    where: { profileId },
    include: { catalogItem: { select: safeCatalogSelect() } },
    orderBy: { createdAt: "desc" },
    take
  });
  const items = rows
    .filter((row) => !preferenceById.get(row.catalogItemId)?.ignored)
    .filter((row) => !search || row.catalogItem.title.toLowerCase().includes(search) || (row.catalogItem.category ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(search))
    .map((row) => ({ id: row.id, kind: "watchlist", createdAt: row.createdAt, userRating: preferenceById.get(row.catalogItemId)?.rating ?? null, catalogItem: toPublicCatalogItem(row.catalogItem) }));
  res.json({ items });
});

catalogRoutes.patch("/watch/:kind/:id", async (req, res) => {
  const kind = req.params.kind;
  const id = req.params.id;

  if (kind === "progress") {
    const progress = queryNumber(req.body?.progress);
    const positionMs = queryNumber(req.body?.positionMs);
    const durationMs = queryNumber(req.body?.durationMs);
    const completed = typeof req.body?.completed === "boolean" ? req.body.completed : undefined;
    const updated = await prisma.watchProgress.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        ...(progress != null ? { progress: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, progress)) } : {}),
        ...(positionMs != null ? { positionMs: Math.max(0, Math.round(positionMs)) } : {}),
        ...(durationMs != null ? { durationMs: Math.max(0, Math.round(durationMs)) } : {}),
        ...(completed != null ? { completed } : {})
      },
      include: { catalogItem: { select: safeCatalogSelect() } }
    });
    res.json({ item: { id: updated.id, kind, progress: updated.progress, positionMs: updated.positionMs, durationMs: updated.durationMs, completed: updated.completed, updatedAt: updated.updatedAt, catalogItem: toPublicCatalogItem(updated.catalogItem) } });
    return;
  }

  if (kind === "history") {
    const progress = queryNumber(req.body?.progress);
    const playCount = queryNumber(req.body?.playCount);
    const completed = typeof req.body?.completed === "boolean" ? req.body.completed : undefined;
    const updated = await prisma.watchHistory.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        ...(progress != null ? { progress: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, progress)) } : {}),
        ...(playCount != null ? { playCount: Math.max(0, Math.round(playCount)) } : {}),
        ...(completed != null ? { completed } : {})
      },
      include: { catalogItem: { select: safeCatalogSelect() } }
    });
    res.json({ item: { id: updated.id, kind, progress: updated.progress, completed: updated.completed, playCount: updated.playCount, watchedAt: updated.watchedAt, catalogItem: toPublicCatalogItem(updated.catalogItem) } });
    return;
  }

  res.status(400).json({ error: "Only progress and history records can be edited." });
});

catalogRoutes.delete("/watch/:kind/:id", async (req, res) => {
  const kind = req.params.kind;
  const id = req.params.id;
  if (kind === "watchlist") await prisma.watchlistItem.delete({ where: { id } });
  else if (kind === "progress") await prisma.watchProgress.delete({ where: { id } });
  else if (kind === "history") await prisma.watchHistory.delete({ where: { id } });
  else {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Unknown watch record type." });
    return;
  }
  res.json({ ok: true });
});

// FILE: server/src/routes/epgRoutes.ts
================================================================================
import { Router } from "express";
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";

export const epgRoutes = Router();

function asString(value: unknown): string | null { return typeof value === "string" && value.trim() ? value.trim() : null; }
function asDate(value: unknown): Date | null {
  if (typeof value === "number") return new Date(value > 9_999_999_999 ? value : value * 1000);
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    const numeric = Number(value);
    if (Number.isFinite(numeric)) return new Date(numeric > 9_999_999_999 ? numeric : numeric * 1000);
    const parsed = new Date(value);
    if (!Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime())) return parsed;
  }
  return null;
}

epgRoutes.post("/programs", async (req, res) => {
  const programs = Array.isArray(req.body?.programs) ? req.body.programs as Record<string, unknown>[] : [];
  let saved = 0;
  for (const input of programs.slice(0, 2000)) {
    const channelKey = asString(input.channelKey ?? input.channelStableKey);
    const channelTitle = asString(input.channelTitle);
    const title = asString(input.title ?? input.programTitle);
    const startTime = asDate(input.startTime ?? input.startTimeMs);
    const endTime = asDate(input.endTime ?? input.endTimeMs);
    if (!channelKey || !channelTitle || !title || !startTime || !endTime || endTime <= startTime) continue;
    await prisma.epgProgram.upsert({
      where: { channelKey_startTime_title: { channelKey, startTime, title } },
      update: { channelTitle, description: asString(input.description), endTime, source: asString(input.source) ?? "android" },
      create: { channelKey, channelTitle, title, description: asString(input.description), startTime, endTime, source: asString(input.source) ?? "android" }
    });
    saved += 1;
  }
  res.json({ saved });
});

epgRoutes.get("/programs", async (req, res) => {
  const channelKey = asString(req.query.channelKey);
  const now = new Date();
  const programs = await prisma.epgProgram.findMany({
    where: { ...(channelKey ? { channelKey } : {}), endTime: { gte: now } },
    orderBy: [{ startTime: "asc" }],
    take: Math.min(Number(req.query.limit ?? 300) || 300, 1000)
  });
  res.json({ programs });
});

import { decryptSecret, encryptSecret } from "../services/secretCrypto.js";
>>>>>>> 2d831f51136373095ba04205d6c3d0552f9a8e95
import { getAiRecommendations } from "../services/aiRecommendationService.js";
import { enrichCatalogItemWithExternalMetadataIfNeeded } from "../services/metadataService.js";
import { decryptSecret, encryptSecret } from "../services/secretCrypto.js";

export const iptvRoutes = Router();

function asString(value: unknown): string | null {
  return typeof value === "string" && value.trim() ? value.trim() : null;
}

function maskSecret(value: string): string {
  if (value.length <= 2) return "*".repeat(value.length || 1);
  return `${value.slice(0, 1)}${"*".repeat(Math.min(value.length - 2, 8))}${value.slice(-1)}`;
}

iptvRoutes.get("/credentials/latest", async (_req, res) => {
  const serverUserId = asString(res.locals.authUser?.id);
  if (!serverUserId) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Server login required" });
    return;
  }
  const credential = await prisma.iptvCredential.findFirst({
    where: { serverUserId },
    orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" }
  });
  if (!credential) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "No IPTV credentials have been synced for this server account yet. Log in with IPTV once, then press Login so this device can upload it." });
    return;
  }
  res.json({
    credential: {
      id: credential.id,
      profileId: credential.profileId,
      iptvServerUrl: credential.iptvServerUrl,
      iptvUsername: credential.iptvUsername,
      iptvPassword: decryptSecret(credential.iptvPassword),
      androidUserId: credential.androidUserId,
      lastUploadedAt: credential.lastUploadedAt,
      updatedAt: credential.updatedAt
    }
  });
});

iptvRoutes.get("/credentials", async (_req, res) => {
  const serverUserId = asString(res.locals.authUser?.id);
  if (!serverUserId) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Server login required" });
    return;
  }
  const credentials = await prisma.iptvCredential.findMany({
    where: { serverUserId },
    orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" }
  });
  res.json({
    credentials: credentials.map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      profileId: item.profileId,
      iptvServerUrl: item.iptvServerUrl,
      iptvUsername: item.iptvUsername,
      passwordPreview: maskSecret(decryptSecret(item.iptvPassword)),
      androidUserId: item.androidUserId,
      lastUploadedAt: item.lastUploadedAt,
      updatedAt: item.updatedAt
    }))
  });
});

iptvRoutes.post("/credentials", async (req, res) => {
  const serverUserId = asString(res.locals.authUser?.id);
  if (!serverUserId) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Server login required" });
    return;
  }
  const iptvServerUrl = asString(req.body?.serverUrl);
  const iptvUsername = asString(req.body?.username);
  const iptvPassword = asString(req.body?.password);
  if (!iptvServerUrl || !iptvUsername || !iptvPassword) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "serverUrl, username, and password are required" });
    return;
  }

  const saved = await prisma.iptvCredential.upsert({
    where: {
      serverUserId_iptvServerUrl_iptvUsername: {
        serverUserId,
        iptvServerUrl,
        iptvUsername
      }
    },
    update: {
      iptvPassword: encryptSecret(iptvPassword),
      profileId: asString(req.body?.profileId),
      androidUserId: asString(req.body?.androidUserId),
      lastUploadedAt: new Date()
    },
    create: {
      serverUserId,
      profileId: asString(req.body?.profileId),
      iptvServerUrl,
      iptvUsername,
      iptvPassword: encryptSecret(iptvPassword),
      androidUserId: asString(req.body?.androidUserId),
      lastUploadedAt: new Date()
    }
  });

  res.status(201).json({
    credential: {
      id: saved.id,
      profileId: saved.profileId,
      iptvServerUrl: saved.iptvServerUrl,
      iptvUsername: saved.iptvUsername,
      passwordPreview: maskSecret(iptvPassword),
      androidUserId: saved.androidUserId,
      lastUploadedAt: saved.lastUploadedAt
    }
  });
});

iptvRoutes.post("/watch-event", async (req, res) => {
  await ingestWatchEvent(req.body as Record<string, unknown>);
  res.status(204).send();
});

iptvRoutes.post("/catalog-metadata", async (req, res) => {
  const items = Array.isArray(req.body?.items) ? req.body.items as Record<string, unknown>[] : [];
  const saved: unknown[] = [];
  let enriched = 0;
  const enrichLimit = Math.min(Number(req.body?.enrichLimit ?? 15) || 15, 50);
  for (const item of items) {
    const savedItem = await upsertCatalogItem(item);
    saved.push(savedItem);
    if (enriched < enrichLimit) {
      const result = await enrichCatalogItemWithExternalMetadataIfNeeded(savedItem.id).catch(() => null);
      if (result) enriched += 1;
    }
  }
  res.json({ saved: saved.length, enriched });
});

iptvRoutes.get("/recommendations", async (req, res) => {
  const profileId = String(req.query.profileId ?? req.query.userId ?? "default");
  const result = await getAiRecommendations({
    profileId,
    mood: "any",
    contentType: "any",
    limit: 20,
    useWebSearch: false
  });
  res.json({
    items: result.items.map((item) => item.catalogItem),
    summary: result.summary
  });
});

iptvRoutes.get("/preferences", async (req, res) => {
  const profileId = String(req.query.profileId ?? req.query.userId ?? "default");
  const preferences = await prisma.userCatalogPreference.findMany({
    where: { profileId },
    include: { catalogItem: { select: { stableKey: true } } },
    take: 5000
  });
  res.json({
    ignoredStableKeys: preferences.filter((item) => item.ignored).map((item) => item.catalogItem.stableKey),
    preferences: preferences.map((item) => ({
      stableKey: item.catalogItem.stableKey,
      rating: item.rating,
      ignored: item.ignored
    }))
  });
});

iptvRoutes.post("/preferences", async (req, res) => {
  const profileId = asString(req.body?.profileId) ?? String(req.query.profileId ?? req.query.userId ?? "default");
  const stableKeys = Array.isArray(req.body?.stableKeys)
    ? req.body.stableKeys.map(String).map((key) => key.trim()).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 500)
    : [];
  const incomingItems = Array.isArray(req.body?.items) ? req.body.items as Record<string, unknown>[] : [];

  for (const item of incomingItems) {
    await upsertCatalogItem(item);
  }

  const rating = req.body?.rating == null ? undefined : Number(req.body.rating);
  const ignored = typeof req.body?.ignored === "boolean" ? req.body.ignored : undefined;
  if (rating !== undefined && ![-1, 0, 1].includes(rating)) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "rating must be -1, 0, or 1." });
    return;
  }
  if (rating === undefined && ignored === undefined) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "rating or ignored is required." });
    return;
  }
  if (stableKeys.length === 0) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "stableKeys is required." });
    return;
  }

  await upsertProfile(profileId, res.locals.authUser?.id);
  const items = await prisma.catalogItem.findMany({ where: { stableKey: { in: stableKeys } }, select: { id: true } });
  const saved = await Promise.all(items.map((item) =>
    prisma.userCatalogPreference.upsert({
      where: { profileId_catalogItemId: { profileId, catalogItemId: item.id } },
      update: {
        ...(rating !== undefined ? { rating: rating === 0 ? null : rating } : {}),
        ...(ignored !== undefined ? { ignored } : {})
      },
      create: {
        profileId,
        catalogItemId: item.id,
        rating: rating === undefined || rating === 0 ? null : rating,
        ignored: ignored ?? false
      }
    })
  ));

  res.json({ saved: saved.length });
});

iptvRoutes.get("/catalog", async (req, res) => {
  const profileId = String(req.query.profileId ?? req.query.userId ?? "default");
  const ignored = await prisma.userCatalogPreference.findMany({ where: { profileId, ignored: true }, select: { catalogItemId: true } });
  const ignoredIds = ignored.map((item) => item.catalogItemId);
  const items = await prisma.catalogItem.findMany({
    where: { isBlocked: false, id: { notIn: ignoredIds } },
    select: safeCatalogSelect(),
    orderBy: { addedAt: "desc" },
    take: 100
  });
  res.json({ items: items.map(toPublicCatalogItem) });
});

================================================================================
// FILE: server/src/routes/pairingRoutes.ts
================================================================================
import { randomBytes } from "node:crypto";
import { Router, type Request } from "express";
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";
import { requireServerUser } from "../services/authService.js";
import { config } from "../config.js";

const codeAlphabet = "ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZ23456789";
const pairingMinutes = 10;

export const pairingRoutes = Router();

pairingRoutes.post("/start", async (req, res) => {
  const deviceName = typeof req.body?.deviceName === "string" ? req.body.deviceName.trim().slice(0, 80) : null;
  const now = Date.now();
  const expiresAt = new Date(now + pairingMinutes * 60_000);
  const deviceCode = await uniqueDeviceCode();
  const baseUrl = publicBaseUrl(req);

  await prisma.devicePairing.create({
    data: {
      deviceCode,
      deviceName,
      expiresAt
    }
  });

  res.status(201).json({
    deviceCode,
    pairingUrl: `${baseUrl}/pair?code=${encodeURIComponent(deviceCode)}`,
    qrPayload: `${baseUrl}/pair?code=${encodeURIComponent(deviceCode)}`,
    expiresAt: expiresAt.toISOString(),
    pollIntervalSeconds: 2
  });
});

pairingRoutes.get("/status", async (req, res) => {
  const deviceCode = normalizeCode(typeof req.query.deviceCode === "string" ? req.query.deviceCode : "");
  if (!deviceCode) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "deviceCode is required." });
    return;
  }

  const pairing = await prisma.devicePairing.findUnique({ where: { deviceCode } });
  if (!pairing) {
    res.status(404).json({ status: "not_found" });
    return;
  }

  if (pairing.status === "pending" && pairing.expiresAt.getTime() <= Date.now()) {
    await prisma.devicePairing.update({
      where: { id: pairing.id },
      data: { status: "expired" }
    });
    res.json({ status: "expired" });
    return;
  }

  if (pairing.status === "approved" && pairing.deviceToken && pairing.username) {
    if (!pairing.consumedAt) {
      await prisma.devicePairing.update({
        where: { id: pairing.id },
        data: { consumedAt: new Date() }
      });
    }
    res.json({
      status: "approved",
      syncServerUrl: publicBaseUrl(req),
      syncServerUsername: pairing.username,
      syncServerToken: pairing.deviceToken,
      displayName: pairing.displayName,
      expiresAt: pairing.expiresAt.toISOString()
    });
    return;
  }

  res.json({
    status: pairing.status,
    expiresAt: pairing.expiresAt.toISOString()
  });
});

pairingRoutes.post("/approve", requireServerUser, async (req, res) => {
  const deviceCode = normalizeCode(typeof req.body?.deviceCode === "string" ? req.body.deviceCode : "");
  if (!deviceCode) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "deviceCode is required." });
    return;
  }

  const pairing = await prisma.devicePairing.findUnique({ where: { deviceCode } });
  if (!pairing) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Pairing code was not found." });
    return;
  }
  if (pairing.status !== "pending") {
    res.status(409).json({ error: `Pairing code is already ${pairing.status}.` });
    return;
  }
  if (pairing.expiresAt.getTime() <= Date.now()) {
    await prisma.devicePairing.update({ where: { id: pairing.id }, data: { status: "expired" } });
    res.status(410).json({ error: "Pairing code expired. Start pairing again on the TV." });
    return;
  }

  const authUser = res.locals.authUser;
  if (!authUser) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Server login required to approve pairing." });
    return;
  }

  const updated = await prisma.devicePairing.update({
    where: { id: pairing.id },
    data: {
      status: "approved",
      serverUserId: authUser.id,
      username: authUser.username,
      displayName: authUser.displayName,
      deviceToken: randomBytes(32).toString("base64url"),
      approvedAt: new Date()
    }
  });

  res.json({
    status: updated.status,
    deviceName: updated.deviceName,
    username: updated.username,
    displayName: updated.displayName,
    approvedAt: updated.approvedAt?.toISOString()
  });
});

pairingRoutes.post("/cancel", async (req, res) => {
  const deviceCode = normalizeCode(typeof req.body?.deviceCode === "string" ? req.body.deviceCode : "");
  if (!deviceCode) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "deviceCode is required." });
    return;
  }

  await prisma.devicePairing.updateMany({
    where: { deviceCode, status: "pending" },
    data: { status: "cancelled" }
  });
  res.json({ ok: true });
});

async function uniqueDeviceCode(): Promise<string> {
  for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 10; attempt += 1) {
    const code = generateCode();
    const existing = await prisma.devicePairing.findUnique({ where: { deviceCode: code } });
    if (!existing) return code;
  }
  throw new Error("Could not generate a pairing code.");
}

function generateCode(): string {
  const raw = randomBytes(6);
  const chars = Array.from(raw, (byte) => codeAlphabet[byte % codeAlphabet.length]);
  return `${chars.slice(0, 3).join("")}-${chars.slice(3, 6).join("")}`;
}

function normalizeCode(value: string): string {
  const cleaned = value.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]/g, "");
  return cleaned.length === 6 ? `${cleaned.slice(0, 3)}-${cleaned.slice(3)}` : value.toUpperCase().trim();
}

function publicBaseUrl(req: Request): string {
  if (config.publicBaseUrl.trim()) return config.publicBaseUrl.trim().replace(/\/$/, "");
  const forwardedProto = req.header("x-forwarded-proto")?.split(",")[0]?.trim();
  const proto = forwardedProto || req.protocol || "http";
  return `${proto}://${req.get("host")}`;
}

// FILE: server/src/routes/socialRoutes.ts

import { Router } from "express";
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";
import { safeCatalogSelect, toPublicCatalogItem } from "../services/catalogService.js";
import { broadcastSocialEvent } from "../realtime/socialRealtime.js";
import { createSocialToken } from "../services/socialTokenService.js";
import {
  asString,
  clearWatchPresence,
  buildMediaShareFromCatalog,
  createViewingParty,
  createMessage,
  ensureSocialUser,
  formatFriendship,
  formatMessage,
  formatRoom,
  formatViewingParty,
  getOrCreateRoom,
  getActiveViewersForCatalog,
  getUnreadCount,
  joinRoom,
  leaveRoom,
  requestFriendship,
  resolveCatalogItemId,
  respondToFriendship,
  respondToViewingPartyInvite,
  safeMediaPayload,
  upsertWatchPresence
} from "../services/socialService.js";

export const socialRoutes = Router();

type AuthResponse = { locals: { authUser?: unknown } };

async function currentSocialUser(res: AuthResponse) {
  return ensureSocialUser(res.locals.authUser ?? {});
}

function safeJsonParse<T>(value: string | null | undefined, fallback: T): T {
  if (!value) return fallback;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(value) as T;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function listInput(value: unknown): string[] {
  return Array.isArray(value) ? value.map(String).map((item) => item.trim()).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 100) : [];
}

function limitFromQuery(value: unknown, fallback = 50, max = 100): number {
  const parsed = Number(value ?? fallback);
  return Math.max(1, Math.min(Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : fallback, max));
}

function normalizeRoomType(value: unknown): string {
  const roomType = asString(value) ?? "discussion";
  if (["watchParty", "discussion", "direct", "group"].includes(roomType)) return roomType;
  return "discussion";
}

async function ensureRoomExists(roomId: string) {
  return prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: roomId } });
}

async function messageCursor(roomId: string, before: string | null) {
  if (!before) return undefined;
  const message = await prisma.chatMessage.findFirst({ where: { id: before, roomId }, select: { createdAt: true } });
  return message ? { createdAt: { lt: message.createdAt } } : undefined;
}

socialRoutes.get("/session", async (_req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const token = createSocialToken({ userId: user.userId, username: user.username, displayName: user.displayName });
  res.json({
    user,
    token,
    websocketUrl: "/ws/social?token=<token>",
    expiresInSeconds: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60
  });
});

socialRoutes.get("/me", async (_req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const socialUser = await prisma.socialUser.findUnique({ where: { id: user.userId } });
  res.json({ user: socialUser });
});

socialRoutes.get("/users", async (_req, res) => {
  const current = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const serverUsers = await prisma.serverUser.findMany({
    select: { id: true, username: true, displayName: true }
  });
  for (const user of serverUsers) {
    await prisma.socialUser.upsert({
      where: { serverUserId: user.id },
      update: {
        username: user.username,
        displayName: user.displayName ?? user.username
      },
      create: {
        serverUserId: user.id,
        username: user.username,
        displayName: user.displayName ?? user.username
      }
    });
  }
  const users = await prisma.socialUser.findMany({
    where: { id: { not: current.userId } },
    select: {
      id: true,
      username: true,
      displayName: true,
      avatarUrl: true,
      status: true,
      lastSeenAt: true
    },
    orderBy: [{ status: "asc" }, { displayName: "asc" }],
    take: 100
  });
  res.json({ users });
});

socialRoutes.put("/me", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const displayName = asString(req.body?.displayName)?.slice(0, 80);
  const avatarUrl = asString(req.body?.avatarUrl)?.slice(0, 1000);
  const bio = asString(req.body?.bio)?.slice(0, 500);
  const favoriteGenres = listInput(req.body?.favoriteGenres).slice(0, 20);
  const updated = await prisma.socialUser.update({
    where: { id: user.userId },
    data: {
      ...(displayName ? { displayName } : {}),
      ...(avatarUrl ? { avatarUrl } : {}),
      ...(bio ? { bio } : {}),
      favoriteGenresJson: favoriteGenres.length > 0 ? JSON.stringify(favoriteGenres) : undefined,
      lastSeenAt: new Date()
    }
  });
  res.json({ user: updated });
});

socialRoutes.get("/users/:userId", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await prisma.socialUser.findUnique({
    where: { id: req.params.userId },
    select: {
      id: true,
      username: true,
      displayName: true,
      avatarUrl: true,
      status: true,
      bio: true,
      favoriteGenresJson: true,
      lastSeenAt: true,
      createdAt: true
    }
  });
  if (!user) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Social user not found" });
    return;
  }

  const sharedRooms = await prisma.chatRoom.findMany({
    where: { participants: { some: { userId: user.id } } },
    include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } },
    orderBy: [{ lastMessageAt: "desc" }, { updatedAt: "desc" }],
    take: 20
  });

  const sharedLists = await prisma.sharedMediaList.findMany({
    where: { createdByUserId: user.id },
    include: { items: { include: { catalogItem: true }, take: 8, orderBy: { sortOrder: "asc" } } },
    orderBy: { createdAt: "desc" },
    take: 10
  });

  res.json({
    user: {
      ...user,
      favoriteGenres: user.favoriteGenresJson ? safeJsonParse<string[]>(user.favoriteGenresJson, []) : []
    },
    sharedRooms: sharedRooms.map((room) => formatRoom(room)),
    sharedLists: sharedLists.map((list) => ({
      id: list.id,
      title: list.title,
      description: list.description,
      createdAt: list.createdAt,
      items: list.items.map((item) => toPublicCatalogItem(item.catalogItem))
    }))
  });
});

});

socialRoutes.get("/rooms", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const requestedCatalogItemId = asString(req.query.catalogItemId);
  const catalogItemId = await resolveCatalogItemId(requestedCatalogItemId);
  const roomType = asString(req.query.roomType);
  if (requestedCatalogItemId && !catalogItemId) {
    res.json({ rooms: [] });
    return;
  }
  const rooms = await prisma.chatRoom.findMany({
    where: {
      ...(catalogItemId ? { catalogItemId } : {}),
      ...(roomType ? { roomType } : {}),
      OR: [
        { roomType: { in: ["watchParty", "discussion", "group"] } },
        { participants: { some: { userId: user.userId } } }
      ]
    },
    include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } },
    orderBy: [{ lastMessageAt: "desc" }, { updatedAt: "desc" }],
    take: limitFromQuery(req.query.limit)
  });

  const formatted: unknown[] = [];
  for (const room of rooms) formatted.push(formatRoom(room, await getUnreadCount(room.id, user.userId)));
  res.json({ rooms: formatted });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await getOrCreateRoom({
    title: asString(req.body?.title),
    roomType: normalizeRoomType(req.body?.roomType),
    catalogItemId: asString(req.body?.catalogItemId),
    createdByUserId: user.userId,
    participantUserIds: listInput(req.body?.participantUserIds)
  });
  const fullRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: room.id }, include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } } });
  res.status(201).json({ room: formatRoom(fullRoom ?? room) });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms/:roomId/control", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: req.params.roomId } });
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }
  const action = asString(req.body?.action) ?? "heartbeat";
  const positionMs = Math.max(0, Math.floor(Number(req.body?.positionMs ?? 0) || 0));
  const durationMs = Math.max(0, Math.floor(Number(req.body?.durationMs ?? 0) || 0));
  const party = await prisma.viewingParty.findFirst({ where: { roomId: room.id }, orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" } });
  const playbackState = action === "pause" ? "paused" : action === "play" ? "playing" : action === "seek" ? "seeking" : action;
  const updatedParty = party
    ? await prisma.viewingParty.update({ where: { id: party.id }, data: { playbackState, currentPositionMs: positionMs, durationMs, controlledByUserId: user.userId, lastControlAt: new Date() } })
    : await prisma.viewingParty.create({
        data: {
          roomId: room.id,
          createdByUserId: user.userId,
          catalogItemId: room.catalogItemId,
          catalogKey: room.catalogItemId ?? undefined,
          catalogTitle: room.catalogTitle ?? room.title,
          catalogType: room.catalogType,
          title: room.title,
          status: "active",
          playbackState,
          currentPositionMs: positionMs,
          durationMs,
          controlledByUserId: user.userId,
          lastControlAt: new Date()
        }
      });
  const payload = { type: "watchPartyControl", roomId: room.id, action, playbackState, positionMs, durationMs, controlledByUserId: user.userId, lastControlAt: updatedParty.lastControlAt };
  broadcastSocialEvent(room.id, payload);
  res.json({ party: updatedParty, control: payload });
});

socialRoutes.get("/rooms/:roomId/control", async (req, res) => {
  const room = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: req.params.roomId } });
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }
  const party = await prisma.viewingParty.findFirst({ where: { roomId: room.id }, orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" } });
  res.json({ party });
});

socialRoutes.get("/rooms/:roomId", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
    where: { id: req.params.roomId },
    include: {
      _count: { select: { participants: true } },
      participants: { include: { user: true }, orderBy: { lastSeenAt: "desc" } },
      catalogItem: { select: safeCatalogSelect() }
    }
  });
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }

  res.json({
    room: formatRoom(room, await getUnreadCount(room.id, user.userId)),
    catalogItem: room.catalogItem ? toPublicCatalogItem(room.catalogItem) : null,
    participants: room.participants.map((participant) => ({
      id: participant.user.id,
      displayName: participant.user.displayName,
      username: participant.user.username,
      avatarUrl: participant.user.avatarUrl,
      status: participant.user.status,
      isActive: participant.isActive,
      lastSeenAt: participant.lastSeenAt
    }))
  });
});

socialRoutes.get("/rooms/:roomId/messages", async (req, res) => {
  const room = await ensureRoomExists(req.params.roomId);
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }

  const cursorWhere = await messageCursor(req.params.roomId, asString(req.query.before));
  const messages = await prisma.chatMessage.findMany({
    where: {
      roomId: req.params.roomId,
      deletedAt: null,
      ...(cursorWhere ?? {})
    },
    include: { sender: true, reactions: { include: { user: true } } },
    orderBy: { createdAt: "desc" },
    take: limitFromQuery(req.query.limit)
  });
  res.json({ messages: messages.reverse().map(formatMessage) });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms/:roomId/messages", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await ensureRoomExists(req.params.roomId);
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }

  const message = await createMessage(req.params.roomId, user.userId, {
    clientMessageId: asString(req.body?.clientMessageId) ?? undefined,
    messageType: asString(req.body?.messageType) ?? undefined,
    text: asString(req.body?.text) ?? "",
    sharePayload: req.body?.sharePayload
  });
  broadcastSocialEvent(req.params.roomId, { type: "messageCreated", roomId: req.params.roomId, message });
  res.status(201).json({ message });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms/:roomId/messages/:messageId/reactions", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const reaction = asString(req.body?.reaction)?.slice(0, 32);
  if (!reaction) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Reaction is required" });
    return;
  }

  const message = await prisma.chatMessage.findFirst({ where: { id: req.params.messageId, roomId: req.params.roomId } });
  if (!message) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Message not found" });
    return;
  }

  const saved = await prisma.chatReaction.upsert({
    where: { messageId_userId_reaction: { messageId: message.id, userId: user.userId, reaction } },
    update: {},
    create: { messageId: message.id, userId: user.userId, reaction }
  });
  broadcastSocialEvent(req.params.roomId, { type: "reactionAdded", roomId: req.params.roomId, messageId: message.id, reaction, user });
  res.status(201).json({ reaction: saved });
});

socialRoutes.delete("/rooms/:roomId/messages/:messageId/reactions", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const reaction = asString(req.body?.reaction ?? req.query.reaction)?.slice(0, 32);
  if (!reaction) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Reaction is required" });
    return;
  }

  await prisma.chatReaction.deleteMany({ where: { messageId: req.params.messageId, userId: user.userId, reaction } });
  broadcastSocialEvent(req.params.roomId, { type: "reactionRemoved", roomId: req.params.roomId, messageId: req.params.messageId, reaction, user });
  res.json({ ok: true });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms/:roomId/read", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await ensureRoomExists(req.params.roomId);
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }
  await prisma.chatParticipant.upsert({
    where: { roomId_userId: { roomId: req.params.roomId, userId: user.userId } },
    update: { lastReadAt: new Date(), lastSeenAt: new Date() },
    create: { roomId: req.params.roomId, userId: user.userId, lastReadAt: new Date(), lastSeenAt: new Date() }
  });
  res.json({ ok: true });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms/:roomId/join", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await ensureRoomExists(req.params.roomId);
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }
  await joinRoom(req.params.roomId, user.userId);
  broadcastSocialEvent(req.params.roomId, { type: "userJoined", roomId: req.params.roomId, user });
  res.json({ ok: true });
});

socialRoutes.post("/rooms/:roomId/leave", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await ensureRoomExists(req.params.roomId);
  if (!room) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Room not found" });
    return;
  }
  await leaveRoom(req.params.roomId, user.userId);
  broadcastSocialEvent(req.params.roomId, { type: "userLeft", roomId: req.params.roomId, user });
  res.json({ ok: true });
});

socialRoutes.post("/share/media", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const roomId = asString(req.body?.roomId);
  let room = roomId ? await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: roomId } }) : null;
  const catalogItemId = asString(req.body?.catalogItemId);
  if (!room) {
    room = await getOrCreateRoom({
      title: asString(req.body?.roomTitle) ?? undefined,
      roomType: normalizeRoomType(req.body?.roomType),
      catalogItemId,
      createdByUserId: user.userId
    });
  }

  const mediaPayload = catalogItemId ? await buildMediaShareFromCatalog(catalogItemId) : safeMediaPayload(req.body?.media ?? req.body ?? {});
  const message = await createMessage(room.id, user.userId, {
    messageType: "mediaShare",
    text: asString(req.body?.text) ?? `Shared ${mediaPayload.title}`,
    sharePayload: mediaPayload
  });
  broadcastSocialEvent(room.id, { type: "sharedMedia", roomId: room.id, share: mediaPayload, message });
  res.status(201).json({ room: formatRoom(room), message, share: mediaPayload });
});

socialRoutes.post("/recommendations", async (req, res) => {
  const sender = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const targetUserId = asString(req.body?.targetUserId);
  const catalogItemId = asString(req.body?.catalogItemId);
  const note = asString(req.body?.text)?.slice(0, 500);

  if (!targetUserId || !catalogItemId) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "targetUserId and catalogItemId are required" });
    return;
  }

  const [target, catalogItem] = await Promise.all([
    prisma.socialUser.findUnique({ where: { id: targetUserId } }),
    prisma.catalogItem.findUnique({ where: { id: catalogItemId } })
  ]);

  if (!target) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Recipient not found" });
    return;
  }
  if (!catalogItem || catalogItem.isBlocked) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Catalog item not found" });
    return;
  }

  const room = await getOrCreateRoom({
    title: `${sender.displayName ?? sender.username ?? "Viewer"} and ${target.displayName ?? target.username ?? "Viewer"}`,
    roomType: "direct",
    createdByUserId: sender.userId,
    participantUserIds: [target.id]
  });

  const share = await buildMediaShareFromCatalog(catalogItem.id);
  const message = await createMessage(room.id, sender.userId, {
    messageType: "mediaShare",
    text: note || `Recommended: ${catalogItem.title}`,
    sharePayload: { ...share, recommended: true }
  });
  broadcastSocialEvent(room.id, { type: "mediaRecommended", roomId: room.id, share, message });
  res.status(201).json({ room: formatRoom(room), message, share });
});

socialRoutes.post("/share/list", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const title = asString(req.body?.title) ?? "Shared list";
  const description = asString(req.body?.description);
  const catalogItemIds = listInput(req.body?.catalogItemIds);
  if (catalogItemIds.length === 0) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "At least one catalogItemId is required" });
    return;
  }

  const roomId = asString(req.body?.roomId);
  let room = roomId ? await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: roomId } }) : null;
  if (!room) {
    room = await getOrCreateRoom({ title, roomType: "discussion", createdByUserId: user.userId });
  }

  const validItems = await prisma.catalogItem.findMany({ where: { id: { in: catalogItemIds } }, select: { id: true } });
  const validIds = new Set(validItems.map((item) => item.id));
  if (validIds.size === 0) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "No valid catalog items found" });
    return;
  }

  const list = await prisma.sharedMediaList.create({
    data: {
      title: title.slice(0, 120),
      description: description?.slice(0, 500),
      createdByUserId: user.userId,
      roomId: room.id,
      items: {
        create: catalogItemIds.filter((id) => validIds.has(id)).map((catalogItemId, index) => ({ catalogItemId, sortOrder: index }))
      }
    },
    include: { items: { include: { catalogItem: true }, orderBy: { sortOrder: "asc" } } }
  });

  const sharePayload = {
    listId: list.id,
    title: list.title,
    description: list.description,
    items: list.items.map((item) => safeMediaPayload({
      catalogItemId: item.catalogItem.id,
      title: item.catalogItem.title,
      type: item.catalogItem.type,
      year: item.catalogItem.year,
      posterUrl: item.catalogItem.coverUrl,
      backdropUrl: item.catalogItem.backdropUrl,
      description: item.catalogItem.description,
      rating: item.catalogItem.rating,
      genre: item.catalogItem.genreJson ? safeJsonParse<string[]>(item.catalogItem.genreJson, []) : []
    }))
  };
  const message = await createMessage(room.id, user.userId, {
    messageType: "listShare",
    text: `Shared list: ${title}`,
    sharePayload
  });
  broadcastSocialEvent(room.id, { type: "sharedList", roomId: room.id, share: sharePayload, message });
  res.status(201).json({ room: formatRoom(room), list: sharePayload, message });
});

socialRoutes.get("/lists", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const lists = await prisma.sharedMediaList.findMany({
    where: {
      OR: [
        { createdByUserId: user.userId },
        { room: { participants: { some: { userId: user.userId } } } }
      ]
    },
    include: {
      createdBy: true,
      room: true,
      items: { include: { catalogItem: true }, orderBy: { sortOrder: "asc" } }
    },
    orderBy: { createdAt: "desc" },
    take: limitFromQuery(req.query.limit)
  });
  res.json({
    lists: lists.map((list) => ({
      id: list.id,
      title: list.title,
      description: list.description,
      createdAt: list.createdAt,
      createdBy: { id: list.createdBy.id, displayName: list.createdBy.displayName, username: list.createdBy.username },
      room: list.room ? formatRoom(list.room) : null,
      items: list.items.map((item) => toPublicCatalogItem(item.catalogItem))
    }))
  });
});

socialRoutes.get("/lists/:listId", async (req, res) => {
  const list = await prisma.sharedMediaList.findUnique({
    where: { id: req.params.listId },
    include: {
      createdBy: true,
      room: true,
      items: { include: { catalogItem: true }, orderBy: { sortOrder: "asc" } }
    }
  });
  if (!list) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "Shared list not found" });
    return;
  }
  res.json({
    list: {
      id: list.id,
      title: list.title,
      description: list.description,
      createdAt: list.createdAt,
      createdBy: { id: list.createdBy.id, displayName: list.createdBy.displayName, username: list.createdBy.username },
      room: list.room ? formatRoom(list.room) : null,
      items: list.items.map((item) => toPublicCatalogItem(item.catalogItem))
    }
  });
});

socialRoutes.get("/inbox", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const rooms = await prisma.chatRoom.findMany({
    where: { participants: { some: { userId: user.userId } } },
    include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } },
    orderBy: [{ lastMessageAt: "desc" }, { updatedAt: "desc" }],
    take: limitFromQuery(req.query.limit)
  });
  const formatted: unknown[] = [];
  for (const room of rooms) formatted.push(formatRoom(room, await getUnreadCount(room.id, user.userId)));
  res.json({ rooms: formatted });
});

socialRoutes.get("/discussions", async (req, res) => {
  const requestedCatalogItemId = asString(req.query.catalogItemId);
  const catalogItemId = await resolveCatalogItemId(requestedCatalogItemId);
  if (requestedCatalogItemId && !catalogItemId) {
    res.json({ discussions: [] });
    return;
  }
  const rooms = await prisma.chatRoom.findMany({
    where: { roomType: "discussion", ...(catalogItemId ? { catalogItemId } : {}) },
    include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } },
    orderBy: [{ lastMessageAt: "desc" }, { updatedAt: "desc" }],
    take: limitFromQuery(req.query.limit)
  });
  res.json({ discussions: rooms.map((room) => formatRoom(room)) });
});

socialRoutes.post("/discussions", async (req, res) => {
  const user = await currentSocialUser(res);
  const room = await getOrCreateRoom({
    title: asString(req.body?.title),
    roomType: "discussion",
    catalogItemId: asString(req.body?.catalogItemId),
    createdByUserId: user.userId,
    participantUserIds: listInput(req.body?.participantUserIds)
  });
  if (asString(req.body?.text)) {
    const message = await createMessage(room.id, user.userId, { text: asString(req.body?.text) ?? "" });
    broadcastSocialEvent(room.id, { type: "messageCreated", roomId: room.id, message });
  }
  const fullRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: room.id }, include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } } });
  res.status(201).json({ room: formatRoom(fullRoom ?? room) });
});

================================================================================
// FILE: server/src/routes/userRoutes.ts
================================================================================
import { Router } from "express";
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";
import { hashPassword, requireAdmin } from "../services/authService.js";
import {
  getTmdbRequestToken,
  createTmdbSession,
  getTmdbAccountDetails,
  getTmdbAccountWatchlist,
} from "../services/tmdbService.js";

export const userRoutes = Router();

userRoutes.get("/me", async (_req, res) => {
  if (!res.locals.authUser) {
    res.json({ user: null });
    return;
  }
  try {
    const user = await prisma.serverUser.findUnique({
      where: { id: res.locals.authUser.id },
      select: {
        id: true,
        username: true,
        displayName: true,
        isAdmin: true,
        tmdbSessionId: true,
        tmdbAccountId: true,
        tmdbUsername: true,
        createdAt: true,
        updatedAt: true,
      },
    });
    res.json({
      user: user ? {
        ...user,
        tmdbLinked: Boolean(user.tmdbSessionId && user.tmdbAccountId),
        tmdbSessionId: undefined,
      } : null
    });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch user details." });
  }
});

userRoutes.get("/me/tmdb/watchlist", async (req, res) => {
  if (!res.locals.authUser) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized" });
    return;
  }
  const user = await prisma.serverUser.findUnique({
    where: { id: res.locals.authUser.id },
    select: { tmdbSessionId: true, tmdbAccountId: true },
  });
  if (!user?.tmdbSessionId || !user.tmdbAccountId) {
    res.json({ items: [], linked: false });
    return;
  }
  const rawType = typeof req.query.type === "string" ? req.query.type : "all";
  const type = rawType === "movie" || rawType === "tv" ? rawType : rawType === "series" ? "tv" : "all";
  const limit = Math.min(Number(req.query.limit ?? 40) || 40, 100);
  try {
    const items = await getTmdbAccountWatchlist(user.tmdbSessionId, user.tmdbAccountId, type, limit);
    res.json({ items, linked: true });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(503).json({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Failed to fetch TMDB watchlist." });
  }
});

// Direct link endpoint
userRoutes.post("/me/tmdb/link", async (req, res) => {
  if (!res.locals.authUser) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized" });
    return;
  }
  const tmdbSessionId = typeof req.body?.tmdbSessionId === "string" ? req.body.tmdbSessionId.trim() : "";
  const tmdbAccountId =
    typeof req.body?.tmdbAccountId === "string" || typeof req.body?.tmdbAccountId === "number"
      ? String(req.body.tmdbAccountId).trim()
      : "";
  const tmdbUsername = typeof req.body?.tmdbUsername === "string" ? req.body.tmdbUsername.trim() : "";

  if (!tmdbSessionId) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "tmdbSessionId is required." });
    return;
  }

  try {
    const updatedUser = await prisma.serverUser.update({
      where: { id: res.locals.authUser.id },
      data: {
        tmdbSessionId,
        tmdbAccountId: tmdbAccountId || null,
        tmdbUsername: tmdbUsername || null,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        username: true,
        displayName: true,
        isAdmin: true,
        tmdbSessionId: true,
        tmdbAccountId: true,
        tmdbUsername: true,
      },
    });
    res.json({ user: updatedUser });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to link TMDB account." });
  }
});

// Unlink TMDB endpoint
userRoutes.post("/me/tmdb/unlink", async (_req, res) => {
  if (!res.locals.authUser) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized" });
    return;
  }
  try {
    const updatedUser = await prisma.serverUser.update({
      where: { id: res.locals.authUser.id },
      data: {
        tmdbSessionId: null,
        tmdbAccountId: null,
        tmdbUsername: null,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        username: true,
        displayName: true,
        isAdmin: true,
        tmdbSessionId: true,
        tmdbAccountId: true,
        tmdbUsername: true,
      },
    });
    res.json({ user: updatedUser });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to unlink TMDB account." });
  }
});

// Get request token for OAuth flow
userRoutes.get("/me/tmdb/request-token", async (_req, res) => {
  if (!res.locals.authUser) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized" });
    return;
  }
  try {
    const tokenData = await getTmdbRequestToken();
    res.json(tokenData);
  } catch (error) {
    const msg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Failed to generate TMDB request token.";
    res.status(500).json({ error: msg });
  }
});

// Create session from approved request token
userRoutes.post("/me/tmdb/create-session", async (req, res) => {
  if (!res.locals.authUser) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized" });
    return;
  }
  const requestToken = typeof req.body?.requestToken === "string" ? req.body.requestToken.trim() : "";
  if (!requestToken) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "requestToken is required." });
    return;
  }

  try {
    const { session_id } = await createTmdbSession(requestToken);
    const accountDetails = await getTmdbAccountDetails(session_id);

    const updatedUser = await prisma.serverUser.update({
      where: { id: res.locals.authUser.id },
      data: {
        tmdbSessionId: session_id,
        tmdbAccountId: String(accountDetails.id),
        tmdbUsername: accountDetails.username,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        username: true,
        displayName: true,
        isAdmin: true,
        tmdbSessionId: true,
        tmdbAccountId: true,
        tmdbUsername: true,
      },
    });
    res.json({ user: updatedUser });
  } catch (error) {
    const msg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Failed to link TMDB account from token.";
    res.status(500).json({ error: msg });
  }
});

userRoutes.get("/", requireAdmin, async (_req, res) => {
  const users = await prisma.serverUser.findMany({
    select: {
      id: true,
      username: true,
      displayName: true,
      isAdmin: true,
      createdAt: true,
      updatedAt: true
    },
    orderBy: { username: "asc" }
  });
  res.json({ users });
});

userRoutes.post("/", requireAdmin, async (req, res) => {
  const username = typeof req.body?.username === "string" ? req.body.username.trim() : "";
  const password = typeof req.body?.password === "string" ? req.body.password : "";
  const displayName = typeof req.body?.displayName === "string" ? req.body.displayName.trim() : "";
  const isAdmin = req.body?.isAdmin === true;
  if (!username || username.length < 3) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Username must be at least 3 characters." });
    return;
  }
  if (!password || password.length < 8) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Password must be at least 8 characters." });
    return;
  }

  const user = await prisma.serverUser.create({
    data: {
      username,
      passwordHash: hashPassword(password),
      displayName: displayName || username,
      isAdmin
    },
    select: {
      id: true,
      username: true,
      displayName: true,
      isAdmin: true,
      createdAt: true
    }
  });
  res.status(201).json({ user });
});

// FILE: server/src/services/aiRecommendationService.ts
