// FILE: server/src/services/socialService.ts
================================================================================
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";
import { safeCatalogSelect, toPublicCatalogItem } from "./catalogService.js";

type AuthUser = {
  id?: string;
  username?: string;
  displayName?: string | null;
  isAdmin?: boolean;
};

export type SocialContext = {
  userId: string;
  username?: string | null;
  displayName?: string | null;
};

type MediaShareInput = {
  catalogItemId?: string;
  title?: string;
  type?: string;
  year?: string | number | null;
  posterUrl?: string | null;
  backdropUrl?: string | null;
  description?: string | null;
  rating?: number | string | null;
  genre?: string[] | string | null;
};


function isLikelyStreamUrl(value: string | null): boolean {
  if (!value) return false;
  const lower = value.toLowerCase();
  return (
    lower.includes('/live/') ||
    lower.includes('/movie/') ||
    lower.includes('/series/') ||
    lower.includes('username=') ||
    lower.includes('password=') ||
    lower.endsWith('.m3u8') ||
    lower.endsWith('.ts') ||
    lower.includes('player_api.php')
  );
}

function safeUrl(value: unknown): string | null {
  const url = asString(value);
  if (!url || isLikelyStreamUrl(url)) return null;
  return url.slice(0, 1000);
}

export type SocialMessageInput = {
  clientMessageId?: string;
  messageType?: string;
  text?: string;
  sharePayload?: unknown;
};

export type WatchPresenceInput = {
  catalogItemId?: string | null;
  catalogKey?: string | null;
  catalogTitle?: string | null;
  catalogType?: string | null;
  roomId?: string | null;
  positionMs?: number | string | null;
  durationMs?: number | string | null;
  playbackState?: string | null;
  deviceName?: string | null;
};

export function asString(value: unknown): string | null {
  return typeof value === "string" && value.trim() ? value.trim() : null;
}

export function safeJson(value: unknown): string | null {
  if (value == null) return null;
  return JSON.stringify(value);
}

export function parseJsonObject<T>(value: string | null | undefined, fallback: T): T {
  if (!value) return fallback;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(value) as T;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

export function safeMediaPayload(input: MediaShareInput): MediaShareInput {
  return {
    catalogItemId: asString(input.catalogItemId) ?? undefined,
    title: asString(input.title) ?? "Untitled",
    type: asString(input.type) ?? "movie",
    year: input.year == null ? null : String(input.year),
    posterUrl: safeUrl(input.posterUrl),
    backdropUrl: safeUrl(input.backdropUrl),
    description: asString(input.description),
    rating: input.rating == null ? null : Number(input.rating),
    genre: Array.isArray(input.genre) ? input.genre.map(String).slice(0, 12) : asString(input.genre)
  };
}


function sanitizeSharePayload(messageType: string, sharePayload: unknown): unknown {
  if (!sharePayload || typeof sharePayload !== "object") return sharePayload ?? null;

  if (messageType === "mediaShare") {
    return safeMediaPayload(sharePayload as MediaShareInput);
  }

  if (messageType === "listShare") {
    const payload = sharePayload as { title?: unknown; description?: unknown; items?: unknown };
    const items = Array.isArray(payload.items)
      ? payload.items.slice(0, 100).map((item) => safeMediaPayload(item as MediaShareInput))
      : [];
    return {
      listId: asString((payload as { listId?: unknown }).listId) ?? undefined,
      title: asString(payload.title) ?? "Shared list",
      description: asString(payload.description),
      items
    };
  }

  return null;
}

export async function ensureSocialUser(authUser: AuthUser): Promise<SocialContext> {
  const hasServerUser = Boolean(authUser.id);
  const fallbackId = authUser.id ?? "anonymous";
  const username = authUser.username ?? fallbackId;
  const displayName = authUser.displayName ?? username;
  const socialUser = hasServerUser
    ? await prisma.socialUser.upsert({
        where: { serverUserId: fallbackId },
        update: {
          username,
          displayName,
          status: "online",
          lastSeenAt: new Date()
        },
        create: {
          serverUserId: fallbackId,
          username,
          displayName,
          status: "online",
          lastSeenAt: new Date()
        }
      })
    : await prisma.socialUser.upsert({
        where: { id: "anonymous" },
        update: { username, displayName, status: "online", lastSeenAt: new Date() },
        create: { id: "anonymous", username, displayName, status: "online", lastSeenAt: new Date() }
      });
  return {
    userId: socialUser.id,
    username: socialUser.username,
    displayName: socialUser.displayName
  };
}

export async function getSocialUserByServerUserId(serverUserId: string): Promise<SocialContext | null> {
  const user = await prisma.socialUser.findUnique({ where: { serverUserId } });
  if (!user) return null;
  return { userId: user.id, username: user.username, displayName: user.displayName };
}


export async function ensureSocialUserByPayload(payload: SocialContext): Promise<SocialContext> {
  const user = await prisma.socialUser.upsert({
    where: { id: payload.userId },
    update: { status: "online", lastSeenAt: new Date() },
    create: {
      id: payload.userId,
      username: payload.username ?? payload.userId,
      displayName: payload.displayName ?? payload.username ?? payload.userId,
      status: "online",
      lastSeenAt: new Date()
    }
  });
  return { userId: user.id, username: user.username, displayName: user.displayName };
}

export async function touchSocialUser(userId: string, status = "online"): Promise<void> {
  await prisma.socialUser.update({ where: { id: userId }, data: { status, lastSeenAt: new Date() } }).catch(() => undefined);
}

export async function getOrCreateRoom(input: {
  title?: string | null;
  roomType?: string | null;
  catalogItemId?: string | null;
  createdByUserId: string;
  participantUserIds?: string[];
}) {
  const roomType = input.roomType ?? "discussion";
  const catalogItemId = await resolveCatalogItemId(input.catalogItemId ?? null);
  if (catalogItemId && ["watchParty", "discussion"].includes(roomType)) {
    const existing = await prisma.chatRoom.findFirst({ where: { catalogItemId, roomType } });
    if (existing) {
      await joinRoom(existing.id, input.createdByUserId);
      for (const userId of input.participantUserIds ?? []) await joinRoom(existing.id, userId);
      return existing;
    }
  }

  const catalogItem = catalogItemId ? await prisma.catalogItem.findUnique({ where: { id: catalogItemId } }) : null;
  const room = await prisma.chatRoom.create({
    data: {
      title: input.title ?? catalogItem?.title ?? (roomType === "watchParty" ? "Watch Party" : "Discussion"),
      roomType,
      catalogItemId,
      catalogTitle: catalogItem?.title ?? null,
      catalogType: catalogItem?.type ?? null,
      posterUrl: catalogItem?.coverUrl ?? null,
      backdropUrl: catalogItem?.backdropUrl ?? null,
      createdByUserId: input.createdByUserId
    }
  });

  await joinRoom(room.id, input.createdByUserId);
  for (const userId of input.participantUserIds ?? []) await joinRoom(room.id, userId);
  return room;
}

export async function resolveCatalogItemId(value: string | null): Promise<string | null> {
  if (!value) return null;
  const catalogItem = await prisma.catalogItem.findFirst({
    where: {
      OR: [
        { id: value },
        { stableKey: value },
        { streamId: value }
      ]
    },
    select: { id: true }
  });
  return catalogItem?.id ?? null;
}

async function resolveCatalogItem(value: string | null) {
  if (!value) return null;
  return prisma.catalogItem.findFirst({
    where: {
      OR: [
        { id: value },
        { stableKey: value },
        { streamId: value }
      ]
    },
    select: safeCatalogSelect()
  });
}

function asInt(value: unknown, fallback = 0): number {
  const parsed = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(parsed)) return fallback;
  return Math.max(0, Math.floor(parsed));
}

function activePresenceCutoff(): Date {
  return new Date(Date.now() - 2 * 60 * 1000);
}

export async function upsertWatchPresence(userId: string, input: WatchPresenceInput) {
  const resolved = await resolveCatalogItem(input.catalogItemId ?? input.catalogKey ?? null);
  const catalogKey = asString(input.catalogKey) ?? resolved?.stableKey ?? resolved?.id;
  if (!catalogKey) throw new Error("catalogKey or catalogItemId is required");

  const room = await getOrCreateRoom({
    title: asString(input.catalogTitle) ?? resolved?.title ?? "Watching Together",
    roomType: "watchParty",
    catalogItemId: resolved?.id ?? catalogKey,
    createdByUserId: userId
  });
  const roomId = asString(input.roomId) ?? room.id;
  await joinRoom(roomId, userId);

  const presence = await prisma.watchPresence.upsert({
    where: { userId_catalogKey: { userId, catalogKey } },
    update: {
      roomId,
      catalogItemId: resolved?.id ?? null,
      catalogTitle: asString(input.catalogTitle) ?? resolved?.title ?? catalogKey,
      catalogType: asString(input.catalogType) ?? resolved?.type ?? null,
      positionMs: asInt(input.positionMs),
      durationMs: asInt(input.durationMs),
      playbackState: asString(input.playbackState) ?? "watching",
      deviceName: asString(input.deviceName)?.slice(0, 120),
      lastHeartbeatAt: new Date(),
      endedAt: null
    },
    create: {
      userId,
      roomId,
      catalogItemId: resolved?.id ?? null,
      catalogKey,
      catalogTitle: asString(input.catalogTitle) ?? resolved?.title ?? catalogKey,
      catalogType: asString(input.catalogType) ?? resolved?.type ?? null,
      positionMs: asInt(input.positionMs),
      durationMs: asInt(input.durationMs),
      playbackState: asString(input.playbackState) ?? "watching",
      deviceName: asString(input.deviceName)?.slice(0, 120)
    },
    include: { user: true, room: true }
  });
  return formatWatchPresence(presence);
}

export async function clearWatchPresence(userId: string, catalogKey?: string | null) {
  const where = { userId, ...(catalogKey ? { catalogKey } : {}), endedAt: null };
  await prisma.watchPresence.updateMany({ where, data: { endedAt: new Date(), playbackState: "stopped" } });
}

export async function getActiveViewersForCatalog(value: string) {
  const resolved = await resolveCatalogItem(value);
  const keys = [value, resolved?.id, resolved?.stableKey, resolved?.streamId].filter(Boolean) as string[];
  const presence = await prisma.watchPresence.findMany({
    where: {
      endedAt: null,
      lastHeartbeatAt: { gte: activePresenceCutoff() },
      OR: [
        { catalogKey: { in: keys } },
        ...(resolved?.id ? [{ catalogItemId: resolved.id }] : [])
      ]
    },
    include: { user: true, room: true },
    orderBy: { lastHeartbeatAt: "desc" },
    take: 100
  });
  return presence.map(formatWatchPresence);
}

export function formatWatchPresence(presence: any) {
  return {
    id: presence.id,
    roomId: presence.roomId,
    catalogItemId: presence.catalogItemId,
    catalogKey: presence.catalogKey,
    catalogTitle: presence.catalogTitle,
    catalogType: presence.catalogType,
    positionMs: presence.positionMs,
    durationMs: presence.durationMs,
    playbackState: presence.playbackState,
    deviceName: presence.deviceName,
    lastHeartbeatAt: presence.lastHeartbeatAt,
    user: presence.user ? {
      id: presence.user.id,
      username: presence.user.username,
      displayName: presence.user.displayName,
      avatarUrl: presence.user.avatarUrl,
      status: presence.user.status
    } : null,
    room: presence.room ? formatRoom(presence.room) : null
  };
}

export async function requestFriendship(userId: string, otherUserId: string) {
  if (userId === otherUserId) throw new Error("Cannot friend yourself");
  const other = await prisma.socialUser.findUnique({ where: { id: otherUserId } });
  if (!other) throw new Error("Social user not found");
  const inverse = await prisma.socialFriendship.findUnique({
    where: { requesterUserId_addresseeUserId: { requesterUserId: otherUserId, addresseeUserId: userId } },
    include: { requester: true, addressee: true }
  });
  if (inverse?.status === "pending") {
    return prisma.socialFriendship.update({
      where: { id: inverse.id },
      data: { status: "accepted", respondedAt: new Date() },
      include: { requester: true, addressee: true }
    });
  }
  if (inverse) return inverse;
  return prisma.socialFriendship.upsert({
    where: { requesterUserId_addresseeUserId: { requesterUserId: userId, addresseeUserId: otherUserId } },
    update: { status: "pending", respondedAt: null },
    create: { requesterUserId: userId, addresseeUserId: otherUserId, status: "pending" },
    include: { requester: true, addressee: true }
  });
}

export async function respondToFriendship(userId: string, friendshipId: string, status: string) {
  const normalized = status === "accepted" ? "accepted" : status === "blocked" ? "blocked" : "declined";
  const friendship = await prisma.socialFriendship.findUnique({ where: { id: friendshipId } });
  if (!friendship || ![friendship.requesterUserId, friendship.addresseeUserId].includes(userId)) {
    throw new Error("Friend request not found");
  }
  return prisma.socialFriendship.update({
    where: { id: friendshipId },
    data: { status: normalized, respondedAt: new Date() },
    include: { requester: true, addressee: true }
  });
}

export function formatFriendship(friendship: any, currentUserId: string) {
  const other = friendship.requesterUserId === currentUserId ? friendship.addressee : friendship.requester;
  return {
    id: friendship.id,
    status: friendship.status,
    createdAt: friendship.createdAt,
    respondedAt: friendship.respondedAt,
    otherUser: other ? {
      id: other.id,
      username: other.username,
      displayName: other.displayName,
      avatarUrl: other.avatarUrl,
      status: other.status,
      lastSeenAt: other.lastSeenAt
    } : null,
    direction: friendship.requesterUserId === currentUserId ? "outgoing" : "incoming"
  };
}

export async function createViewingParty(userId: string, input: {
  catalogItemId?: string | null;
  catalogKey?: string | null;
  title?: string | null;
  scheduledFor?: string | null;
  inviteUserIds?: string[];
}) {
  const catalog = await resolveCatalogItem(input.catalogItemId ?? input.catalogKey ?? null);
  const room = await getOrCreateRoom({
    title: asString(input.title) ?? `Watch Party: ${catalog?.title ?? asString(input.catalogKey) ?? "Movie Night"}`,
    roomType: "watchParty",
    catalogItemId: catalog?.id ?? asString(input.catalogKey),
    createdByUserId: userId,
    participantUserIds: input.inviteUserIds
  });
  const party = await prisma.viewingParty.create({
    data: {
      roomId: room.id,
      createdByUserId: userId,
      catalogItemId: catalog?.id ?? null,
      catalogKey: asString(input.catalogKey) ?? catalog?.stableKey ?? catalog?.id ?? null,
      catalogTitle: catalog?.title ?? asString(input.title) ?? "Viewing Party",
      catalogType: catalog?.type ?? null,
      title: asString(input.title) ?? `Watch Party: ${catalog?.title ?? "Movie Night"}`,
      scheduledFor: asString(input.scheduledFor) ? new Date(asString(input.scheduledFor)!) : null,
      invites: {
        create: (input.inviteUserIds ?? []).filter((id) => id !== userId).map((inviteeId) => ({ userId: inviteeId }))
      }
    },
    include: { room: { include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } } }, createdBy: true, invites: { include: { user: true } } }
  });
  await createSystemMessage(room.id, "Viewing party created.");
  return formatViewingParty(party);
}

export async function respondToViewingPartyInvite(userId: string, inviteId: string, status: string) {
  const normalized = status === "accepted" ? "accepted" : "declined";
  const existing = await prisma.viewingPartyInvite.findFirst({ where: { id: inviteId, userId }, select: { id: true } });
  if (!existing) throw new Error("Invite not found");
  const invite = await prisma.viewingPartyInvite.update({
    where: { id: existing.id },
    data: { status: normalized, respondedAt: new Date() },
    include: { party: { include: { room: { include: { _count: { select: { participants: true } } } }, createdBy: true, invites: { include: { user: true } } } }, user: true }
  });
  if (normalized === "accepted") await joinRoom(invite.party.roomId, userId);
  return formatViewingParty(invite.party);
}

export function formatViewingParty(party: any) {
  return {
    id: party.id,
    title: party.title,
    status: party.status,
    scheduledFor: party.scheduledFor,
    catalogItemId: party.catalogItemId,
    catalogKey: party.catalogKey,
    catalogTitle: party.catalogTitle,
    catalogType: party.catalogType,
    playbackState: party.playbackState ?? "idle",
    currentPositionMs: party.currentPositionMs ?? 0,
    durationMs: party.durationMs ?? 0,
    controlledByUserId: party.controlledByUserId ?? null,
    lastControlAt: party.lastControlAt ?? null,
    room: party.room ? formatRoom(party.room) : null,
    createdBy: party.createdBy ? {
      id: party.createdBy.id,
      username: party.createdBy.username,
      displayName: party.createdBy.displayName,
      avatarUrl: party.createdBy.avatarUrl
    } : null,
    invites: Array.isArray(party.invites) ? party.invites.map((invite: any) => ({
      id: invite.id,
      status: invite.status,
      createdAt: invite.createdAt,
      respondedAt: invite.respondedAt,
      user: invite.user ? {
        id: invite.user.id,
        username: invite.user.username,
        displayName: invite.user.displayName,
        avatarUrl: invite.user.avatarUrl,
        status: invite.user.status
      } : null
    })) : []
  };
}

export async function joinRoom(roomId: string, userId: string) {
  await prisma.chatParticipant.upsert({
    where: { roomId_userId: { roomId, userId } },
    update: { isActive: true, lastSeenAt: new Date(), leftAt: null },
    create: { roomId, userId, isActive: true, lastSeenAt: new Date() }
  });
}

export async function leaveRoom(roomId: string, userId: string) {
  await prisma.chatParticipant.upsert({
    where: { roomId_userId: { roomId, userId } },
    update: { isActive: false, leftAt: new Date(), lastSeenAt: new Date() },
    create: { roomId, userId, isActive: false, leftAt: new Date(), lastSeenAt: new Date() }
  });
}

export async function createMessage(roomId: string, senderUserId: string, input: SocialMessageInput) {
  await joinRoom(roomId, senderUserId);
  const text = (asString(input.text) ?? "").slice(0, 2000);
  const messageType = asString(input.messageType) ?? (input.sharePayload ? "mediaShare" : "text");
  const clientMessageId = asString(input.clientMessageId);

  if (!text && !input.sharePayload && messageType !== "system") {
    throw new Error("Message cannot be empty");
  }

  if (clientMessageId) {
    const existing = await prisma.chatMessage.findFirst({
      where: { roomId, clientMessageId, senderUserId },
      include: { sender: true }
    });
    if (existing) return formatMessage(existing);
  }

  const message = await prisma.chatMessage.create({
    data: {
      roomId,
      senderUserId,
      clientMessageId,
      messageType,
      text,
      sharePayloadJson: safeJson(sanitizeSharePayload(messageType, input.sharePayload))
    },
    include: { sender: true }
  });

  await prisma.chatRoom.update({
    where: { id: roomId },
    data: {
      lastMessagePreview: text.slice(0, 160) || (messageType === "listShare" ? "Shared a list" : messageType === "mediaShare" ? "Shared a title" : "New message"),
      lastMessageAt: message.createdAt,
      updatedAt: new Date()
    }
  });

  return formatMessage(message);
}

export async function createSystemMessage(roomId: string, text: string) {
  const room = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id: roomId } });
  if (!room) return null;
  const senderId = room.createdByUserId;
  if (!senderId) return null;
  return createMessage(roomId, senderId, { messageType: "system", text });
}

export function formatMessage(message: any) {
  const reactions = Array.isArray(message.reactions)
    ? message.reactions.reduce((acc: Record<string, { count: number; users: Array<{ id: string; displayName?: string | null }> }>, reaction: any) => {
        const key = String(reaction.reaction ?? "");
        if (!key) return acc;
        acc[key] ??= { count: 0, users: [] };
        acc[key].count += 1;
        acc[key].users.push({ id: reaction.userId, displayName: reaction.user?.displayName ?? reaction.user?.username ?? null });
        return acc;
      }, {})
    : {};

  return {
    id: message.id,
    clientMessageId: message.clientMessageId,
    roomId: message.roomId,
    senderUserId: message.senderUserId,
    senderDisplayName: message.sender?.displayName ?? message.sender?.username ?? "Unknown",
    senderAvatarUrl: message.sender?.avatarUrl ?? null,
    messageType: message.messageType,
    text: message.text,
    createdAt: message.createdAt,
    editedAt: message.editedAt,
    deletedAt: message.deletedAt,
    reactions,
    sharePayload: parseJsonObject(message.sharePayloadJson, null)
  };
}

export function formatRoom(room: any, unreadCount = 0) {
  return {
    id: room.id,
    title: room.title,
    roomType: room.roomType,
    catalogItemId: room.catalogItemId,
    catalogTitle: room.catalogTitle,
    catalogType: room.catalogType,
    posterUrl: room.posterUrl,
    backdropUrl: room.backdropUrl,
    createdByUserId: room.createdByUserId,
    participantCount: room._count?.participants ?? room.participants?.length ?? 0,
    lastMessagePreview: room.lastMessagePreview,
    lastMessageAt: room.lastMessageAt,
    unreadCount
  };
}

export async function getUnreadCount(roomId: string, userId: string): Promise<number> {
  const participant = await prisma.chatParticipant.findUnique({ where: { roomId_userId: { roomId, userId } } });
  const readAt = participant?.lastReadAt ?? new Date(0);
  return prisma.chatMessage.count({ where: { roomId, createdAt: { gt: readAt }, NOT: { senderUserId: userId } } });
}

export async function buildMediaShareFromCatalog(catalogItemId: string): Promise<MediaShareInput> {
  const item = await prisma.catalogItem.findUnique({ where: { id: catalogItemId }, select: safeCatalogSelect() });
  if (!item) throw new Error("Catalog item not found");
  return safeMediaPayload({
    catalogItemId: item.id,
    title: item.title,
    type: item.type,
    year: item.year,
    posterUrl: item.coverUrl,
    backdropUrl: item.backdropUrl,
    description: item.description,
    rating: item.rating,
    genre: parseJsonObject<string[]>(item.genreJson, [])
  });
}

// FILE: server/src/services/socialTokenService.ts
================================================================================
import { createHmac, timingSafeEqual } from "node:crypto";
import { config } from "../config.js";

export type SocialTokenPayload = {
  userId: string;
  username?: string | null;
  displayName?: string | null;
  exp: number;
};

function base64UrlEncode(value: string): string {
  return Buffer.from(value, "utf8").toString("base64url");
}

function base64UrlDecode(value: string): string {
  return Buffer.from(value, "base64url").toString("utf8");
}

function sign(data: string): string {
  return createHmac("sha256", config.socialTokenSecret).update(data).digest("base64url");
}

export function createSocialToken(payload: Omit<SocialTokenPayload, "exp">, ttlSeconds = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60): string {
  const fullPayload: SocialTokenPayload = {
    ...payload,
    exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + ttlSeconds
  };
  const encodedPayload = base64UrlEncode(JSON.stringify(fullPayload));
  return `${encodedPayload}.${sign(encodedPayload)}`;
}

export function verifySocialToken(token: string): SocialTokenPayload | null {
  const [encodedPayload, signature] = token.split(".");
  if (!encodedPayload || !signature) return null;

  const expected = sign(encodedPayload);
  const expectedBuffer = Buffer.from(expected);
  const actualBuffer = Buffer.from(signature);
  if (expectedBuffer.length !== actualBuffer.length || !timingSafeEqual(expectedBuffer, actualBuffer)) return null;

  try {
    const payload = JSON.parse(base64UrlDecode(encodedPayload)) as SocialTokenPayload;
    if (!payload.userId || payload.exp < Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)) return null;
    return payload;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

// FILE: server/src/services/tmdbService.ts
================================================================================
import { config } from "../config.js";

async function tmdbFetch(
  path: string,
  params: Record<string, string | number | undefined> = {},
  method = "GET",
  body?: any
) {
  if (!config.tmdbApiKey) {
    throw new Error("TMDB API key is not configured on the server.");
  }
  const url = new URL(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3${path}`);
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(params)) {
    if (value != null && String(value).trim()) {
      url.searchParams.set(key, String(value));
    }
  }
  const headers: Record<string, string> = {
    accept: "application/json",
    "content-type": "application/json",
  };
  if (config.tmdbApiKey.startsWith("ey")) {
    headers.authorization = `Bearer ${config.tmdbApiKey}`;
  } else {
    url.searchParams.set("api_key", config.tmdbApiKey);
  }

  const response = await fetch(url.toString(), {
    method,
    headers,
    body: body ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errorText = await response.text().catch(() => "");
    throw new Error(`TMDb API error (${response.status}): ${errorText || response.statusText}`);
  }

  return response.json();
}

function imageUrl(path?: string | null, size = "w500"): string | null {
  return path ? `https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/${size}${path}` : null;
}

function yearFrom(value?: string | null): string | null {
  const match = String(value ?? "").match(/\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b/);
  return match?.[1] ?? null;
}

function publicTmdbItem(record: Record<string, unknown>, mediaType: "movie" | "tv", sourceLabel: string) {
  return {
    id: String(record.id ?? ""),
    streamId: "",
    title: String(record.title ?? record.name ?? "Untitled"),
    type: mediaType === "tv" ? "series" : "movie",
    contentType: mediaType === "tv" ? "series" : "movie",
    year: yearFrom(String(record.release_date ?? record.first_air_date ?? "")),
    rating: typeof record.vote_average === "number" ? record.vote_average : null,
    description: String(record.overview ?? ""),
    coverUrl: imageUrl(String(record.poster_path ?? "")),
    backdropUrl: imageUrl(String(record.backdrop_path ?? ""), "w1280"),
    metadataProvider: "TMDb",
    metadataId: String(record.id ?? ""),
    tmdbId: String(record.id ?? ""),
    sourceLabel,
  };
}

export async function getTmdbRequestToken(): Promise<{ request_token: string; authentication_url: string }> {
  const data = (await tmdbFetch("/authentication/token/new")) as {
    success: boolean;
    request_token: string;
  };
  if (!data.success || !data.request_token) {
    throw new Error("Failed to generate TMDB request token.");
  }
  return {
    request_token: data.request_token,
    authentication_url: `https://www.themoviedb.org/authenticate/${data.request_token}`,
  };
}

export async function createTmdbSession(requestToken: string): Promise<{ session_id: string }> {
  const data = (await tmdbFetch("/authentication/session/new", {}, "POST", {
    request_token: requestToken,
  })) as { success: boolean; session_id: string };
  if (!data.success || !data.session_id) {
    throw new Error("Failed to create TMDB session. Ensure the token has been approved by the user.");
  }
  return { session_id: data.session_id };
}

export async function getTmdbAccountDetails(sessionId: string): Promise<{ id: number; username: string }> {
  const data = (await tmdbFetch("/account", { session_id: sessionId })) as {
    id: number;
    username: string;
  };
  if (!data.id) {
    throw new Error("Failed to retrieve TMDB account details.");
  }
  return {
    id: data.id,
    username: data.username,
  };
}

export async function getTmdbCollection(
  collection: "popular" | "top_rated" | "trending",
  type: "movie" | "tv" | "all" = "movie",
  limit = 40
) {
  const mediaTypes: Array<"movie" | "tv"> = type === "all" ? ["movie", "tv"] : [type];
  const items: unknown[] = [];
  const maxItems = Math.max(1, Math.min(limit, 300));
  const pagesPerType = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(maxItems / mediaTypes.length / 20));
  for (const mediaType of mediaTypes) {
    const path = collection === "trending" ? `/trending/${mediaType}/day` : `/${mediaType}/${collection}`;
    for (let page = 1; page <= pagesPerType && items.length < maxItems; page += 1) {
      const data = await tmdbFetch(path, { language: "en-US", page }) as { results?: unknown[] };
      const results = Array.isArray(data.results) ? data.results : [];
      if (results.length === 0) break;
      items.push(...results.map((item) =>
        publicTmdbItem(
          item as Record<string, unknown>,
          mediaType,
          `TMDb ${collection.replace("_", " ")}`
        )
      ));
    }
  }
  return items.slice(0, maxItems);
}

export async function getTmdbAccountWatchlist(
  sessionId: string,
  accountId: string,
  type: "movie" | "tv" | "all" = "all",
  limit = 40
) {
  const mediaTypes: Array<"movie" | "tv"> = type === "all" ? ["movie", "tv"] : [type];
  const items: unknown[] = [];
  for (const mediaType of mediaTypes) {
    const data = await tmdbFetch(`/account/${accountId}/watchlist/${mediaType}`, {
      session_id: sessionId,
      language: "en-US",
      sort_by: "created_at.desc",
      page: 1,
    }) as { results?: unknown[] };
    const results = Array.isArray(data.results) ? data.results : [];
    items.push(...results.map((item) =>
      publicTmdbItem(item as Record<string, unknown>, mediaType, "TMDb Watchlist")
    ));
  }
  return items.slice(0, Math.max(1, Math.min(limit, 100)));
}

// FILE: server/src/services/webSearchService.ts
================================================================================
import { prisma } from "../lib/prisma.js";

export type WebSearchResult = {
  title: string;
  url: string;
  snippet: string;
  source: "duckduckgo" | "instantAnswer" | "fallback";
};

const cooldownByQuery = new Map<string, number>();
const cooldownMs = 1500;
const cacheTtlMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

function cleanResult(result: Partial<WebSearchResult>, source: WebSearchResult["source"]): WebSearchResult | null {
  const title = String(result.title ?? "").trim();
  const url = String(result.url ?? "").trim();
  const snippet = String(result.snippet ?? "").trim();
  if (!title && !snippet) return null;
  return {
    title: title || "DuckDuckGo result",
    url,
    snippet,
    source
  };
}

async function searchWithDuckDuckScrape(query: string, maxResults: number): Promise<WebSearchResult[]> {
  const module = (await import("duck-duck-scrape")) as {
    search?: (query: string, options?: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<{ results?: Array<Record<string, unknown>> }>;
  };
  if (!module.search) return [];
  const response = await module.search(query, { safeSearch: "STRICT" });
  return (response.results ?? [])
    .slice(0, maxResults)
    .map((result) =>
      cleanResult(
        {
          title: typeof result.title === "string" ? result.title : undefined,
          url: typeof result.url === "string" ? result.url : undefined,
          snippet: typeof result.description === "string"
            ? result.description
            : typeof result.snippet === "string"
              ? result.snippet
              : undefined
        },
        "duckduckgo"
      )
    )
    .filter((result): result is WebSearchResult => result != null);
}

async function searchWithInstantAnswer(query: string, maxResults: number): Promise<WebSearchResult[]> {
  const url = `https://api.duckduckgo.com/?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&format=json&no_html=1&skip_disambig=1`;
  const response = await fetch(url);
  if (!response.ok) return [];
  const data = (await response.json()) as {
    AbstractText?: string;
    AbstractURL?: string;
    Heading?: string;
    RelatedTopics?: Array<{ Text?: string; FirstURL?: string }>;
  };
  const results: WebSearchResult[] = [];
  const abstractResult = cleanResult(
    { title: data.Heading, url: data.AbstractURL, snippet: data.AbstractText },
    "instantAnswer"
  );
  if (abstractResult) results.push(abstractResult);
  for (const topic of data.RelatedTopics ?? []) {
    const result = cleanResult(
      { title: topic.Text?.split(" - ")[0], url: topic.FirstURL, snippet: topic.Text },
      "instantAnswer"
    );
    if (result) results.push(result);
  }
  return results.slice(0, maxResults);
}

export async function searchWeb(query: string, options: { maxResults?: number } = {}): Promise<WebSearchResult[]> {
  const normalizedQuery = query.trim().slice(0, 200);
  const maxResults = Math.max(1, Math.min(options.maxResults ?? 5, 10));
  if (!normalizedQuery) return [];

  try {
    const cached = await prisma.webSearchCache.findUnique({ where: { query: normalizedQuery } });
    if (cached && cached.expiresAt > new Date()) {
      return JSON.parse(cached.resultsJson) as WebSearchResult[];
    }
  } catch {
    return [];
  }

  const lastSearchAt = cooldownByQuery.get(normalizedQuery) ?? 0;
  if (Date.now() - lastSearchAt < cooldownMs) return [];
  cooldownByQuery.set(normalizedQuery, Date.now());

  let results: WebSearchResult[] = [];
  try {
    results = await searchWithDuckDuckScrape(normalizedQuery, maxResults);
  } catch {
    results = [];
  }

  if (results.length === 0) {
    try {
      results = await searchWithInstantAnswer(normalizedQuery, maxResults);
    } catch {
      results = [];
    }
  }

  try {
    await prisma.webSearchCache.upsert({
      where: { query: normalizedQuery },
      update: {
        resultsJson: JSON.stringify(results),
        expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + cacheTtlMs)
      },
      create: {
        query: normalizedQuery,
        resultsJson: JSON.stringify(results),
        expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + cacheTtlMs)
      }
    });
  } catch {
    return results;
  }

  return results;
}

      url?: string;
      description?: string;
      snippet?: string;
    }>;
  }>;

// FILE: server/scripts/init-sqlite.mjs
================================================================================
import { PrismaClient } from "@prisma/client";

const prisma = new PrismaClient();

const statements = [
  `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "Profile" (
    "id" TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    "name" TEXT,
    "userId" TEXT,
    "isKids" BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
    "createdAt" DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    "updatedAt" DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
  )`,
  `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "ServerUser" (
    "id" TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    "username" TEXT NOT NULL,
    "passwordHash" TEXT NOT NULL,
    "displayName" TEXT,
    "isAdmin" BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
    "createdAt" DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    "updatedAt" DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
  )`,
  `CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "ServerUser_username_key" ON "ServerUser"("username")`,
  `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "CatalogItem" (
    "id" TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    "stableKey" TEXT NOT NULL,
    "streamId" TEXT,
    "title" TEXT NOT NULL,
    "type" TEXT NOT NULL,

  `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "SharedMediaList" (

  )`,

    CONSTRAINT "SharedMediaListItem_catalogItemId_fkey" FOREIGN KEY ("catalogItemId") REFERENCES "CatalogItem" ("id") ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
  )`,

  `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "SharedMediaListItem_catalogItemId_idx" ON "SharedMediaListItem"("catalogItemId")`
];

try {
  for (const statement of statements) {
    await prisma.$executeRawUnsafe(statement);
  }
  console.log("SQLite schema is ready.");
} finally {
  await prisma.$disconnect();
}
